MRSMaYsSAT-SadunVEN-Ven.MN-MoonTUP-Jupite，Mcy-Mercuy GMN-Gemimi， CR-Cancv,LEO,VRG- Vingo,LBR Libxa, ScP-Scarpio,SA CAP- Capnicogn, Aas-Aguarius,Psc· Pisces 


See the Kalachakra. There we count from Jeeva etc. and Delta. In the 4th Pada of Mrigasira Jeeva is in Sagittarius and Deha in Aries. Therefore, by deducting the total years of Sagittarius from Gemini namely 77 from 90 years 9 months we get the expired period of Taurus, namely 13 years, 9 months. By deducting this from the present 16 years of Venus, we will get 2 years 3 months as the balance of Dasha at birth. Accordingly, like Vimshottari Dasha, the order of Dasha will be Taurus, Aries, Sagittarius, Scorpio etc. 

<table><tr><td>The planet</td><td>Mars</td><td>1</td><td>9 Rahu</td><td>8</td><td>7</td><td>6</td><td>5</td><td>4</td><td>3</td></tr><tr><td>s at birth</td><td>2</td><td>Ketu</td><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td><td>Rahu Moon</td></tr><tr><td>Lord of Dasha</td><td>Taurus</td><td>Aries</td><td>Sagittarius</td><td>Scorpio</td><td>Libra</td><td>Virg o</td><td>Le o</td><td>Canc er</td><td>Gemini</td></tr><tr><td>Years</td><td>2</td><td>7</td><td>10</td><td>7</td><td>16</td><td>9</td><td>5</td><td>21</td><td>9</td></tr><tr><td>Month s</td><td>3</td><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td></tr></table>

# पदस्य भुक्तघट्याद्यैाः स्वाब्दमानं हिं ििाः । भभोगाङ् गिहृिं भुक्तं भोग्यं मानाद् तर्शोथधिम् ॥ ९२॥

92. Multiply the past Ghatikas, palas etc. of the present Pada of Nakshatra by the number of years and divide the product by the fourth part of Bhabhog. The years etc. so obtained may then be deducted from the total Dasha period. In, result will be the balance of Dasha at birth in years, months etc. 

Alternative Method 

# चन्द्राङ्कांशकला भुक्तााः स्वाब्दमानहिा हृिााः । द्वद्वशत्या भुक्तर्र्षाद्यं ज्ञेयं भोग्यं ििो बुधैाः ॥ ९३॥

93. The past kalas (कला) of the Navamsha in which the Moon may be posited should be multiplied by the years allotted to the Moon and the product be divided by 200. The resulting years etc. will be the expired portion of the Dasha. By deducting the balance from the total number of years, is obtained the balance of Dasha at birth. 

Note: In modern terminology, we mention the longitude of the planets in rashi, degrees and minutes. The 'minutes' are kala, 

Example: Suppose that at the time of birth of a person in Krittika Nakshatra the longitude of the Moon (Chandra Spast- चन्द्र स्पष्ट) is 1/4/50. This converted into kalas will be 2090. Divide by 800 the kalas of one Nakshatra the result will be the 2nd Nakshatra namely Bharini and the remainder will be 490. These will be the past kalas of Krittika. There are 200 kalas in one Pada (Navamsha). Divide 490 the past kalas of Krittika by 200. We will then get 2 as past Padas and the remainder 90 will represent the past kalas of the present Nakshatra. By multiplying this by 83 the Dasha years, we will get 7470 which divided by 200 will indicate the expired portion of the Dasha as 37 years, 4 months and 6 days. By deducting the years of Dehamsa commencing from Taurus in the order Taurus, Aries Pisces, Aquarius $( 1 6 + 7 + 1 0 + 4 = 3 7 )$ ), we will get 0 years, 4 months and 6 days. This will be the expired portion of Capricorn. Deducting this from 4 the Dasha period of Capricorn, we get the balance of Dasha of Capricorn, namely 3 years, 7 months. and. 24 days. See in this connection the Savya Kalachakra. 

<table><tr><td>10</td><td>9</td><td>1</td><td>2</td><td>3</td><td>4</td><td>1</td><td>12</td><td>11</td><td></td></tr><tr><td>Capricorn</td><td>Sagittarius</td><td>Aries</td><td>Taurus</td><td>Gemini</td><td>Taurus</td><td>Aries</td><td>Piscies</td><td>Aquarius</td><td></td></tr><tr><td>3</td><td>10</td><td>7</td><td>16</td><td>9</td><td>16</td><td>7</td><td>10</td><td>4</td><td>Yearss</td></tr><tr><td>7</td><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td><td>Month</td></tr><tr><td>24</td><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td><td>Dayss</td></tr></table>

सव्याख्ये प्रथमांशो याः स देह इति कथ्यिे । 

अन्त्यांशो जीर्सञ्ज्ज्ञाः स्याद् तर्लोममपसव्यके ॥ ९४॥ 

देहाद्वदं गणयेि् सव्ये जीर्ाद्वदमपसव्यके । 

एर्ं तर्ज्ञाय दैर्ज्ञस्तिस्तत्फलमाद्वदशेि् ॥ ९५॥ 

94-95. In the Savya Chakra the first Amsa (अंश) is called Deha $( \overrightarrow { G } \overrightarrow { 6 } )$ and the last Amsa (अंश) Jeeva (जीव). The opposite is the case in the Apsavya Chakra (first Amsa is Jeeva and the last Deha). Therefore, the calculations should be based on the Deha etc. in the Savya Chakra and on Jeeva etc. in Apsavya Chakra. 

Movements (Gati गतत) of Rāśhis (Signs) in the Kalachakra 

कालचक्रगतिाः प्रोक्ता ष्टरधा पूर्वमहष्टर्षवथभाः । 

मण्डूकाख्या गतििैका मकव टीसञ्ज्ज्ञकाऽपिा ॥ ९६॥ 

सस ंहार्लोकनाख्या च िृिीया परिकीतिविा । 

उत्प्लुत्य गमनं तर्ज्ञा मण्डूकाख्यं प्रचक्षिे ॥ ९७॥ 

पृष्ठिो गमनं नाम मकव टीसञ्ज्ज्ञकं िथा । 

र्ाणाच्च नर्पयविं गतिाः ससंहार्लोकनम् ॥ ९८॥ 

96-98. There are three kinds of movements (Gati) of the Rāśhis in the Kalachakra, namely, Mandooki (मण्डूकी), Markati (मकध टी) and Simhavlokan (शसंहावलोकन). The movement of one sign by jumping over one sign is known as Mandook motion. Backward movement to the previous sign is called Markati gati (गतत). The movement of a sign to the 5th and 9th sign is said to be Simhavlokan. 

कन्याककव टयोाः ससंहयुग्मयोमवण्डूय्की गतिाः । 

ककव के सरिणोिेर्ं कथ्यिे मकव टीं गतिाः ॥ ९९॥ 

# मीनर्ृसिकयोिापमेर्षयोाः सैंद्वहकी गतिाः । इति सथञ्चन्त्य तर्ज्ञेयं कालचक्रदशाफलम् ॥ १००॥

99-100. Movement from Virgo to Cancer and from Leo to Gemini is Mandooki gati. Movement from Leo to Cancer is Markati gag, Movement from Pisces to Scorpio and from Sagittarius to Aries is Simhavlokan gati. 

Effects of Dasha of signs as a result of these movements (गतत) 

मण्डूकगतिकाले द्वह सव्ये बन्धुजने भयम् । ष्टपरोर्ा तर्र्षशिागग्नज्विचोिाद्वदजं भयम् ॥ १०१॥ के सिीयुग्ममण्डूके मािुमविण्माद्वदशेि् । स्वमृतिं िाजथभतिं र्ा सगन्नपािभयं भर्ेि् ॥ १०२॥ 

101-102. The effects of the Dasha of the signs with Mandookigati in the savya chakra are distress to friends, relations, parents and elders, and there is likely to be cause for trouble from poison, weapons, thieves and enemies. In the Mandook Dasha of the movement of sign from Leo to Gemini, there is likelihood of the death of the mother or self, trouble from Government (or king) and possibility of brain fever. 

मकव टीगमने सव्ये धनधान्यपशुक्षयाः । ष्टपिुमविणमालस्यं ित्समानां च र् मृतिाः ॥ १०३॥ 

103. The effects of the Dasha of sign with Markati gati (गतत) in the savya chakra, are loss of wealth. Agricultural products and animals, death of father or an elderly close relation, and feeling of lethargy. 

सव्ये ससंहार्लोके िु पशुभीतिभवर्ेन्नृणाम् । सुहृत्स्नेहाद्वदनाशि समानजनपीडनम् ॥ १०४॥ पिनं र्ाष्टप कू पादौ तर्र्षशस्र्िागग्नजं भयम् । र्ाहनाि् पिनं र्ाष्टप ज्विातिवाः िाननाशनम् ॥ १०५॥ 

104-105. The effects of the Dasha of the signs with Simhavlokan gati (गतत) in the savya chakra are, possibility of injury from animals, loss of amity with friends, distress to near relations, drowning in a well, fall from animals, possibility, of harm from poison, weapons and diseases and destruction of residential dwelling. 

मण्डूकगमने र्ामे िीसुिाद्वदप्रपीडनम् । ज्विं च श्वापदाद् भीतिं र्देद् तर्ज्ञाः पदच्युतिम् ॥ १०६॥ मकव टीगमने र्ाऽष्टप जलभीतिं पदच्युतिम् । ष्टपिुनाशं नृपक्रोधं दगािण्याटनं ु र्देि् ॥ १०७॥ 

# सस ंहार्लोकने र्ामे पदभ्रंशाः ष्टपिुमृवतिाः ।

# ित्समानमृतिर्ाऽष्टप फलमेर्ं तर्श्रचियेि् ॥ १०८॥

106-108. In the Dasha of the signs with the Mandooki gati in the Apsavya chakra, the effects will be distress to wife and conditions and loss of children, possibility of feverish conditions and Joss of position. 

In the Dasha of the signs with the Markati gati there may be danger from watery places, loss of position, distress to father, punishment from Government and wandering in the forests. 

In the Dasha of signs with the Simhavlokan gati in the Apsavya chakra, there may be destruction of the dwelling and death of father etc. 

मीनाि् िु र्ृसिके यािे ज्विो भर्ति तनसििाः । 

कन्यािाः ककव टे यािे भ्रािृबन्धुतर्नाशनम् ॥ १०९॥ 

ससंहात्तु तमथुने यािे ण्डिया व्याथधभवर्ेद् ध्रुर्म् । 

ककव टाच्च हिौ यािे र्धो भर्ति देद्वहनाम् ॥ ११०॥ 

ष्टपिृबन्धुमृतिं तर्द्याच्चापान्मेर्षे गिे पुनाः । 

भयं पापखगैयुवक्ते शुभखेटयुिे शुभम् ॥ १११॥ 

109-111: If the movement be from Pisces to Scorpio, the native may suffer from fever. If the movement be from Virgo to Cancer, there may be loss of brothers and kinsmen. If it be from Leo to Gemini, there may be ill health of the wife. If it be from Leo to Cancer, the native may die. If it be from Sagittarius to Aries, there may be death of uncles and similar relations. If the sign be in conjunct ion with a malefic, adverse conditions may be expected in the Dasha of that sign. Favourable effects will be felt in its Dasha if the sign be in conjunction with a benefice. 

शुभं र्ाऽप्यशुभं र्ाऽष्टप कालचक्रदशाफलम् । 

िासशद्वदक्भागिो र्ाष्टप पूर्ाद्वदद्वदग्िभििाि् ॥ ११२॥ 

िष्टद्दगार्भागे र्क्तव्यं िद्दशासमये नृणाम् । 

यथोपदेशमागेण सर्ेर्षां द्वद्वजसत्तम ॥ ११३॥ 

112-113. O Brahmin! In the Kalachakra Dasha favourable and unfavourable effects may be predicted after taking into account the directions of the signs and planets. 

कन्यािाः ककव टे यािे पूर्वभागे महत्फलम् । 

उत्तिं देशमाश्रित्य शुभा यारा भतर्ष्यति ॥ ११४॥ 

ससंहात्तु तमथुने यािे पूर्वभागं तर्र्जवयेि् । 

कायािेऽष्टप च नैऋत्यां सुखं यारा भतर्ष्यति ॥ ११५॥ 

ककव टाि् ससंहभे यािे कायवहातनि दसक्षणे । दसक्षणां द्वदशमाश्रित्य प्रत्यगागमनं भर्ेि् ॥ ११६॥ मीनात्तु र्ृसिके यािे उदग् गच्छति सङ्कटम् । चापाच्च मकिे यािे सङ्कटं जायिे ध्रुर्म् ॥ ११७॥ चापान्मेर्षे िु यारायां व्याथधबवन्धो मृतिभवर्ेि् । र्ृसिके िु सुखं सम्पि् िीप्राब्दप्ति द्वद्वजोत्तम ॥ ११८॥ ससंहाच्च ककव टे यािे पष्टचचमां र्जवयेष्टद्दशम् । शुभयोगे शुभं ब्रूयादशुभे त्वशुभं फलम् ॥ ११९॥ 

114-119. If the movement be from Virgo to Cancer, good results are realised in places located in the East and at that time journeys to the places in the North prove fruitful. Unfavourable effects will be felt in places located in the West and the South. It will be advisable not to undertake journeys in those directions in the Dasha of these signs. 

If the movement be from Leo to Gemini, no journey should be undertaken to places located in the East. However, the journeys to the South-West will prove fruitful in the Dasha of those signs if the movement be from Cancer to Leo, the journeys during that period to the South will prove unfavourable and result in loss, and the native has to return from the South to the West. 

If the movement be from Pisces to Scorpio, there will be distress if the native goes to the North. The same would happen if the movement be from Sagittarius to Capricorn. There may be ill health, imprisonment or death if the movement be from Sagittarius to Aries. There may be gains of comforts and property and marriage if the movement be from Sagittarius to Scorpio. 

It will not be advisable to undertake journeys to the West during the related period if the movement be from Leo to Cancer. But favourable results should be predicted if the signs are in conjunction with benefices and adverse if the conjunction be with malefic. 

शूििौिि मेर्षांशे लक्ष्मीर्ांि र्ृर्षांशके । तमथुनांशे भर्ेज्ज्ञानी ककांशे नृपतिभवर्ेि् ॥ १२०॥ ससंहांशे िाजमान्यि कन्यांशे पण्डण्डिो भर्ेि् । िुलांशे िाजमन्त्री स्याद् र्ृसिकांशे च तनधवनाः ॥ १२१॥ चापांशे ज्ञानसम्पन्नो मिकांशे च पापकृ ि् । कु म्भांशे च र्णणक्कमा मीनांशे धनधान्यर्ान् ॥ १२२॥ 

120-122. According to the above-mentioned Kalachakra the person born in the Amsas of the various signs will be as under: - Aries Amsa-Brave and a thief. 

Taurus Amsa-Wealthy 

Gemini Amsa-Learned 

Cancer Amsa-King (or like a king) 

Leo Amsa-Respected by king (Government) 

Virgo Amsa--Learned 

Libra Amsa-Minister or Adviser 

Sagittarius Amsa-Sinful 

Aquarius Amsa-Businessman 

Pisces Amsa-Wealthy. 

देहो जीर्ोऽथर्ा युक्तो ितर्भौमाष्टकव िाहुथभाः । 

एकै कयोगे मृत्युाः स्याद् बहुयोगे िु का कथा ॥ १२३॥ 

क्रू िैयुवक्ते िनौ िोगं जीर्े युक्ते महद् भयम् । 

आधी िोगो भर्ेद् द्वाभ्यांअपमृत्युष्टस्र्िथभभवर्ेि् ॥ १२४॥ 

चिुथभवमृवतिमापन्नो देहे जीर्ेऽशुभैयुविे । 

युगपद्देहजीर्ौ च क्रू िग्रहयुिौ िदा ॥ १२५॥ 

िाजचोिाद्वदभीतिि मृतििाष्टप न संशयाः । 

र्तिर्ाधा िर्ौ ज्ञेया क्षीणेन्दौ च जलाद् भयम् ॥ १२६॥ 

कु जे शिकृ िा पीडा र्ायुर्ाधा बुधे भर्ेि् । 

गुल्मर्ाधा शनौ ज्ञेया िाहौ के िौ तर्र्षाद् भयम् ॥ १२७॥ 

देहजीर्गृहे यािो बुधो जीर्ोऽथर्ा भृगुाः । 

सुखचम्पत्किााः सर्े िोगशोकतर्नाशनााः ॥ १२८॥ 

123-128. If the Deha or Jeeva Rāśis are be in conjunction with the Sun, Mars, Saturn or Rahu the native will die. Worse results may be expected if the conjunction be with two or all of them. If there be a malefic in Deha sign the native suffers ill health and a malefic in a Jeeva sign will make the native very timid. If the conjunction be with two malefics there will be distress and diseases. Three malefic will cause premature death. Four will cause definite death. if both the Deha and Jeeva signs are occupied by malefic, there will be fear of the king and thieves and death of the native. If the Sun be in the Deha or Jeeva sign, there will be danger from fire. Moon will there cause danger from water, Mars from weapons, Mercury from windy troubles, Saturn from gulma (गुल्म) (a disease), and Rahu and Ketu from poison. If the Deha Jeeva signs are occupied by Mercury, Jupiter and Venus, the native will be wealthy and will enjoy all kinds of comforts and good health. Mixed results may be expected if the signs are occupied by both benefices and malefic. 

तमिगृहैि संयुक्ते तमिं फलमर्ाप्नुयाि् । 

पापक्षेरदशाकाले देहजीर्ौ िु दाःखखिौ ु । 

शुभक्षेरदशाकाले शुभं भर्ति तनसििम् ॥ १२९॥ 

शुभयुक्ताशुभक्षेरदशा तमिफला स्मृिा । 

क्रू ियुक्तशुभक्षेरदशा तमिफला िथा ॥ १३०॥ 

129-130. In the Dasha of the signs owned by malefics the body and soul will be in distress. The effects will be favourable in the Dasha of the signs owned by benefices. If a malefic sign is occupied by a benefice planet or if a benefice sign is occupied by a malefic planet, the effects will be of a mixed nature. 

Effects of Kalachakra Dasha of the signs in the Ascendant and other houses. 

जनानां जन्मकाले िु यो िासशस्तनुभार्गाः । 

िस्य चक्रदशाकाले देहािोग्यं सुखं महि् ॥ १३१॥ 

शुभे पूणवसुखं पापे देहे िोगाद्वदसम्भर्ाः । 

स्वोच्चाद्वदगिखेटाढ्ये िाज्यमानधनाप्तयाः ॥ १३२॥ 

131-132. In the Kalachakra Dasha of the sign in the Ascendant (Lagna Rāśhi) the body remains healthy and the native spends a life with many kinds of comforts. If that sign be a benefice one, the good effects are realised fully. If it be a malefic sign there is likelihood of ill health. If a planet in exaltation or in its own sign occupies the Ascendant, the native is respected by the king or government and acquires wealth. 

धनभार्े च यो िासशस्तस्य चक्रदशा यदा । 

िदा सुभोजनं पुरण्डिसुखं च धनाप्तयाः ॥ १३३॥ 

तर्द्याब्दप्तर्ाक्पटुत्वं च सुगोष्ठ्या कालयापनम् । 

शुभक्षे फलमेर्ं स्याि् पापभे फलमन्यथा ॥ १३४॥ 

133-134. In the Chakra Dasha of the sign in the second house, the native receives good food, enjoys happiness of wife and children, gains wealth, achieves progress in the educational sphere, becomes a clever conversationalist and moves in good society. If the sign be a benefice, good effects are realised in full, otherwise the effects would be of a mixed nature. 

िृिीयभार्िाशेस्तु कालचक्रदशा यदा । 

िदा भ्रािृसुखं शौयं धैयं चाष्टप महत्सुखम् ॥ १३५॥ 

स्वणाभिणर्िाब्दप्ताः सम्मानं िाजसंसद्वद । 

शुभक्षे फलमेर्ं स्याि् पापक्षे फलमन्यथा ॥ १३६॥ 

135-136. Happiness from co-born, valour, patience, comforts, acquisition of gold, ornaments and clothes and recognition by the king or government, are the effects 

in the Kalachakra Dasha of the sign in the third house. If the sign be a benefice, the good results are realised in full, otherwise adverse effects may also be experienced. 

सुखभार्गिक्षवस्य कालचक्रदशा यदा । िदा बन्धुसुखं भूतमगृहिाज्यसुखाप्तयाः ॥ १३७॥ आिोग्यमथवलाभि र्िर्ाहनजं सुखम् । शुभक्षे शोभनं ज्ञेयं पापभे फलमन्यथा ॥ १३८॥ 

137-138. Good relations with kinsmen, acquisition of land, house or kingdom, conveyances and clothes and enjoyment of sound health, are the effects of the Chakra Dasha of the sign in the fourth. house. If the sign be a benefice one, the good effects are realised in full. If it be a malefic sign adverse results are also experienced. 

सुिभार्गिक्षवस्य कालचक्रदशा यदा । सुििीिाज्यसौख्याब्दप्तिािोग्यं तमरसङ्गमाः ॥ १३९॥ तर्द्याबुणद्धयशोलाभो धैयं च तर्क्रमोदयाः । शुभिाशौ शुभं पूणं पापक्षे फलमन्यथा ॥ १४०॥ 

139-140. Being blessed with wife and children, favours from Government, enjoyment of sound health, good relations with friends, achievement of fame, good progress in the educational sphere, patience and valour, are the effects of the Chakra Dasha of the sign in the fifth house. If the sign be a benefice one the good results are enjoyed in full. If the sign be a malefic one, adverse effects are also experienced. 

रिपुभार्गिक्षवस्य कालचक्रदशा यदा । िदा चोिाद्वदभूपागग्नतर्र्षशिभयं महि् ॥ १४१॥ प्रमेहगुल्मपण्ड् र्ाद्वदिोगाणामष्टप सम्भर्ाः । पापक्षे फलमेर्ं स्याि् शुभक्षे तमिमाद्वदशेि् ॥ १४२॥ 

141-142. Danger from the king (government), fire and weapons and possibility of suffering from diabetes, Gulma and jaundice are the effects in the Chakra Dasha of the sign in the sixth house. If the sign be a malefic one, the above adverse effects will be experienced in full. There will be some mitigation of evil effects in the case of a benefice sign. 

जायाभार्गिक्षवस्य कालचक्रदशा यदा । िदा पाणणग्रहाः पत्नीपुरलाभाद्वदकं सुखम् ॥ १४३॥ कृ ष्टर्षयोधनर्िाब्दप्तनृवपपूजा महद्यशाः । शुभिाशौ फलं पूणं पापिाशौ च िद्दलम् ॥ १४४॥ 

143-144. Marriage, conjugal happiness, being blessed with children, gain of agricultural products, cows and clothes, favours and recognition from the king (government) and achievement of fame, are the effects in the Chakra Dasha of the sign in the seventh house. The beneficial results will be experienced in full if the sign be a benefice one. Meagre good effects will be realised in the case of a malefic sign. 

मृत्युभार्स्थििक्षवस्य कालचक्रदशा िदा । 

िाननाशं महद् दाःखं ु बन्धुनाशं धनक्षयम् ॥ १४५॥ 

दारिद्र्यमन्नतर्द्वोपमरिभीतिं च तनद्वदवशेि् । 

पापिाशौ फलं पूणं शुभिाशौ च िद्दलम् ॥ १४६॥ 

145-146. Destruction of residential house, distress, loss of wealth, poverty and danger from enemies, are the effects of the Chakra Dasha of the sign in the eighth house. The adverse effects will be realised in full if the sign be a malefic one, some mitigation in evil effects may be expected in the case of a benefice sign. 

धमवभार्गिक्षवस्य कालचक्रदशा यदा । 

िदा पुरकलराथवकृ ष्टर्षगेहसुखं र्देि् ॥ १४७॥ 

सत्कमवधमवसंससणद्धं महज्जनपरिग्रहम् । 

शुभिाशौ शुभं पूणं पापिाशौ च िद्दलम् ॥ १४८॥ 

147-148. Felicity in respect of wife, children. house, agricultural activities, performance of good and pious deeds, progress in religious inclinations and privilege of moving in the society of great religious leaders, are the effects in Chakra Dasha of the sign in the ninth house (Dharma Bhava). The good results will be realised in full in the case of a benefice sign. Very meagre good effects will be experienced in the event of the sign being a malefic one. 

कमवभार्गिक्षवस्य कालचक्रदशा यदा । 

िाज्याब्दप्तभूवपसम्मानं पुरदािाद्वदजं सुखम् ॥ १४९॥ 

सत्कमवफलमैश्वयं सद्गोष्ठ्या कालयापनम् । 

शुभिाशौ फलं पूणं पापिाशौ च तमश्रििम् ॥ १५०॥ 

149-150. Acquisition of kingdom (very high position in government), recognition from the king (government), happiness from wife and children, success in ventures and performance of pious deeds, are the effects in the Chakra Dasha of the sign in the tenth house (Karma Bhava). The good results will be realised in full in the case of a benefice sign. Good effects will be few in the event of a sign being malefic. 

लाभभार्स्थििक्षवस्य कालचक्रदशा यदा । 

पुरिीबन्धुसौख्याब्दप्तभूवपप्रीतिमवहत्सुखम् ॥ १५१॥ 

# धनर्िाब्दप्तिािोग्यं सिां सङ्गि जायिे । शुभिाशौ फलं पूणं पापिाशौ च खण्डण्डिम् ॥ १५२॥

151-152 Felicity from wife, children and kinsmen, receipt of favours from government, acquisition of wealth and clothes and association with good people, are the effects in the Chakra Dasha of the sign in the eleventh house (Labha Bhava). The good effects will be enjoyed in full in the case of a benefice sign. Very little good will happen if the sign be a malefic one. 

व्ययभार्गिक्षवस्य कालचक्रदशा िदा । उद्योगभङ्गमालस्यं देहपीडां पदच्युतिम् ॥ १५३॥ दारिद्यं कमवर्ैफल्यं िथा व्यथवव्ययं र्देि् । पापिाशौ फलं त्वेर्ं शुभिाशौ च िद्दलम् ॥ १५४॥ 

153-154. Failure in efforts and ventures, pain in the body, loss of position, poverty and unnecessary expenditures are the effects in the Kalachakra Dasha of the sign in the twelfth house (Vyaya Bhava). The adverse effects will be experienced in full in the case of a malefic sign. Some good may happen if the sign be a benefice. 

Notes: A sign owned by a benefice planet is treated as benefice and that owned by a malefic as malefic. 

As described above the effects of Kalachakra Dasha of the signs in the 6th, 8th and 12th houses are adverse and they are favourable for the signs in the other houses. The Dasha of the signs with Mandooki, Markati and Simhavlokan movements (gati) are un favourable and the Dasha of the other signs are favourable. 

लग्नाद्वदव्ययपयविं भानां चिदशां ब्रुर्े । िस्माि् िदीशपयविं सङ् ख्यामर दशां तर्दाःु ॥ १५५॥ मेर्षाद्वदष्टरष्टरभैज्ञेयं पदमोजपदे क्रमाि् । दशाब्दानयने काया गणना व्युत्क्रमाि् समे ॥ १५६॥ 

155-156. Now I shall describe to you the Chara Dasha of the signs (Rāśhis) of the twelve houses. In this Dasha system the number of years of Dasha is reckoned from the Rashi up to the house in which its lord is posited. The peculiar feature of this system is that every three signs from Aries etc. have four Padas. For the odd (1,3) Padas, the counting is done from Rashi onwards up to the Rashi in which its lord is housed. For the even Padas (2, 4) this counting is done in the reverse order. 

र्ृसिकाथधपिी द्वौ च के िुभौमौ स्मृिौ द्वद्वज । शतनिाहु च कु म्भस्य स्वातमनौ परिकीतिविो ॥ १५७॥ 

157. In this system Mars and Ketu are both lords of Scorpio. Similarly, Saturn and Rahu are lords of Aquarius. 

द्वद्वनाथक्षेरयोिर ष्टक्रयिे तनणवयोऽधुना । द्वार्ेर्ाथधपिी तर्प्र युक्तौ स्वक्षे स्थििौ यद्वद ॥ १५८॥ र्र्षव द्वादशकं िर न चेदेकाद्वद श्रचियेि् । एकाः स्वक्षेरयोऽन्यस्तु पिर यद्वद संस्थििाः ॥ १५९॥ िदाऽन्यर स्थििं नाथं परिगृह्य दशां नयेि् । द्वार्प्यन्यक्षवगौ िौ चेि् िमोमवध्ये च यो बली ॥ १६०॥ िि एर् दशा ग्राह्या क्रमाद् र्ोत्क्रमिो द्वद्वजाः । बलस्याऽर तर्चािे स्यादग्रहाि् सग्रहो बली ॥ १६१॥ द्वार्ेर् सग्रहौ िौ चेि् बली िराथधकग्रहाः । ग्रहयोगसमानत्वे ज्ञेयं िासशबलाद् बलम् ॥ १६२॥ ज्ञेयाििस्थििद्वन्द्वााः क्रमिो बलशासलनाः । िासशसत्त्वसमानत्वे बहुर्र्षो बली भर्ेद् ॥ १६३॥ एकाः स्वोच्चगििाऽन्याः पिर यद्वद संस्थििाः । गृह्णीयादच्चखेटिंु िासशमन्यं तर्हाय र्ै ॥ १६४॥ उच्चखेटस्य सद्भार्े र्र्षवमेकं च तनसक्षपेि् । िथैर् नीचखेटस्य र्र्षवमेकं तर्शोधयेि् ॥ १६५॥ एर्ं सर्ं समालोच्य जािकस्य फलं र्देि् ॥ १६६॥ 

158-166. Now I will tell you about the working out of the Dasha years or Scorpio and Aquarius. If both the lords of the two Rāśhis - Scorpio and Aquarius-are posited in their own rāśhis, their Dasha, will be of 12 years. Otherwise the Dasha will be of the number of years, indicated by the number counted from that rashi to the rashi occupied by its lord. If one planet be in his own sign and the other in any other sign, the Dasha will be of the number of years counted from the above first sign to the Other. If the lords are in different signs the counting is to be done up to the sign which is stronger. The sign which has a planet posited in it, is considered more powerful than the sign without a planet in it. If both be with planets in them, the one with more planets would be considered more powerful. If both signs. are housed by an equal number of planets, the strength of the sign itself should be taken into account. The principle for considering the strength $( { \overline { { \mathfrak { A } } } } { \overline { { \mathfrak { C } } } } )$ of the sign is that the fixed sign is considered stronger than the movable one and the dual sign is considered more powerful than the fixed sign. If there be equality in the strength of the signs, then to determine the number of years of Dasha, counting should be done up to the sign with bigger number. If one sign be occupied by a planet in exaltation, the counting should be done up to that sign only. In addition, 1(one) should be added in the number of years in the case of sign with an exalted planet and 1 (one) should be deducted from the number of years in 

the case of the sign with a planet in debilitation. The prediction should be made after calculating the Dasha in this manner. 

# क्रमादत्क्रमिो ु र्ाऽष्टप धमवभार्पदक्रमाि् । लग्निासशं समािभ्य तर्ज्ञििदशां नयेि् ॥ १६७॥

167: If the sign in the ninth house from the Ascendant be in an odd Pada, the counting should be from the sign in the Ascendant onwards. The counting would be in the reverse order if the Pada be even. The Dasha of signs have to be fixed keeping this in view. 


Example:


<table><tr><td></td><td></td><td>Mars</td><td>Moon
Rahu</td></tr><tr><td>Lagna Mercury
Jupiter Venus</td><td rowspan="2" colspan="2"></td><td></td></tr><tr><td>Sun</td><td>Ketu</td></tr><tr><td></td><td>Saturn</td><td></td><td></td></tr></table>

In the above Libra is the sign in the 9th house in an odd Pada. Amongst the lords of the Ascendant Saturn and Rahu, Rahu is associated with a planet. Therefore, Rahu is more powerful than Saturn. Therefore, counting should be done up to Rahu. Aquarius is in even Pada, therefore, counting has to be done from Aquarius up to Rahu in the reverse order by which the Chara Dasha for Aquarius would come to 8 years. 

Aries is in odd Pada. Therefore, the Chara Dasha for Aries will be one year. The Dasha of other signs should be calculated in the same manner. 


Illustrative Table


<table><tr><td>Signs</td><td>Aquarius</td><td>Pisces</td><td>Aries</td><td>Taurus</td><td>Gemini</td><td>Cancer</td></tr><tr><td>Dasha Years</td><td>8</td><td>1</td><td>1</td><td>9</td><td>8</td><td>1</td></tr><tr><td>Signs</td><td>Leo</td><td>Virgo</td><td>Libra</td><td>Scorpio</td><td>Sagittarius</td><td>Capricorn</td></tr><tr><td>Dasha</td><td>7</td><td>7</td><td>4</td><td>6</td><td>2</td><td>5</td></tr><tr><td>Years</td><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td></tr></table>

After the expiry of these Dasha once, Aquarius will again become the starting point for the Dasha again. 

Sthira Dasha 

अथाऽहं सम्प्रर्क्ष्यातम स्थििसञ्ज्ज्ञां दशां द्वद्वज । 

चिे सप्त स्थििे चाऽष्टौ द्वन्द्वे नर् समााः स्मृिााः ॥ १६८॥ 

स्थिित्वाच्च दशाब्दानां स्थििाख्येति तनगद्यिे । 

ब्रह्मखेटाश्रििक्षाद्वददवशेयं परिर्िविे ॥ १६९॥ 

168-169. The Sage Said-Now I am going to describe the Sthira Dasha. In this Dasha system 7 years, 8 years and 9 years, are the Dasha spans of the movable (चर), fixed $( \sqrt { 2 0 } , 0$ and dual (द्विस्वाभाव) signs in that order. In this system, the Dasha of the 12 signs begins from the Brahma Grahashrit rashi. The Dasha are counted onwards from the odd signs and in the reverse order from the even signs. 

योऽसौ ब्रह्मग्रहाः प्रोक्ताः कथं स ज्ञायिे मुने । 

इति स्पष्टििं ब्रूद्वह कृ पाऽस्तस्त यद्वद िे मगय ॥ १७०॥ 

र्षष्ठाष्टव्ययनाथेर्षु यो बली तर्र्षमक्षवगाः । 

पृष्ठस्थििो भर्ेद् ब्रह्मां बसलनो लग्नजाययोाः ॥ १७१॥ 

कािकादष्टमेशो र्ा ब्रह्माऽप्यष्टभार्गाः । 

शनौ पािे च ब्रह्मत्त्वे ब्रह्मा िरर्षष्ठखेचिाः ॥ १७२॥ 

बहर्ो लक्षणक्रािा ज्ञेयस्तेष्वथधकांशकाः । 

अंशसाम्ये बलाथधक्याद् तर्ज्ञेयो ब्रह्मखेचिाः ॥ १७३॥ 

170-173. Maitreya said--O great Sage I now please, enlighten me how the Brahma Graha is picked out in a chart. 

The Sage said-From amongst the lord of the 6th, the 5th and the 12th the planet who may possess the greatest strength and be in the Ascendant or the 7th with strength, the one posited in an odd sign within sixth house from the house concerned, is called the Brahma Graha (ब्रह्म रह). The lord of the 8th house in the 8th is also accepted as Brahma Graha. If Saturn or Rahu Ketu obtain Brahmatva (ब्रह्मत्व - qualifications of Brahma Graha), they become Brahma Graha. If a number of planets obtain Brahmatva, the one with largest number of degrees would become Brahma Graha. If there is parity in the degrees of such planets, the most powerful amongst them would become Brahma Graha. 

Note: If the lord of the 8th is in the 8th, he would be Brahma Graha. Other planets posited in the 8th houses are treated as Brahma Grahas. If there be no planet in the 8th, the planet in an odd sign within 6 signs from the Ascendant or the 7th would become Brahma Graha. If a number of planets qualify for this position, the one with more degrees should be taken as Brahma Graha. The actual degrees of Rahu would be those which are arrived at after deducting from 30. 

<table><tr><td></td><td></td><td>Mars</td><td>Moon
Rahu</td></tr><tr><td>Lagna Mercury
Jupiter Venus</td><td rowspan="2" colspan="2"></td><td></td></tr><tr><td>Sun</td><td></td></tr><tr><td>Ketu</td><td>Saturn</td><td></td><td></td></tr></table>


Graha Spast (Longitudes of planets)


<table><tr><td></td><td>R</td><td>D</td><td>M</td><td>S</td></tr><tr><td>Sun</td><td>9</td><td>29</td><td>36</td><td>53</td></tr><tr><td>Moon</td><td>2</td><td>22</td><td>6</td><td>58</td></tr><tr><td>Mars</td><td>1</td><td>0</td><td>56</td><td>21</td></tr><tr><td>Mercury</td><td>10</td><td>13</td><td>6</td><td>26</td></tr><tr><td>Jupiter</td><td>10</td><td>13</td><td>41</td><td>58</td></tr><tr><td>Venus</td><td>10</td><td>20</td><td>4</td><td>2</td></tr><tr><td>Saturn</td><td>7</td><td>13</td><td>24</td><td>27</td></tr><tr><td>Rahu</td><td>2</td><td>13</td><td>55</td><td>34</td></tr><tr><td>Ascendant</td><td>10</td><td>16</td><td>28</td><td>5</td></tr></table>

Rahu's degrees etc. after deducting from 30 would be $1 6 ^ { \circ } - 4 ^ { \prime } - 2 6 "$ 

Here it may be mentioned that some learneds in Hindu Astrology adopt the method of counting from the Sun onwards while others follow the system of counting 

from Atmakaraka onwards. We are of the view that the system of reckoning from Atmakaraka onwards is more logical and practicable in this Dasha system. 

In accordance with the system described in the chapter dealing with the Atmakaraka, the Sun here has traversed the maximum number of degrees, will be Atmakarka and Venus who comes next with degrees, will be Amatya (अमात्य). After that comes Rahu, Karaka for brother, Jupiter Karaka for mother, Saturn Karaka for father, Mercury Karaka for son. Moon Karaka for ghati and Mars Karaka for wife, 


Illustrative Table


<table><tr><td>Atmakaraka</td><td>Amatya</td><td>Brother</td><td>Mother</td><td>Father</td><td>Son</td><td>Gnati</td><td>Wife</td></tr><tr><td>Sun</td><td>Venus</td><td>Rahu</td><td>Jupiter</td><td>Saturn</td><td>Mercury</td><td>Moon</td><td>Mars</td></tr></table>

There is no planet in the 8th house but there are three benefices in the Ascendant and they aspect the 7th house. Therefore, Ascendant would be treated as the strongest. Counting backwards up to six signs from the Ascendant, we find that the lord of the 8th Mercury occupies the odd sign Aquarius. Thus, lords of the Dasha of the 12 signs would be from Aquarius onwards.

# Yogardha Dasha

योगाधे च दशामानं द्वयोयोगाधवसन्तम्मिम् । लग्नसप्तमप्राण्याद्वददवशेयं च प्रर्िविे ॥ १७४॥ 

174. The spans of Dasha of the signs in the Yogardha Dasha system are half of the total of the of Chara and Sthira Dasha. The Dasha will commence from the sign of the Ascendant or the seventh house whichever is stronger. The order of the Dasha of the 12 signs will be counted onwards if the opening Dasha sign is an odd one. If it be an even sign the Dasha will be in the reverse order. 

Example: It will be seen that in the birth chart given earlier the sign of the Ascendant is stronger than the sign of the 7th house. It is an odd sign. So, the Dasha will start from Aquarius onwards. The Chara Dasha of Aquarius is of 8 years and Sthira Dasha is also of 8 years. The Dasha of Aquarius in the Yogardha Dasha system will consequently be of 8 years $1 \%$ of $8 { + } 8$ ). The Chara Dasha of Pisces is one year and Sthira Dasha is of 9 years. Thus, the Dasha of Pisces here will be of 5 years $\%$ of 1 $+ 9 )$ . The Dasha of the remaining signs may be worked out in the same manner. 


Illustrative Table


<table><tr><td>Sign</td><td>Aquarius</td><td>Pisces</td><td>Aries</td><td>Taurus</td><td>Gemini</td><td>Cancer</td></tr><tr><td>Dasha Years</td><td>8</td><td>5</td><td>4</td><td>8½</td><td>8½</td><td>4</td></tr><tr><td>Sign</td><td>Leo</td><td>Virgo</td><td>Libra</td><td>Scorpio</td><td>Sagittarius</td><td>Capricorn</td></tr><tr><td>Dasha Years</td><td>8</td><td>8</td><td>5½</td><td>7</td><td>5½</td><td>4½</td></tr></table>

Kendradi Dasha (के न्द्रादि िशा) 

लग्नसप्तमयोमवध्ये यो िासशबवलर्ान् भर्ेि् । 

ििाः के न्द्राद्वदसंिानां िाशीनाञ्च बलक्रमाि् ॥ १७५॥ 

कािकादष्टप िाशीनां खेटानां चैर्मेर् द्वह । 

दशाब्दाििर्ज्ज्ञेयााः खेटानां च स्वभार्थध ॥ १७६॥ 

175-176. In this system, there are Dasha of fixed signs in the Kendra etc. from the Ascendant or the 7th house, whichever is stronger. If the Ascendant or the 7th with strength be in an odd sign the Kendra etc. are counted in the onward order. If it be in an even sign the counting will be in the backward or reverse order. In them also the Dasha would be in the order of comparative strength of the signs. The order of Dasha would be the same as reckoned from the Atmakaraka. The spans of Dasha would be the same as they are in the Chara Dasha. In Calculating the years of Dasha of planets counting is done from the planet to his own sign. The years of Dasha would be the number arrived at by counting up to the sign of the planet which is stronger or more in number. 

Note: Under this system Dasha are of two kinds - namely, Lagna Kendradi (लग्न के न्द्राद्वद) and Atmakaraka Kendradi (आत्म कारक के न्द्राद्वद). There are also Kendradi Rashi Dasha (के न्द्राद्वद राशश दशा) or Kendradi Graha Dasha (के न्द्राद्वद रह दशा) in both the Dasha system mentioned above. 

Example: See the birth chart given earlier. Amongst the Ascendant Aquarius and the 7th Leo, the Ascendant is stronger Therefore, the first Dasha will be of the Ascendant and thereafter of its Kendra signs - Taurus, Leo and Scorpio. In the order of the comparative strength the Dasha will be of Taurus, Scorpio and Leo. In the Panaphara houses (2, 5, 8, 11) from amongst Pisces, Gemini, Virgo and Sagittarius, in order of comparative strength the Dasha will be first of Gemini and then of Sagittarius, Pisces and Virgo. In the Apoklima houses from amongst Aries, Cancer, Libra and Capricorn, in order of comparative strength, the first Dasha will be of Capricorn and thereafter of Aries, Cancer and Libra. 

Dasha years-As indicated in dealing with Chara Dasha Aquarius is in an even Pada. Consequently, counted backwards from its lords Saturn to Rahu the number is 

more. Therefore, the Dasha will be of 8 years. The years of Dasha of other sign, may be calculated in the same manner. 


Illustrative Table


<table><tr><td>Sign</td><td>Aquarius</td><td>Taurus</td><td>Scorpio</td><td>Leo</td><td>Gemini</td><td>Sagittarius</td></tr><tr><td>Dasha years</td><td>8</td><td>6</td><td>6</td><td>7</td><td>8</td><td>2</td></tr><tr><td>Sign</td><td>Pisces</td><td>Virgo</td><td>Capricorn</td><td>Aries</td><td>Cancer</td><td>Libra</td></tr><tr><td>Dasha years</td><td>1</td><td>7</td><td>2</td><td>1</td><td>1</td><td>1</td></tr></table>

Similarly, amongst Atmakaraka Sun and his 7th Cancer. the sign Capricorn occupied by the Atmakaraka is stronger. This is an even sign. Consequently, at first there will be Dasha of Capricorn etc. Kendra signs in the order of their strength. Thereafter by going in the reverse order there will be Dasha of Apoklima signs. After that will come the Dasha of Scorpio and other Panaphara signs in the order of their strength. 

Example of Atmakaraka Kendradi Graha Dasha 

The Atmakaraka is the Sun in Capricorn. Capricorn is an even sign. Consequently, the planets occupying Kendra. Apoklima and Panaphara houses will have their Dasha in the reverse order according to their strength. Capricorn is occupied by the Sun only, the first Dasha will, therefore, be of the Sun There are no planets in Kendras to him (signs 7, 4, 1). In Apoklima (signs 9, 3) are the Moon, Rahu and Ketu. Amongst them in the order of strength, the Dasha lords will be Rahu, Ketu and the Moon. In Panaphara houses (signs 8, 2, 11) in the order of strength the Dasha will be of Venus, Jupiter, Mercury, Mars and Saturn. The span of Dasha will be equal to the number up to the own sign of the planet concerned (in the onward and reverse orders). Here the Atmakaraka Sun is in an even sign. Therefore, by counting up to his own sign Leo in the reverse order the Dasha of the Sun will be of 5 years. The Dasha years of the other planets may be calculated in the same manner. 

द्वद्विाश्यथधपक्षेटस्य गण्येदभयार्थध ु । 

उभयोथधवक सङ् ख्या कािकस्य दशा समााः ॥ १७७॥ 

177. If a planet owns two signs (except the Sun and the Moon and barring Rahu and Ketu, all the planets own two signs), the Dasha years will be equal to the number which is greater when counted from the sign occupied by him. 

Karaka Dasha 

आत्मकािकमािभ्य कािकाख्यदशा क्रमाि् । 

# लग्नाि् कािकपयविं सङ् ख्यामर दशां तर्दाःु ॥ १७८॥

178. The system under which the first Dasha is of the Atmakaraka and the subsequent Dasha are of the remaining 7 karakas in their order is known as Kara ka Dasha. In this system, the Dasha years are equal to the number of signs counted from the Ascendant up to the Karaka concerned. 

Example: The Atmakaraka is the Sun. He is in the 12th to the Ascend ant. There is thus a difference of 11 signs between the Atmakaraka and the Ascendant. Therefore, his Dasha will be of 11 years. After this comes Amatya Karaka Venus. According to the principle “वषध िादंश ति” etc. the Dasha of Venus will be of 12 years. The Dasha of other Karakas have to be worked out in the same manner. 


Illustrative Table


<table><tr><td>Atma</td><td>Atmatya</td><td>Brother</td><td>Mother</td><td>Father</td><td>Son</td><td>Gnati</td><td>Wife</td></tr><tr><td>Sun</td><td>Venus</td><td>Rahu</td><td>Jupiter</td><td>Saturn</td><td>Mercury</td><td>Moon</td><td>Mars</td></tr><tr><td>11</td><td>12</td><td>4</td><td>12</td><td>9</td><td>12</td><td>4 Years</td><td>3 Years</td></tr><tr><td>Years</td><td>Years</td><td>Years</td><td>Years</td><td>Years</td><td>Years</td><td></td><td></td></tr></table>

# Mandooka Dasha

मण्डूकापिपयाया ष्टरकू टाख्यदशा द्वद्वज । लग्नसप्तमयोमवध्ये यो िासशबवलर्ान् भर्ेि् ॥ १७९॥ ििाः क्रमेणौजिाशौ समे नेया िथोऽत्क्रमाि् । ष्टरकू टानां च तर्ज्ञेयााः स्थििर्च्च दशा समााः ॥ १८०॥ 

179-180. Under this system, the Dasha commences from the Ascendant or the 7th house whichever is stronger. If the sign of commencement is an odd sign the Dasha of 3 Moveable signs, 3 Fixed signs and 3 Dual signs will be counted in the onwards order. They will be in the reverse order in the case of an even sign. In this system, the Dasha years will be the same as in Sthira Dasha system (7 years for Movable signs, 8 years for Fixed signs and 9 years for Dual signs). In this system, every Dasha is of the next 3rd sign (after leaving out two signs). For example, after Aquarius Dasha comes the Dasha of Taurus after leaving out Pisces and Aries. After Pisces Dasha comes the Dasha of Gemini after leaving out Aries and Taurus. It is for this reason that this system has been named as Mandooka Dasha. 

Example-In the birth chart given earlier, the Ascendant is stronger than the 7th. The sign of the Ascendant is odd and Fixed. Consequently, the first Dasha will be of Aquarius followed by the Dasha of the other Fixed signs Taurus, Leo and Scorpio 4 Dual signs and four Movable signs. 

# Illustrative Table

# Shoola Dasha

तनयाणस्य तर्चािाथं कै सिछू लदशा स्मृिा । लग्नसप्तमिो मृत्युभयोयो बलर्ान् भर्ेि् ॥ १८१॥ िदाद्वदतर्वर्षमे तर्प्र क्रमादत्क्रमिाः ु समे । दशाब्दााः स्थििर्त्तर बसलमािकभे मृतिाः ॥ १८२॥ 

181-182. Some learneds have designed the Shoola Dasha for determining the time of death. In this system, the Dasha commences from the 2nd or the 8th house whichever is stronger. If the sign be an odd one, the order of the Dasha of the signs will be onwards. It will be backwards in the case of an even sign. The Dasha years in this system are as adopted for the Sthira Dasha. There is possibility of the death in Dasha of the Maraka (killer) sign which has greater strength. 

Example-See for example birth chart given earlier. There are no planets in the 2nd or 8th. But the lord of the 2nd from the Ascendant (Jupiter) is stronger than the lord of the 8th (Mercury). Consequently, the Dasha of the 12 signs will commence from Pisces in the reverse order.

<table><tr><td>Sign</td><td>Pisces</td><td>Aquarius</td><td>Capricorn</td><td>Sagittarius</td><td>Scorpio</td><td>Libra</td></tr><tr><td>Dasha Years</td><td>9</td><td>8</td><td>7</td><td>9</td><td>8</td><td>7</td></tr><tr><td>Sign</td><td>Virgo</td><td>Leo</td><td>Cancer</td><td>Gemini</td><td>Taurus</td><td>Aries</td></tr><tr><td>Dasha Years</td><td>9</td><td>8</td><td>7</td><td>9</td><td>8</td><td>7</td></tr></table>

# Trikona Dasha

जन्मलग्नष्टरकोणेर्षु यो िासशबवलर्ान् भर्ेि् । िमाभ्यव नयेद् धीमान् चरिपयायर्द् दशाम् ॥ १८३॥ क्रमादत्क्रमिोु ग्राह्यं ष्टरकोणं तर्र्षमे समे । ष्टरकोणाख्यदशा प्रोक्ता समा नाथार्सानकााः ॥ १८४॥ 

183-184. In this system, the first Dasha Commences from the strongest amongst the signs in trine (व्िकोण) to the Ascendant (1, 5, 9). The Dasha system is similar to the Chara Dasha. Here also the Dasha of the signs will be in the onwards order in the case of odd signs and in the reverse order in the case of even. The Dasha years will be similar to that of Chara Dasha have been named Trikona because of the commencement of the Dasha from the signs in Trine. 

Example-Refer to the birth chart given earlier. Amongst the Ascendant, 5th and 9th, the Ascendant is the strongest. Therefore, the order of the Dasha will be Aquarius, Gemini, Libra, Pisces, Cancer, Scorpio, Aries. Leo Sagittarius, Taurus, Virgo, Capricorn. 


Illustrative Table


<table><tr><td>Sign</td><td>Aquarius</td><td>Gemini</td><td>Libra</td><td>Pisces</td><td>Cancer</td><td>Scorpio</td></tr><tr><td>Dasha Years</td><td>8</td><td>8</td><td>4</td><td>11</td><td>1</td><td>11</td></tr><tr><td>Sign</td><td>Aries</td><td>Leo</td><td>Sagittarius</td><td>Taurus</td><td>Virgo</td><td>Capricorn</td></tr><tr><td>Dasha Years</td><td>1</td><td>6</td><td>10</td><td>9</td><td>7</td><td>2</td></tr></table>

# Dirga Dasha

लग्नाद् धमवस्य िद्दष्टिाशीनां ृ च दशास्तिाः । 

दशमस्य च िद्दृष्टिाशीनां च नयेि् पुनाः ॥ १८५॥ 

एकादशस्य िद्दृष्टिाशीनां स्थििर्ि् समााः । 

प्रर्ृत्ता दृग् र्शाद्यस्माद् दृग्दशेयं ििाः स्मृिा ॥ १८६॥ 

चिे व्युत्क्रमिो ग्राह्या दृग्योग्यााः स्थििभे क्रमाि् । 

तर्र्षमे क्रमिो द्वन्द्वे िाशयो व्युत्क्रमाि् समे ॥ १८७॥ 

185-187. In this system, the order of the Dasha is as follows 

(1) The ninth sign from the Ascendant. 

(2) The signs aspected by the sign in the ninth house. 

(3) The sign in the 10th from the Ascendant. 

(4) The signs aspected by the sign in the 10th house. 

(5) The sign in the 11th from the Ascendant, and 

(6) The signs aspected by the sign in the 11th house. 

As this system is mostly based on aspects, it has been named Driga Dasha 

Three different processes are adopted for the Movable, Fixed and, Dual signs, from the 9th, 10th and 11th houses. According to them the aspected sign from the Movable sign is. counted backwards and the aspected sign from the Fixed sign is 

counted onwards. In the case of the Dual sign if it is odd, the counting is onwards and the order is backwards in, case of an even sign for the aspected signs. 

Note: The intention is that from the point of view of aspect, the process of aspected sign should be started from the sign which is nearest. In this way in the case of Movable Signs, the rāśhis at their back (previous to them) are nearest to them. In the case of Fixed sign, the signs after them are considered as nearest in respect of aspects, In the case of Dual signs the sign on both sides are treated equally. It is for this reason that in their case difference of order has been made for odd and even signs. In this connection readers, may refer to Rashi Drishtikathana Adhyaya (Chapter -8) Verse 9 and the table after that. 

Example-In the example birth chart the sign of 9th house, namely Libra, is a Movable sign. Therefore, the first Dasha will be of Libra and thereafter will be the Dasha of the Signs aspected by Libra, namely Leo, Taurus, Aquarius. The sign of the 10th house is Scorpio (a fixed sign). Therefore, the first Dasha will be of Scorpio and thereafter will be the Dasha of signs aspected by Scorpio, namely Capricorn, Aries and Cancer (onwards order). The sign of the 11th house is Sagittarius (a Dual odd sign). Therefore, there will be Dasha of Sagittarius, Pisces, Gemini and Virgo in that order. The years of Dasha will be the same as prescribed for the Sthira Dasha. 


Illustrative Table


<table><tr><td>Sign</td><td>Libra</td><td>Leo</td><td>Taurus</td><td>Aquarius</td><td>Scorpio</td><td>Capricorn</td></tr><tr><td>Dasha Years</td><td>7</td><td>8</td><td>8</td><td>8</td><td>8</td><td>7</td></tr><tr><td>Sign</td><td>Aries</td><td>Cancer</td><td>Sagittarius</td><td>Pisces</td><td>Gemini</td><td>Virgo</td></tr><tr><td>Dasha Years</td><td>7</td><td>7</td><td>9</td><td>9</td><td>9</td><td>9</td></tr></table>

# Lagnadi Rashi Dasha

ऋक्षे लग्नाद्वदिाशीनां दशा िासशदशा स्मृिा । 

भयािं ितर्थभतनवघ्नं भभोगतर्हृिं फलम् ॥ १८८॥ 

िाश्याद्यं लग्निाश्यादौ योज्यं द्वादशशेष्टर्षिम् । 

िदािभ्य क्रमादोजे दशा ज्ञेयोत्क्रमाि् समे ॥ १८९॥ 

188-189. In this system, there are Dasha of all the 12 signs including the Ascendant in every Nakshatra. Consequently, the Bhayat at birth may be multiplied by 12 and then the product be divided by Bhabhog. The Rashi, degree etc. so available may be added to the longitude of the Lagna (Ascendant). From the rashi, becoming available by doing so, will start the Dasha of the 12 signs (if that rashi be odd, the counting will be onwards. It will be in the reverse order if the rashi be even). 

Example-The Janma Nakshatra is Mrigasira. Bhayat is 58, 15 (58 Ghatikas and 15 palas) or 3495 palas. By multiplying it by 12 we get 41940 palas. Bhabhog is 59, 31 or 3571 palas. By dividing 41940 by 3571 we get 11, 22, 20, 17 that is Pisces 22 degrees, 20 minutes and 17 seconds. Adding this to the longitude of Lagna, namely 10, 26, 28, 5, we get the rashi etc. as 10, 18, 48, 22 (The actual total is 22, 18, 48, 22. From this 12 Rāśhis have to be deducted to get the actual rāśhis etc.). Consequently, 

the Dasha of the 12 signs will start from Aquarius. The years of Dasha in this system will be the same as adopted for the Sthira Dasha. 

# दशाब्दा भुक्तभागघ्ना ष्टरंशिा तर्हृिाह् फलम् ।

# भुक्तं र्र्षाद्वदकं ज्ञेयं भोग्यं मानाद् तर्शोथधिम् ॥ १९०॥

190. For finding the balance of Dasha at birth, multiply the expired degree etc., by the Dasha years of the first Dasha sign and divide it by 30. The years etc., so arrived at, may be deducted from the Dasha years. The result will indicate the balance of Dasha at birth in years, months etc. 

Example-The expired degrees etc., of the Dasha commencing sign are 18, 48, 22. By multiplying them by 8 (the Dasha years of Aquarius) we get 150, 76, 56. By dividing it by 30 we get 5 years 0 months 23 days, 23 hours and 12 Ghatikas. Deducting it from 8 years we will get 2 years 11 months, 24 days, 0 hours and 48 Ghatikas as balance of Dasha at birth. 


Illustrative Table


<table><tr><td>Sign</td><td>Aquarius</td><td>Pisces</td><td>Aries</td><td>Taurus</td><td>Gemini</td><td>Cancer</td></tr><tr><td>Years</td><td>2</td><td>9</td><td>7</td><td>8</td><td>9</td><td>7</td></tr><tr><td>Months</td><td>11</td><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td></tr><tr><td>Days</td><td>24</td><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td></tr><tr><td>Sign</td><td>Leo</td><td>Virgo</td><td>Libra</td><td>Scorpio</td><td>Sagittarius</td><td>Capricorn</td></tr><tr><td>Years</td><td>8</td><td>9</td><td>7</td><td>8</td><td>9</td><td>7</td></tr></table>

# Panchswara Dasha

अकािादीन् स्विान् पञ्च प्रथमं तर्न्यसेि् क्रमाि् । 

काद्वदहािांल्लिखेद् र्णान् स्विाधो ङञणोल्लििान् ॥ १९१॥ 

तियवक् पङ् गक्तक्रमेणैर् पञ्चपञ्चतर्भागिाः । 

न प्रोक्ता ङञणा र्णा नामादौ सन्ति िे नद्वह ॥ १९२॥ 

चेद् भर्न्ति िदा ज्ञेया गजडास्ते यथाक्रमाि् । 

यर स्विे स्वनामाद्यर्णवाः स्याि् ित्स्विादयाः ॥ १९३॥ 

क्रमाि् पञ्च दशाधीशााः द्वादशद्वादशाब्दकााः । 

स्विाणां च क्रमाज्ज्ञेयााः दशास्विदवशादयाः ॥ १९४॥ 

191-194. Beginning from Akaradi (अकाराद्वद) 5 swaras (अ, इ, उ, ए, ओ) write underneath them the Varnas (वणध) in 6 lines. Leave out the letters ङ, ञ and ण because they are not used in names. If they are found in any name, ग may be substituted for ङ. ज for ञ and ड for ण for working out the Dasha and making predictions. in this manner, 

the Swara under which the first Varna of the name of the native is found, will determine the order of the Dasha of the foe swaras. Dasha are of 12 years for all the five swaras. In the Dasha of every swara, there will be Antardasa of all the five Swaras in the same order. 

Example-The birth is in the 4th Pada of Mrigasira. Therefore, the first letter of the name will be Kakar (ककार). Its swara is अ: Therefore, Dasha will be of five swaras commencing from अ. 

<table><tr><td colspan="6">Panch Swara Table</td></tr><tr><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td><td>waras</td></tr><tr><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td><td rowspan="6"></td></tr><tr><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td></tr><tr><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td></tr><tr><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td></tr><tr><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td></tr><tr><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td></tr><tr><td>2</td><td>2</td><td>2</td><td>2</td><td>2</td><td>ears</td></tr></table>

<table><tr><td colspan="5">Panch Swara Dasha Table</td></tr><tr><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td></tr><tr><td>2</td><td>2</td><td>2</td><td>2</td><td>2</td></tr></table>

# Yogini Dasha

पूर्वमेर् मया प्रोक्ता र्णवदाख्या दशा द्वद्वज । 

इदानीं शम्भुना प्रोक्ता कथ्यिे योगगनी दशा ॥ १९५॥ 

मङ्गला ष्टपङ्गला धन्या भ्रामिी भद्वद्रका िथा । 

उल्का ससद्धा सङ्कटा च योगगन्योऽष्टौ प्रकीतिविााः ॥ १९६॥ 

मङ्गलािोऽभर्च्चन्द्राः ष्टपङ्गलािो द्वदर्ाकिाः । 

धन्यािो देर्पूज्योऽभूद् भ्रामिीिोऽभर्ि् कु जाः ॥ १९७॥ 

भद्वदवकािो बुधो जािस्तथोल्कािाः शनैििाः । 

ससद्धािो भागवतर् जािाः सङ्कटािस्तमोऽभर्द् ॥ १९८॥ 

जन्मक्षव च ष्टरथभयुवक्तं र्सुथभभागमाहिेि् । 

एकाद्वदशेर्षे तर्ज्ञेया योगगन्योाः मङ्गलाद्वदकााः ॥ १९९॥ 

195-199. The Sage said-O Brahmin! I have already given you the description of Panch Swara Dasha. Now I will acquaint you with the Yogini Dasha as described by Lord Mahadeva. There are 8 Yoginis namely, 1. Mangala, 2. Pingala, 3. Dhanya, 4. Bhramari, 5. Bhadrika, 6. Ulka, 7. Siddha and 8. Sankata. The Moon, the Sun, Jupiter, Mars, Mercury. Saturn, Venus and Rahu, are born from Mangala, Pingala, 

Dhanya, Bhramari, Bhadrika, Ulka, Siddha and Sankata, in that order. Add 3 to the Janma Nakshatra and divide it by 8. The remainder I etc. will indicate the Yogini Dasha of Mangala etc. The Dasha of Mangala, Pingala, Dhanya, Bhramari, Bhadrika, Ulka, Siddha and Sankata are of 1, 2, 3, 4, 5, 6, 7 and 8 years respectively. The balance of Dasha at birth should be worked out from the Bhayat and Bhabhog etc., as already explained earlier. 

Example-The Janma Nakshatra is Mrigasira. Its number is 5. By adding 3 to this number we get 8. By dividing 8 by 8 we will get zero as remainder which means that the birth took Place in the Dasha of 8th Yogini, namely Sankata. 

Pinda Amsa Nisarga Dasha 

एकाद्येकोत्तिा ज्ञेयााः क्रमादासां दशासमााः । 

नक्षरयािभोगाभ्यां भुक्तं भोग्यं च साधयेि् ॥ २००॥ 

येर्षां यदायुाः सम्प्रोक्तं पैण्डमांशं तनसगवजम् । 

िक्षि् िेर्षां दशा ज्ञेया पैण्डी चांशी तनसगवजा ॥ २०१॥ 

बली लग्नाकव चन्द्राणां यत्तस्य प्रथमा दशा । 

ित्के न्द्राद्वदगिानां च ज्ञेया बलर्शात्तिाः ॥ २०२॥ 

200-202. The Pinda Dasha, Amsa Dasha and Nisarga Dasha, will be the same as Pindayu, Amsayu and Nisargayu, the method of determination of which has already been explained previously. The order of Dasha will be as follow. The first Dasha will be of the Lagna (Ascendant), the Sun or the Moon whoever is stronger. The subsequent Dasha will be of planets in Kendra to them, then of planets in Panaphara houses and lastly of planets in Apoklima houses. The Dasha and Antardasa of the Lagna and seven planets will also be in the same order. (Rahu Ketu do not find place in this Dasha system). 

अष्टर्गवबलेनैर्षां फलातन परिश्रचियेि् । 

अष्टर्गवदशािैिााः कथथिााः पूर्वसूरिथभाः ॥ २०३॥ 

203. The effects of these Dasha will be in accordance with the Ashtaka Varga Bala (अष्टक वगध बल), which subject will be dealt with later. These Dasha are also called Ashtaka Varga Dasha. 

Sandhya Dasha 

पिायुद्वादशो भागस्तस्य सन्ध्या प्रकीतिविा । 

िन्तन्मिा लग्नभादीनां क्रमाि् सन्ध्यादशा स्मृिा ॥ २०४॥ 

204. Sandhya is the Dwadashamsa Ayurdaya (िादशांश आयुदाय) of the Param Ayurdaya (परम आयुदाय) (maximum possible life span). In Sandhya Dasha the Dasha of all the signs from Lagna onwards is of 1/12 the years of Param Ayurdaya. 

Example-In the example birth chart the Lagna is Aquarius. Therefore, the Dasha of all the signs commencing from Aquarius will be of 10 years as the Paramayurdaya is 120 years.

<table><tr><td>Sign</td><td>Aquarius</td><td>Pisces</td><td>Aries</td><td>Taurus</td><td>Gemini</td><td>Cancer</td></tr><tr><td>Dasha Years</td><td>10</td><td>10</td><td>10</td><td>10</td><td>10</td><td>10</td></tr><tr><td>Sign</td><td>Leo</td><td>Virgo</td><td>Libra</td><td>Scorpio</td><td>Sagittarius</td><td>Capricorn</td></tr><tr><td>Dasha Years</td><td>10</td><td>10</td><td>10</td><td>10</td><td>10</td><td>10</td></tr></table>

# Pachaka Dasha in Sindhya Dasha

सन्ध्या िसगुणा काया चन्द्रर्तिहृिा फलम् । 

संिाप्यं प्रथमे कोष्ठे िदधं ष्टरर्षु तर्न्यसेि् ॥ २०५॥ 

ष्टरभागं र्सुकोष्ठेर्षु तर्न्यस्य ित्फलं र्देि् । 

एर्ं द्वादशभार्ेर्षु पाचकातन प्रकल्पयेि् ॥ २०६॥ 

205-206: By multiplying the Dasha years of Sandhya Dasha by 6 and dividing the product by 31, the years, months etc., so arrived at may be put in one apartment of a Table. Thereafter half of these years, months etc., may be written in the next three apartments. The remaining 8 apartments may be filled in by one third of the aforesaid years, months etc. In this manner Pachaka Dasha in Sandhya Dasha of every Bhava (house) can be worked out and predictions may be made from it. 

Example-The Sandhya Dasha of the Lagna is 10 years. By multiplying it by 6 we get 60. By dividing 60 by 31 we get 1 year 11 months 6 days (round). This may be written in the first apartment. Half of this period viz., 0 years 11 months and 18 days (round figure) may be written in the next three apartments. Thereafter one third of the 1 year, 11 months, 6 days may be written in remaining 8 apartments. This process will complete the Pachaka Dasha Table which is given below:
