# Tara Dasha

तर्ंशत्तरिदशेर्ाऽर कै सिि् िािादशा स्मृिा । 

आशङ्कु िागुशबुके श्वाद्वदिानेर्षु िािकााः ॥ २०७॥ 

अन्मसम्पन्तत्वपत्क्षेमप्रत्यरिाः साधको बधाः । 

मैरं पिममैरं च के न्द्रिबसलनो ग्रहाि् ॥ २०८॥ 

ज्ञेया िािादशा तर्प्र नामिुल्यफलप्रदा । 

यस्य के न्द्रे स्थििाः खेटो दशेयं िस्य कीतिविा ॥ २०९॥ 

207-209. O Brahmin! Some learneds have given consideration to Tara Dasha which is like Vimshottari Dasha. In this Dasha Janma, Sampat etc. in their order replace the Sun, Moon, etc., housed in Kendras. This Dasha is applied in those cases only where there are planets in Kendras. If there are a number of planets, the first Dasha will belong to the strongest amongst them. 

Example-In the birth chart given earlier, Jupiter is strongest amongst all the planets in Kendras. Therefore, the first Dasha will belong to Jupiter. Dasha years will be the same as described for Vimshottari Dasha. 


Illustrative Table


<table><tr><td>Planet</td><td>Jupiter</td><td>Sat</td><td>Mercury</td><td>Ketu</td><td>Venus</td><td>Sun</td><td>Moon</td><td>Mars</td><td>Rah</td></tr><tr><td>ara</td><td>Pratya</td><td>Sadha</td><td>Vadha</td><td>Maitra</td><td>Atimaitra</td><td>Janma</td><td>Sampat</td><td>Vipat</td><td>Ksh</td></tr><tr><td>Years</td><td>16</td><td>19</td><td>17</td><td>7</td><td>20</td><td>6</td><td>10</td><td>7</td><td>18</td></tr></table>

इति िे कथथिा तर्प्र दश भेदा अनेकधा । 

एिदिदवशाभेदान् कथगयष्यातम चाग्रिाः ॥ २१०॥ 

210. O Brahmin! I have now completed the description the different kinds of Dasha (that are followed by the learneds). I will give the description of their Antardasa (Sub-periods) later. 

# अथ दशाफलाद्यायः ॥४७॥

# Chapter 47. Effects of Dasha

िुिाि बहु धा भेदा दशानां च मया मुने । फलं च कीदृशं िासां कृ पया मे िदच्यिाम् ु ॥१॥ 

1. Maitreya said-O Sage! You have told me about the different kinds of Dasha. Now be kind enough to enlighten me with the effects of Dasha. 

साधािणं तर्सशष्टञ्च दशानां द्वद्वतर्धं फलम् । ग्रहाणां च स्वभार्ेन िानस्थितिर्शेन च ॥२॥ 

2. The Sage replied- O Brahmin! There are two kinds of effects of Dasha - general and distinctive. The natural characteristics of the planets cause the general effects and the distinctive effects are realised by their placements etc. 

ग्रहर्ीयानुसािेण फलं ज्ञेयं दशासु च । आद्यद्रेष्काणगे खेटे दशािम्भे फलं र्देि् ॥३॥ दशामध्ये फलं र्ाच्यं मध्यद्रेष्काणगे खगे । अिे फलं िृिीयिे व्यस्तं खेटे च र्क्रगे ॥४॥ 

3-4: The effects of the Dasha of the planets are in accordance with their strength. The effects of a planet in the first Drekkana are realised at the commencement of the Dasha. The planet in the second Drekkana makes its effects felt in the middle of the Dasha. The effects of the planet in the third Drekkana are experienced at the end of the Dasha. If the planet be retrograde the effects would be in the reverse order, that is, the effects of such a planet in 3rd Drekkana are felt at the commencement of the Dasha and that of the retrograde planets in the first Drekkana are experienced at the end of the Dasha. 

The Dasha effects of Rahu and Ketu who are always retrograde will always be realised in the reverse order described above. 

दशािम्भे दशादीशे लग्नगे शुभदृग्युिे । स्वोच्चे स्वभे स्वमैरे र्ा शुभं िस्य दशाफलम् ॥५॥ र्षष्ठाऽष्टमव्ययिे च नीचास्तरिपुभस्थििे । अशुभं ित्फलं चाऽथ ब्रुर्े सर्वदशाफलम् ॥६॥ 

5-6: The effects are favourable if, at the commencement of the Dasha, the Dasha lord be in the Ascendant, in his sign of exaltation, in his own sign or in a friend's 

sign. The results are unfavourable if the Dasha lord be in the 6th, the 8th, or the 12th house, in his sign of debilitation or in an inimical sign. 

Effects of the Sun's Vimshottari Dasha 

मूलष्टरकोणे स्वक्षेरे स्वोच्चे र्ा पिमोच्चगे । 

के न्द्रष्टरकोणलाभिे भाग्यकमाथधपैयुविे ॥७॥ 

सूये बलसमायुक्ते तनजर्गवबलैयुविे । 

िस्तस्मन्दाये महि् सौख्यं धनलाभाद्वदकं शुभम् ॥८॥ 

अत्यिं िाजसन्मानमश्वांदोल्याद्वदकं शुभम् । 

सुिाथधपसमायुक्ते पुरलाभं च तर्न्दति ॥९॥ 

धनेशस्य च सम्बन्धे गजािैश्वयवमाद्वदशेि् । 

र्ाहनाथधपसम्बन्धे र्ाहनारयलाभकृ ि् ॥१०॥ 

नृपलिुष्टष्टतर्वत्ताढ्याः सेनाधीशाः सुखी निाः । 

र्िर्ाहनलाभि दशायां बसलनो िर्ेाः ॥११॥ 

7-11. During the Dasha of the Sun, there is acquisition of wealth, great felicity and honours from Government, if at the time of birth the Sun be in his own sign, in his sign of exaltation, in a Kendra, in the (11th), be associated with the lord of the 9th or the 10th and strong in his Varga. The native will be blessed with a son (children) if the Sun be with the lord of the 5th. He will acquire elephants and other kinds of wealth if the Sun be associated with the lord of the 2nd. He will enjoy comforts of conveyances if the Sun be associated with the lord of the 4th. He attains a high position like that of Army Chief by the beneficence of the king (Government) and enjoys all kinds of happiness. Thus, during the Dasha of a strong (and favourable) Sun, there are acquisitions of clothes, agricultural products, wealth, honours and conveyances etc. 

नीचे र्षडष्टके रिाःफे दबवले ु पापसंयुिे । 

िाहुके िुसमायुक्ते दह्स्िानाथधपसंयुिे ु ॥१२॥ 

िस्तस्मन्दाये महापीडा धनधान्यतर्नाशकृ ि । 

िाजकोपाः प्रर्ासि िाजदण्डो धनक्षयाः ॥१३॥ 

ज्विपीडा यशोहातनबवन्धुतमरतर्िोधकृ ि । 

ष्टपिृक्षयभयं चैर् गृहे त्वशुभमेर् च ॥१४॥ 

ष्टपिृर्गे मनस्तापं जन्द्वेर्षं च तर्न्दति । 

शुभदृष्टष्टयुिे सूये मध्ये िस्तस्मन् क्वश्रचत्सुखम् । 

पापग्र्हेण सन्दष्टेृ र्देत्पापफलं बुधाः ॥१५॥ 

12-15. During the Dasha of the Sun there will be advertise, loss of wealth, punishment from Government, exile, defamation, opposition by kinsmen, distress to 

father, inauspicious happening at home; distress to paternal and maternal uncles etc., anxiety and inimical relations with other people for no reason whatsoever, should the Sun be in his sign of debilitation (Libra), be weak in the 6th, the 8th or the 12th house or be associated with malefic planets or the lord of the 6th, the 8th or the 12th house. There will be some favourable effects at times if in the above situations, the Sun be aspected by benefice planets. The effects will always be unfavourable by the aspect malefic planets. 

# Effects of the Dasha of Moon

एर्ं सूयवफलं तर्प्र संक्षेपादद्वदिं ु मया । 

तर्ंशोत्तिीमिेनाथ ब्रुर्े चन्द्रदशाफलम् ॥१६॥ 

स्वोच्चे स्वक्षेरगे चैर् के न्द्रे लाभष्टरकोणगे । 

शुभग्रहेण संयुक्ते पूणे चन्द्रेबलैयुविे ॥१७॥ 

कमवभाग्याथधपैयुवक्ते र्ाहनेशबलैयुविे । 

आद्यिैश्वयवसौभाग्यधनधान्याद्वदलाभकृ ि ॥१८॥ 

गृहे िु शुभकायाणण र्ाहनं िाजदशवनम् । 

यत्नकायाथवससणद्धाः स्याद् गृहे लक्ष्मीकटाक्षकृ ि् ॥१९॥ 

तमरप्रभुर्शाद्भाग्यं िाज्यलाभं महत्सुखम् । 

अश्वान्दोल्याद्वदलाभं च श्वेिर्िाद्वदकं लभेि् ॥२०॥ 

पुरलाभाद्वदसिोर्षं गृहगोधनसंकु लम् । 

धनिानगिे चन्द्रे िुङ्गे स्वक्षेरगेऽष्टप र्ा ॥२१॥ 

अनेकधनलाभं च भाग्यर्ृणद्धमवहत्सुखम् । 

तनक्षेपिाजसन्मानं तर्द्यालाभं च तर्न्दति ॥२२॥ 

16-22. O Brahmin! After describing the effects of the Dasha of the Sun in brief, I will now come to the effects of the Vimshottari Dasha of the Moon. During the Dasha of the Moon from its commencement to the end, there will be opulence and glory, good fortune, gain of wealth, auspicious functions at home, dawn of fortune, attainment of a high position in Government (acquisition of Kingdom), acquisition of conveyance, clothes, birth of children and acquisition of cattle, should the Moon be in her sign of exaltation, in her own sign, in Kendra, in the 11th, 9th or 5th, be associated or aspected by benefices, be fully powerful and be associated with the lord of the 10th, the 9th or the 4th. There will be extra ordinary gains of wealth and luxuries if such a Moon be in the 2nd house. 

नीचे र्ा क्षीणचन्द्रे र्ा धनहातनभवतर्ष्यति । 

दसिक्ये ु बलसंयुक्ते क्वश्रचत्सौख्यं क्वश्रचद्धनम् ॥२३॥ 

दबवले ु पापसंयुक्ते देहजाड्यं मनोरुजम् । भृत्यपीडा तर्त्तहातनमािृर्गवजनाद्वधाः ॥२४॥ र्षष्ठाष्टमव्यये चन्द्रे दबवले ु पापसंयुिे । िाजद्वेर्षो मनोदाःखं ु धनधान्याद्वदनाशनम् ॥२५॥ मािृक्लेर्षं मनस्तापं देहजाड्यं मनोरुजम् । दाःिे ु चन्द्रे बलैयुवक्ते क्वश्रचिाभं क्वश्रचत्सुखम् । देहजाड्यं क्वश्रचच्चैर् शान्त्या िर शुभं द्वदशेि् ॥२६॥ 

23-26: Should the Moon be in her sign of debilitation or waning, there will be loss of wealth in her Dasha. If the Moon be in 3rd house, there will be happiness off and on. If the Moon be associated with malefic there will be idiocy, mental tension, trouble from employees and mother and loss of wealth. If the waning Moon be in the 6th, the 8th or the 12th or be associated with malefic, there will be inimical relations with Government, loss of wealth, distress to mother and similar evil effects. If a strong Moon be posited in the 6th, the 8th or the 12th, there will be troubles and good time off and on. 

Effects of the Dasha of Mars 

स्वभोच्चाद्वदगिस्यैर्ं नीचशरुभगस्य च । ब्रर्ीतम भूतमपुिवस्य शुभाऽशुभदशाफलम् ॥२७॥ पिमोच्चगिे भौमे स्वोच्चे मूलष्टरकोणगे । स्वक्षे के न्द्रष्टरकोणे र्ा लाभे र्ा धनगेऽष्टप र्ा ॥२८॥ सम्पूणवबलसंयुक्ते शुभदृष्टे शुभांशके । िाज्यलाभं भूतमलाभं धनधान्याद्वदलाभकृ ि् ॥२९॥ आथधक्यं िाजसम्मानं र्ाहनाम्बिभूर्षणम् । तर्देशे िानलाभं च सोदिाणां सुखं लभेि् ॥३०॥ के न्द्रे गिे सदा भौमे दसिक्येु बलसंयुिे । पिाक्रमाद्वद्वत्तलाभो युद्धे शरुजयो भर्ेि् ॥३१॥ कलरपुरतर्भर्ं िाजसम्मानमेर् च । दशादौ सुखमाप्नोति दशािे कष्टमाद्वदशेि् ॥३२॥ 

27-32. Should Mars be in his sign of exaltation, in his Moola-Trikona, in his own sign, in Kendra, in the 11th or the 2nd with strength, be in a benefice Amsa (Navamsha) and be associated with a benefice, there will be during his Dasha acquisition of kingdom (attainment of a high administrative or political position in Government, gain of wealth and land, recognition by Government), gain of wealth from foreign countries and acquisition of conveyances and ornaments. There will also be I happiness and good relations with co-born. If Mars with strength be in a Kendra or the 

3rd house, there will be gain of wealth through valour, victory over enemies, happiness from wife and children. There will, however, be possibility of some unfavourable effects at the end of the Dasha. 

# नीचाद्वददष्टभार्िे ु भौमे बलतर्र्सजविे

# पापयुक्ते पापदृष्टे सा दशा नेष्टदागयका ॥३३॥

33. Should the Mars be in his sign of debilitation, be weak, be in an inauspicious house (6, 8 or 12) or be associated or aspected by malefic, there will be, in his Dasha, loss of wealth, distress and similar unfavourable effects. 

Note: Mars being lord of a Kendra and Trikona is a Yoga karaka planet for the Cancer and Leo Ascendants. Being a lord of the 2nd and 9th, he is also very good for the Pisces Ascendants. For the natives of these Ascendants, therefore, Mars gives very beneficial effects during his Dasha if he is not afflicted in any way. 

Effects of the Dasha of Rahu 

एर्ं िाहोि के िोि कथयातम गृहाद्वदकम् । 

ियोदवशाफलज्ञप्त्यै िर्ाऽग्रे द्वद्वजनन्दन ॥३४॥ 

िाहोस्तु र्ृर्षभं के िोर्ृवसिकं िुङ्गसंज्ञकम् । 

मूलष्टरकोणकं ज्ञेयं युग्मं चापं क्रमेण च ॥३५॥ 

कु म्भाली च गृहौ प्रोक्तौ कन्यामीनौ च के नश्रचि् । 

िद्दाये बहुसौख्यं च धनधान्याद्वदसम्पदाम् ॥३६॥ 

तमत्र्प्प्रभुर्शाद्वदष्टं र्ाहनं पुरसम्भर्ाः । 

नर्ीनगृहतनमाणं धमवश्रचिा महोत्सर्ाः ॥३७॥ 

तर्देशिाजसन्मानं र्िालङ्कािभूर्षणम् । 

शुभयुक्ते शुभैदृवष्टे योगकािकसंयुिे ॥३८॥ 

के न्द्रष्टरकोओणलाभे र्ा दसिक्ये ु शुभिासशगे । 

महािाजप्रसादेन सर्वसम्पत्सुखार्हम् ॥३९॥ 

34-39: In order to clarify the effects of the Dasha of Rahu, I shall first mention the signs of exaltation and debilitation of Rahu and Ketu. The sign of exaltation of Rahu is Taurus. The sign of exaltation of Ketu is Scorpio. The Moola-Trikona of Rahu and Ketu are Gemini and Sagittarius respectively. The own signs of Rahu and Ketu are Aquarius and Scorpio in that order. Some learned have expressed the view that Virgo is the own sign of Rahu and Pisces is the own sign of Ketu. 

Should Rahu be in his sign of exaltation, etc. there will he, during the Dasha of Rahu, great happiness from acquisition of wealth, agricultural products etc., acquisition of conveyances with the help of friends and Government, construction of a new house, birth of sons (children), religious inclinations, recognition from Government of foreign countries and gain of wealth, clothes, etc. If Rahu be associated or aspected by benefices, be in a benefice sign and be in the 1st, the 4th, 

the 7th, the 10th, the 11th or the 3rd house, there will be during his Dasha all kinds of comforts by the beneficence of the Government, acquisition of wealth through a foreign Government or sovereign and felicity at home. 

यर्नप्रभुसन्मानं ग्र्हे कल्याणसम्भर्म् । िन्ध्रे र्ा व्ययगे िाहौ िद्दाये कष्टमाद्वदशेि् ॥४०॥ पापग्रहेण सम्बन्धे मािकग्र्हसंयुिे । नीचिासशगिे र्ाष्टप िानभ्रंशो मनोव्यथा ॥४१॥ तर्नाशो दािपुराणां कु स्थत्सिान्नं च भोजनम् । दशादौ देहपीडा च धनधान्यपरिच्युतिाः ॥४२॥ दशामध्ये िु सौख्यं स्याि् स्वदेशे धनलाभकृ ि् । दशािे कष्टमाप्नोति िानभ्रंशो मनोव्यथा ॥४३॥ 

40-43. If Rahu be in the 8th or the 12th, there will be during his Dasha all kinds of troubles and distress. If Rahu be associated with a malefic or maraka (killer) planet or be in his sign of debilitation (Scorpio), there will be loss of position, destruction of his residential house, mental agony, trouble to wife and children and misfortune of getting bad food. There will be loss of wealth at the commencement of the Dasha, some relief and gain of wealth in his own country and distress and anxieties during the last portion of the Dasha. 

Notes: Rahu becomes a Yoga karaka if he gets associated with a Yoga karaka planet. In these circumstances, he gives very beneficial results in his Dasha if he is well placed and un-afflicted. 

Effects of the Dasha of Jupiter 

याः सर्ेर्षु नाभोगेर्षु बुधैितिशुभाः स्मृिाः । िस्य देर्ेन्द्रपूज्यस्य कथयातम दशाफलम् ॥४४॥ 

44. Now I am going to describe the effects of the Dasha of Jupiter, the great benefice and preceptor of the Gods. 

मूलष्टरकोणलाभे र्ा िुंगांशे स्वांशगेऽष्टप र्ा ॥४५॥ िाज्यलाभं महापौरुर्षं िाजसन्मानकीिवनम् । गजर्ासजसमायुक्तं देर्ब्राह्मणपूजनम् ॥४६॥ 

दािपुराद्वदसौख्यं च र्ाहनांबिलाभजम् । यज्ञाद्वदकमवससणद्धाः स्याद्वेदाििर्णाद्वदकम् ॥४७॥ महािाजप्रसादेनाऽभीष्टससणद्धाः सुखार्हा । 

# आन्दोसलकाद्वदलाभि कल्याणं च महत्सुखम् ॥४८॥

45-48. If the Jupiter be in his sign of exaltation, in his own sign, in his Moola-Trikona, in the 10th, the 5th or the 9th, in his own or exalted Navamsha, there will be during his Dasha, acquisition of kingdom (attainment of high political or administrative position in Government), great felicity, recognition by Government acquisition of conveyances and clothes, devotion to deities and Brahmins, happiness in respect of his wife and children and success in performance of religious sacrifices, (oblations-यज्ञ-कायध) 

पुरदािाद्वदलाभि अन्नदानं महब्दत्प्रयम् । 

नीचास्तपापसंयुक्ते जीर्ै रिष्फाष्टसंयुिे ॥४९॥ 

िानभ्रंशं मनस्तापं पुरपीडामहद्भयम् । 

पश्वाद्वदधनहातनि िीथवयाराद्वदकं लभेि् ॥५०॥ 

आदौ कष्टफलं चैर् चिुष्पाज्जीर्लाभकृ ि् । 

मध्यािे सुखमाप्नोति िाजसम्मानर्ैभर्म् ॥५१॥ 

49-51. Should Jupiter be in his sign of debilitation, combust in association with malefic or in the 6th or the 8th, there will be during his Dasha loss of residential premises, anxiety, Distress to children, loss of cattle and pilgrimage (visit to religious places). The Dasha will give some unfavourable effects at its commencement only. During the latter part of the Dasha, there will be good effects like gain of wealth, awards from and recognition by Government. 

Effects or the Dasha or Saturn 

अथ सर्ेर्षु खेटेर्षु योऽतिहीनाः प्रकीतिविाः । 

िस्य भास्किपुरस्य कथयातम दशाफलम् ॥५२॥ 

52. Now I will describe to you the effects of the Dasha of the Saturn who is considered the, vilest and most inferior (हीन) amongst all the planets. 

स्वोच्चे स्वक्षेरगे मन्दे तमरक्षेरेऽथ र्ा यद्वद । 

मूलष्टरकोणे भाग्ये र्ा िुंगांशे स्वांशगेऽष्टप र्ा ॥५३॥ 

दसिक्ये ु लाभगे चैर् िाजसम्मानर्ैभर्म् । 

सत्कीतिवधवनलाभि तर्द्यार्ादतर्नोदकृ ि् ॥५४॥ 

महािाजप्रसादेन गजर्ाहनभूर्षणम् । 

िाजयोगं प्रकु र्ीि सेनाधीशान्महत्सुखम् ॥५५॥ 

लक्ष्मीकटाक्षश्रचिातन िाज्यलाभं किोति च । 

गृहे कल्याणसम्पथत्तदािपुराद्वदलाभकृ ि् ॥५६॥ 

53-56. Should Saturn be in his sign of exaltation, in his own or Moola-Trikona or friendly sign, in his own or exalted Navamsha and in the 3rd or the 11th, there will be during his Dasha, recognition by Government, opulence and glory, name and fame, success in educational sphere, acquisition of conveyances and ornaments etc., gain of wealth, favours from Government, attainment of a high position like commander of an army, acquisition of kingdom, benevolence of goddess Lakshmi, gain of property and birth of children. 

र्षष्ठाष्टमव्यये मन्दे नीचे र्ाऽस्तङ्गिेऽष्टप र्ा । 

तर्र्षशिाद्वदपीडा च िाभ्रंशं महद्भयम् ॥५७॥ 

ष्टपिृमािृतर्योगं च दािपुराद्वदपीडनम् । 

िाजर्ैसाःअम्यकायाणण ह्यतनष्टं बन्धनं िथा ॥५८॥ 

शुभयुक्ते सक्षिे मन्दे योगकािकसंयुिे । 

के न्द्रष्टरकोणलाभे र्ा मीनगे कामुवके शनौ ॥५९॥ 

िाज्यलाभं महोत्साहं गजश्वाम्बिसंकु लम् ॥६०॥ 

57-60. If Saturn be in the 6th, the 8th, the 12th, in his, sign of debilitation, or combust, there will be during the Dasha of Saturn, ill effects from poison, injury from weapons separation from father, distress to wife and children, disaster as a result of displeasure of Government, imprisonment etc. If Saturn be, aspected by or associated with a benefice, be in Kendra or Trikona in Sagittarius or Pisces, there will be, acquisition of kingdom (attainment of a high position in Government), conveyances and clothes. 

Notes: Saturn being lord of Kendra and Trikona is a Yoga karaka planet for the Taurus and Libra ascendants. He will, therefore, yield very beneficial results during his Dasha if he is well placed and un-afflicted. 

Effects of the Dasha of Mercury 

अथ सर्वनभोगेर्षु याः कु मािाः प्रकीतिविाः । 

िस्य िािेशपुरस्य कथयातम दशाफलम् ॥६१॥ 

61. Now I am going to describe the effects of the Dasha of Mercury who is called a Kumar (in his teens) amongst all the planets. 

स्वोच्चे स्वक्षेरसंयुक्ते के न्द्रलाभष्टरकोणगे । 

तमरक्षेरसमायुक्ते सौम्ये दाये महत्सुखम् ॥६२॥ 

धनधान्याद्वदलाभं च सत्कीतिवधनसम्पदाम् । 

ज्ञानाथधक्यं नृपप्रीतिं सत्कमवगुणर्द्धवनम् ॥६३॥ 

पुरदािाद्वदसौख्यं च देहािोग्यं महत्सुखम् । 

क्षीिेण भोजनं सौख्यं व्यापािािभिे धनम् ॥६४॥ 

# शुभदृष्टष्टयुिे सौम्ये भाग्ये कमाथधपे दशा । आथधपत्ये बलर्िी सम्पू्फव लदाद्वदका ॥६५॥

62-65. If Mercury be in his sign of exaltation, in his own sign. in a friendly sign or in the 11th, 5th or the 9th there will be during his Dasha, acquisition of wealth, gain of reputation, improvement in knowledge, benevolence of Government, auspicious functions, happiness from wife and children, good health, availability of sweetish preparations, profits in business, etc. If Mercury be aspected by a benefice be in the 9th, or be lord of the 10th, the aforesaid beneficial results will be experienced in full and there will be great felicity all round. 

पापग्रहयुिे दृष्टे िाजद्वेर्षं मनोरुजम् । बन्धुजनतर्िोधं च तर्देशगमनं लभेि् ॥६६॥ पिप्रेष्यं च कलहं मूिवकृ च्छान्महन्भयम् । र्षष्ठाष्टमव्यये सौम्ये लाभभोगाथवनाशनम् ॥६७॥ 

र्ािपीडां धनं चैर्ं पाण्डु िोगं तर्तनद्वदवशेि् । नृपचौिागग्नभीतिं च कृ ष्टर्षगोभूतमनाशनम् ॥६८॥ दशादौ धनधान्यं च तर्द्यालाभं महत्सुखम् । पुरकल्याणसम्पथत्ताः सन्मागे धनलाभकृ ि् ॥६९॥ मध्ये निेन्द्रसन्मानमिे दाःखंु भतर्ष्यति ॥७०॥ 

66-70. If Mercury be associated with a Malefic, there will be during his Dasha, punishment by Government, inimical relations with Kinsmen, journey to a foreign country, dependence on others and possibility of urinary troubles. If Mercury be in the 6th, the 8th or the 12th, there will be loss of wealth due to indulgence in lascivious activities, possibility of suffering from Rheumatism and jaundice, danger of thefts and malevolence of Government, loss of land and cattle, etc. At the commencement of the Dasha of Mercury, there will be gains of wealth, betterment in the educational sphere, birth of children and happiness. In the middle of the Dasha, there will be recognition from Government. The last part of the Dasha will be distressful. 

Effects of the Dasha of Ketu 

यस्तमोग्रहयोमवध्ये कबन्धाः कथ्यिे बुधैाः । िस्य के िोरिदानीं िे कथेयातम दशाफलम् ॥७१॥ 

71. Now I will tell you about the Dasha of Ketu who is a headless trunk (कबन्ध) amongst all the plants. 

के न्द्रे लाभे ष्टरकोणे र् शुभिाशौ शुभेसक्षिे । 

स्वोच्चे र्ा शुभर्गे र्ा िाजप्रीतिं मनोनुगम् ॥७२॥ देशाग्रामाथधपत्यं च र्ाहनं पुरसम्भर्म् । देशाििप्रयाणं च तनद्वदवशेि् िि् सुखार्हम् ॥७३॥ पुरदािसुखं चैर् चिुष्पाज्जीर्लाभकृ ि् । दसिक्ये ु र्षष्ठलाभे र्ा के िुदाये सुखं द्वदशेि् ॥७४॥ िाज्यं किोति तमरांशं गजर्ासजसमन्तििम् । दशदौ िाजयोगि दशामध्ये महद्भयम् ॥७५॥ 

अिे दिाटनंू चैर् देहतर्िमणं िथा । धने िन्ध्रे व्यये के िौ पापदृष्टष्टयुिेसक्षिे ॥७६॥ तनगडं बन्धुनाशं च िानभ्रंशं मनोरुजम् । शूद्रसङ्गाद्वदलाभं च कु रुिे िोगसंकु लम् ॥७७॥ 

72-77. Should Ketu be in a Kendra, Trikona or the 11th, in a benefice sign, in his sign of exaltation or in his own sign, there will be during his Dasha, cordial relations with the King (Government), desired headship of a country or village, comforts of conveyances, happiness from children, gain from foreign countries, happiness from wife and acquisition of cattle. If Ketu be in the 3rd, the 6th or the 11th, there will be in his Dasha, acquisition of kingdom (attainment of a high position in Government), good relations with friends and opportunities for acquisition of elephants. At the commencement of Ketu Dasha, there will be Raja-yoga. During the middle portion of the Dasha, there will be possibilities of fearfulness and in the last part there will be sufferings from ailments and journeys to distant places. If Ketu be in 2nd, 8th or 12th, or be aspected by a malefic, there will be imprisonment, destruction of kinsmen and residential premises, anxieties, company of menials, and diseases. 

Effects of the Dasha of Venus 

अथ भूिेर्षु याः शुक्रा मदरूपेण तिष्ठति । िस्य दैत्यगुिोतर्वप्र कथयातम दशाफलम् ॥७८॥ 

78. Now I will describe the effects of the Dasha of Venus who is the incarnate of intoxication, ecstasy delight and pride amongst all the planets. 

पिमोच्चगिे शुक्रे स्वोच्चे स्वक्षेरके न्द्रगे । नृपाऽथभर्षेकसम्प्राब्दप्तर्ाहनाऽम्बिभूर्षणम् ॥७९॥ गजाश्वपशुलाभं च तनत्यं तमष्ठान्नभोजनम् । अखण्डमण्डलाधीशािाजसन्मानर्ैभर्म् ॥८०॥ मृदङ्गर्ाद्यघोर्षं च गृहे लक्ष्मीकटाक्षकृ ि् । 

# ष्टरकोणिे तनजे िस्तस्मन् िाज्याथवगृहहसम्पदाः ॥८१॥

# तर्र्ाहोत्सर्कायाणण पुरकल्याणर्ैभर्म् । सेनाथधपत्यं कु रुिे इष्टबन्धुसमागनम् ॥८२॥

79-82. Should Venus be in his sign of exaltation, in his own sign or in. Kendra or Trikona, there will be during his Dasha, acquisition of fancy clothes, ornaments, conveyances, cattle and land etc., availability of sweet preparations every day, recognition from the sovereign, luxurious functions of songs and dances etc. by the benevolence of Goddess Lakshmi. If Venus be in his Moola-Trikona, during his Dasha, there will definitely be acquisition of kingdom (attainment of a high position in Government), acquisition of a house, birth of children and grandchildren, celebration of marriage in the family, attainment of a high position like the commander of an army, visits of friends, recovery of lost wealth, property or kingdom (reinstatement in a high position). 

नष्टिाज्याद्धनप्राब्दप्तं गृहे गोधनसङ् ग्रहम् । र्षष्ठाष्टमव्यये शुक्रे नीचे र्ा व्ययिासशगे ॥८३॥ आत्मबन्धुजनद्वेर्षं दािर्गाद्वदपीडनम् । व्यर्सायारलं नष्टं गोमद्वहष्याद्वदहातनकृ ि् ॥८४॥ दािपुराद्वदपीडा र्ा आत्मबन्धुतर्योगकृ ि् । 

83-84½: If Venus be in the 6th, the 8th or the 12th, there will be during is Dasha, inimical relations with kinsmen 1 distress to wife, losses in business, destruction of cattle and separation from relations, 

भाग्यकमाथधपत्येन लग्नर्ाहनिासशगे ॥८५॥ िद्दशायां महत्सौख्यं देशग्रामाथधपालिा । देर्ालयिडागाद्वदपुण्यकमवसु संग्रहाः ॥८६॥ अन्नदाने महत्सौख्यं तनत्यं तमष्ठान्नभोजनम् । उत्साहाः कीतिवसम्पत्ती िीपुरधनसम्पदाः ॥८७॥ 

85-87. Should Venus be in the 4th, as lord of the 9th or the 10th, there will be during his Dasha, attainment of ruler-ship of a country or village, performance of pious deeds like building of reservoirs, temples and giving grains etc., in charity, availability of sweet preparations every day, vigour in work, name and fame and happiness from wife and children. 

स्वभुक्तौ फलमेर्ं स्याद्बलान्यन्यातन भुगक्तर्षु । द्वद्विीयद्यूननाथे िु देहपीडा भतर्ष्यति ॥८८॥ 

# िद्दोर्षपरिहािाथं रुद्रं र्ा त्र्यम्बकं जपेि् । स्वेिां गां मद्वहर्षीं दव्यादािोग्यं च ििो भर्ेि् ॥८९॥

88-89. Similar are the effects of Venus in his sub-periods. If Venus be lord of the 2nd or the 7th (two maraka houses), there will be during his Dasha, physical pains and troubles. To get alleviation from those troubles the native should perform Shatarudreeya (शतरुद्रीय) or Mrityunjaya Japa in the prescribed manner and give in charity a cow or female buffalo. 

Note: Being lord of a Kendra and Trikona, Venus is a yoga karaka planet for the Capricorn and Aquarius ascendants. Being lord of the 2nd and the 9th, he is a very auspicious planet for the Virgo Ascendant. During his Dasha Venus will yield very beneficial results in respect of these Ascendants, if he is well placed and is not afflicted in any way. 

# अथ तिशेषनक्षत्रदशाफलाध्यायः ॥४८॥

# Chapter 48. Distinctive Effects of Nakshatra Dasha or of Vimshottari Dasha lords of various houses

िानस्थितिर्शेनैर्ं फलं प्रोक्तं पुिािनैाः । 

तमथो भार्ेशसम्बन्धात्फलातन कथयाम्यहम् ॥१॥ 

1. If the lord of the 10th be placed in an auspicious house, in his sign of exaltation etc., his Dasha effects will be favourable. The effects will be adverse if the lord of the 10th is in his sign of debilitation and occupies an inauspicious house. This proves that an inauspicious planet in his sign of exaltation etc., will not produce infavourable results if placed in an auspicious house and a benefice being in his sign of debilitation and being posited in an, inauspicious house will produce adverse effects. Now I will describe the effects of the Dasha of the lords of various houses & who are related to each other. 

लग्नेशस्य गशाकाले सत्कीतिदेहजं सुखम् । 

धनेशस्य दशायां िु क्लेशो र्ा मृत्युिो भयम् ॥२॥ 

सहजेशदशाकाले ज्ञेयं पापफलं नृणाम् । 

सुखाधीशदशायां िु गृहभूतमसुखं भर्ेि् ॥३॥ 

पञ्चमेशस्य पाके च तर्द्याब्दप्ताः पुरजं सुखम् । 

िोगेशस्य दशाकाले देहपीडा रिपोभवयम् ॥४॥ 

2-4. There will be physical well-being in the Dasha of the lord of the Ascendant, distress and possibility of death in the Dasha of the lord of the 2nd, unfavourable effects in the Dasha of the lord of the 3rd, acquisition of house and land in the Dasha of the lord of the 4th, progress in educational sphere and happiness from the children in the Dasha of the lord of the 5th and danger from enemies and ill health in the Dasha of the lord of the 6th. 

सप्तमेशस्य पाके िु िीपीडा मृत्युिो भयम् । 

अष्टमेशदशाकाले मृत्युभीतिधवनक्षतिाः ॥५॥ 

धमवशस्य दशायां च भूरििाभो यशाःसुखम् । 

दशमेशदशाकाले सम्मानं नृपसंसद्वद ॥६॥ 

लाभेशस्य दशाकाले लाभे बाधा रुजोभयम् । 

# व्ययेशस्य दशा नृणां बहुकष्टप्रदा द्वद्वज ॥७॥ दशािम्भे शुभिाने स्थििस्याष्टप शुभं फलम् । अशुभिानगस्यैर्ं शुभस्याष्टप न शोभनम् ॥८॥

5-8. There will be distress to wife and the possibility of the death of the native, in the Dasha of the lord of the 7th, possibility of death and financial losses in the Dasha of the lord of the 8th, improvement in educational sphere, religious mindedness and unexpected gains of wealth in the Dasha of the lord of the 9th, recognition from and awards by Government in the Dasha of the lord of the 10th, obstacles in gains of wealth and possibility of diseases in the Dasha of the lord of the 11th and distress and danger from diseases in the Dasha of the lord of the 12th house. 

A planet posited in an auspicious house like Trikona etc., at the commencement of the Dasha, produces favourable results in his Dasha. The planet posited in the 6th, the 8th or the 12th at that time, yields only adverse results during his Dasha. It is, therefore, essential that the placement of a planet at the time or birth and at the commencement of the Dasha should both be taken into account for the assessment of the Dasha effects. 

Note: It has been stated that the lords of the 2nd, 3rd, 6th, 7th, 8th, 11th and 12th will produce evil effects during their Dasha. The 2nd and 7th are known as maraka houses. There is possibility of death or death like suffering during their Dasha. But these two other houses have many other good indications, for the 2nd house is called the house of wealth. There will definitely be gains of wealth during the Dasha of the lord of the 2nd if he is well placed in the birth chart. Similarly tile 7th house indicates marriage amongst other things. If the lord of the 7th is well placed, there will be auspicious celebrations during his Dasha. 

In Chapter 34 it is stated that the lord of 3rd, 6th and 11th will give evil effects. Our view which is based on long experience is that these lords will not give unfavourable effects if they are in the 3rd, 6th and 11th respectively in their own signs. The placement of the lord of the 11th in the 2nd and of the lord of the 2nd in the 11th gives rise to a very powerful Dhana yoga. 

The 6th, 8th and 12th are Dusthanas (inauspicious houses). All authorities on Hindu Astrology agree in this respect. But even for these houses, some recognised authorities have made exceptions in certain circumstances. In this connection, it would be relevant to invite attention of the readers to Chapter VI of Mantreswara’s Phaladeepika. According to Mantreswara the lords of the 6th, the 8th and the 12th also produce yoga effects in the following circumstances: 

(1) If the 6th house is occupied or aspected by malefic and the lord of the 6th is in Dusthanas (6th, 8th or 12th), such a disposition produces Harsha yoga. The person born in Harsha yoga will be endowed with happiness, enjoyment, good fortune and a strong constitution will overcome his enemies, and will be afraid to commit sinful acts. He will become a friend of illustrious and prominent people. He will have wealth, splendour, friends, fame and sons. 

(2) If the lord of the 8th house is placed in the 6th, the 8th or the 12th, the yoga caused is known as Sarala Yoga. The person born in this Yoga will be long-lived, 

resolute, Tearless, prosperous and will be endowed with learning, children and riches. He will achieve success in his undertakings, overcome his foes, be pure, and widely celebrated. 

(3) If the lord of the 12th be in a Dusthanas and be aspected by or associated with malefic, the Yoga so produced is called Vimala Yoga. The person born in this Yoga will spend little and save much money. He will be good to everybody. He will be happy and independent and will have respectable profession or conduct and will be renowned for his good qualities. 

It is but natural that the above lords will produce Yoga effects during their Dasha. 

पञ्चमेशेन युक्तस्य कमेशस्य दशा शुभा । नर्मेशेन युक्तस्य कमेशस्यातिशभना ॥९॥ पञ्चमेशेन युक्तस्य ग्रहस्याष्टप दशा शुभा । िथा धमवपयुक्तस्य दशा पिमशोभना ॥१०॥ सुखेशसद्वहिस्याष्टप धमेशस्य दशा शुभा । पञ्चमिानगस्याष्टप मानेशस्य दशाशुभा ॥११॥ एर्ं ष्टरकोणनाथानां के न्द्रिानां दशााः शुभााः । िथा कोणस्थििानां च के न्द्रेशानां दशााः शुभााः ॥१२॥ के न्द्रेशाः कोणभार्िाः कोणेशाः के न्द्रगो यद्वद । ियोदवशां शुभां प्राहुज्योतिाःशाितर्दो जनााः ॥१३॥ 

9-13. If the lord of the 9th and 10th be in conjunction with the lord of the 5th, their Dasha produce beneficial results. 

If any other planet be associated with the lord of the 5th, his Dasha will be favourable. The Dasha of the lords of the 10th and 4th produce favourable effects if they be associated with the lord of the 9th. If the lord of Kendra be in a Trikona or the lord of Trikona be in a Kendra, their Dasha prove extremely favourable. 

र्षष्ठाष्टमव्ययाधीशा अष्टप कोणेशसंयुिा । िेर्षां दशाऽष्टप शुभदा कथथिा कालकोतर्दैाः ॥१४॥ कोणेशो यद्वद के म्द्रिाः के न्द्रेशो यद्वद कोणगाः । िाभ्यां युक्तस्य खेटस्य दृष्टष्टयुक्तस्य चैियोाः ॥१५॥ दशां शुभप्रदां प्राहुतर्वद्वांसो दैर्श्रचिकााः । लग्नेशो धमवभार्िो धमेशो लग्नगो यद्वद ॥१६॥ एियोस्तु दशाकाले सुखधमवसमुद्भर्ाः । कमेशो लग्निासशिो लग्नेशाः कमवभार्गाः ॥१७॥ ियोदवशातर्पाके िु िाज्यलाभो भर्ेदध्रुर्म् ् । 

14- 17½: The Dasha of the lords of the 6th, the 8th or the 12th also become favourable if they get associated with the lord of a Trikona. If the lord of a Kendra be in a Trikona or the lord of the Trikona in Kendra, the Dasha of the planet associated with either of them, becomes favourable. The Dasha of a planet aspected by the lord of a Kendra or Trikona is also favourable. If the lord of 9th be in the Ascendant and the lord of the Ascendant in the 9th, the Dasha of both of them will produce extremely beneficial results. There will be acquisition of a kingdom (attainment of a high position in Government) in the Dasha of the lords of the Ascendant and 10th, if the lord of the 10th be in the Ascendant and the lord of the Ascend ant be in the 10th. 

ष्टरर्षडायगिानां च ष्टरर्षडायाथधपैयुवजम् ॥१८॥ शुभानामष्टप खेटानां दशा पापफलप्रदा । मािकिानगानां च मािके शयुजामष्टप ॥१९॥ िन्ध्रिानगिानां च दशाऽतनष्टफलप्रदा । एर्ं भार्ेशसम्बन्धादिनीयं ू दशाफलम् ॥२०॥ 

18-20. The Dasha of the lord of the 3rd, 6th and 11th, of the planets posited in them and of the planets in conjunction with the above, will prove unfavourable. The Dasha of the planets associated with the lords of Maraka house, namely the 2nd and 7th, in the 2nd or 7th, and of the planet posited in the 8th, will produce unfavourable effects. Thus, the Dasha should be considered favourable after taking into account the placement of a planet and his relationship of one planet with the other. 

Notes: What the above is intended to convey is that the Dasha of the lords of Kendra’s and Trikona and of the planets related to them will be favourable and the Dasha of the lords of other houses and the planets associated with or aspected by them, will be unfavourable. 

It would be pertinent to point out at this juncture that it has been stated earlier that the Dasha of Rahu and Ketu if posited in the 3rd, 6th and 11th would be favourable. This should be kept in view. There are some con traditions in almost all the ancient classical works and they should be made use of in judicious manner. Rahu and Ketu give favourable results in the 3rd, 6th and 11th, the three Upachaya (उपचय) houses. 

# अथ कालचक्रदशाफलाध्यायः ॥४९॥

# Chapter 49. Effects of the Kalachakra Dasha

िरादौ िासशनाथानां सूयादीनां फलं ब्रुर्े ॥१॥ 

िक्तष्टपत्ताद्वदिो व्याथधं नृणामकव फलं र्देि् । 

धनकीतिवप्रजार्ृणद्धर्िाभिणदाः शशी ॥२॥ 

ज्विमाशु द्वदशेि् पैत्त्यं ग्रण्डिस्फोटं कु जस्तथा । 

प्रजानां च धनानां च सदा र्ृणद्धं बुधो द्वदशेि् ॥३॥ 

धनं कीतिं प्रजार्ृणद्धं नानाभोगं बृहस्पतिाः । 

तर्द्यार्ृणद्धतर्वर्ाहि गृहं धान्यं भृगोाः फलम् ॥४॥ 

िापाथधक्यं महद्दाःखं ु बन्धुनाशाः शनेाः फलम् । 

एर्मकाद्वदयोगेन र्देद्रासशदशाफलम् ॥५॥ 

1-5. The Sage said-O Brahmin! I am now going to describe to you the effects of the Kalachakra Dasha. 

During the Dasha of the rashi (sign) owned or occupied by the Sun, there will be ill health due to the blood or bile troubles. In the Dasha of the rashi owned or occupied by the Moon, there will be gain of wealth and clothes, name and fame and birth of children. In the Dasha of the rashi owned or occupied by Mars, there will be bilious fever, gout and wounds. In the Dasha of the rashi owned or occupied by Mercury, there will be acquisition of wealth and birth of children. In the Dasha of the rashi owned and occupied by Jupiter there will be increase in the number of children, acquisition of wealth and enjoyment. In the Dasha of the rashi owned or occupied by Venus, there will be acquisition of learning, marriage and gain of wealth. In the Dasha of the rashi occupied by Saturn, there will be all kinds of adverse happenings. 

The effects of Dasha on the basis of the Navamsha of each Rashi 

The effects of the Dasha of Padas of Aries 

मेर्षे िु िक्तपीडा च र्ृर्षभे धान्यर्द्धवनम् । 

तमथुने ज्ञानसम्पान्निान्द्रे धनपतिभवर्ेि् ॥६॥ 

सूयवक्षे शरुबाधा च कन्या िीणां च नाशनं । 

िासलके िाजमन्तन्त्रत्वं र्ृसिके मिणं भर्ेि् ॥७॥ 

6-7. In the Kalachakra Dasha of Aries in Aries Navamsha, there will be distress due to troubles caused by the pollution of blood. In the Dasha of Aries in the 

Navamsha of Taurus, there will be increase in wealth and agricultural product. In, the Navamsha of Gemini, there will be advancement of knowledge. In the Navamsha of Cancer there will be acquisition of wealth, in the Leo Navamsha danger from enemies, in the Virgo Navamsha distress to wife, in the Libra Navamsha kingship, in Scorpio Navamsha death and no Sagittarius Navamsha acquisition of wealth. Such be the effects of the 9 Padas of Aries. In assessing the net effects, the nature of planet occupying the rashi should also be taken into account. 

Notes: In the example of Kalachakra Dasha in Chapter 46, there was balance of 2 years and 3 months of the Dasha of Taurus at the birth. The lord of Taurus is Venus. Therefore, there would be advancement of learning during the Dasha. In addition, a result of the Navamsha of Taurus in Aries, there will be increase in the agricultural products. But at birth Mars occupies Taurus (see example horoscope in Chapter 46) and there are quarter aspects of its lord Venus and other benefices. There will therefore, be medium increase in wealth and agricultural product. 

Effects of the Dasha of Navamsha Rashi of Taurus 

अथवलाभो भर्ेच्चापे मेर्षस्य नर्भागके । 

मकिे पापकमाणण कु म्भे र्ाणणज्यमेर् च ॥८॥ 

मीने सर्ाथवससणद्धि र्ृसिके ष्वगग्निो भयम् । 

िौसलके िाजपूज्यि कन्यायां शरुर्धवनम् ॥९॥ 

शसशभे दािसम्बाधा ससंहे च त्वसक्षिोगकृ ि् । 

तमथुने र्ृथत्तबाधा स्याद्वर्षभस्यृ नर्ांशके ॥१०॥ 

8-10. In the Dasha of Capricorn Navamsha in Taurus, there will be tendency to perform undesirable deeds along with more adverse effects. In the Aquarius Navamsha there will be profits in business, in the Pisces Navamsha success in all ventures, in the Dasha of Scorpio Navamsha - danger from fire, in the Dasha of Libra Navamsha recognition from Government and reverence from all, in the Dasha of Virgo Navamsha-danger from enemies, in, the Dasha of Cancer Navamsha- distress to wife, in the Dasha of Leo Navamsha- diseases of eyes and in the Dasha of Gemini Navamsha-obstacles in earning livelihood. Such will be the effects of the 9 Navamsha of Taurus. Similar interpretation should be made of further verses on this subject. 

Effect of the Dasha of Navamsha of Gemini 

र्ृर्षभे त्वथवलाभाि मेर्षे िु ज्वििोगकृ ि् । 

मीने िु मािुलप्रीतिाः कु म्भे शरुप्रर्द्धवनम् ॥११॥ 

मृगे चौिस्य सम्बाधा धनुष्टर्ष शिर्धवनम् । 

मेर्षे िु शिसंघािो र्ृर्षभे कलहो भर्ेि् ॥१२॥ 

11-12. In Gemini, in the Dasha of the Taurus Amsa, there will be acquisition of wealth, in the Dasha of Aries Amsa attacks of fever, in the Dasha of Pisces Amsaaffectionate relations with maternal uncle, in the Dasha of Aquarius Amsa increase in 

the number of enemies, in the Dasha of Capricorn Amsa-danger from thieves, in the Dasha of Sagittarius Amsa increase in the stock of weapons, in the Dasha of Taurus Amsa injury by some weapon and in the Dasha of Gemini Amsa enjoyment. 

Effects of Dasha of the Navamsha Rāśhis of Cancer 

तमथुने सुखमाप्नोति तमथुनस्य नर्ांशके । 

ककव टे सङ्कटप्राब्दप्ताः ससंहे िाजप्रकोपकृ ि् ॥१३॥ 

कन्यायां भ्रािृपूजा र् िौसलके ष्टप्रयकृ न्निाः । 

र्ृसिके ष्टपिृबाधा स्याि् चापे ज्ञानधनोदयाः ॥१४॥ 

मकिे जलभीतिाः स्याि् कु म्भे धान्यतर्र्धवनम् । 

मीने च सुखसम्पथत्ताः ककव टस्य नर्ांशके ॥१५॥ 

13-15. In Cancer, in the Dasha of Cancer Amsa there will be distress, in the Dasha of Leo Amsa-displeasure of the Sovereign, in the Dasha of Virgo Amsareverence from Kinsmen, in the Dasha of Libra Amsa-beneficence, in the Dasha of Scorpio Amsa-creation of obstacles by father, in the Dasha of Sagittarius Amsaincrease of learning and wealth, in the Dasha of Capricorn Amsa-danger from water, in the Dasha of Aquarius Amsa-increase in the production of agricultural products, and in the Dasha of the Pisces Amsa-acquisition of more wealth and enjoyment. 

Effects of the Dasha of the Navamsha Rāśhis of Leo 

र्ृसिके कलाः पीडा िौसलके ह्यथधकं फलम् । 

कन्यायामतिलाभि शशांके मृगबाथधका ॥१६॥ 

ससंहे च पुरलाभि तमथुने शरुर्द्धवनम् । 

र्ृर्षेाः चिुष्पदािाभो मेर्षांशे पशुिो भयम् । 

मीने िु दीघवयारा स्याि् ससंहस्य नर्भागके ॥१७॥ 

16-17. In Leo, in the Dasha of Navamsha of Scorpio there will be distress and disputes, in the Dasha of Libra Amsa-extraordinary gains, in the Dasha of Virgo Amsagains of wealth, in the Dasha of Cancer Amsa-danger from wild animals, in the Dasha of Leo Amsa-birth of a son, in the Dasha of Gemini Amsa-increase of enemies, in the Dasha of Taurus Amsa - gains from sale of cattle, in the Dasha of Aries Amsa-danger from animals and in the Dasha of Pisces Amsa-journeys to distant places. 

Effects of Dasha of Navamsha Rāśhis of Virgo 

कु म्भे िु धनलाभि मकिे द्रव्यलाभकृ ि् । 

धनुष्टर्ष भ्रािृसंसगो मेर्षे मािृतर्र्द्धवनम् ॥१८॥ 

र्ृर्षभे पुरर्ृणद्धाः स्यान्तन्मथुने शरुर्द्धवनम् । 

शसशभे िु ण्डियां प्रीतिाः ससंहे व्याथधतर्र्द्धवनम् ॥१९॥ 

18-19. In Virgo, in the Dasha of Aquarius Amsa there will be acquisition of wealth, in the Dasha of Capricorn Amsa - financial gains, in the Dasha or Sagittarius Amsa-mingling with kinsmen, in the Das of Aries Amsa-happiness from mother, in the Dasha of Taurus Amsa--birth of children, in the Dasha of Gemini Amsa--increase in enemies, in the Dasha of Cancer Amsa - love with some woman, in the Dasha of Leo Amsa-aggravation of diseases, and in the Dasha of Virgo Amsa-birth of more children. 

Effects or Dasha of Navamsha Rashi of Libra 

कन्यायां पुरर्ृणद्धाः स्यात्कन्याया नर्मांशके । 

िुलायामथवलाभि र्ृसिके भ्रािृर्द्धवनम् ॥२०॥ 

चापे च िािसौख्यं च मृगे मािृतर्िोथधिा । 

कु म्भे पुराथवलाभि मीने शरुतर्िोथधिा ॥२१॥ 

अलौ जायातर्िोधि िुले च जलबाधिा । 

कन्यायां धनर्ृणद्धाः स्याि् िुलाया नर्भागके ॥२२॥ 

20-22. In Libra, in the Dasha of Libra Amsa there will be financial gains, in the Dasha of Scorpio Amsa good relations with kinsmen, in the Dasha of Sagittarius Amsa-happiness from father, in the Dasha of Capricorn Amsa-disputes with mother, in the Dasha of Aquarius Amsa-birth of son and financial gains, in the Dasha of Pisces Amsa-entanglement with enemies, in the Dasha of Scorpio Amsa-disputes with women, in the Dasha of Libra Amsa-danger from water, and in the Dasha -of Virgo Amsa-more financial gains. 

Effects of the Dasha or Navamsha Rashi, of Scorpio 

ककव टे ह्यथवनाशि ससंहे िाजतर्िोथधिा । 

तमथुने भूतमलाभि र्ृर्षभे चाऽथवलाभकृ ि् ॥२३॥ 

मेर्षे सपाद्वदभीतिाः स्यान्मीने चैर् जलाद् भयम् । 

कु म्भे व्यापाििो लाभो मकिेऽष्टप रुजो भयम् ॥२४॥ 

चापे िु धनलाभाः स्याद् र्ृसिकस्य नर्ांशके । 

23-24½: In Scorpio, in the Dasha of Cancer Amsa there will be financial gains in the Dasha of Leo Amsa-opposition to the king (Government), in the Dasha of Gemini Amsa-acquisition of land, in the Dasha of Taurus Amsa-financial gains, in the Dasha of Aries Amsa--danger from reptiles, in the Dasha of Pisces Amsa-danger from water, in the Dasha of Aquarius Amsa-profits in business, in the Dasha of Capricorn Amsaprofit in business, in the Dasha of Capricorn Amsa-possibility of suffering from diseases, and in the Dasha of Sagittarius Amsa - financial gains. 

Effects of the Dasha of Navamsha Rāśhis of Sagittarius 

मेर्षे िु धनलाभाः स्याद् र्ृर्षे भूतमतर्र्द्धवनम् ॥२५॥ 

तमथुने सर्वससणद्धाः स्यात्ककव टे सर्वससणद्धकृ ि् । 

ससंहे िु पूर्वर्ृणद्धाः स्यात्कन्यायां कलहो भर्ेि् ॥२६॥ 

िौसलके चाथवलाभाः स्याद् र्ृसिके िोओगमाप्नुयाि् । 

चापे िु सुिर्ृणद्धाः स्याच्चापस्य नर्मांशके ॥२७॥ 

25-27. In Sagittarius, in the Dasha of Aries Amsa there will be financial gains, in the Dasha of Taurus Amsa-acquisition of more land, in the Dasha of Gemini Amsasuccess in ventures, 

in the Dasha of Cancer Amsa-success all round, in the Dasha of Leo Amsaincrease in the accumulated wealth, in the Dasha of Virgo Amsa-disputes, in the Dasha of Libra Amsa-financial gains, in the Dasha of Scorpio- Amsa-affliction with diseases, and in the Dasha of Sagittarius Amsa-happiness from children (birth of son etc.). 

Effects of the Dasha of Navamsha Rāśhis of Capricorn 

मकिे पुरलाभाः स्यात्कु म्भे धान्यतर्र्द्धवनम् । 

मीने कल्याणमाप्नोति र्ृसिके तर्र्षबाथधिा ॥२८॥ 

िौसलके त्वथवलाभि कन्यायां शरुर्द्धवनम् । 

शसशभे स्र्/इयमाप्नोति ससंहे िु मृगबाथधिा ॥२९॥ 

28-29, In Capricorn, in the Dasha of Capricorn Amsa there will be happiness from children, in the Dasha of Aquarius Amsa-gain of agricultural products, in the Dasha of Pisces Amsa-well-being, in the Dasha of Scorpio Amsa-danger from poison, in the Dasha of Libra Amsa-financial gains, in the Dasha of Virgo Amsa - increase in enemies, in the Dasha of Cancer Amsa - acquisition of property, in the Dasha of Leo Amsa- danger from wild animals and in the Dasha of Gemini Amsa-danger of falling from a tree. 

Effects of the Dasha of Navamsha Rāśhis of Aquarius 

तमथुने र्ृक्षबाधा च मृगस्य नर्भागके । 

र्ृर्षभे त्वथवलाभि मेर्षभे त्वसक्षिोगकृ ि् ॥३०॥ 

मीने िु दीघवयारा स्यात्कु म्भे धनतर्र्द्धवनम् । 

मकिे सर्वससणद्धाः स्याच्चापे शरुतर्र्द्धवनम् ॥३१॥ 

मेर्षे सौख्यतर्नाशि र्ृर्षभे मिणं भर्ेि् । 

युग्मे कल्याणमाप्नोति कु म्भस्य नर्मांशके ॥३२॥ 

30-32. In Aquarius, in the Dasha of Taurus Amsa-there will be financial gains, in the Dasha of Aries Amsa-diseases of the eyes in the Dasha of Pisces Amsajourneys to distant places, in t ne Dasha of Aquarius Amsa-increase in wealth, in the Dasha of Capricorn Amsa-success in all kinds of ventures, in the Dasha of Sagittarius Amsa-more enemies, in the Dasha of Aries Amsa-loss of happiness and enjoyment, in the Dasha of Taurus Amsa-death, in the Dasha of Gemini Amsa-well-being. 

Effects of the Dasha of the Navamsha Rāśhis of Pisces 

ककव टे धनर्ृष्टद्दाः स्याि् ससंहे िु िाजपूजनम् । 

कन्यायामथवलाभस्तु िुलायां लाभमाप्नुयाि् ॥३३॥ 

र्ृसिके ज्विमाप्नोति चापे शरुतर्र्द्धवनम् । 

मृगे जायातर्िोधि कु म्भे जलतर्िोधिा ॥३४॥ 

मीने िु सर्वसौभाग्यं मीनस्य नर्भागके । 

दशाअंशक्रमेणैर्ं ज्ञात्वा सर्वफलं र्देि् ॥३५॥ 

33-34½: In the Pisces, in the Dasha of Cancer Amsa-there will be increase in wealth, in the Dasha of Leo Amsa-recognition by Government, in the Dasha of Virgo Amsa-financial gains, in the Dasha of Libra Amsa-gains from all sources, in the Dasha of Scorpio Amsa -fever, in the Dasha of Sagittarius Amsa-more enemies, in the Dasha of Capricorn Amsa-conjugal disputes, in the Dasha of Aquarius Amsa- danger from water and in the Dasha of Pisces Amsa-good fortune all round. 

In this manner on the Kala-Chakra, prepared on the basis of the Pada of the Janma Nakshatra, the Dasha of the Navamsha rāśhis and their duration can be assessed and prediction can be made for the whole life of the native. Appropriate remedial measures (recitation of mantras, oblations etc.) should be taken to alleviate the adverse effects cause by malefic Dasha 

क्रू िग्रहदशाकाले शान्तिं कु याद्वद्वचक्षणाः । 

यि् प्रोक्तं िाजयोगादौ संज्ञाध्याये च यि् फलम् ॥३६॥ 

ित्सर्ं चरकाले द्वह सुबुद्ध्या योजयेद् बुधाः । 

इति संक्षेपिाः प्रोक्तं कालचक्रदशाफलम् ॥३७॥ 

36-37. The effects of Dasha in Raja-yoga etc. have already been described in Vol. 1 of this book. The same should be applied in a judicious manner in the Kalachakra. These are in brief the effects of Kala-chakra Dasha. 

# अथ चरादददशाफलाध्यायः ॥५०॥

# Chapter 50. Effects of the Chara etc. Dasha

चिस्थििाद्वदसञ्ज्ज्ञा या दशााः प्रोक्तााः पुिा द्वद्वज । 

शुभाऽशुभफलं िासां कथयातम िर्ाऽग्रिाः ॥ १॥ 

लग्नाद्वदद्वादशािानां भार्ानां फलकीिवने । 

ित्तद्राशीशर्ीयेण यथायोग्यं प्रयोजयेि् ॥ २॥ 

बलयुक्ते च िाशीशे पूणं िस्य िदा फलम् । 

फलं मध्यय्बले मध्यं बलहीने तर्पयवयाः ॥ ३॥ 

1-3. The Sage said-O Brahmin! I have already described the Chara etc. Dasha. Now I am going to tell you the effects of these Dasha. 

The effects of the Dasha of the rāśhis should be judged from the strength of the lords of rāśhis and whether they are benefices or malefic. If the lord of a rashi possesses full strength, the effects of the Dasha of the rashi will be realised in full. The effects of the Dasha will be of medium nature if the strength is medium. If the lord of rashi possesses little strength, the effects, will be experienced accordingly. 

यो यो दशाप्रदो िासशस्तस्य िन्ध्रष्टरकोणके । 

पापखेटयुिे तर्प्र िद्दशा दाःखदागयका ु ॥ ४॥ 

िृिीयर्षष्ठगे पापे ज्याद्वदाः परिकीतिविाः । 

शुभखेटयुिे िर जायिे च पिाजयाः ॥ ५॥ 

लाभिे च शुभे पापे लाभो भर्ति तनसििाः । 

यदा दशाप्रदो िासशाः शुभखेटयुिो द्वद्वज ॥ ६॥ 

शुभक्षेरे द्वह िद्राशेाः शुभं ज्ञेयं दशाफलम् । 

पापयुक्ते शुभक्षेरे पूर्ं शुभमसत्पिे ॥ ७॥ 

पापक्षे शुभसंयुक्ते पूर्ं सौख्यं ििोऽशुभम् । 

पापक्षेरे पापयुक्ते सा दशा सर्वदखदा ु ॥ ८॥ 

शुभक्षेरदशा िाशौ युक्ते पापशुभैद्वद्ववज ॥ ९॥ 

पूर्ं कष्टं सुखं पिागन्नतर्वशङ्कं प्रजायिे । 

शुभक्षेरे शुभं र्ाच्यं पापक्षे त्वशुभं फलम् ॥ १०॥ 

4-10. If there be malefic in the 8th, the 5th and the 9th from a Dasha rashi (that is, the rashi whose Dasha is in operation), the effects of the Dasha of that rashi will be distressful. If there be malefic in the 3rd; and the 6th from a Dasha rashi, the effects or the Dasha will be victory over enemies and happiness. If there be benefices in the 3rd and the 6th from the Dasha rashi, there will be defeat in its Dasha. If there be benefices or malefic in the 11th from the Dasha rashi, there will be conquests and happiness in its Dasha. If the Dasha rashi be occupied by or be owned by a benefice, the effects of its Dasha will be beneficial. If a Dasha rashi owned by a benefice, is occupied b; a malefic, favourable effects will be experienced in the first part of the Dasha and they will be adverse in the latter part. If a Dasha rashi owned by a malefic is occupied by a benefice, the effects of the Dasha will be the same. A Dasha rashi owned and occupied by a malefic will always yield in-favourable results. The reverse will be the case in the case of the Dasha rashi owned and occupied by a benefice. If a Dasha rashi owned by a benefice is occupied by both benefice and malefic planets, the effects of Dasha will be adverse in its first part and favourable in the latter part. 

द्वद्विीये पञ्चमे सौम्ये िाजप्रीतिजवयो ध्रुर्म् । पापे िर गिे ज्ञेयमशुभं िद्दशाफलम् ॥ ११॥ चिुथे िु शुभं सौख्यमािोग्यं त्वष्टमे शुभे । धमवर्ृणद्धगुवरुजनात्सौख्यं च नर्मे शुभे ॥ १२॥ तर्पिीिे तर्पयासो तमिे तमिं प्रकीतिविम् । पाके भोगे च पापाढ्ये देहपीडा मनोव्यथा ॥ १३॥ सप्तमे पाकभोगाभ्यां पापे दािातिविीरििा । चिुथे िानहातनाः स्यात्पञ्चमे पुरपीडनम् ॥ १४॥ दशमे कीतिवहातनाः स्यान्नर्मे ष्टपिृपीडनम् । पाकाद्रद्रागिेु पापे पीडा सर्ाप्यबाथधका ॥ १५॥ उक्तिानगिे सौम्ये ििाः सौख्यं तर्तनद्वदवशेि् । के न्द्रिानगिे सौम्ये लाभाः शरुजपप्रदाः ॥ १६॥ जन्मकालग्रहस्थित्या सगोचगग्रहैिष्टप । तर्चारििैाः प्रर्क्तव्यं ित्तद्रासशद/साफलम् ॥ १७॥ 

11-17. The assessment of the effects of the Dasha of the Dasha rashi should be made after taking into account the disposition of the planets in the rashi at birth and the disposition of planets during the Dasha. If the Dasha rashi be well disposed both at the time of birth and during its Dasha, the beneficial results will be realised in full. If it be ill-disposed during the Dasha, the effects will be of mixed nature. If the Dasha rashi be ill disposed both at the time of birth and during its Dasha, only evil effects will be experienced. 

िद्दशा शुभदा प्रोक्ता तर्पिीिे तर्पयवयाः ॥ १८॥ 

ष्टरकोणिन्ध्ररिष्फिैाः शुभपापैाः शुभाऽशुभम् । 

िद्दशायां च र्क्तव्यं फलं दैर्तर्दा सदा ॥ १९॥ 

18 – 19. The effects of the Dasha will be, favourable if it is occupied by a benefice and there is also a benefice in the rashi previous to it. If the rashi be occupied by a malefic, the effects will be of adverse nature. If there be benefices in the 5th and the 9th, the effects, of its Dasha will be favourable. Reverse will be the case if the 5th and the 9th are occupied by malefic. 

मेर्षककव िुलानक्रिाशीनां च यथाक्रमम् । 

बाधा स्तानातन सम्प्रोक्ता कु भगोससंहर्ृसिकााः ॥ २०॥ 

पाके शाक्राििाशौ र्ा बाधािाने शुभेििे । 

स्थििे सति महाशोको बन्धनव्यसनामयााः ॥ २१॥ 

20-21. Aquarius, Taurus, Leo and Scorpio are Badhaka houses for the four moveable rashi - Aries, Cancer, Libra and Capricorn, in that order. In other words, the 11th rāśhis a moveable sign is its Badhaka house. If there be a malefic in the house occupied by its lord or in Badhaka house of that rashi, there will be occasions of great sorrow, imprisonment and diseases during the Dasha. 

उच्चस्वक्षवग्र्हे िस्तस्मञ्छु भं सौख्यं धनागमाः । 

िच्छू न्यं चेदसौख्यं स्यात्तद्दशा न फलप्रदा ॥ २२॥ 

22. The Dasha of a rashi will be favourable if it is occupied by its own lord or an exalted planet. The Dasha of a, rashi not occupied by any planet will be adverse. 

बाधकव्ययर्षडिन्ध्रे िाहुयुक्ते महद्भयम् । 

प्रिाने बन्धनप्राप्ती िाजपीडा रिपोभयम् ॥ २३॥ 

िव्याििाहुशनयो भुगक्तिाशौ स्थििा यद्वद । 

िद्रासशथभक्तौ पिनं िाजकोपान् महद्भयम् ॥ २४॥ 

भुगक्तिासशष्टरकोणे िु नीचखेटाः स्थििो यद्वद । 

िद्राशौ र्ा युिे नीचे पापे मृत्युभयं र्देि् ॥ २५॥ 

23-25. There will be great danger, imprisonment during a journey, displeasure of Government and danger from enemies, in the Dasha and Anta r Dasha of the rashi from which its Badhaka house, the 12th, the 6th and the 8th are occupied by Rahu. There will be losses due to the displeasure of the king and danger therefrom in the Antardasa (sub-period} of the rashi that is occupied by the Sun, Mars, Rahu and Saturn. There will be possibility of death if the 5th and the 9th from the Antardasa rashi are occupied by debilitated or malefic planet. 

भुगक्तिाशौ स्विुङ्गिे ष्टरकोणे र्ाष्टप खेचिे । यदा भुगक्तदशा प्राप्ता िदा सौख्यं लभेन्निाः ॥ २६॥ नगिग्रामनाथत्वं पुरलाभं धनागमम् । कल्याणं भूरिभाग्यं च सेनपत्यं महोन्निम् ॥ २७॥ पाके श्विो जीर्दृष्टाः शुभिासशस्थििो यद्वद । िद्दशायां धनप्राब्दप्तमवङ्गलं पुरसम्भर्म् ॥ २८॥ 

26-28. There will be enjoyment, acquisition of chief-ship of a town or village, birth of a son, financial gains, well-being, dawn of fortune, attainment of the position of a commander of an army and progress all round if there he an exalted planet in the Trikona from the Antardasa rashi. There will be in his Dasha financial gains, well-being and birth of a son if the planet who is the lord of the Dasha be in a benefice sign and be aspected by Jupiter. 

ससिाससिभयुग्माि सूयवस्य रिपुिाशयाः । कौष्टपविौसलघटािेन्द्रोभौमस्य रिपुिाशयाः ॥ २९॥ घटमीननृयुल्तौसलकन्या ज्ञस्य ििाः पिम् । ककव मीनासलकु म्भाि िाशयो रिपर्ाः स्मृिााः ॥ ३०॥ र्ृर्षिौसलनृयुक्कन्यािाशयो रिपर्ो गुिोाः । ससंहासलककव चापाि शुकस्य रिपुिाशयाः ॥ ३१॥ मेर्षससंहधनुाःकौष्टपवककव टा शतनशरर्ाः । एर्ं ग्राहििदाशां श्रचियेत्कोतर्दो द्वद्वज ॥ ३२॥ 

29-32. Taurus, Libra, Capricorn, Aquarius and Gemini are the inimical rāśhis of the Sun. The inimical rāśhis of the Moon and other planets may be reckoned similarly. If a planet be in an inimical rashi, his Dasha will he full of adversities. The effects of the Dasha of rāśhis and planets should be judged after taking into account the above rules. 

ये िाजयोगदा ये च शुभमध्यमिा ग्रहााः । यस्माद्वा द्वद्वष्टरिुयविााः ग्रहााः शुभफलप्रदााः ॥ ३३॥ िद्दशानां शुभं ब्रूयाद्राजयोगाद्वदसम्भर्म् । शुभद्वयाििगिाः पापोऽष्टप शुभदाः स्मृिाः ॥ ३४॥ 

33-34. The Dasha of that planet will be favourable who is Raja-yoga-karaka, who is disposed between two benefices (that is, there are benefices in the 2nd and the 12th houses to that planet) and who has benefices in the 2nd, 3rd and 4th houses from him. A malefic planet becomes favourable if he is disposed between benefices. 

गिा शुभदशामध्यं दशा सौम्यस्य शोभना । 

शुभा यस्य ष्टरकोणिस्तद्दशाष्टप शुभप्रदा ॥ ३५॥ 

आिम्भािो तमरशुभिाश्योयवद्वद फलं शुभम् । 

प्रतििाश्यैर्मव्दाद्यं तर्भज्य ित्फलं र्देि् ॥ ३६॥ 

35-36. The whole of the Dasha of a planet who is related to a friendly and benefice planet at the commencement and the end of the Dasha, will be favourable. In an unfavourable Dasha, the Antardasa of a benefice (planet or rashi) becomes favourable. The Dasha of a planet or rashi, who has benefices in the 5th or the 9th from it, is also favourable. In this manner, the effects of the Dasha should be judged after taking into account the dispositions of the planet or rashi, at the commencement and at the end of the Dasha. 

आिम्भात्तष्टररकोणे िु सौम्ये िु शुभभार्हेि् । 

शुभिाशौ शुभािम्भे दशा स्यादतिशोभना ॥ ३७॥ 

शुभाद्वदिाशौ पापिेद्दशािम्भे शुभा स्मृिा । 

शुभािम्भे कथा के ति प्रािम्भस्य फलं र्देि् ॥ ३८॥ 

आिम्भे पापिाशौ र्ा यदीशो दबवलो ु द्वद्वज । 

नीचादौ िद्दशाद्यिे र्देद्भाग्यतर्पयवयम् ॥ ३९॥ 

37-39. The Dasha of the planets and rāśhis who have benefices in the Trikona from them is favourable. If the Dasha of a benefice rashi commences in a benefice rashi, it will be very favourable. If an evil Dasha commences in a benefice rashi, it is also favourable. Therefore, the commencement of Dasha should always be kept in view in assessing the results of the Dasha. There will be loss of fortune if a t the commencement of the Dasha there be a malefic rashi or the lord of the Dasha rashi be in debilitation. 

यर स्थििो नीचखेटण्डिकोणे र्ाऽथ नीचगाः । 

िथा िाशीश्विे नीचे सम्बन्धो नीचखेटकै ाः ॥ ४०॥ 

भाग्यस्य तर्पिीित्वं किोत्येर् द्वद्वजोत्तम । 

धनधान्याद्वदहातनि देहे िोगभयं िथा ॥ ४१॥ 

40-41. There will be loss of fortune, wealth and agricultural products and inflict ion with disease during the Dasha of the rashi occupied by a debilitated planet, or if there be a debilitated planet in the 5th from it or the 9th or whose lord be debilitated or related to a debilitated planet. 

िाहोाः के िोि कु म्भाद्वद र्ृसिकाद्वद चिुष्टयम् । 

स्वभं िर समािम्भस्तद्दशायां शुभं भर्ेि् ॥ ४२॥ 

42. Four rāśhis from Aquarius and four rāśhis from Scorpio belong to Rahu and Ketu respectively. If Rahu and Ketu be in any one of the aforesaid rāśhis, the Dasha will be productive of beneficial results. 

यद्दशायां शुभं ब्रूयात्स चेन्मािकसंस्थििाः । यस्तस्मन् िाशौदशािाःस्यात्तस्तस्मन् दृष्टे युिेऽष्टप र्ा ॥ ४३॥ शुक्रे ण तर्धुना र्ा स्याद्राजकोपाद्धनक्षयाः । दशाििेदरिक्षेरे िाहुदृष्टयुिेऽष्टप र्ा ॥ ४४॥ इदं फलं शनेाः पाके न तर्श्रचन्त्यं द्वद्वजोत्तम । दशाप्रदे नक्रिाशौ न तर्श्रचन्त्यतमदं फलम् ॥ ४५॥ 

43-45. If a planet whose Dasha is otherwise considered favourable be posited in a maraka house, or if the rashi in which his Dasha comes to an end be aspected by Venus or Moon, there will be in his Dasha displeasure of government and loss of wealth. 

िाहुदवशािे सर्वस्वनाशो मिणबन्धने । दशागन्नर्ासनं र्ा स्यात्कष्टं र्ा महदश्निेु ॥ ४६॥ िष्टररकोणगिे पापे तनियाद्दाःखमाद्वदशेि् ु । एर्ं शुभाशुभं सर्ं तनियेन र्देद् बुधाः ॥ ४७॥ 

46-47. There will be Joss of everything, imprisonment, death exile from the country and great distress at the end of the Dasha of Rahu, the above effects will definitely be realised if there be malefic in the 5th and the 9th from Rahu. Beneficial and adverse effects should be predicted in this manner. 

िाह्वाद्याश्रिििासशस्तु भर्ेद्यद्वद दशाप्रदाः । िर कालेऽष्टप पूर्ोक्तं श्रचिनीयं प्रयत्निाः ॥ ४८॥ द/सािम्भो दशािो र्ा मािके चेन्न शोभनम् । िस्तस्मन्नेर् च िाहुिन्निोधो द्रव्यनाशनाः ॥ ४९॥ यर क्वाष्टप च भे िाहौ दशािम्भे तर्नाशनम् । गृहभ्रंशाः समुष्टद्दष्टो धने िाहुधनातिवकृ ि् ॥ ५०॥ 

48-50. The same would be the effects in the Dasha of the rashi occupied by malefic like Rahu etc. The association of a maraka planet with the rashi at the' time of commencement or end of its Dasha is not productive of good effects. If such planet be Ra h u there will be imprisonment or loss of wealth. 

चन्द्र्शुक्रौ द्वादश चेद्राजकोपो भर्ेदध्रुर्म्् । भौमके िू िर यद्वद र्धोऽग्नेमवहिी व्यथा ॥ ५१॥ 

# चेन्द्रशुक्रौ धने तर्प्र यद्वद िाज्यं प्रयच्छिाः । दशािम्भे दशािे च द्वद्विीयितमदं फलम् ॥ ५२॥

51-52. The natural characteristics of the house occupied by Rahu are harmed at the commencement of the Dasha. If such house be 2nd, there will be loss of wealth. If the Moon and Venus be in the 12th there will be losses due to the displeasure of government. If Mars and Ketu be so disposed there will be death or danger from fire. There will be acquisition of kingdom if the Venus and Moon be in the 2nd at the commencement of the Dasha. This means that the effects (good or bad) of the house in which the Moon and Venus are posited at the commencement and end of Dasha, are strengthened. Thus, their disposition in the 6th, the 8th and the 12th will produce only adverse effects. 

एर्मगवलभार्ानां फलं तर्ज्ञैाः प्रदसशविम् । यस्य पापाः शुभो र्ाऽष्टप ग्रहस्तस्तष्ठेच्छु भागवले ॥ ५३॥ िेन द्रष्टर ेसक्षिे लग्नं पाबल्यायोपकल्प्प्यिे । यद्वद पश्येदग्रहस्तन्न् तर्पिीिागवलस्थििाः ॥ ५४॥ िद्भार्स्य दशायास्तु तर्पिीिफलं भर्ेि् । सद्दृष्टेऽष्टप शुभं ब्रूयागन्नतर्वशङ्कं द्वद्वजोत्तम ॥ ५५॥ 

53-55: Similarly, the learneds have described the effects of the house with Argala (सागधल). If there be an auspicious Argala causing benefice or malefic planet of rashi and the Ascendant be aspected by him that rashi will prevail. Here Ascendant is the secondary condition. If the planet causing uninterrupted Argala, aspects a rashi, that rashi will prevail. In other words, good effects will be derived in the Dasha of that rashi. The Dasha of the rashi, which is not aspected by auspicious Argala or of a rashi with Vipreet Argala, will not be favourable. The Dasha of that rashi which is aspected by a benefice will also be favourable. 

यस्तस्मन्भार्े शुभस्वातमसम्बन्धस्तुङ्गखेचिाः । स्यात्तद्भार्दशायां िु अन्त्यैश्वयवमखण्डण्डिम् ॥ ५६॥ यद्भार्ेशाः स्वाथविासशमथधतिष्ठति पश्यति । स्यािद्भार्दशाकाले धनलाभो महत्तिाः ॥ ५७॥ यस्माद्व्ययगिो यस्तु िद्दशायां धनक्षयाः । यस्माष्टररकोणगााः पापास्तरात्मशुभनाशनम् ॥ ५८॥ पुरहातनाः ष्टपिुाः पीडा मनस्तापो महान् भर्ेि् । यस्माष्टररको्गा रिाःफिन्ध्रेशाकािसूयवजााः ॥ ५९॥ 

56-59: Financial gains will be derived in the Dasha of the rashi which is occupied by its benefice lord or by an exalted planet who is aspected by him. There Page 482 

will be loss of wealth if such a planet be in the 12th to the rashi (or house). There will be destruction of all good effects, distress to children and father and mental agony in the Dasha of the rashi if there be malefic in the 5th and the 9th from the rashi. Evil effects will be experienced in the Dasha of the rashi which is occupied by the lord of the 8th, the lord of the 12th, the Sun, Mars or Saturn. 

पुरपीडा द्रव्यहातनस्तर के त्वद्वहसङ्गमे । 

तर्देशभ्रमणं क्लेशो भयं चैर् पदे पदे ॥ ६०॥ 

िस्मारर्षष्ठाष्टमे क्रू िनीचखेटादयाः स्थििााः । 

िोगशरुनृपालेभ्यो मुहुाः पीडा सुदाःसहा ु ॥ ६१॥ 

यस्माच्चिुथवाः क्रू िाः स्याद्भगृहक्षेरनाशनम् ू । 

पशुहातनस्तर भौमे गृहदाहाः प्रमादकृ ि् ॥ ६२॥ 

शनौ हृदयशूलं स्यात्सूये िाजप्रकोपनम् । 

सर्वस्वहिणं िाहौ तर्र्षचौिाद्वदजं भयम् ॥ ६३॥ 

60-63. The Dasha of the rashi will cause distress to children, exile to a foreign country and continuous disturbances in his life if Rahu and Ketu be in the Trikona to the rashi. There will be danger from enemies, king and disease in the Dasha of the rashi the 6th and the 8th from which are occupied by malefic, debilitated or combust planets. There will be destruction of house, land and agricultural field s if there be a malefic or debilitated planet in the 4th from the rashi. There will be loss of house due to negligence if such a planet be Mars, heart pains and danger from government if the planet be Saturn and losses all round, danger from poison and thieves if the planet be Rahu. 

यस्माद् दशमभे िाहुाः पुण्यिीथाटनं भर्ेि् । 

यस्मात्कमायभाग्यक्षवगिाः शोभनखेचिााः ॥ ६४॥ 

तर्द्याथवधमवसत्कमवख्यातिपौरुर्षससद्धयाः । 

यिाः पञ्चमकामारिगिााः स्वोच्चशुभग्रहााः ॥ ६५॥ 

पुरदािाद्वदसम्प्राब्दप्तनृवपपूजा मह्स्त्तिा । 

यस्मान्पुरायकमाम्बुनर्लग्नाथधपााः स्थििााः ॥ ६६॥ 

ित्तद्भार्ाथवससणद्धाः स्याच्छर ेयो योगानुसाििाः । 

64-66½: There will be pilgrimage to holy places in the Dasha of the rashi who has Rahu in the 10th to it. There will be gain of earning, religious rites, gain of wealth, renown for good deeds and success in efforts and ventures in the Dasha of the rashi the 10th, the 11th and the 9th from which are occupied by benefices. There will be birth of children, happiness from wife and recognition by Government in the Dasha of the rashi from which the 5th, the 7th and the 9th are occupied by benefice or exalted planets. During the Dasha of the houses (rāśhis) occupied by the lords of the 5th, the 

11th, the 10th, the 4th, the 9th, or the Ascendant there will be growth of these houses (good effects). 

The good effects will be in proportion to the strength of the houses and the planet occupying them. 

यस्तस्मन् गुरुर्ा शुक्रोर्ा शुभेशो र्ाष्टप संस्थििाः ॥ ६७॥ कल्याणं सर्वसम्पथत्ति् देर्ब्राह्मणिपवनम् । यरचिुथे िुङ्गखेटााः शुभस्वामी ग्रहि र्ा ॥ ६८॥ र्ाहनग्रामलाभि पशुर्ृणद्धि भूयसी । िर चन्द्रे च लाभाः स्याद्बहुधान्यिसान्तििाः ॥ ६९॥ पूणे तर्धौ तनथधप्राब्दप्तलवभेद्वा मणणसञ्जयम् । िर सुक्रे भृदङ्गाद्वदर्ाद्यगानपुिस्कृ िाः ॥ ७०॥ 

67-70. In the Dasha of rashi (house) there will be well beings, increase in opulence and glory and devotion to deities and Brahmins, if it is occupied by Jupiter, Venus or lord of a Trikona. There will be acquisition of more conveyance and cattle etc., in the Dasha of the rashi (house), the 4th from which is occupied by an exalted planet or lord of a Trikona. The Moon there will give things like grains, ghee etc. Full Moon will favour with a treasure and jewels etc. Venus there will provide enjoyment from music etc. 

आन्दोसलकाब्दप्तजीर्े िु कनकान्दोसलका ध्रुर्म् । लग्नकमेशभाग्येशिुङ्गिशुभयोगिाः ॥ ७१॥ सर्ोत्कर्षवमहैश्वयवसाम्राज्याद्वदमहत्फलम् । एर्ं ित्तद्भार्दायफलं यत्स्याद्वद्वश्रचियेि् ॥ ७२॥ 

71-72. There will be enjoyment of the palanquin like conveyance in the Dasha of the rashi (house) from which the 41 is occupied by Jupiter. There will be success in all venture great opulence and glory, acquisition of a kingdom (attainment of a high position etc.), during the Dasha of a rashi (house) which has the yoga of the lord of the Ascendant, lords of the 9th and the 10th, an exalted planet or benefices. The effects of the Dasha of various houses should be judged in this manner. 

एकै कोडुदशा स्वीयैगुवणैिष्टादशात्मथभ । थभन्नं फलतर्पाकं िु कु याद्वै श्रचरसंयुिम् ॥ ७३॥ पिमोच्चे िुङ्गमारे िदर्ाक्तदपयवष्टप ु । मूलष्टरकोणभे स्वक्षे स्वाथधतमरग्रहस्य भे ॥ ७४॥ ित्कालसुहृदो गेहे उदासीनस्य भे िथा । शिोभेऽथधरिपोभे च नीचािादर्ध्वदेू शभे ॥ ७५॥ 

73-77. The effects of the Dasha of each rashi or planet (Nakshatra Dasha) depend on their 18 different kinds of conditions. They are deep exaltation, exaltation, dispositions on their either side, Moola-Trikona, own sign, Adhimitra sign, Tatkalik Mitra’s sign, natural sign, enemy's sign, Adhishatru’s sign, deep debilitation, debilitated or enemy's Varga, own Varga, disposition in a Kendra, disposition in a Trikona, defeated in planetary war, deep combustion. 

िस्मादर्ाङ् नीचमार नीचािे पिमांशके । 

नीचारिर्गे सखले स्वर्गे के न्द्रकोणभे ॥ ७६॥ 

व्यर्स्थििस्य खेटस्य समिे पीष्टडिस्य च । 

गाढपूढस्य च दशापश्रचतिाः स्वगुणैाः फलम् ॥ ७७॥ 

पिमोच्चगिो यस्तु योऽतिर्ीयवसमन्तििाः । 

सम्पूणाख्या दशा िस्य िाज्यभूग्यशुभप्रदा ॥ ७८॥ 

लक्ष्मीकटाक्षश्रचिानां श्रचिर्ासगृहप्रदा । 

िुङ्गमारगिस्याष्टप िथा र्ीयाथधकस्य च ॥ ७९॥ 

पूणाख्या बहुलैश्वयवदागयन्याष्टप रुजप्रदा । 

अतिनीचगिस्याष्टप दबवलस्य ु ग्रहस्य िु ॥ ८०॥ 

रिक्ता त्वतनष्टफलदा व्याध्यनथवमृतिप्रदा । 

अत्युच्चेऽप्यतिनीचिे मध्यगस्यार्िोद्वहणी ॥ ८१॥ 

तमरोच्चभार्प्राप्तस्य मध्याख्या ह्यथवदा दशा । 

नीचािादच्चभागािं ु भर्षट्के मध्यगस्य च ॥ ८२॥ 

दशा चािोद्वहणी नीचरिपुभांशगिस्य च । 

अधमाख्या भयक्लेशव्याथधदाःखतर्र्थधवनी ु ॥ ८३॥ 

नामानुरूपफलदााः पाककाले दशा इमााः । 

78-83½: Acquisition of kingdom (attainment of a high position in government), enjoyment and acquisition of more property are the effects of the whole Dasha or the planet who is m deep exaltation and is fully equipped with all the Ill kinds of strength (Shad-bala), great opulence and glory with some possibility of affliction with disease are the effects of the planet placed in his sign of exaltation. The Dasha of a planet in deep debilitation is called rikta (ररक्त-void). Diseases, Loss of wealth and danger of death are the effects of the Dasha of such a planet. The Dasha of the planet who in a condition in between exaltation and deep debilitation is known as avrohini (अवरोद्वहणी - descending). The Dasha of the planet in exaltation or in a friend's sign is called Madhya (मध्या - middle order). This Dasha also yields moderately good effects. The Dasha of a planet placed in a condition in between deep debilitation and deep 

exaltation is called rohini (रोद्वहणी ascending). The Dasha of a planet placed in between the debilitated and enemy Navamsha is called Adhama (अर्मा - evil). Dangers of various kinds, distress and sorrows are the results of the Dasha of such a planet. These Dasha give results according to their nomenclature. 

![image](https://cdn-mineru.openxlab.org.cn/result/2026-05-02/fb53458b-f342-410d-a5b1-a44fc9147e60/f682f74a9889570a3a22c78211cb74e273ab06fcf37755d47b41a320faf0c80e.jpg)


84-87. The Dasha of other planets become auspicious and augment the fortune if the lord of the 9th and Jupiter are in any way related with yoga, Kendra or the house concerned etc. The planet with yoga of good fortune at birth produces good effects when he is free from retrogression and becomes direct. The weakness, inabilities and yogas of other planets should also be taken in to account in judging their effects. All those Dasha give full, medium and little effects in accordance with the disposition of the planets in the Kendra, Panaphara or Apoklima houses. 

![image](https://cdn-mineru.openxlab.org.cn/result/2026-05-02/fb53458b-f342-410d-a5b1-a44fc9147e60/a636585286f0df7a99baef9d38a95d687b600b407624bb790d0bec52f1b679d6.jpg)


88-89½: The planets in Shirshodaya rāśhis (शीषोदय राशी) Ubhayodaya (उभयोदय) Rāśhis and Prishthodaya (पृष्ठोदय) Rāśhis, yield their results respectively at the commencement of the Dasha, in the middle of the Dasha and at the end of the Dasha. All the planets yield auspicious, results in the Antardasa of Naisargika (नैसगगधक, natural, constant) and Tatkalik (तत्काशलक -according to position) friends. The results will be adverse in the Antardasa of inimical planets. 

![image](https://cdn-mineru.openxlab.org.cn/result/2026-05-02/fb53458b-f342-410d-a5b1-a44fc9147e60/9f2d710e43d92eebfed5c7b9c6e339699b23a65808ec071738b75b498ba9d2ff.jpg)


िस्यां िाज्याद्वदसम्पथत्तपूर्वकं शुभमीियेि् । 

दाःिानरिपुगेहिनीचक्रू ियुिा ु च या ॥ ९२॥ 

िस्यामनथवकलहं िोगमृत्युभयाद्वदकम् । 

तबन्दभूयस्त्वशून्यत्वर्शाि् ु स्वीयाष्टर्गवके ॥ ९३॥ 

र्ृणद्धं हातनं च िद्रासशभार्स्य स्वगृहात्क्रमाि् । 

भार्योजनया तर्द्यात्सुिचत्र्याद्वदशुभाऽशुभम् ॥ ९४॥ 

धात्वाद्वदिासशभेदाच्च धात्वाद्वदग्रहयोगिाः । 

शुभपापनशाभेदाच्छु भपापयुिैिष्टप ॥ ९५॥ 

इष्टातनष्टिानभेदाि् फलभेदाि् समुन्नयेि् । 

एर्ं सर्वग्रहाणां च स्वां स्वामिदवशामष्टप ॥ ९६॥ 

90-96 (Antardasa of rāśhis), There are Antardasa of the 12 rāśhis commencing from the rashi in which the lord of the Dasha is posited. There will be auspicious results like acquisition of kingdom (attainment of a high position in government) in the Antardasa of a rashi which is occupied by its own lord or a friendly planet. There will be inauspicious results like loss of wealth, disputes, danger from diseases etc., in the Antardasa of the rashi which may be the 6th, the 8th or the 12th or occupied by a malefic, debilitated planet or a planet housed in an inimical sign. The rashi which contains more auspicious marks in the Ashtaka-Varga will yield benefice effects in its Antardasa. Adverse will be the effects of the Antardasa of the rashi which contains more inauspicious marks. For assessing the results, the rashi from which the Dasha commences, should be treated as the Ascendant and the houses thereafter should be assumed to have the characteristics as if they are so from the Ascendant; Thus the 2nd house from that rashi will be the house of the wealth, the 3rd of co-born and so on. 

There will be gains or losses of Dhatus (र्ातु) etc. assigned to the rāśhis and the planets in the Antardasa of the rāśhis concerned. 

In judging the effects of the Antardasa of the planets, their benefice and malefic nature, relations with the malefic or benefice aspects on them and their disposition in the 6th, the 8th or the 12th etc. should all be kept in view. 

स्विासशिो िासशभुगक्तं प्रकल्प्प्य फलमीियेि् । 

अिििदवशां स्वीयां तर्भज्यैर्ं पुनाः पुनाः ॥ ९७॥ 

97. The results, of the Antardasa (Sub periods) and, Pratyantar Dasha of the rāśhis, be assessed in the manner, explained in this chapter. 

# अथाऽन्तदिशाध्यायः ॥५१॥

# Chapter 51. Working out of Antardasa (sub periods) of planet & Rashi in Vimshottari etc. Dasha systems

दशाब्दााः स्वस्वमानघ्नााः सर्ायुयोगभासजिााः । 

पृथगिदवशा एर्ं प्रत्यििदशाद्वदकााः ॥ १॥ 

1. For finding out the span of the Antardasa of a planet in the Dasha of the same or another planet, multiply the Dasha years of the former with the Dasha years of the latter and divide the product by the total Dasha of the same or any other planet in the Antardasa of another planet. Multiply the years etc. of the Antardasa with the Dasha years of the other planet and divide the product by the total Dasha years of all the planets. The figure so available in months etc. will represent the Pratyantar Dasha of the former. 

Notes: We have to find out the period of the Antardasa of the Venus in the Dasha of Venus under the Vimshottari system. The Dasha period of Venus is 20 years. Total Dasha years are 120 years. The Antardasa of Venus will be $2 0 \times 2 0 = 4 0 0 \div 1 2 0$ $= 3$ years 4 months. 

There is another method of finding out the term or Antardasa. Multiply the number of years of the Dasha of the planet by the Dasha years of the planet whose Antardasa is required. Then cutting off the last digit of the product-multiply it by 3 and keep the figure so available as days. Suppose, we want to find out the Antardasa of Mercury in the Dasha of Saturn. Mercury's Dasha years are 17. Saturn's Dasha years are 19.17 X $\begin{array} { r } { { 1 9 } = 3 2 3 } \end{array}$ . By adopting the above methods, the Antardasa of Mercury will be 32 months and 9 days, or 2 years, 8 months and 9 days. 

Pratyantar Dasha 

We have to find out the Pratyantar Dasha of Venus in the Antardasa of Venus. The Antardasa of Venus is of 3 years and 4 months or 40 months. The Dasha years of Venus are 20 Years or 240 months. The Dasha years of all the planets are 120 years or 1440 months. Pratyantar Dasha of Venus will be-

$4 0 \times 2 4 0 = 9 6 0 0$ months $\div$ 1440 months $= 6$ months and 20 days. 

आदार्िदवशा पाकपिेस्तत्क्रमिोऽपिााः । 

एर्ं प्रत्यििादौ च क्रमो ज्ञेयो तर्चक्षणैाः ॥ २॥ 

2. In every Dasha the first Antardasa belongs to the lord of the Dasha. Then the further Antardasa belong to the other 9 planets in the same order as followed for the Dasha. The same applies to Pratyantar Dasha. 

Notes: For ready reference, is given a Table of Antardasa, under the Vimshottari Dasha system.

Ketu's Dasha 7 Years

The Tables of Pratyantar Dasha will be given later. 

The Antardasa of Chara Planets in Chan etc. Dasha 

भुगक्तनवर्ानां िुल्या स्याद् तर्भाज्या नर्धा दशा । 

आदौ दशापिेभुवगक्तस्तत्के न्द्राद्वदयुजां ििाः ॥ ३॥ 

तर्द्याि् क्रमेण भुक्त्यंशानेर्ं सूक्ष्मदशाद्वदकम् । 

बलक्रमाि् फलं तर्ज्ञैर्वक्तव्यं पूर्विीतििाः ॥ ४॥ 

3-4. The Antardasa of the Charadi (चराद्वद) Kendradi (के न्द्राद्वद) Dasha of the Planets are worked out by dividing the Dasha years by 9. The first Dasha will invariably be of the lord of the Dasha. Thereafter there will be Antardasa of planets posited in Kendras, Panapharas and Apoklimas irrespectively according to their strength. 

Antardasa of rāśhis 

कृ त्वाऽकव धा िासशदशां िाशेभुवगक्तं क्रमाद् र्देि् । 

प्रत्यिदवशाद्येर्ं कृ त्वा ित्तत्फलं र्देि् ॥ ५॥ 

5. The Antardasa of rāśhis is worked out by dividing the Dasha years by 12 (in other words, 1/12th part of the Dasha years of a rashi is the period of its Antardasa). Pratyantar Dasha of the Antardasa are also calculated in the same manner. 

The order of Antardasa of rāśhis 

आद्यसप्तमयोमवध्ये यो िासशबवलर्ांस्तिाः । 

ओजे दशािये गण्यााः क्रमादत्क्रमिाः ु समे ॥ ६॥ 

6. The Antardasa will start from the Dasha rashi or from the rashi 7th therefrom, whichever is stronger. The Antardasa are in the onwards order if the Dasha rashi is odd, in the reverse order if it is even. 

अराऽपिो तर्शेर्षोऽस्तस्त ब्रर्ीतम िमहं द्वद्वज । चिेऽनुल्लििमागवाः स्याि् र्षष्ठर्षष्ठाद्वदकााः स्थििे ॥ ७॥ उभये कण्टकाज् ज्ञेया लग्नपञ्चमभाग्यिाः । चिस्थििद्वद्वस्वभार्ेष्वोजेर्षुाः प्राक् क्रमो मिाः ॥ ८॥ िेष्वेर् ष्टरर्षु युग्मेर्षु ग्राह्यं व्युत्क्रमिोऽखखलम् । एर्मुल्लिखखिो िासश पाकिासशरुदीयुविे ॥ ९॥ स एर् भोगिासशाः स्याि् पयाये प्रथमे स्मृिाः । आद्याद् यार्तिथाः पाकाः पयाये यर दृश्यिे ॥ १०॥ िस्माि् िार्तिथो भोगाः पयाये िर गृह्यिाम् । िद्वददं चिपयायस्थििपयाययोद्ववयोाः ॥ ११॥ ष्टरकोणाख्यदशायां च पाकभोगप्रकल्पनम् । पाके भोगे च पापाढ्ये देपपीडा नमोव्यथा ॥ १२॥ 

7-12. O Brahmin! Now I will acquaint you with the special characteristics of the order of the Antardasa of the rāśhis. 

If the Dasha rashi be a moveable one, the Antardasa of the 12 rāśhis are in the onwards or reverse order. If the Dasha asraya (दशा आश्रय) rashi be a fixed one, the Antardasa will start from it and thereafter there will be Antardasa of every sixth rashi. If the Dasha asraya (दशाश्रय) rashi be a dual one, the first Antardasa will belong to it. Thereafter there will be Antardasa of rāśhis in Kendra to it, rāśhis in Kendra to the 5th from it and rāśhis in Kendra to the 9th from it in that order. In the case of all kinds of rāśhis, namely moveable, fixed or dual, the order will be onwards, if the Dasha asraya rashi be an odd one, and in the reverse order if it be an even one. The so called Dasha asraya (दशाश्रय) rashi is known as Paka rashi (पाक राशश). In the first order rashi which is Paka-rashi is also called Bhoga rashi (भोग राशश). Later if the Dasha prad (दशाप्रद) rashi be even, then the Bhoga rashi will be that which is at the same rashi distance as the Dasha asraya rashi is from the Dashaprada rashi. For the Chara, Sthira and Trikona Dasha, the Paka and Bhoga should be determined in this manner. If Paka and Bhoga rāśhis be associated with malefic, there will be pain in the body and mental agony. There will be enjoyment if they be associated with benefices. 

Notes: We have to work out the order of the Antardasa in the Chara Dasha of Aquarius. Aquarius is a fixed and odd rashi. Therefore, starting from Aquarius there will be in onwards the Antardasa of every sixth Rashi. Thus, the first Antardasa will be of Aquarius, then of Cancer, the sixth rashi from it, and later of Sagittarius, the sixth 

rashi from Cancer, and so on. The Dasha years are 8, therefore the Antardasa of the 12 rāśhis will be of 8 months each. 


Illustrative Table


<table><tr><td>Rashi</td><td colspan="2">Aquarius</td><td>Cancer</td><td colspan="2">Sagittarius</td><td>Taurus</td><td>Libra</td><td>Pisces</td></tr><tr><td>Y</td><td>0</td><td>0</td><td>0</td><td>0</td><td></td><td>0</td><td>0</td><td>0</td></tr><tr><td>M</td><td>8</td><td>8</td><td>8</td><td>8</td><td></td><td>8</td><td>8</td><td>8</td></tr><tr><td colspan="9">Rashi Leo Capricorn Gemini Scorpio Aries Virgo</td></tr><tr><td>Y</td><td>0</td><td>0</td><td>0</td><td>0</td><td>0</td><td>0</td><td></td><td></td></tr><tr><td>M</td><td>8</td><td>8</td><td>8</td><td>8</td><td>8</td><td>8</td><td></td><td></td></tr></table>
