र्षष्ठाष्टमव्यये जीर्े दायेशान्नीचगेऽष्टप र्ा । चौिाद्वहव्रणभीतिं च धनधान्याद्वदनाशनम् ॥ ५५॥ पुरदािातर्योगं च त्विीर्क्लेशसम्भर्म् । आदौ सुभफलं चैर् अिे क्लेशकिं र्देि् ॥ ५६॥ 

55-56. Danger from thieves’ snakes and wounds, destruction of wealth, separation from wife and children, physical distress etc., will be the results if Jupiter be in his sign of debilitation or be in the 6th, the 8th or the 12th from the Ascendant. Though, some good effects may be felt at the commencement of the Antardasa, there will he only adverse results later. 

दायेशात्के न्द्रकोणे र्ा दसिक्ये ु लाभगेऽष्टप र्ा । शुभयुक्ते नृपप्रीतितर्वश्रचराम्बिभूर्षणम् ॥५७॥ दिदेशप्रयाणं ू च स्वबन्धुजनपोर्षणम् । भोजनाम्बिपश्वाद्वद भुक्त्यादौ देहपीडनम् ॥५८॥ अिे िु िानचलनमकस्मात्कलहो भर्ेि् । 

57-58½: There will be gains of many varieties of garments, ornaments by the beneficence of the king, foreign journeys, taking care of kinsmen, availability of decent food, if Jupiter be associated with a benefice in Kendra, Trikona, the 3rd or the 11th from the lord of the Dasha (Ketu). 

द्वद्विीयद्यूननाथे िु ह्यपमृत्युभवतर्ष्यति ॥५९॥ िद्दोर्षपरिहािाथं सशर्साहस्रकं जपेि् । महामृत्युञ्जयं जाप्यं सर्ोपद्रर्नाशनम् ॥६०॥ 

59-60. Fear of premature death will be caused if Jupiter be the lord of the 2nd or the 7th from the Ascendant. 

The remedial measures to obtain relief from the above evil effects are Mrityunjaya Japa recitation of Shiva Sahastranaam. 

Effects or the Antardasa or Saturn 

के िोििगविे मन्दे स्वदशायां िु पीडनम् । बन्धोाः क्लेशो मनस्तापििुष्पाज्जीर्लाभकृ ि् ॥६१॥ िाजकायवकलापेन धननाशो महद्भयम् । िानाच्च्च्युतिाः प्रर्ासि मागे चौिभयं भर्ेि् ॥६२॥ आलस्यं मनसो हातनिाष्टमे व्ययिासशगे । 

61-62½: Effects like distress to self and kinsmen, agony, increase in cattle wealth, loss of wealth as a result of imposition of fines by government, resignation from the existing post, journeys to foreign lands, and danger of thieves during travelling, will be derived in the Antardasa of Saturn in the Dasha of Ketu, if Saturn be deprived of strength and dignity. Then; will be loss of wealth and lethargy, if Saturn be in the 8th or the 12th from the Ascendant. 

मीनष्टरकोणगे मन्दे िुलायां स्वक्षवगेऽष्टप र्ा ॥६३॥ 

के न्द्रष्टरकोणलाभे र्ा दसिक्ये ु र्ा शुभांशके । शुभदृष्टयुिे चैर् सर्वकायाथवसाधनम् ॥६४॥ स्वप्रभोि महत्सौख्यं भ्रमणं च सुखार्हम् । स्वग्रामे सुखसम्पथत्ताः स्वर्गे िाजदशवनम् ॥६५॥ 

63-65. Success in all ventures, happiness from the employer, comforts during journeys, increase in happiness and property in one's own village, audience' with the king (visits to high dignitaries), etc., will be the results, if Saturn be in Trikona in Pisces, in Libra (his sign of exaltation), in his own sign or be in an auspicious Navamsha or be associated with a benefice in Kendra, Trikona or the 3rd from the Ascendant. 

Notes: According to Brihat Jataka Saturn in Libra, Pisces, Sagittarius, Capricorn and Aquarius in the Ascendant gives Raja-yoga. 

दायेशारर्षष्ठरिाःफे र्ा अष्टमे पापसंयुिे । देहिापो मनस्तापाः काये तर्घ्नो महद्भयम् ॥६६॥ आलस्यं मानहातनि ष्टपिृमारोतर्वनाशनम् । द्वद्विीयद्यूननाथे िु ह्यपमृत्युभयं भर्ेि् ॥६७॥ िद्दोर्षपैहािाथं तिलहोमं च काियेि् । कृ ष्णां गां मद्वहर्षीं दद्यादायुिािोग्यर्ृद्धये ॥६८॥ 

66-68: There will be physical distress, agony, obstacles in ventures, lethargy, defamation, death of parents, if Saturn be associated with a malefic, in the 6th, 8th or the 12th from the lord of the Dasha (Ketu). Fear of premature death may be expected if Saturn be the lord of the 2nd or 7th from the Ascendant. 

The remedial measures to obtain relief from the above evil effects are performance of Havana with sesame seeds (ततल) and giving a black cow or female buffalo in charity. 

Effects of the Antardasa of Mercury 

के िोििगविे सौम्ये के न्द्रलाभष्टरकोणगे । स्वोच्चे स्वक्षेरसंयुक्ते िाज्यलाभो महत्सुखम् ॥६९॥ सत्कथािर्णं दानं धमवससणद्धाः सुखार्हा । भूलाभाः पुरलाभि शुभगोष्ठीधनागमाः ॥७०॥ अयत्नाद्धमवलन्तब्धि तर्र्ाहि भतर्ष्यति । गृहे शुभकिं कमव र्िाभिणभूर्षणम् ॥७१॥ 

69-71. Effects like acquisition of a kingdom (attainment of a high position in government) enjoyments, charities, gain of wealth and land, birth of a son, celebration of religious functions and functions like marriage suddenly, well-being in the family, gain of clothes, ornaments etc., will be derived in the Antardasa of Mercury in the 

Dasha of Ketu, if Mercury be in a Kendra or Trikona from the Ascendant, be in his sign of exaltation or in his own sign. 

# भाग्यकमाथधपैयुवक्ते भाग्यर्ृणद्धाः सुखार्हा । तर्द्वद्गोष्ठीकथाथभि कालक्षेपो भतर्ष्यति ॥७२॥

72. There will be association with the men of learning, dawn of fortune and listening to religious discourses, if Mercury be associated with the lord of the 9th or the 10th. 

र्षष्ठाष्टमव्यये सौम्ये मन्दािाद्वहयुिेसक्षिे । तर्िोधो िाजर्गैि पिगेहतनर्ासनम् ॥७३॥ र्ाहनाम्बिपश्वाद्वदधनधान्याद्वदनाशकृ ि् । भुक्त्यादौ शोभनं प्रोक्तं मध्ये सौख्यं धनागमाः ॥७४॥ अिे क्लेशकिं चैर् दािपुराद्वदपीडनम् । 

73-74½, Antagonism with government officials, residing in other people's houses, destruction of wealth, clothes, conveyances and cattle, will be the results if Mercury be associated with Saturn, Mars or Rahu in the 6th, the 8th or the 12th from the Ascendant. There will be some beneficial effects of the commencement of the Dasha, still better results in the middle but inauspicious at the end. 

दायेशात्के न्द्रगे सौम्ये ष्टरकोणे लाभगेऽष्टप र्ा ॥७५॥ देहािोग्यं महांिाभाः पुरकल्याणर्ैभर्म् । भोजनाम्बिपश्वाद्वदव्यर्सायेऽथधकं फलम् ॥७६॥ 

75-76. There will be good health, happiness from son, opulence and glory, availability of good food and clothes and abnormal profits in business, if Mercury be in a Kendra, Trikona or the 11th from the lord of it Dasha, Ketu). 

दायेशारर्षष्ठिन्ध्रे र्ा व्यये र्ा बलर्सजविे । िद्भक्त्यादौ ु महाक्लेशो दािपुराद्वदपीडनम् ॥७७॥ िाजभीतिकििैर् मध्ये िीथवकिो भर्ेि् । द्वद्विीयद्यूननाथे िु ह्यपमृत्युभवतर्ष्यति ॥७८॥ िद्दोर्षपरिहािाथं तर्ष्णुसाहस्रकं जपेि् । ििाः सुखमर्ाप्नोति िीहिेि प्रसादिाः ॥७९॥ 

77-79. Distress, unhappiness and troubles to wife and children and danger from the king (government) may be expected at the commencement of the Antardasa if Mercury be weak in the 6th, the 8th or the 12th from the lord of the Dasha (Ketu). There will, however, be visits to sacred places in the middle of the Dasha. Fear of 

premature death will be caused if Mercury be the lord of the 2nd or the 7th from the Ascendant. 

The remedial measure to obtain relief from the above evil effect is recitation of Vishnu Sahastranaam. 

# अथ शुक्रान्तदिशाफलाध्यायः ॥ ६०॥

# Chapter 60. Effects of the Antardasa in the Dasha of Venus

Effects of the Antardasa of Venus 

अथ स्वािगविे शुक्रे लग्नात्के न्द्रष्टरकोणगे । 

लाभे र्ा बलसंयुक्ते िद्भक्तौ ु च शुभं फलम् ॥ १॥ 

तर्प्रमूलाद्धनप्राब्दप्तगोमद्वहष्याद्वदलाभकृ ि् । 

पुरोत्सर्ाद्वदसिोर्षो गृहे कल्याणसम्भर्ाः ॥ २॥ 

सन्मानं िाजसम्मानं िाज्यलाभो महत्सुखम् । 

1-2½: Effects like gain of wealth, cattle etc., through Brahmins, celebrations in connection with the birth of a so, well-being, recognition from the king (government), acquisition, of a kingdom (attainment of a high position in government), will be derived in the Antardasa of Venus in his own Dasha, if Venus be in Kendra, Trikona or the 11th from the Ascendant ad be endowed with strength. 

स्वोच्चे र्ा स्वक्षवगे र्ाष्टप िुङ्गांशे र्ांशगेऽष्टप र्ा ॥ ३॥ 

नूिनालयतनमाणं तनत्यं तमष्ठान्नभोजनम् । 

कलरपुरतर्भर्ं तमरसंयुक्तभोजनम् ॥ ४॥ 

अन्नदानं ष्टप्रयं तनत्यं दनधमाद्वदसङ् ग्रहाः । 

महािाजप्रसादेन र्ाहनाम्बिभूर्षणम् ॥ ५॥ 

व्यर्सायात्फलाथधक्यं चिुष्पाज्जीर्लाभकृ ि् । 

प्रयाणं पसिमे भागे र्ाहनाम्बिलाभकृ ि् ॥ ६॥ 

3-6. Construction of a new house, availability of sweet preparations, happiness to wife and children, companionship with a friend, giving grains etc. in charity, beneficence of the king (Government) gain of clothes, conveyances and ornaments, success in business, increase in the number of cattle, gain of garments by performing journeys in the western direction, etc., will be the results, if Venus be in his sign of exaltation, in his own sign or be in exalted or own Navamsha. 

लग्नाद्युपचये शुक्रे शुभग्रहयुिेसक्षिे । 

तमरांशे िुङ्गलाभेशयोगलािकसंयुिे ॥ ७॥ 

िाज्यलाभो महोत्साहो िाजप्रीतिाः शुभार्हा । 

# गृहे कल्याणसम्पथत्तदािपुराद्वदर्द्धवनम् ॥ ८॥

7-8. There will be acquisition of a kingdom (high position in government), enthusiasm, beneficence of the king (government), well-being in the family, increase in the number of wives, children and wealth, etc., if Venus be associated with or aspected by a benefice and be in a friendly Navamsha, in the 3rd, the 6th or the 11th from the Ascendant. 

र्षष्ठाष्टमव्यये शुक्रे पापयुक्ते ऽथ र्ीसक्षिे । चौिाद्वदव्रणभीतिि सर्वर जनपीडनम् ॥ ९॥ िाजद्वािे जनद्वेर्ष इष्टबन्धुतर्नाशनम् । दािपुराद्वदपीडा च सर्वर जनपीडनम् ॥ १०॥ 

9-10. Danger from thieves etc., antagonistic relations with government officials, destruction of friends and kinsmen, distress to wife and children, may be expected if Venus be associated with or aspected by a malefic in the 6th, the 8th or the 12th from the Ascendant. 

द्वद्विीयद्यूननाथे िु स्थििे चेन्मिणं भर्ेि् । ििव दगाजपं ु कु याद्धनुदानं च काियेि् ॥ ११॥ 

11. There will be fear of death, if Venus be the lord of the 2nd or the 7th from the Ascendant. 

Remedial measures to obtain relief from the above evil effects are Durga Patha and giving a cow in charity. 

Effects of the Antardasa of the Sun 

शुक्रस्यािगविे सूये सिापो िाजतर्ग्रहाः । दायादकलहिैर् स्वोच्चनीचतर्र्सजविे ॥ १२॥ 

12. There will be a period of agony, wrath of the king (government), quarrels with the coparceners etc., in the Antardasa of the Sun in the Dasha of Venus if the Sun be in any sign other than his sign of exaltation or debilitation. 

Notes: This verse does not appear to be correctly worded because the Sun does produce good effects in position other than exaltation or debilitation. The position is correctly stated in the Chowkambha version of this verse which reads as under, 

Page 433 शुिस्यान्तगधते सूये सन्तापो राजभभिः कशलिः । 

दायादात् कलहश्चैव शुभक्षेिात्य राशशगे ॥ १२॥ 

स्वोच्चे स्वक्षेरगे सूये तमरक्षे के न्द्रकोणगे । दायेशात्के न्द्रकोणे र्ा लाभे र्ा धनगेऽष्टप र्ा ॥ १३॥ िद्भक्तौु धनलाभाः स्याद्राज्यिीधनसम्पदाः । 

13-15, Effects like acquisition of a kingdom (attainment of a high position in government) and wealth, happiness from wife and children, happiness from employer, meeting with friends, happiness from parents, marriage, name and fame, betterment of fortune, birth of a son etc., will be experienced if the Sun be in his sign of exaltation, in his own sign in Kendra Trikona, the 2nd or the 11th from the Ascendant or the lord of the Dasha (Venus). 

िथाष्टमे व्यये सूये रिपुिासशस्थििेऽष्टप र्ा । नीचे र्ा पापर्गविे देहिापो मनोरुजाः ॥ १६॥ स्वजनोपरिसंक्लेशो तनत्यं तनष्ठु िभार्षणम् । ष्टपिृपीडा बन्धुहानी िाजद्वािे तर्िोधकृ ि् ॥ १७॥ व्रणपीडाद्वहबाधा च स्वगृहे च भयं िथा । नानािोगभयं चैर् गृहक्षेराद्वदनाशनम् ॥ १८॥ 

16-18. Distress, agony, distress to members of the family, harsh language, distress to father, loss of kinsmen, wrath of the king (government), danger at home, many diseases, destruction of agricultural production, etc., will be the results, if the Sun be in the 6th, the 8th or the 12th from the Ascendant, or be in his sign of debilitation or in an enemy's sign. 

सप्तमाथधपिौ सूये ग्रहबाधा भतर्ष्यति । िद्दोर्षपरिहािाथं सूयवप्रीतिं च काियेि् ॥ १९॥ शुक्रस्यािगविे चन्द्रे के न्द्रलाभष्टरकोणगे । स्वोच्चे स्वक्षेरगे चैर् भाग्यनाथेनसंयुिे ॥ २०॥ 

19-20: There will be evil influence of the planets if the Sun be the 3rd of the 2nd or the 7th from the Ascendant. 

Worship of the Sun is the remedial measure to obtain relief from the above evil effects. 

Effects of the Antardasa of the Moon 

शुभयुक्ते पूणवचन्द्रे िाज्यनाथेन संयुिे । िद्बक्तौ ु र्ाहनादीनां लाभं गेहे महत्सुखम् ॥ २१॥ महािाजप्रसादेन गजािैश्वयवमाद्वदशेि् । महानदीस्नानपुण्यं देर्ब्राह्मणपूजनम् ॥ २२॥ 

21-22. Effects like gain of wealth, conveyances, clothes by the beneficence of the king, happiness in the family, great opulence and glory, devotion to deities and Brahmins, will be derived in the Antardasa of the Moon in the Dasha of Venus if the Moon be in her sign of exaltation, in her own sign, be associated with the lord of the 9th, benefices or the lord of the 10th or be in a Kendra, Trikona or the 11th. 

गीिर्ाद्यप्रसङ्गाद्वदतर्द्वज्जनतर्भूर्षणम् । 

गोमद्वहष्याद्वदर्ृणद्धि व्यर्सायेऽथधकं फलम् ॥ २३॥ 

भोजनाम्बिसौख्यं च बन्धुसंयुक्तभोजनम् । 

23-23½: In the above circumstances, there will also be association with musicians and men of learning and receiving of decorations, gain of cows, buffaloes and other cattle, abnormal profits in business, dining with brothers etc. 

नीचे र्ात्सङ्गिे र्ाष्टप र्षष्ठाष्टमव्ययिासशगे ॥ २४॥ 

दायेशारर्षष्ठगे र्ाष्टप िन्ध्रे र्ा व्ययिासशगे । 

ित्काले धननाशाः स्यात्सञ्चिेि महद्भयम् ॥ २५॥ 

देहायासो मनस्तापो िाजद्वािे तर्िोधकृ ि् । 

तर्देशगमनं चैर् िीथवयाराद्वदकं फलम् ॥ २६॥ 

दािपुराद्वद पीडा च तनजबन्धुतर्योगकृ ि् । 

24-26½: Loss of wealth, fears, physical distress, agony, wrath of the king (government), journeys to foreign lands or pilgrimage, distress to wife and children and separation from kinsmen, will be the results if the Moon be in her sign of debilitation, combust or be in the 6th, the 8th or the 12th from the Ascendant or the lord of the Dasha (Venus). 

दायेशात्के न्द्रलाभिे ष्टरकोणे सहजेऽष्टप र्ा ॥ २७॥ 

िाजप्रीतिकिी चैर् देशग्रामाथधपत्यिा । 

धैयं यशाः सुखं कीतिवर्ाहनाम्बिभूर्षणम् ॥ २८॥ 

कू पािामिडागद्वदतनमाणं धनसङ् ग्रहाः । 

भुक्तयादौ देहसौख्यं स्यादिे क्लेशस्तथा भर्ेि् ॥ २९॥ 

27-29: There will be sovereignty over a province or village by the beneficence of the king (government), of clothes etc., construction of a reservoir, increase in wealth etc., if the Moon be in a Kendra, Trikona, the 3rd or the 11th from the lord of the Dasha (Venus). There will be physical fitness at the commencement of the Antardasa and physical distress in its last portion. 

Notes: Though it is not mentioned, it is but natural that the effects of the Moon being lord of the 2nd and the 7th will be the same as predicted for other planets earlier in every case. 

# Effects of the Antardasa of Mars

शुक्रस्यािगविे भौमे लग्नात्के न्द्रष्टरकोणगे । 

स्वोच्चे र्ा स्वक्षवगे भौमे लाभे र्ा बलसंयुिे ॥ ३०॥ 

लग्नाथधपेन संयुक्ते कमवभाग्येशसंयुिे । 

िद्भक्तौ ु िाजयोगाद्वदसम्पदं शोभनां र्देि् ॥ ३१॥ 

र्िाभिणभूम्यादेरिष्टससणद्धाः सुखार्हा । 

30-31½: Effects like acquisition of kingdom (attainment of a high position in government), property, clothes, ornaments, land and desired objects, will be derived in the Antardasa of Mars in the Dasha of Venus, if Mars he in Kendra, Trikona or the 11th from the Ascendant or be in his sign of exaltation or his own signs or be associated with the lord of the Ascendant, 9th or the 10th. 

िथाऽष्टमे व्यये र्ाऽष्टप दायेशाद्वा िथैर् च ॥ ३२॥ 

शीिज्विाद्वदपीडा च ष्टपिृमािृभयार्हा । 

ज्विाद्यथधकिोगाि िानभ्रंशो मनोरुजा ॥ ३३॥ 

स्वबन्धुजनहातनि कलहो िाजतर्ग्रहाः । 

िाजद्वािजनद्वेर्षो धनधान्यव्ययोऽथधकाः ॥ ३४॥ 

32-34. There win be fever from cold, diseases like fever to parents, loss of position, quarrels, antagonism with the king (government) and government officials, extravagant expenditure etc., if Mars be in the 6th, the 8th or the 12th from the Ascendant or the lord of the Dasha. 

व्यर्सायात्फलं नेष्टं ग्रामभूम्याद्वदहातनकृ ि् । 

द्वद्विीयद्यूननाथे िु देहर्ाधा भतर्ष्यति ॥ ३५॥ 

35. Physical distress, losses in profession, Joss of village, land etc., will be the results, if Mars be the lord of the 2nd or the 7th from the Ascendant. 

Notes: Though remedial measure is not mentioned, we believe that giving a bull in charity will enable the native to obtain relief from the evil effects. 

Effects of the Antardasa of Rahu 

शुक्रस्यािगविे िाहौ के न्द्रलाभष्टरकोणगे । 

स्वोच्चे र्ा शुभसन्दष्टेृ योगकािकसंयुिे ॥ ३६॥ 

िद्भक्तौ ु बहुसौख्यं च धनधान्याद्वदलाभकृ ि् । 

इष्टबन्धुसमाकीणं भर्नं च समाद्वदशेि् ॥ ३७॥ 

यािुाः कायाथवससणद्धाः स्याि् पशुक्षेराद्वदसम्भर्ाः । 

36-37½: Effects like great enjoyment, gain of wealth, visits of friends, successful journeys, gain of cattle and land etc., will be derived in the Antardasa of Rahu in the Dasha of Venus, if Rahu be in Kendra or Trikona or the 11th, be in his sign of exaltation or in his own sign or be associated with or aspected by benefices. 

लग्नाद्युपचये िाहौ िद्भगक्ताः ु सुखदा भर्ेि् ॥ ३८॥ शरुनाशो महोत्साहो िाजप्रीतिकिी शुभा । भुक्त्यादौ शिमासांि अिे ज्विमजीणवकृ ि् ॥ ३९॥ 

38-39. Enjoyments, destruction of enemy, enthusiasm beneficence of the king, will be the results, if Rahu be in the 3rd, the 6th, the 10th or the 11th from the Ascendant. Good effects will be experienced up to 5 months from the commencement of the Antardasa but at the end of the Dasha there will be danger from fevers and indigestion. 

कायवतर्घ्नमर्ाप्नोति सञ्चिे च मनोव्यथा । पिं सुखं च सौभाग्यं महािाज इर्ाऽश्निे ु ॥ ४०॥ नैऋिीं द्वदशमाश्रित्य प्रयाणं प्रभुदशवनम् । यािुाः कायाथवससणद्धाः स्यात्स्वदेशे पुनिेष्यति ॥ ४१॥ उपकािो ब्राह्मणानां िीथवयाराफलं भर्ेि् । 

40-41½: In the above circumstances except for obstacles in ventures and journeys, and worries, there will be all enjoyments like those of a king. Journey, to foreign lands will bring success and the person will return safely to his homeland. There will also be blessing from Brahmins and auspicious results consequent to visits to holy places. 

दायेशाद्रन्ध्रभार्िे व्यये र्ा पापसंयुिे ॥ ४२॥ अशुभं लभिे कमव ष्टपिृमािृजनार्थध । सर्वर जनतर्द्वेर्षं नानारूपं द्वद्वजोत्तम ॥ ४३॥ द्वद्विीये सप्तमे र्ाष्टप देहालस्य तर्तनद्वदवशेि् । िद्दोर्षपरिहािाथं मृत्युञ्जयजपं चिेि् ॥ ४४॥ 

42-44: There will be inauspicious effects on self and parents and antagonism with people, if Rahu be associated with a malefic in the 8th or the 12th from the lord of the Dasha (Venus). Physical distress will be caused if Rahu be the lord of the 2nd or the 7th from the Ascendant. 

Remedial measure to obtain relief from the above evil effects is Mrityunjaya Japa. 

Effects of the Antardasa of Jupiter 

शुक्रस्यािगविे जीर्े स्वोच्चे स्वक्षेरके न्द्रगे । 

दायेशाच्छु भिासशिे भाग्ये र्ा पुरिासशगे ॥ ४५॥ 

नष्टिाज्याद्धनप्राब्दप्ततमष्टाथाम्बिसम्पदम् । 

तमरप्रभोि सन्मानं धनधान्यं लभेन्निाः ॥ ४६॥ 

िाजसम्मानकीतिं च अश्वान्दोलाद्वदलाभकृ ि् । 

तर्द्वत्प्रभुसमाकीणं शािापरििमम् ॥ ४७॥ 

पुरोत्सर्ाद्वदसिोर्षतमष्टबन्धुसमागमम् । 

ष्टपिृमािृसुखप्राब्दप्तं पुराद्वदसौख्यमाद्वदशेि् ॥ ४८॥ 

45-48. Effects like recovery of the lost kingdom (reinstatement) in a high position in (government), acquisition of desired grains, clothes and property etc., reverence from the friends and the king (government) and gain of wealth, recognition from the king, good reputation, gain of conveyances, association with employer and men of learning, industriousness in the study of Shastra, birth of a son, satisfaction, visits of close friends, happiness to parents and son etc., will be derived in the Antardasa of Jupiter in the Dasha of Venus, if Jupiter be in his sign, of exaltation, in his own sign or in Kendra or Trikona to the Ascendant or the lord of the Dasha (Venus). 

दायेशारर्षष्ठिासशिे व्यये र्ा पापसंयुिे । 

िाजचौिाद्वदपीडा च देहपीडा भतर्ष्यति ॥ ४९॥ 

आत्मरुग्बन्धुकष्टं स्यात्कलहेन मनोव्यथा । 

िानच्युतिं प्रर्ासं च नानािोगं समाप्नुयाि् ॥ ५०॥ 

49-50: There will be danger from the king (government), and thieves, distress to self and kinsmen, quarrels, mental agony, loss of position, going away to foreign lands and danger of many kinds of diseases, if Jupiter be in the 6th, the 8th or the 12th from the lord of the Dasha (Venus) and be associated with a malefic. 

द्वद्विीयसप्तमाधीशे देहबाधा भतर्ष्यति । 

िद्दोर्षपरिहािाथं महामृत्युञ्जयं चिेि् ॥ ५१॥ 

51. There will be physical distress if Jupiter be the lord of the 2nd and the 7th. The remedial measure to obtain relief from the above vii effects is Mrityunjaya Japa. 

Effects of the Antardasa of Saturn 

शुक्रस्यािगविे मन्दे स्वोच्चे िु पिमोच्चगे । 

स्वक्षवके न्द्रष्टरकोणिे िुङ्गांशे स्वांशगेऽष्टप र्ा ॥ ५२॥ 

िद्भक्तौ ु बहुसौख्यं स्याद्वदष्टबन्धुसमागमाः । 

िाजद्वािे च सम्मानं पुष्टरकाजन्मसम्भर्ाः ॥ ५३॥ 

पुण्यिीथवफलर्ाब्दप्तदानधमाद्वदपुण्यकृ ि् । 

# स्वप्रभोि पदार्ाब्दप्ताः नीचिे क्लेशभाग्यभर्ेि् ॥ ५४॥

52-54. Effects like great enjoyments, visits of friends an, kinsmen recognition from the king (government) birth of a daughter, visits to holy places and sacred shrines, conferment of authority by the king (government), will be derived in the Antardasa of Saturn in the Dasha of Venus, if Saturn be in his sign of exaltation in his own sign in Kendra, Trikona or in his own Navamsha. 

देहालस्यमर्ाप्नोति िथाऽयादथधकव्ययम् । िथाष्टमे व्यये मन्दे दायेशाद्वा िथैर् च ॥ ५५॥ भुक्त्यादौ तर्तर्धा पीडा ष्टपिृमािृजनार्थध । दािपुराद्वदपीडा च पिदेशाद्वदतर्भ्रमाः ॥ ५६॥ व्यर्सायात्फलं नष्टं गोमद्वहष्याद्वदहातनकृ ि् । द्वद्विीयसप्तमाधीशे देहबाधा भतर्ष्यति ॥ ५७॥ 

55-57: There will be lethargy and more expenditure than income, if Saturn be in his sign of debilitation. Many kinds of distresses and troubles at the commencement of the Antardasa, distress to parents, wife and children, going away to foreign lands, losses in profession, destruction of cattle, etc., will be the results, if Saturn be in the 8th, the 11th or the 12th from the Ascendant or the lord of the Dasha (Venus). There will be physical distress if Saturn be the lord of the 2nd or the 7th from the Ascendant. 

िद्दोर्षपरिहािाथं तिलहोमं च काियेि् । मृत्युञ्जयजपं कु याच्चण्डीपाठमाथष्टप र्ा ॥ ५८॥ स्वयं र्ा ब्राह्मणद्वािा यथाशगक्त यथातर्थध । ििाः शान्तिमर्ाप्नोति सशर्ाशम्भुप्रसादिाः ॥ ५९॥ 

58-59-The remedial measures to obtain relief from the above evil effects are Havana with sesame seeds (ततल), Mrityunjaya Japa, and Durga-Saptashati Patha (by self or through a Brahmin). 

Effects of the Antardasa of Mercury 

स्वोच्चे र्ा स्वक्षवगे र्ाष्टप िाजप्रीतिकिं शुभम् ॥ ६०॥ सौभाग्यं पुरलाभि सन्मागेण धनागमाः । पुिाणधमविर्णं शृङ्गारिजनसङ्गमाः ॥ ६१॥ इष्टबन्धुजनाकीणं शोथभिं िस्य मब्दन्दिम् । स्वप्रभोि महत्सौख्यं तनत्यं तमष्ठान्नभोजनम् ॥ ६२॥ 

60-62. Effects like dawn of fortune, birth of a son, gain of wealth through judgement of court, listening to stories from Puranas, association with persons competent in poetry etc., visits of close friends, happiness from employer, availability of sweetish preparations etc., will be derived in the Antardasa of Mercury in the Dasha of Venus, if Mercury be in Kendra, Trikona or the 11th from the Ascendant, (or from the lord of the Dasha Venus) in his sign of exaltation or in his own sign. 

दायेशारर्षष्ठिन्ध्रे र्ा व्यये र्ा बलर्सजविे । 

पापदृष्टे पापयुक्ते चिुष्पाज्जीर्हातनकृ ि् ॥ ६३॥ 

अन्यालयतनर्ासि मनोर्ैकल्यसम्भर्ाः । 

व्यापािेर्षु च सर्ेर्षु हातनिेर् न संशयाः ॥ ६४॥ 

भुक्त्यादौ शोभनं प्रोक्तं मध्ये मध्यफलं द्वदशेि् । 

अिे क्लेशकिं चैर् शीिर्ािज्विाद्वदकम् ॥ ६५॥ 

63-65. If Mercury be in the 6th, the 8th or the 12th from the lord of Dasha (Venus) or be weak or be associated with a malefic, there will be agony, loss of cattle, residence in other people's houses, and losses in business. There will be some good effects at the commencement, moderate in the middle portion and distress from fever etc., at the end of the Antardasa. 

सप्तमाधीशदोर्षेण देहपीडा भतर्ष्यति । 

िद्दोर्षपरिहािाथं तर्ष्णुसाहस्रकं जपेि् ॥ ६६॥ 

66. There will be physical distress if Mercury be the lord of the 2nd or the 7th from the Ascendant. 

The remedial measure to obtain relief from the above evil effects is recitation of Vishnu Sahastranaam. 

Effects of the Antardasa of Ketu 

शुक्रस्यािगविे के िौ स्वोच्चे र्ा स्वक्षवगेऽष्टप र्ा । 

योगकािकसम्बन्धे िानर्ीयवसमन्तििे ॥ ६७॥ 

भुक्त्यादौ शुभमाथधक्यागन्नत्यं तमष्ठान्नभोजनम् । 

व्यर्सायात्फलाथधक्यं गोमहोष्याद्वदर्ृणद्धकृ ि् ॥ ६८॥ 

67-68. Auspicious effects like availability of sweetish preparations, abnormal gains in profession and increase in cattle wealth, will be derived from the very commencement of the Antardasa of Ketu in the Dasha of Venus, if Ketu be in his sign of exaltation, in his own sign or be related to a yoga karaka planet or be possessed of positional strength. 

Notes: It is not laid down anywhere in which house does Ketu get positional strength. 

धनधान्यसमृणद्धि सङ् ग्रामे तर्जयो भर्ेि् । 

भुक्त्यिे द्वह सुखं चैर् भुक्त्यादौ मध्यमं फलम् ॥ ६९॥ 

मध्ये मध्ये महत्कष्टं पिादािोग्यमाद्वदशेि् । 

69-69½: In the above circumstances, there will be definite victory in the war at the end of the Antardasa. Moderate results will be experienced in the middle portion of the Antardasa and there will also be feeling of distress sometimes 

दायेशाद्रन्ध्रभार्िे व्यये र्ा पापसंयुिे ॥ ७०॥ 

चौिाद्वहव्रणपीडा च बुणद्धनाशो महद्भयम् । 

सशिोरुजं मनस्तापमकमवकलहं र्देि् ॥ ७१॥ 

प्रमेहभर्िोगं च नानामागे धनव्ययाः । 

भायापुरतर्िोधि गमनं कायवनाशनम् ॥ ७२॥ 

70-72. There will be danger from snakes, thieves, wounds, loss of power of thinking, headache, agony, quarrels without any cause or reason, diabetes, excessive expenditure, antagonism with wife and children, going away to foreign land, loss in ventures, if Ketu be in the 8th or the 12th from the lord of the Dasha (Venus) or be associated with a malefic. 

द्वद्विीयद्यूननाथे िु देहबाधा भतर्ष्यति । 

िद्दोर्षपरिहािाथं मृत्युञ्जयजपं चिेि् ॥ ७३॥ 

छागदानं प्रकु र्ीि सर्वसम्पत्प्रदायकम् । 

शुक्रप्रीतिकिीं शान्तिं ििाः सुखमर्ाप्नुयाि् ॥ ७४॥ 

73-74: There will be physical distress if Ketu be the lord of the 2nd or the 7th from the Ascendant. 

The remedial measures to obtain relief from the above effects are Mrityunjaya Japa and giving a goat in charity. Remedial measures for appeasing Venus will also prove beneficial 

# अथ प्रत्यन्तदिशाफलाध्यायः ॥ ६१॥

# Chapter 61. Effects of Pratyantar Dasha in the Antardasa of Planets

How to calculate the Pratyantar Dasha 

पृथक् स्वस्वदशामानैहवन्यादिदवशातमतिम् । भ्येत्सर्वदशायोगैाः फलं प्रत्यििं क्रमाि् ॥ १॥ 

1. By multiplying the years etc. of Antardasa of planets separately by Dasha years of each planet and dividing the product by total span of the Vimshottari Dasha, namely 120 years, we will arrive at the Pratyantar Dasha of each planet. 

Example: We have to find out the Pratyantar Dasha of the Sun in the Antardasa and Dasha of the Sun. The span of Antardasa namely 3 month 18 days converted into days comes to 108 days. 

The Pratyantar Dasha will be $1 0 8 \times 6 = 6 4 8 \div 1 2 0$ 

$= 5$ days 24 Ghatikas 

The Pratyantar Dasha of the Moon in the Antardasa and, Dasha of the Sun will be 

108 days $\times 1 0 = 1 0 8 0 \div 1 2 0 = 9$ days 

Tables are given below showing the Pratyantar Dasha of all the planets in the Antardasa in the Dasha of the Sun. 

Antardasa of the Sun

Effects of Pratyantar Dasha in the Antardasa of the Sun 

तर्र्ादो तर्त्तहातनि दािातिवाः सशिसस व्यथा । 

िव्यििे बुधैज्ञेयं िस्य प्रत्यििे फलम् ॥ २॥ 

2. Sun-Sun (This means P. Dasha of the Sun in the Antardasa of the Sun)- Argument with other persons, loss of wealth, distress to wife, headache etc. The above are general effects. Such inauspicious effects will not be produced if the Sun be in Trikona etc., be the lord of an auspicious house, be in an auspicious house an, benefice Varga. All other Pratyantar effects should be judged in this manner. 

उद्वेगाः कलहिैर् तर्त्तहातनमवनोव्यथा । 

िव्यििे तर्जानीयाि् चन्द्रप्रत्यििे फलम् ॥ ३॥ 

3. Sun-Moon -Excitement, quarrels, loss of wealth, mental agony etc. 

िाजभीतिाः शिभीतिबवन्धनं बहुसङ्कटम् । 

शरुर्तिकृ िा पीडा कु जप्रत्यििे फलम् ॥ ४॥ 

4. Sun-Mars-Danger from the king and weapons, imprisonment, distress from enemies and fire. 

श्लेष्मव्याथधाः शिभीतिएधनहातनमवहद्भयम् । 

िाजभङ्गस्तथा रासो िाहुप्रत्यििे फलम् ॥ ५॥ 

5. Sun-Rahu - Disorder of phlegm, danger of weapon, loss of wealth, destruction of kingdom and mental agony. 

शरुनाशो जयो र्ृणद्धर्विहेमाद्वदभूर्षणम् । 

अश्वयानाद्वदलाभि गुरुप्रत्यििे फलम् ॥ ६॥ 

6. Sun- Jupiter - Victory, increase in, wealth, gain of gold, garments, conveyances etc. 

धनहातनाः पशोाः पीडा महोद्वेगो महारुजाः । 

अशुभं सर्वमाप्नोति शतनप्रत्यििे जनाः ॥ ७॥ 

7. Sun-Saturn---Loss or wealth, distress to cattle, excitement, diseases etc. 

# तर्द्यालाभो बन्धुसङ्ग भोज्यप्राब्दप्तधवनागमाः । धमवलाभो नृपात्पूजा तबधप्रत्यििे भर्ेि् ॥ ८॥

8. Sun-Mercury-Affectionate relations with kinsmen, availability of good food, gains of wealth, religious mindedness, reverence from the king (government.). 

प्राणभीतिमवहाहानी िाजभीतिि तर्ग्रहाः । शरुणाञ्च महार्ादो के िोाः प्रत्यििे भर्ेि् ॥ ९॥ 

9. Sun-Ketu-Danger to life, loss of wealth, danger from the king (government) trouble with the enemies. 

द्वदनातन समरूपाणण लाभोऽप्यल्पो भर्ेद्वदह । स्वल्पा च सुखसम्पथत्ताः शुक्रप्रत्यििे भर्ेि् ॥ १०॥ 

10. Sun-Venus-Moderate effects or some gains of wealth may be expected. Antardasa of the Moon 

Pratyantar Dasha in the Antardasa of the Moon

# Effects or the Pratyantar Dasha in the Antardasa of the Moon

भूमोज्यधनसम्प्राप्ती िाजपूजामहत्सुखम् । लाभिन्द्राििे ज्ञेयं चन्द्रप्रत्यििे फलम् ॥ ११॥ 

11. Moon-Moon - Acquisition of land, wealth and property, reverence from the king (government), and availability of sweetish preparations. 

मतिर्ृणद्धमवहापूज्याः सुखं बन्धुजनैाः सह । धनागमाः शरुभयं कु जप्रत्यििे भर्ेि् ॥ १२॥ 

12. Moon-Mars-Wisdom and discretion, reverence from the people, increase in wealth, enjoyments to kinsmen but there will be danger from enemy. 

भर्ेत्कल्याणसम्पत्ती िाजतर्त्तसमागमाः । अशुभैिल्पमृत्युअि िाहुप्रत्यििे द्वद्वज ॥ १३॥ 

13. Moon-Rahu-Well-being and gain of wealth from the king (Government), danger of death if Rahu he associated with a malefic. 

र्िलाभो महािेजो ब्रह्मज्ञानं च सद्गिोाःु । िाज्यालङ्किणार्ाब्दप्तगुवरुप्रत्यििे फलम् ॥ १४॥ 

14. Moon-Jupiter- Enjoyments, increase in dignity and glory, gain knowledge through the preceptor, acquisition of a kingdom (high position in Government) and gems etc. 

दद्वदवनेु लभिे पीडां र्ािष्टपत्ताद्वद्वशेर्षिाः । धनधान्ययशोहातनाः शतनप्रत्यििे भर्ेि् ॥ १५॥ 

15. Moon-Saturn- Bilious troubles, loss of wealth, and name and fame. 

पुरजन्महयप्राब्दप्ततर्वद्यालाभो महोन्नतिाः । शुक्लर्िान्नलाभि बुधप्रत्यििे भर्ेि् ॥ १६॥ 

16. Moon-Mercury- Birth of a son, acquisition of a horse and other conveyances, success in education progress, gain of white garments and grains. Page 594 Page 594 

ब्राह्मणेन समं युद्धमपमृत्युाः सुखक्षयाः । 

सर्वर जायिे क्लेशाः के िोाः प्रत्यििे भर्ेि् ॥ १७॥ 

17. Moon-Ketu-Quarrels with Brahmins, fear of premature death, loss of happiness, and distress all round. 

धनलाभो महत्सौख्यं कन्याजन्म सुभोजनम् । 

प्रीतिि सर्वलोके भ्यो भृगुप्रत्यििे तर्धोाः ॥ १८॥ 

18. Moon-Venus- Gain of wealth, enjoyments, birth of a daughter, availability of sweet preparations and cordial relations with all. 

अन्नागमो र्िलाभाः शरुहातनाः सुखागमाः । 

सर्वर तर्जयप्राब्दप्ताः सूयवप्रत्यििे तर्धोाः ॥ १९॥ 

19. Moon-Sun-Gain of happiness, grains and garments, victories everywhere. Antardasa of Mars

Pratyantar Dasha in the Antardasa of the Moon

Effects of Pratyantar Dasha in the Antardasa of Mars 

शरुभीतिं कसलं घोिं िक्तस्रार्ं मृिेभवयम् । 

कु जस्यािदवशायां च कु जप्रत्यििे र्देि् ॥ २०॥ 

20. Mars-Mars-Danger from enemies, quarrels, and fear of premature death on account of blood diseases. 

बन्धनं िाजभङ्गि धनहातनाः कु भोजनम् । 

कलहाः शरुथभतनवत्यं िाहुप्रत्यििे भर्ेि् ॥ २१॥ 

21. Mars-Rahu-Destruction of wealth and kingdom (fall of Government), unpalatable food and quarrels with the enemy. 

मतिनाशस्तथा दाःखं ु सिापाः कलहो भर्ेि् । 

तर्फलं श्रचन्तििं सर्ं गुिोाः प्रत्यििे भर्ेि् ॥ २२॥ 

22. Mars-Jupiter- Loss of intelligence, distress, sorrows, quarrels and nofulfilment of any ambition. 

स्वातमनाशस्तथा पीडा धनहातनन्मवहाभयम् । 

र्ैकल्यं कलहिासो शनेाः प्रत्यििे भर्ेि् ॥ २३॥ 

23. Mars-Saturn- Destruction of the employer, distress, loss of wealth, danger from enemies, anxiety, quarrels and sorrows. 

सर्वथा बुणद्धनाशि धनहातनज्वविस्तनौ । 

# र्िान्नसुहृदां नाशो बुधप्रत्यििे भर्ेि् ॥ २४॥

24. Mars-Mercury- Loss of intelligence, loss of wealth, fevers and loss of grains, garments and friends. 

आलस्य च सशिाःपीडा पापिोगोऽपमृत्युकृ ि् । िाजभीतिाः शिघािो के िोाः प्रत्यििे भर्ेि् ॥ २५॥ 

25. Mars-Ketu- Distress from diseases, lethargy, premature death, danger from the king and weapons. 

चाण्डालात्सङ्कटिासो िाजशािभयं भर्ेि् । अतिसािाऽथ र्मनं भृगोाः प्रत्यििे भर्ेि् ॥ २६॥ 

26. Mars-Venus-Distress from Chandals (चण्डाल) sorrow, danger from the king and weapons, dysentery and vomiting. 

भूतमलाभोऽथवसम्पथत्ताः सिोर्षो तमरसङ्गतिाः । सर्वर सुखमाप्नोति िर्ेाः प्रत्यििे जनाः ॥ २७॥ 

27. Mars-Son-Increase in landed property and wealth satisfaction, visits of friends, happiness all round. 

याम्यां द्वदसश भर्ेिाभाः ससिर्ितर्भूर्षणम् । संससणद्धाः सर्वकायाणां तर्धोाः प्रत्यििे भर्ेि् ॥ २८॥ 

28. Mars-Moon Gains of white garments etc., from the southern direction, success in all venture 


Antardasa of Rahu Pratyantar Dasha in the Antardasa of the Rahu

<table><tr><td></td><td colspan="9">Pratyantar Dasha in the Antardasa of the Ketu</td></tr><tr><td></td><td>Ket u</td><td>Venu s</td><td>Su n</td><td>Moo n</td><td>Mar s</td><td>Rah u</td><td>Jupiter r</td><td>Satur n</td><td>Mercur y</td></tr><tr><td>Month</td><td>0</td><td>2</td><td>0</td><td>1</td><td>0</td><td>1</td><td>1</td><td>1</td><td>1</td></tr><tr><td>Days</td><td>22</td><td>3</td><td>10</td><td>1</td><td>22</td><td>26</td><td>20</td><td>29</td><td>23</td></tr><tr><td>Ghatik a</td><td>3</td><td>0</td><td>54</td><td>30</td><td>3</td><td>42</td><td>24</td><td>54</td><td>33</td></tr></table>

<table><tr><td></td><td colspan="9">Pratyantar Dasha in the Antardasa of the Venus</td></tr><tr><td></td><td>Venu</td><td>Su</td><td>Moo</td><td>Mar</td><td>Rah</td><td>Jupiter</td><td>Satur</td><td>Mercur</td><td>Ket</td></tr><tr><td></td><td>s</td><td>n</td><td>n</td><td>s</td><td>u</td><td>r</td><td>n</td><td>y</td><td>u</td></tr><tr><td>Month</td><td>6</td><td>1</td><td>3</td><td>2</td><td>5</td><td>4</td><td>5</td><td>5</td><td>2</td></tr><tr><td>Days</td><td>0</td><td>24</td><td>0</td><td>3</td><td>12</td><td>24</td><td>21</td><td>3</td><td>3</td></tr><tr><td>Ghatik a</td><td>0</td><td>0</td><td>0</td><td>0</td><td>0</td><td>0</td><td>0</td><td>0</td><td>0</td></tr></table>

<table><tr><td></td><td colspan="9">Pratyantar Dasha in the Antardasa of the Sun</td></tr><tr><td></td><td>Su</td><td>Moo</td><td>Mar</td><td>Rah</td><td>Jupiter</td><td>Satur</td><td>Mercur</td><td>Ket</td><td>Venu</td></tr><tr><td></td><td>n</td><td>n</td><td>s</td><td>u</td><td>r</td><td>n</td><td>y</td><td>u</td><td>s</td></tr><tr><td>Month</td><td>0</td><td>0</td><td>0</td><td>1</td><td>1</td><td>1</td><td>1</td><td>0</td><td>1</td></tr><tr><td>Days</td><td>16</td><td>27</td><td>18</td><td>18</td><td>13</td><td>21</td><td>15</td><td>18</td><td>24</td></tr></table>

Ghatik

Effects of Pratyantar Dasha in the Antardasa of Rahu 

बन्धनं बहुधा िोगो बहुघािाः सुहृद्भयम् । 

िाह्विदवशायां च ज्ञेयं िाह्वििे फलम् ॥ २९॥ 

29. Rahu-Rahu-imprisonment, disease, danger of injuries from weapons. 

सर्वर लभिे मानं गजाश्वं च धनागमम् । 

िाहोििदवशायां च गुिोाः प्रत्यििे जनाः ॥ ३०॥ 

30. Rahu-Jupiter- Reverence everywhere, acquisition of conveyances like elephants etc., gain of wealth. 

बन्धनं जायिे घोिं सुखहातनमवहद्भयम् । 

प्रत्यहं र्ािपीडा च शनेाः प्रत्यििे भर्ेि् ॥ ३१॥ 

31. Rahu-Saturn-Rigorous imprisonment, loss of enjoyments, danger from enemies, affliction with rheumatism. 

सर्वर बहुधा लाभाः िीसङ्गाच्च तर्शेर्षिाः । 

पिदेशभर्ा ससणद्धबुवधप्रत्यििे भर्ेि् ॥ ३२॥ 

32. Rahu-Mercury Gain in all ventures, abnormal, gain through wife. 

# बुणद्धनाशो भयं तर्घ्नो धनहातनमवहद्भयम् । सर्वर कलहोद्वेगौ के िोाः प्रत्यििे फलम् ॥ ३३॥

33. Rahu-Ketu- Loss of intelligence, danger from enemies, obstacles, loss of wealth, quarrels, excitement. 

# योगगनीभ्यो भयं भूयादश्वहातनाः कु भोजनम् । िीनाशाः कु लजं शोकं शुक्रप्रत्यििे भर्ेि् ॥ ३४॥

34. Rahu Venus-Danger from Yogini, danger from the king, loss of conveyances, availability of unpalatable food, loss of wife, sorrow in the family. 

# ज्वििोगो महाभीतिाः पुरपौराद्वदपीडनम् । अल्पमृत्युाः प्रमादि िर्ेाः प्रत्यििे भर्ेि् ॥ ३५॥

35. Rahu-Sun-Danger from enemies, fevers, distress to children, fear of premature death, negligence. 

# उद्वेगकलहो श्रचिा मानहातनमवहद्भयम् । ष्टपिुतर्वकलिा देहे तर्द्योाः िर्ेाः प्रत्यििे भर्ेि् ॥ ३६॥

36. Rahu-Moon-Excitement, quarrels, worries, loss of reputation, fear, distress to father. 

# भगन्दिकृ िा पीडा िक्तष्टपत्तप्रपीडनम् । अथवहातनमवहोद्वेगाः कु जप्रत्यििे फलम् ॥ ३७॥

37. Rahu-Mars- Septic boil in the anus (भगन्दर), distress due to bite and pollution of blood, loss of wealth, excitement.

Effects of the Pratyantar Dasha in the Antardasa of Jupiter 

हेमलाभो धान्यर्ृणद्ध कल्याणं सुफलोदयाः । गुिोििदवशायां च भर्ेद् गुर्वििे फलम् ॥ ३८॥ 

38. Jupiter-Jupiter- Acquisition of gold, increase in wealth etc. 

गोभूतमहयलाभाः स्यात्सर्वर सुखसाधनम् । सङ् ग्रहो ह्यन्नपानादेाः शनेाः प्रत्यििे भर्ेि् ॥ ३९॥ 

39. Jupiter-Saturn-increase in lands, conveyances, grains 

तर्द्यालाभो र्िलाभो ज्ञानलाभाः समौगक्तकाः । सुहृदां सङ्गमाः स्नेहो बुधप्रत्यििे भर्ेि् ॥ ४०॥ 

40. Jupiter-Mercury- Success in educational sphere, acquisition of clothes and gems like pearl etc. visits of friends. 

जलभीतिस्तथा चौयं बन्धनं कलहो भर्ेि् । अपमृत्युभवयं घोिं के िोाः प्रत्यििे द्वद्वज ॥ ४१॥ 

41. Jupiter-Ketu-Danger from water and thieves. 

नानातर्द्याथवसम्प्राब्दप्तहेमर्ितर्भूर्षण 

लभिे क्षेमसिोर्षं भृगोाः प्रत्यििे जनाः ॥ ४२॥ 

42. Jupiter-Venus- Several kinds of learnings, gain of gold, clothes, ornaments, well-being and satisfaction. 

नृपािाभस्तथा तमराब्दत्पिृिो मािृिोऽष्टप र्ा । सर्वर लभिे पूजां िर्ेाः प्रत्यििे जनाः ॥ ४३॥ 

43. Jupiter-Sun-Gain from the king (Government), friends and parents, reverence everywhere. 

सर्वदाःखतर्मोक्षि ु मुक्तलाभो हयस्य च । 

ससद्ध्यन्ति सर्वकायाणण तर्धो प्रत्यििे द्वद्वज ॥ ४४॥ 

44. Jupiter-Moon-No distress, gain of wealth and conveyances, success in ventures. 

शिभीतिगवदे पीडा र्तिमाद्द्यमजीणविा । 

पीडा शरुकृ िा भूरिभौमप्रत्यििे भर्ेि् ॥ ४५॥ 

45. Jupiter-Mars-Danger from weapons, pain in anus, burning in stomach, indigestion, distress from enemies. 

चाण्डालेन तर्िधाः स्याद्भयं िेभ्यो धनक्षतिाः । 

कष्टं जीर्ाििे ज्ञेयं िाहोाः प्रत्यििे ध्रुर्म् ॥ ४६॥ 

46, Jupiter-Rahu-Antagonism with menials (चाण्डालाद्वद) and loss of wealth and distress, through them. 


Antardasa of Saturn



Pratyantar Dasha in the Antardasa of the Saturn


<table><tr><td></td><td>Saturn</td><td>Mercury</td><td>Ketu</td><td>Venu s</td><td>Su n</td><td>Moo n</td><td>Marss</td><td>Rah u</td><td>Jupiter r</td></tr><tr><td>Month</td><td>5</td><td>5</td><td>2</td><td>6</td><td>1</td><td>3</td><td>2</td><td>5</td><td>4</td></tr><tr><td rowspan="2">Days Ghatik a</td><td>21</td><td>3</td><td>3</td><td>0</td><td>24</td><td>0</td><td>3</td><td>12</td><td>24</td></tr><tr><td>28</td><td>25</td><td>10</td><td>30</td><td>9</td><td>15</td><td>10</td><td>27</td><td>24</td></tr><tr><td>Palas</td><td>30</td><td>30</td><td>30</td><td>0</td><td>0</td><td>0</td><td>30</td><td>0</td><td>0</td></tr></table>


Pratyantar Dasha in the Antardasa of the Mercury


<table><tr><td></td><td>Mercury</td><td>Ketu</td><td>Venu s</td><td>Su n</td><td>Moo n</td><td>Mar s</td><td>Rah u</td><td>Jupiter r</td><td>Saturn n</td></tr><tr><td>Month</td><td>4</td><td>1</td><td>5</td><td>1</td><td>2</td><td>1</td><td>4</td><td>4</td><td>5</td></tr><tr><td rowspan="2">Days Ghatik a</td><td>17</td><td>26</td><td>11</td><td>18</td><td>20</td><td>26</td><td>25</td><td>9</td><td>3</td></tr><tr><td>16</td><td>31</td><td>30</td><td>27</td><td>45</td><td>31</td><td>11</td><td>12</td><td>25</td></tr><tr><td>Palas</td><td>30</td><td>30</td><td>0</td><td>0</td><td>0</td><td>30</td><td>0</td><td>0</td><td>30</td></tr></table>

<table><tr><td></td><td>Moo n</td><td>Mar s</td><td>Rah u</td><td>Jupite r</td><td>Satur n</td><td>Mercur y</td><td>Ket u</td><td>Venu s</td><td>Su n</td></tr><tr><td>Month</td><td>1</td><td>1</td><td>2</td><td>2</td><td>3</td><td>2</td><td>1</td><td>3</td><td>0</td></tr><tr><td rowspan="2">Days Ghatik a</td><td>17</td><td>3</td><td>25</td><td>15</td><td>0</td><td>20</td><td>3</td><td>5</td><td>28</td></tr><tr><td>30</td><td>15</td><td>30</td><td>0</td><td>15</td><td>45</td><td>15</td><td>0</td><td>30</td></tr></table>


Pratyantar Dasha in the Antardasa of the Mars


<table><tr><td>Mar</td><td>Rah</td><td>Jupiter</td><td>Satur</td><td>Mercur</td><td>Ket</td><td>Venu</td><td>Su</td><td>Moo</td></tr><tr><td>s</td><td>u</td><td>r</td><td>n</td><td>y</td><td>u</td><td>s</td><td>n</td><td>n</td></tr></table>

<table><tr><td>Month</td><td>0</td><td>1</td><td>1</td><td>2</td><td>1</td><td>0</td><td>2</td><td>0</td><td>1</td></tr><tr><td>Days Ghatik</td><td>23</td><td>29</td><td>23</td><td>3</td><td>26</td><td>23</td><td>6</td><td>19</td><td>3</td></tr><tr><td>a</td><td>16</td><td>51</td><td>12</td><td>10</td><td>31</td><td>16</td><td>30</td><td>57</td><td>15</td></tr><tr><td>Palas</td><td>30</td><td>0</td><td>0</td><td>30</td><td>30</td><td>30</td><td>0</td><td>0</td><td>0</td></tr></table>


Pratyantar Dasha in the Antardasa of the Rahu


<table><tr><td></td><td>Rah u</td><td>Jupiter r</td><td>Satur n</td><td>Mercur y</td><td>Ket u</td><td>Venu s</td><td>Su n</td><td>Moo n</td><td>Mar s</td></tr><tr><td>Month</td><td>5</td><td>4</td><td>5</td><td>4</td><td>1</td><td>5</td><td>1</td><td>2</td><td>1</td></tr><tr><td rowspan="2">Days Ghatik a</td><td>3</td><td>16</td><td>12</td><td>25</td><td>29</td><td>21</td><td>21</td><td>25</td><td>29</td></tr><tr><td>54</td><td>48</td><td>27</td><td>21</td><td>51</td><td>0</td><td>18</td><td>30</td><td>51</td></tr></table>


Pratyantar Dasha in the Antardasa of the Jupiter


<table><tr><td></td><td>Jupiter</td><td>Saturn</td><td>Mercury</td><td>Ketu</td><td>Venu</td><td>Suun</td><td>Moo ns</td><td>Mar u</td></tr><tr><td>Month</td><td>4</td><td>4</td><td>4</td><td>1</td><td>5</td><td>1</td><td>2</td><td>1</td></tr><tr><td>Days</td><td>1</td><td>24</td><td>9</td><td>23</td><td>2</td><td>15</td><td>16</td><td>23</td></tr><tr><td>Ghatik a</td><td>36</td><td>24</td><td>12</td><td>12</td><td>0</td><td>36</td><td>0</td><td>12</td></tr></table>

Effects of Pratyantar Dasha in the Antardasa of Saturn 

देहपीडा कलेभीतिभवयमन्त्यजलोकिाः । 

दाःखं ु शन्यििे नाना शनेाः तत्यििे भर्ेि् ॥ ४७॥ 

47. Saturn-Saturn-Physical distress, quarrels, danger from menials. 

बुणद्धनाशाः कलेभीतििन्नपानाद्वदहातनकृ ि् । 

धन्हातनभवयं शरोाः सनेाः प्रत्यििे बुधे ॥ ४८॥ 

48. Saturn-Mercury-Loss of intelligence, quarrels, dangers, anxiety about availability of food, loss, of wealth, danger from enemy. 

बन्धाः शरोगृवहे जािो र्णवहातनबवहुक्षुधा । 

श्रचत्ते श्रचिा भयं रासाः के िो प्रत्यििे भर्ेि् ॥ ४९॥ 

49. Saturn-Ketu-Imprisonment in the camp of the enemy, loss of lustre, hunger, anxiety and agony. 

श्रचन्तििं फसलिं र्स्तु कल्याणं स्वजने सदा । 

# मनुष्यकृ तििो लाभाः भृगगाः प्रत्यििे द्वद्वज ॥ ५०॥

50. Saturn-Venus- Fulfilment of ambitions, well-being in the family, success in ventures and gains therefrom. 

# िाजिेजोऽथधकारित्वं स्वगृहे जायिे कसलाः । ज्विाद्वदव्याथधपीडा च िर्ेाः प्रत्यििे भर्ेि् ॥ ५१

51. Saturn-Sun-Conferment of authority by the king quarrels in the family, fevers. 

# स्फीिबुणद्धमवहािम्भो मन्दिेजा बहुव्ययाः । बहुिीथभाः समं भोगो तर्धोाः प्रत्यििे शनौ ॥ ५२॥

52. Saturn-Moon-Development of intelligence, inauguration of big venture, loss of lustre, extravagant expenditure, association with many women. 

# िेजोहातन पुरघािो र्तिभीिी रिपोभवयम् । र्ािष्टपत्तकृ िा पीडा कु जप्रत्यििे भर्ेि् ॥ ५३॥

53. Saturn-Mars-Loss of valour, distress to son, danger from fire and enemy, distress from bile and wind. 

# धननाशो र्िहातनभूवतमनाशो भयं भर्ेि् । तर्देशगमनं मृत्युाः िाहो प्रत्यििे शनौ ॥ ५४॥

54. Saturn-Rahu-Loss of wealth, clothes, land, going away to foreign lands, fear of death. 

# गृहेर्षु स्वीकृ िं श्रछद्रं ह्यसमथो तनिीक्षणे । अथ र्ा कसलमुद्वेगं गुिोाः प्रत्यििे र्देि् ॥ ५५॥

55. Saturn-Jupiter-Inability to prevent losses caused by women, quarrels, excitement. 


Antardasa of Mercury Pratyantar Dasha in the Antardasa of the Mercury

Pratyantar Dasha in the Antardasa of the Saturn


<table><tr><td></td><td>Saturn</td><td>Mercury</td><td>Ketu</td><td>Venu s</td><td>Su n</td><td>Moo n</td><td>Marss</td><td>Rah u</td><td>Jupiter r</td></tr><tr><td>Month</td><td>5</td><td>4</td><td>1</td><td>5</td><td>1</td><td>2</td><td>1</td><td>4</td><td>4</td></tr><tr><td rowspan="2">Days Ghatik a</td><td>3</td><td>17</td><td>26</td><td>11</td><td>18</td><td>20</td><td>26</td><td>25</td><td>9</td></tr><tr><td>25</td><td>16</td><td>31</td><td>30</td><td>27</td><td>45</td><td>31</td><td>21</td><td>12</td></tr><tr><td>Palas</td><td>30</td><td>30</td><td>30</td><td>0</td><td>0</td><td>0</td><td>30</td><td>0</td><td>0</td></tr></table>

Effects of Pratyantar Dasha in the Antardasa of Mercury 

बुणद्धतर्वद्याथवलाभो र्ा र्िलाभो महत्सुखम् । बुधास्यािदवशायाञ्च बुधप्रत्यििे भर्ेि् ॥ ५६॥ 

56. Mercury-Mercury- Gain of intelligence, education, wealth, clothes etc. 

कद्वठनान्नस्य सम्प्राब्दप्तरुदिे िोगसम्भर्ाः । कामलं िक्तष्टपत्तं च के िोाः प्रत्यििे भर्ेि् ॥ ५७॥ 

57. Mercury-Ketu- Coarse food, stomach troubles, eye troubles, distress from bilious and blood disorders. 

उत्तिस्यां भर्ेिाभो हातनाः स्यात्तु चिुष्पदाि् । अथधकािो नृपागािे भृगोाः तत्यनििे भर्ेि् ॥ ५८॥ 

58. Mercury-Venus- Gains from the northern direction, loss of cattle, acquisition of authority from Government. 

िेजोहातनभवर्ेद्रोगस्तनुपीडा यदा कदा । 

जायिे श्रचत्तर्ैकल्यं िर्ेाः प्रत्यििे बुधे ॥ ५९॥ 

59. Mercury-Sun- Loss of splendour, distress from diseases, distress in the heart. 

िीलाभिाथवसम्पथत्ताः कन्यालाभो महद्धनम् । 

लभिे सर्विाः सौख्यं तर्धोाः तत्यििे जनाः ॥ ६०॥ 

60. Mercury-Moon- Marriage, gain of wealth and property, birth of a daughter, enjoyments all round. 

धमवधीधनसम्प्राब्दप्तिौिाग्न्याद्वदप्रपीडनम् । 

िक्तर्िं शिघािं भौमप्रत्यििे भर्ेि् ॥ ६१॥ 

61. Mercury-Mars- Religious mindedness, increase in wealth, danger from fire and enemies, gain of red clothes, injury from a weapon. 

कलहो जायिे िीथभिकस्माद्भयसम्भर्ाः । 

िाजशिाकृ िा भीतिाः िाद्वहाः तत्यििे द्वद्वज ॥ ६२॥ 

62. Mercury Rahu--Quarrels, danger from wife or some other woman, danger from the king (Government), 

िाज्यं िाज्याथधकािो र्ा पूजा िाजसमुद्भर्ा । 

तर्द्याबुणद्धसमृणद्धि गुिोाः प्रत्यििे भर्ेि् ॥ ६३॥ 

63. Mercury-Jupiter- Acquisition of a kingdom, conferment of authority by the king, reverence from the king, education, intelligence. 

र्ािष्टपत्तमहापीडा देहघािसमुद्भर्ा । 

धननाशमर्ाप्नोति शनेाः प्रत्यििे जनाः ॥ ६४॥ 

64. Mercury-Saturn-Bilious and windy troubles, injuries to the body, loss of wealth. 


Antardasa of Ketu



Pratyantar Dasha in the Antardasa of the Ketu

Pratyantar Dasha in the Antardasa of the Mercury


<table><tr><td></td><td>Mercury</td><td>Ketu</td><td>Venu s</td><td>Su n</td><td>Moo n</td><td>Mar s</td><td>Rah u</td><td>Jupiter r</td><td>Satur n</td></tr><tr><td>Month</td><td>1</td><td>0</td><td>1</td><td>0</td><td>0</td><td>0</td><td>1</td><td>1</td><td>1</td></tr><tr><td>Days</td><td>20</td><td>20</td><td>29</td><td>17</td><td>29</td><td>20</td><td>23</td><td>17</td><td>26</td></tr><tr><td>Ghatik a</td><td>24</td><td>49</td><td>30</td><td>51</td><td>45</td><td>49</td><td>33</td><td>36</td><td>31</td></tr><tr><td>Palas</td><td>30</td><td>30</td><td>0</td><td>0</td><td>0</td><td>30</td><td>0</td><td>0</td><td>30</td></tr></table>

Effects of Pratyantar Dasha in the Antardasa of Ketu 

आपत्समुद्भर्ोऽकस्माद्देशििसमागमाः । 

के त्वििेऽथवहातनि के िोाः प्रत्यििे भर्ेि् ॥ ६५॥ 

65. Ketu-Ketu-Sudden disaster, going away to foreign lands, loss of wealth. 

म्लेच्छभीिथवनाशो र्ा नेरिोगाः सशिोव्यथा । 

हातनििुष्पदानां च भृगोाः प्रत्यििे भर्ेि् ॥ ६६॥ 

66. Ketu-Venus-Loss of wealth through a non-Hindu king, eye troubles, headache, loss of cattle. 

तमरैाः सह तर्िोधि स्वल्पमृत्युाः पिाजयाः । 

मतिभ्रंशो तर्र्ादि िर्ेाः तत्यििे भर्ेि् ॥ ६७॥ 

67. Ketu-Sun-Antagonism with friends, premature death, defeat, exchange of arguments. 

अन्ननाशो यशोहातनदेहपीडा मतिभ्रमाः । 

आमर्ािाद्वदर्ृणद्धितर्धोाः तत्यििे भर्ेि् ॥ ६८॥ 

68. Ketu-Moon-Loss of grains, physical distress, misunderstanding, dysentery. 

शिघािेन पािेन पीष्टडिो र्तिपीडया । 

नीचाद्भीिी रिपोाः शङ्का कु जप्रत्यििे भर्ेि् ॥ ६९॥ 

69. Ketu-Mars-Injury from weapons, distress from fire, danger from menials and enemies. 

कातमनीभ्यो भयं भूयात्तथा र्ैरिसमुद्भर्ाः । 

क्षुद्रादष्टप भर्ेद्भीिी िाहोाः प्रत्यििे भर्ेि् ॥ ७०॥ 

70. Ketu-Rahu-Danger from women and enemies, distress caused by menials. 

धनहातनमवहोत्पािो स/ितमरतर्नाशनम् । 

सर्वर लभिे क्लेशं गुिोाः प्रत्यििे फलम् ॥ ७१॥ 

71. Ketu-Jupiter-Loss of friends, wealth and garments, opribrium in the house, troubles from everywhere. 

गोमद्वहष्याद्वदमिणं देहपीडा सुहृद्वधाः । 

स्वल्पाल्पलाभकिणं शनेाः प्रत्यििे फलम् ॥ ७२॥ 

72. Ketu-Saturn- Death of cattle and friends, physical distress, very meagre gain of wealth. 

बुणद्धनाशो महोद्वेगो तर्द्याहातनमवहाभयम् । 

कायवससणद्धनव जायिे ज्ञस्य प्रत्यििे फलम् ॥ ७३॥ 

73. Ketu-Mercury-Loss of understanding, excitement, failure in education, dangers, failure in all ventures. 

Antardasa of Venus 

Pratyantar Dasha in the Antardasa of the Venus 

Venu Su Moo Mar Rah Jupite Satur Mercur Ket s n n s u r n y u
