Pratyantar Dasha in the Antardasa of the Ketu


<table><tr><td></td><td>Ket u</td><td>Venu s</td><td>Su n</td><td>Moo n</td><td>Mar s</td><td>Rah u</td><td>Jupiter r</td><td>Satur n</td><td>Mercur y</td></tr><tr><td>Month</td><td>0</td><td>2</td><td>0</td><td>1</td><td>0</td><td>2</td><td>1</td><td>2</td><td>1</td></tr><tr><td rowspan="2">Days Ghatik a</td><td>24</td><td>10</td><td>21</td><td>5</td><td>24</td><td>3</td><td>25</td><td>6</td><td>29</td></tr><tr><td>30</td><td>0</td><td>0</td><td>0</td><td>30</td><td>0</td><td>0</td><td>30</td><td>30</td></tr></table>

Effects of the Pratyantar Dasha in the Antardasa of Venus 

श्वेिाश्वर्िमुक्ताद्यं द्वदव्यिीजङ्गजं सुखम् । 

लभिे शुक्रििे प्राप्ते शुक्रप्रत्यििे जनाः ॥ ७४॥ 

74. Venus-Venus- Gains of white clothes, conveyances, gems like pearls etc., association with beautiful damsel. 

र्ािज्विाः सशिाःपीडा िाज्ञाः पीडा रिपोिष्टप । 

जायिे स्वल्पलाभोऽष्टप िर्ेाः प्रत्यििे फलम् ॥ ७५॥ 

75. Venus-Sun- Rheumatic fever, headache, danger from the king and enemies and meagre gain of wealth. 

कन्याजन्म नृपािाभो र्िाभिणसंयुिाः । 

िाज्याथधकािसम्प्राब्दप्ताः चन्द्रप्रत्यििे भर्ेि् ॥ ७६॥ 

76. Venus-Moon- Birth of a daughter, gain of clothes etc. from the king, acquisition of authority. 

िक्तष्टपत्ताद्वदिोगि कलहस्ताडनं भर्ेि् । 

महान्द्रक्लेशो भर्ेदि कु जप्रत्यििे द्वद्वज ॥ ७७॥ 

77. Venus-Mars- Blood and bile troubles, quarrels, many kinds of distresses. 

कलहो जायिे िीथभिकस्माद्भयसम्भर्ाः । 

िाजिाः शरुिाः पीडा िाहोाः प्रत्यििे भर्ेि् ॥ ७८॥ 

78. Venus-Rahu-Quarrels with wife, danger, distress from the king and enemies. 

महदद्रव्यं ् महद्राज्यं र्चत्र्प्मुक्ताद्वदभूर्षणम् । 

गजाश्वाद्वदपदप्राब्दप्ताः गुिोाः प्रत्यििे भर्ेि् ॥ ७९॥ 

79. Venus-Jupiter- Acquisition of kingdom, wealth, garments, gems, ornaments and conveyance like elephants etc. 

खिोष्टर छागसम्प्राब्दप्तलोहमार्षतिलाद्वदकम् । 

लभिे स्वल्पपीडाद्वद शनेाः प्रत्यििे जनाः ॥ ८०॥ 

80. Venus-Saturn-Acquisition of donkey, camel, goat, iron, grains, sesame seeds, physical pains 

धनज्ञानमहिाभो िाजिाज्याद्वदकारििा । 

तनक्षेपाद्धनलाभोऽष्टप ज्ञस्य प्रत्यििे भर्ेि् ॥ ८१॥ 

81. Venus-Mercury- Gains of wealth, knowledge, authority from the king, gain of money distributed by others-

अपमृत्युभयं ज्ञेयं देशाद्देशाििागमाः । 

लाभोऽष्टप जायिे मध्ये के िोाः प्रत्यििे द्वद्वज ॥ ८२॥ 

82. Venus-Ketu-Premature death, going away from homeland, gains of wealth at times. 

# अथ सूक्ष्मान्तदिशाध्यायः ॥ ६२॥

# Chapter 62. Effects of the Sookshma-Antardasa in the Pratyantar Dasha of the Various Planets

गुण्या स्वस्वदशार्र्षैाः प्रत्यििदशातमतिाः । 

खाक्रै भक्ता पृथग्लन्तब्धाः सूक्ष्माििदशा भर्ेि् ॥ १॥ 

1. The Sookshma Antardasa is arrived at by multiplying the periods of Pratyantar Dasha separately for each planet by the Dasha years of that planets and then by dividing the product by 120. 

Example: Suppose we have to find out Sookshma-Antardasa of the Sun, in his own Dasha, in his Antardasa and in his Pratyantar Dasha. Dasha period of the Sun is 6 years, Pratyantar Dasha is 5/24 (5 days 24 Ghatikas) or 324 Ghatikas. The Sookshma-Antardasa will be $3 2 4 \times 6 = 1 9 4 4 \div 1 2 0$ 16 Ghatikas and 12 palas. The Sookshma-Antardasa of other planets may be calculated in the same manner. 

Sookshma Dasha in the Pratyantar Dasha of the Sun 

<table><tr><td></td><td>SN</td><td>MN</td><td>MRS</td><td>RH</td><td>JUP</td><td>SAT</td><td>MCY</td><td>KT</td><td>VEN</td></tr><tr><td>Ghatika</td><td>16</td><td>27</td><td>18</td><td>48</td><td>43</td><td>51</td><td>45</td><td>18</td><td>54</td></tr><tr><td>Palas</td><td>12</td><td>0</td><td>54</td><td>36</td><td>12</td><td>18</td><td>54</td><td>54</td><td>0</td></tr></table>

# Pratyantar Dasha of the Sun

तनजभूतमपरित्यागो प्राणनाशभयं भर्ेि् । 

िाननाशो महाहातनाः तनजसूक्ष्मगिे िर्ौ ॥ २॥ 

2. Sun-Sun- (This means Sookshma Dasha of the Sun in his Pratyantar Dasha of the Sun)-going away from homeland, danger of death, loss of position, losses all round. 

देर्ब्राह्म्भगक्ति तनत्यकमवििस्तथा । 

सुप्रीतिाः सर्वतमरिैर् िर्ेाः सूक्ष्मगिे तर्धौ ॥ ३॥ 

3. Sun-Moon-Devotion toward deities and Brahmins, interest in pious deeds, affectionate relations with friends. 

क्रू िकमवितिस्तस्तग्मशरुथभाः परिपीडनम् । 

िक्तस्रार्ाद्वदिोगि िर्ेाः सूक्ष्मगिे कु जे ॥ ४॥ 

4. Sun-Mars-Indulgence in sinful deeds, distress from cruel enemies, bleeding. 

चौिागग्नतर्र्षभीतिि िणे भङ्गाः पिाजयाः । 

दानधमाद्वदहीनि िर्ेाः सूक्ष्मगिे ह्यगौ ॥ ५॥ 

5. Sun-Rahu-Danger from thieves, fire and poison, defeat in war, religious inclination. 

नृपसत्काििाजाहवाः सेर्कै ाः परिपूसजिाः । 

िाजचक्षुगविाः शािाः सूयवसूक्ष्मगिे गुिौ ॥ ६॥ 

6. Sun-Jupiter-Recognition by government, respected by government employees, becoming favourite of the king. 

चौयवसाहसकमाथं देर्ब्राह्मणपीडनम् । 

िानच्युतिं मनोदखं ु िर्ेाः सूक्ष्मगिे शनौ ॥ ७॥ 

7. Sun-Saturn---Causing trouble to respected persons and Brahmins by theft and other bold deeds, going away from one's own place, mental agony. 

द्वदव्याम्बिाद्वदलन्तब्धि द्वदव्यिीपरिभोगगिा । 

अश्रचन्तििाथवससणद्धि िर्ेाः सूक्ष्मगिे बुधे ॥ ८॥ 

8. Sun-Mercury-Gains of fancy garments, association with a beautiful damsel, sudden success in ventures. 

गुरुिाथवतर्नाशि भृत्यदािभर्स्तथा । 

क्वश्रचत्सेर्कसम्बन्धो िर्ेाः सूक्ष्मगिे र्ध्जे ॥ ९॥ 

9. Sun-Ketu-Achievement of glory through wife and employees, loss of wealth, comforts from servants. 

पुरतमरकलराद्वदसाख्यसम्पन्न एर् च । 

नानातर्धा च सम्पत्ती िर्ेाः सूक्ष्मगिे भृगौ ॥ १०॥ 

10. Sun-Venus-Happiness from son, friends, wife, acquisition of many kinds of properties. 

Pratyantar Dasha of the Moon 

भूर्षणं भूतमलाभि सम्मानं नृपपूजनम् । 

# िामसत्त्वं गुरुत्वं च तनजसूक्ष्मगिे तर्धौ ॥ ११॥

11. Moon-Moon-Gain of ornaments and land, reverence, recognition from the king, anger glory. 

दाःखं ु शरुतर्िोधि कु सक्षिोगाः ष्टपिुमृवतिाः । र्ािष्टपत्तकफोद्रेकाः तर्धोाः सूक्ष्मगिे कु जे ॥ १२॥ 

12. Moon-Mars -Distress, antagonism with the enemy, stomach troubles, death of father, troubles due to imbalance of wind, bile and phlegm. 

क्रोधनं तमरबन्धूनां देशत्यागो धनक्षयाः । तर्देशागन्नगडप्राब्दप्ततर्वधोाः सूक्ष्मगिेप्यगौ ॥ १३॥ 

13. Moon-Rahu-Disharmony with friends and kinsmen, going away from homeland, loss of wealth, imprisonment. 

छरचामिसंयुक्तं र्ैभर्ं पुरसम्पदाः । सर्वर सुखमाप्नोति तर्धोाः सूक्ष्मगिे गुिौ ॥ १४॥ 

14. Moon-Jupiter- Opulence and glory with Royal symbols, birth of a son, gain of property, enjoyments all round. 

िाजोपद्रर्भीतिाः स्याद्व्यर्हािे धनक्षयाः । चौिर्ं तर्प्रभीतिि तर्धोाः सूक्ष्मगिे शनौ ॥ १५॥ 

15. Moon-Saturn- Wrath of the king, loss of wealth in business dealings, danger from thieves and Brahmins. 

िाजमानं र्स्तुलाभो तर्देशाद्वाहनाद्वदकम् । पुरपौत्र्प्समृणद्धि तर्धोाः सूक्ष्मगिे बुधे ॥ १६॥ 

16. Moon-Mercury-Reverence from king, gain of wealth, gain of conveyance from a foreign land, increase in the number of children. 

आत्मनो र्ृथत्तहननं सस्यशृङ्गर्ृर्षाद्वदथभाः । अगग्नसूयाद्वदभीतिाः स्याद्वद्वधोाः सूक्ष्मगिे र्ध्जे ॥ १७॥ 

17. Moon-Ketu- Loss in the livelihood earned by sale etc. grains, medicines, cattle etc., danger from fire and Sun's rays (Sun-stroke). 

तर्र्ाहो भूतमलाभि र्िाभिणर्ैभर्म् । िाज्यलाभि कीतिवि तर्धोाः सूक्ष्मगिे भृगौ ॥ १८॥ 

18. Moon-Venus- Marriage, gain of a kingdom, land, garments, ornaments, reputation etc. 

क्लेशारक्लेशाः कायवनाशाः पशुधान्यधनक्षयाः । 

गारर्ैर्षम्यभूतमि तर्धोाः सूक्ष्मगिे िर्ौ ॥ १९॥ 

19. Moon-Sun-Troubles, losses in ventures, destruction of grains and cattle, physical distress. 

Pratyantar Dasha of Mars 

भूतमहातनमवनाःखेदो ह्यपस्मािी च बन्धुयुक् । 

पुिोक्षोभमनस्तापो तनजसूक्ष्मगिे कु जे ॥ २०॥ 

20. Mars-Mars-Sorrows on account of loss of lands, epilepsy imprisonment, unhappiness. 

अङ्गदोर्षो जनाद्भीतिाः प्रमदार्ंशनाशनम् । 

र्तिसपवभयं घोिं भौमे सूक्ष्मगिेऽप्यहौ ॥ २१॥ 

21. Mars-Rahu-Physical distress, danger from the people due to unpopularity, loss of wife and children, danger from fire. 

देर्पूजाितििार मन्त्राभ्युत्थानित्पिाः । 

लोके पूजा प्रमोदि भौमे सूक्ष्मगिे गुिौ ॥ २२॥ 

22. Mars-Jupiter- Devotion towards deities, Mantra siddhi, reverence from the people (popularity), enjoyments. 

बन्धनान्मुच्यिे बद्धो धनधान्यपरिच्छदाः । 

भृत्याथवबहुलाः िीमान् भौमे सूक्ष्मगिे शनौ ॥ २३॥ 

23. Mars-Saturn-Release from imprisonment, happiness on account of wealth, grains, clothes and servants. 

र्ाहनं छारसंयुक्तं िाज्यभोगपिं सुखम् । 

कामश्वासाद्वदका पीडा भौमे सूक्ष्मगिे बुधे ॥ २४॥ 

24. Mars-Mercury-Comforts of Chhatra (छि), Chamar (चामर) etc. (receiving respect as that of a king), breathing troubles. 

पिप्रेतििबुणद्धि सर्वराऽष्टप च गद्वहविा । 

अशुश्रचाः सर्वकालेर्षु भौमे सूक्ष्मगिे र्ध्जे ॥ २५॥ 

25. Mars-Ketu- Indulgence in undesirable deeds at the instance of others, always remains filthy. 

इष्टिीभोगसम्पथत्तरिष्टभोजनसङ् ग्रहाः । इष्टाथवस्याष्टप लाभि भौमे सूक्ष्मगिे भृगौ ॥ २६॥ 

26. Mars-Venus-Enjoyment with women of choice, gains wealth, food etc. 

िाजद्वेर्षो द्वद्वजारक्लेशाः कायाथभप्रयर्ञ्चकाः । लोके ऽष्टप तनन्द्रद्यिामेति भौमे सूक्ष्मगिे िर्ौ ॥ २७॥ 

27, Mars-Sun- Wrath of the king, distress through Brahmins, failure in ventures, odium in public (लोक तनन्दा). 

शुद्धत्वं धनसम्प्राब्दप्तदेर्भाह्मण्वत्सलाः । व्याथधना परिभूयेि् भौमे सूक्ष्मगिे तर्धौ ॥ २८॥ 

28. Mars-Moon-Piousness, gain of wealth, devotion towards deities and Brahmins, danger from diseases. Pratyantar Dasha of Rahu 

लोकोपद्रर्बुणद्धि सर्वकाये मतितर्भ्रमाः । शून्यिा श्रचत्तदोर्षाः स्याि् स्वीये सूक्ष्मगिेऽप्यगौ ॥ २९॥ 

29. Rahu-Rahu-Tendering to create turbulence by people, lack of wisdom in performance of duties, affliction of, the mind. 

दीघविोगी दरिद्रि सर्ेर्षां ष्टप्रयदशवनाः । दानधमवििाः शस्तो िाहोाः सूक्ष्मगिे गुिौ ॥ ३०॥ 

30. Rahu-Jupiter- Affliction with a chronic disease, poverty but revered by the people and the religious mindedness. 

कु मागात्कु स्थत्सिोथवि दष्टिु पिसेर्काः । असत्सङ्गमतिमूवढो िाहोाः सूक्ष्मगिे शनौ ॥ ३१॥ 

31. Rahu-Saturn- Gain of wealth through unfair means, wicked or mean nature, performing other person’s duties, undesirable association. 

िीसम्भोगमतिर्ाग्मी लोकसम्भार्नार्ृिाः । अन्नतमच्छंस्तनुग्लानी िाहोाः सूक्ष्मगिे बुधे ॥ ३२॥ 

32. Rahu-Mercury-Increase in desires for sexual acts with women, eloquence, hunger, physical distress. 

माधुयं मानहातनि बन्धनं चाप्रमाकिम् । पारुष्यं जीर्हातनि िाहोाः सूक्ष्मगिे र्ध्जे ॥ ३३॥ 

33. Rahu-Ketu-politeness, Loss of reputation, imprisonment, cold heartedness, loss of public money. 

बन्धनान्मुच्यिे बद्धाः िानमानाथवसञ्चयाः । कािणाद् द्रव्यलाभि िाहौ सूक्ष्मगिे भृगौ ॥ ३४॥ 

34. Rahu-Venus-Freedom from imprisonment, gain of position and wealth. 

व्यक्ताशो गुल्मिोगि क्रोधहातनस्तथैर् च । र्ाहनाद्वदसुखं सर्ं िाहोाः सूक्ष्मगिे िर्ौ ॥ ३५॥ 

35. Rahu-Sun - Settling down in foreign lands, affliction with Gulma (enlargement of skin), even temperament comfort of conveyances. 

मणणित्नधनर्ाब्दप्ततर्वद्योपासनशीलर्ान् । देर्ाचवनपिो भक्त्या िाहोाः सूक्ष्मगिे तर्धौ ॥ ३६॥ 

36. Rahu-Moon- Gain of gems (Mani), wealth, education, attachment to prayers, good behaviour and devotion towards deities. 

तनसजविे जनतर्द्रार्ो जने क्रोधि बन्धनम् । चौयवशीलितितनवत्यं िाहोाः सूक्ष्मगिे कु जे ॥ ३७॥ 

37. Rahu-Mars- Fleeing after defeat, anger, imprisonment, indulgence in thefts and stealing. 

Effects in the Sookshma Dasha in the Pratyantar Dasha of Jupiter 

शोकनाशो धनाथधक्यमगग्नहोरं सशर्ाचवनम् । र्ाहनं छरसंयुक्तं स्वीये सूक्ष्मगिे गुिौ ॥ ३८॥ 

38. Jupiter-Jupiter-Banishment of sorrows, increase in wealth, performing Havana, devotion to lord Shiva, gains of conveyance, marked with royal symbols. 

व्रिभङ्गो मनस्तापो तर्देशे र्सुनाशनम् । तर्िोधो बन्धुर्ैगवि गुिोाः सूक्ष्मगिे शनौ ॥ ३९॥ 

39. Jupiter-Saturn- Obstacles in fasting, agony, foreign, journeys, loss of wealth, antagonism with kinsmen. 

तर्द्याबुणद्धतर्र्ृणद्धि ससम्मानं धनागमाः । गृहे सर्वतर्धं सौख्यं गुिोाः सूक्ष्मगिे बुधे ॥ ४०॥ 

40. Jupiter-Mercury- Success in Education, increase in intelligence, reverence from the people (popularity), gains of wealth, all sorts of enjoyments and comforts at home. 

# ज्ञानं तर्भर्पाण्डण्डत्ये शाििोिा सशर्ाचवनम् । अगग्नहोरं गुिोभवगक्तगुविोाः सूक्ष्मगिे र्ध्जे ॥ ४१॥

41. Jupiter-Ketu-Knowledge, glory, learning, study of Shastas, worship of Lord Shiva, Havana, devotion towards preceptor. 

िोगान्मुगक्ताः सुखं भोगो धनधान्यसमागमाः । पुरदािाद्वदसौख्यं च गुिोाः सूक्ष्मगिे भृगौ ॥ ४२॥ 

42. Jupiter-Venus- Recovery from diseases, enjoyments, gain of wealth, happiness from wife and children. 

र्ािष्टपत्तप्रकोपि श्लेष्मोद्रेकस्तु दारुणाः । िसव्याद्वदकृ िं शूलं गुिोाः सूक्ष्मगिे िर्ौ ॥ ४३॥ 

43. Jupiter-Sun - Troubles of wind and bile, stomach pains through imbalance of phlegm and Rasas. 

छरचामिसंयुक्तं र्ैभर्ं पुरसम्पदाः । नेरकु सक्षगिा पीडा गुिोाः सूक्ष्मगिे तर्धौ ॥ ४४॥ 

44. Jupiter-Moon- Glory with Umbrella with Royal symbols, celebrations on the birth of a son, distress in eyes and stomach. 

स्र्िीजनाच्च तर्र्षोत्पथत्तबवन्धनं च रुजोभयम् । देशाििगमो भ्रान्तिगुविोाः सूक्ष्मगिे कु जे ॥ ४५॥ 

45. Jupiter-Mars- Administration of poison by wife, imprisonment, danger from diseases, going away to foreign lands, confusion and misunderstandings. 

व्याथधथभाः परिभूिाःस्याच्चौिैिपहृिं धनम् । सपवर्ृसिकभीतिि गुिोाः सूक्ष्मगिेऽप्यगौ ॥ ४६॥ 

46. Jupiter-Rahu-Danger from thieves, snakes and Scorpios, diseases and distresses. 

Pratyantar Dasha of Saturn 

धनहातनमवहाव्याथधाः र्ािपीडा कु लक्षयाः । थभन्नाहािी महादाःखीु तनजसूक्ष्मगिे शनौ ॥ ४७॥ 

47. Saturn-Saturn - Loss of wealth, diseases like rheumatism etc., destruction of the family, taking meals separately from family, full of sorrows. 

र्ाणणज्यर्ृत्तेलाभि तर्द्यातर्भर्मेर् च । 

# िीलाभि महीप्राब्दप्ताः शनेाः सूक्ष्मगिे बुधे ॥ ४८॥

48. Saturn-Mercury- Profits in business, progress in education, increase in wealth and lands. 

चौिोपद्रर्कु ष्ठाद्वदर्ृथत्तक्षयतर्गुम्फनम् । सर्ाङ्गपीडनं व्याथधाः शनेाः सूक्ष्मगिे र्ध्जे ॥ ४९॥ 

49. Saturn-Ketu-Turbulence by thieves, leprosy, loss of livelihood, physical pains. 

ऐश्वयवमायुधाभ्यासाः पुरलाभोऽथभर्षेचनम् । आिोग्यं धनकामौ च शनेाः सूक्ष्मगिे भृगौ ॥ ५०॥ 

50. Saturn-Venus-Opulence and glory, learning use of weapons, birth of a son, coronation, good health and fulfilment of all ambitions. 

िाजिेजोतर्काित्वं स्वगृहे जायिे कसलाः । ष्टकथञ्चत्पीडा स्वदेहोत्था शनेाः सूक्ष्मगिे िर्ौ ॥ ५१॥ 

51. Saturn-Sun-Wrath of the king, quarrels in the family, physical distress. 

स्फीिबुणद्धमवहािम्भो मन्दिेजा बहुव्ययाः । िीपुरैि समं सौख्यं शनेाः सूक्ष्मगिे तर्धौ ॥ ५२॥ 

52. Saturn-Moon - Development of intelligence, inauguration of a big project, loss of lustre, extravagance, happiness from wife and children. 

िेजोहातनमवहोद्वेगो र्तिमान्द्रद्यं भ्रमाः कसलाः । र्ािष्टपत्तकृ िा पीडा शनेाः सूक्ष्मगिे कु जे ॥ ५३॥ 

53. Saturn-Mars-Loss of lustre, excitement, burning in the stomach, misunderstanding, quarrels, wind and bile disorders. 

ष्टपिृमािृतर्नाशि मनोदाःखं ु गुरुव्ययम् । सर्वर तर्फलत्वं च शनेाः सूक्ष्मगिेऽप्यहौ ॥ ५४॥ 

54. Saturn-Rahu-Death' of parents, agony, extravagance, failure in ventures. 

सन्मुद्राभोगसम्मानं धनधान्यतर्र्द्धवनम् । छरचामिसम्प्राब्दप्ताः शनेाः सूक्ष्मगिे गुिौ ॥ ५५॥ 

55. Saturn-Jupiter-Acquisition of gold coins, reverence from the public (popularity), increase in wealth and grains, acquisition of Chhatra (छि) with royal symbol. 

# Pratyantar Dasha of Mercury

सौभाग्यं िाजसम्मानं धनधान्याद्वदसम्पदाः । 

सर्ेर्षां ष्टप्रयदशी च तनजसूक्ष्मगिे बुधे ॥ ५६॥ 

56. Mercury-Mercury- Dawn of fortune, reverence from the king, increase in wealth and property and affectionate relation with all. 

बालग्रहोगग्नभीस्तापाः िीगदोद्भर्दोर्षभाक् । 

कु मागी कु स्थत्सिाशी च बौधे सूक्ष्मगिे र्ध्जे ॥ ५७॥ 

57. Mercury-Ketu-Danger from fire, agony, distress to wife, coarse food and immoral tendencies. 

र्ाहनं धनसम्पथत्तजवलजान्नाथवसम्भर्ाः । 

शुभकीतिवमवहाभोगो बौधे सूक्ष्मगिे भृगौ ॥ ५८॥ 

58. Mercury-Venus- Gain of conveyances, wealth, grains, produced in water, good repute and enjoyments. 

िाडनं नृपर्ैर्षम्यं बुणद्धस्खलनिोगभाक् । 

हातनजवनापर्ादं च बौधे सूक्ष्मगिे िर्ौ ॥ ५९॥ 

59. Mercury-Sun- Injuries, wrath of the king, confusion in mind, diseases, loss of wealth, ridicule in public. 

सुभगाः स्थििबुणद्धि िाजसन्मानसम्पदाः । 

सुहृदां गुरुसञ्चािो बौधे सूक्ष्मगिे तर्धौ ॥ ६०॥ 

60. Mercury-Moon- Good fortune, stability of mind, reverence from the king, gains of property, visits of friends and the preceptor. 

अगग्नदाहो तर्र्षोत्पथत्तजवडत्वं च दरिद्रिा । 

तर्भ्रमि महोद्वेगो बौधे सूक्ष्मगिे कु जे ॥ ६१॥ 

61. Mercury-Mars-Danger from fire and poison, idiocy, poverty, confusion of mind, excitement. 

अगग्नसपवनृपाद्भीतिाः कु च्छर ाद्वदरिपिाभर्ाः । 

भूिार्ेशभ्रमादभ्रान्तिबौधे ् सूक्ष्मगिेप्यहौ ॥ ६२॥ 

62. Mercury-Rahu-Danger from fire, snakes and the victory over enemy with difficulty, opprobrium from goblins. 

गृहोपकिणं भव्यं दानं भोगाद्वदर्ैभर्म् । 

# िाजप्रसादसम्पथत्तबौधे सूक्ष्मगिे गुिौ ॥ ६३॥

63. Mercury-Jupiter- Construction of a house, interest in charities, comforts and enjoyments, increase in opulence, gain of wealth from the king. 

र्ाणणज्यर्ृथत्तलाभि तर्द्यातर्भर्मेर् च । िीलाभि महाव्याब्दप्तबौधे सूक्ष्मगिे शनौ ॥ ६४॥ 

64. Mercury-Saturn-Profits in business, progress in education and increase in wealth, marriage, circumbience or comprehensiveness. 

Pratyantar Dasha of Ketu 

पुरदािाद्वदजं दाःखंु गारर्ैर्षम्यमेर् च । दारिद्र्याद् थभक्षुर्ृथत्ति नैजे सूक्ष्मगिे र्ध्जे ॥ ६५॥ 

65. Ketu-Ketu-Happiness from wife and children, physical troubles, poverty, begging. 

िोगनाशऽथवलाभि गुरुतर्प्रानुर्त्सलाः । सङ्गमाः स्वजनैाः साद्धवके िोाः सूक्ष्मगिे भृगौ ॥ ६६॥ 

66. Ketu-Venus- Freedom from diseases, gains of wealth, devotion towards Brahmins and the- preceptor, union with members of the family. 

युद्धं भूतमतर्नाशि तर्प्रर्ासाः स्वदेशिाः । सुहृद्वद्वपातििातिवि के िोाः सूक्ष्मगिे िर्ौ ॥ ६७॥ 

67. Ketu-San-Quarrels, loss of land, residence in foreign lands, disaster upon friends. 

दासीदाससमृणद्धि युद्धे लन्तब्धजवयस्तथा । लसलिा कीतिवरुत्पन्ना के िोाः सूक्ष्मगिे तर्धौ ॥ ६८॥ 

68. Ketu-Moon Promotion in service, victory in war, good reputation in public (popularity). 

आसने भयमश्वादेिौिदष्टाद्वदपीडनम् ु । गुल्मपीडा सशिोिोगाः के िोाः सूक्ष्मगिे कु जे ॥ ६९॥ 

69. Ketu-Mars-Danger of falling down from horse etc., distress from thieves and the wicked, suffering from Gulma and headache. 

तर्नाशाः िीगुरूणां च दष्टिीसङ्गमािघुाः ु । र्मनं रुथधिं ष्टपत्तं के िोाः सूक्ष्मगिेऽप्यगौ ॥ ७०॥ 

70. Ketu-Rahu- Destruction of wife, father etc., defamation due to association with a wicked woman, vomiting, blood pollution, bilious diseases. 

रिपोतर्विोधाः सम्पथत्ताः सहसा िाजर्ैभर्म् । पशुक्षेरतर्नाशातिवाः के िोाः सूक्ष्मगिे गुिौ ॥ ७१॥ 

71. Ketu-Jupiter-Antagonism with the enemy, increase in property and opulence, distress due to losses in cattle wealth and agricultural production. 

मृर्षा पीडा भर्ेत्क्षुद्रमुखोत्पथत्ति लङ् घनम् । िीतर्िोधाः सत्यहातनाः के िोाः सूक्ष्मगिे शनौ ॥ ७२॥ 

72. Ketu-Saturn-Imaginary distress, little comfort, fasting, antagonism with wife, indulgence in falsehood. 

नानातर्धजनाब्दप्ति तर्प्रयोगोऽरिपीडनम् । अथवसम्पत्समृणद्धि के िोाः सूक्ष्मगिे बुधे ॥ ७३॥ 

73. Ketu-Mercury- Union and separation from many kinds of people, distress to enemy, increase in wealth and property. 

Pratyantar Dasha of Venus 

शरुहातनमवहत्सौख्यं शङ्किालयतनतमवतिाः । िडागकू पतनमाणं तनजसूक्ष्मगिे भृगौ ॥ ७४॥ 

74. Venus-Venus-Destruction of enemies, enjoyments, construction of temples of lord Shiva etc., and reservoirs. 

उिस्तापो भ्रमिैर् गिागितर्चेष्टष्टिम् । क्वश्रचिाभाः क्वश्रचद्धातनभृवगोाः सूक्ष्मगिे िर्ौ ॥ ७५॥ 

75. Venus-Sun-Agony in mind and heart, confusion of mind, wanderings, both losses and gains at different times. 

आिोग्यं धनसम्पाथत्ताः कायवलाभो गिागिैाः । बुणद्धतर्द्यातर्र्ृणद्धाः स्याद् भृगोाः सूक्ष्मगिे तर्धौ ॥ ७६॥ 

76. Venus-Moon-Sound health, increase in wealth, success in ventures through business dealings, progress in education and increase of intelligence. 

जडत्वं रिपुर्ैर्षम्यं देशभ्रंशो महद्भयम् । व्याथधदाःखसमृत्पथत्तभृवगोाः ु सूक्ष्मगिे कु जे ॥ ७७॥ 

77. Venus-Mars-Idiocy, danger from enemy, going away. From homeland, danger from diseases. 

िाज्यागग्नसपवजा भीतिबवन्धुनाशो गुरुव्यथा । 

िानच्युतिमवहाभीतिभृवगोाः सूक्ष्मगिेऽप्यहौ ॥ ७८॥ 

78. Venus-Rahu- Danger from fire and snakes, destruction of kinsmen, resignation from position (service etc.). 

सर्वर कायवलाभि क्षेराथवतर्भर्ोन्नतिाः । 

र्णणग्वृत्तेमवहालन्तब्धभृवगोाः सूक्ष्मगिे गुिौ ॥ ७९॥ 

79. Venus-Jupiter- Success in ventures, increase in wealth and agricultural production, abnormal profits from purchase and sale business. 

शरुपीडा महद्दाःखं ु चिुष्पादतर्नाशनम् । 

स्वगोरगुरुहातनाः स्याद् भृगोाः सूक्ष्मगिे शनौ ॥ ८०॥ 

80. Venus-Saturn- Distress from enemy, sorrows, destruction of cattle, loss of persons belonging to the gotra (गोि) of the native and elders (or preceptors). 

बा्धर्ाद्वदर्षु सम्पथत्तव्यवर्हािो धनोन्नतिाः । 

पुरदािाद्वदिाः सौख्यं भृगोाः सूक्ष्मगिे बुधे ॥ ८१॥ 

81. Venus-Mercury- Increase in wealth with the assistance of kinsmen, gain of wealth through business, happiness from wife and children. 

अगग्निोगो महापीडा मुखनेरसशिोव्यथा । 

सथञ्चिाथात्मनाः पीडा भृगोाः सूक्ष्मगिे र्ध्जे ॥ ८२॥ 

82. Venus-Ketu-Danger from fire, distress from diseases, distress in mouth, eyes and forehead, loss of accumulated wealth, mental agony. 

Notes: It will be noted from the description of effects in Sookshma Dasha that generally, the effects of Sookshma Dasha of malefic in the Pratyantar Dasha of benefices are not favourable and those of benefices in the Pratyantar Dasha of malefic are favourable. If the Pratyantar Dasha and Sookshma Dasha both are favourable, there will be special auspiciousness in effects and if the both are unfavourable, there will be more inauspiciousness in effects. 

# अथ प्राणदशाफलाध्यायः ॥ ६३॥

# Chapter 63. Effects of Prana Dasha in the Sookshma Dasha of the various planets

पृथक् खगदशार्र्षैहवन्याि् सूक्ष्मदशातमतिम् । 

खसूयैतर्वभजेल्लिब्धज्ञेय प्राणदशातमतिाः ॥ १॥ 

1. If we multiply the Sookshma Dasha spans by the Dasha years of each planet and divide the product by 120, we will get the Prana Dasha. 

Example: The Sookshma Dasha of the Sun is 16 Ghatikas and 12 palas or 972 palas. The Prana Dasha of the Sun in his own Sookshma Dasha will be-

$9 7 2 \times 6 = 5 8 3 2 \div 1 2 0 = 4 8$ palas and 36 Vipala. 

Thus 48 palas and 36 Vipala will be Prana Dasha in the Sookshma Dasha of the Sun in his Pratyantar Dasha, Antardasa and Dasha. 

Prana Dasha in the Sookshma Dasha of the Sun 

<table><tr><td>SN MN Ghatikas 2</td><td>MRS 0</td><td>RH 1</td><td>JUP 0</td><td>SAT 2</td><td>MCY 2</td><td>KT 2</td><td>VEN 2</td><td>0</td></tr><tr><td>Palas 42</td><td>48</td><td>21</td><td>56</td><td>25</td><td>9</td><td>33</td><td>17</td><td>56</td></tr><tr><td>Vipala 36</td><td>0</td><td>42</td><td>48</td><td>36</td><td>54</td><td>42</td><td>42</td><td>0</td></tr></table>

The same method is to be adopted for all the planets. 

Sookshma Dasha of the Sun 

प्ॐिल्यं तर्र्षजा बाधा चौिागग्ननृपजं भयम् । 

कष्टं सूक्ष्मदशाकाले िर्ौ प्राणदशां गिे ॥ २॥ 

2. Sun-Sun-Interest in unnatural sexual intercourse, danger from thieves, fire and the king, physical distress. 

सुखं भोजनसम्पथत्ताः संस्कािो नृपर्ैभर्म् । 

उदािाद्वदकृ पाथभि िर्ेाः प्राणगिे तर्धौ ॥ ३॥ 

3. Sun-Moon-Enjoyments, availability of good food, development of intelligence, opulence and glory like that of a king by the beneficence of the generous people. 

भूपोपद्रर्मन्याथे द्रव्यनाशो महद्भयम् । 

# महत्यपचयप्राप्ती िर्ेाः प्राणगिे कु जे ॥ ४॥

4. Sun-Mars-Antagonism with the king with the connivance of others, dangers and great losses. 

अन्नोद्भर्ा महापीडा तर्र्षोत्पथत्ततर्वशेर्षि 

अथागग्निाजथभाः क्लेशो िर्ेाः प्राणगिेऽप्यहौ ॥ ५॥ 

5. Sun-Rahu-Hunger, danger from poison, loss of wealth as a result of punishment by the king. 

नानातर्द्याथवसम्पथत्ताः कायवलाभो गिागिैाः । 

नृपतर्प्रािमे सूक्ष्मे िर्ेाः प्राणगिे गुिौ ॥ ६॥ 

6. Sun-Jupiter-Success in many educational spheres, gain of wealth, success in Ventures as a result of exchange of visits with the king and Brahmins. 

बन्धनं प्राणनाशि श्रचत्तोद्वेगस्तथैर् च । 

बहुबाधा महाहानी िर्ेाः प्राणगिे शनौ ॥ ७॥ 

7. Sun-Saturn-Imprisonment, death, excitement, obstacles and losses in ventures. 

िाजान्नभोगाः सििं िाजलाञ्छानित्पदम् । 

आत्मा सिपवयेदीर्ं िर्ेाः प्राणगिे बुधे ॥ ८॥ 

8. Sun-Mercury-Feeding from the king's kitchen, acquisition of Chhatra and Chamar with royal symbols, attainment of the position of a high dignitary of government. 

अन्योऽन्यं कलहिैर् र्सुहातनाः पिाजयाः । 

गुरुिीबन्धुतर्गैि सूयवप्राणगिे र्ध्जे ॥ ९॥ 

9. Sun-Ketu-Loss of wealth due to quarrels with the preceptor (or elders), wife and kinsmen. 

िाजपूजा धनाथधक्यं िीपुराद्वदभर्ं सुखम् । 

अन्नपानाद्वदभोगाद्वद सूयवप्राणगिे भृगौ ॥ १०॥ 

10. Sun-Venus-Recognition or reverence from the king, increase in wealth, happiness from wife and children, enjoyments from eating and drinking. 

Sookshma Dasha of the Moon 

िीपुराद्वदसुखं द्रव्यं लभिे नूिनाम्बिम् । 

योगससणद्धं समाथधञ्च तनजप्राणगिे तर्धौ ॥ ११॥ 

11. Moon-Moon-Happiness from wife and children, gain of wealth and clothes, yoga siddhi (योग शसद्धि) 

क्षयं कु ष्ठं बन्धुनाशं िक्तस्रार्ान्महद्भयम् । भूिार्ेशाद्वद जायिे तर्धोाः प्राणगिे कु जे ॥ १२॥ 

12. Moon-Mars-Consumption, leprosy, destruction of kinsmen, bleeding, creation of turbulence by friends and goblins (evil spirits). 

सपवभीतितर्शेर्षाण भूिोपद्रर्ान् सदा । दृष्टष्टक्षोभो मतिभ्रंशो तर्धोाः प्राणगिेऽप्यहौ ॥ १३॥ 

13. Moon-Rahu-Danger from snakes, creation of turbulence by evil spirits, weakness of eye sight, confusion of mind. 

धमवर्ृणद्धाः क्षमाप्राब्दप्तदेर्ब्राह्मणपूजनम् । सौभाग्यं ष्टप्रयदृष्टष्टि चन्द्रप्राणगिे गुिौ ॥ १४॥ 

14. Moon-Jupiter- Growth of religious mindedness, forgiveness, devotion towards deities and Brahmins, good fortune, meeting with near and dear ones. 

सहसा देहपिनं शरूपद्रर्र्ेदना । अन्धत्वं च धनप्राब्दप्तिन्द्रप्राणगिे शनौ ॥ १५॥ 

15. Moon-Saturn-Unexpected and sudden, physical distress, creation of troubles by enemies, weakness of eye sight, gain of wealth. 

चामिच्छरसम्प्राप्ती िाज्यलाभो नृपात्तिाः । समत्वं सर्वभूिेर्षु चन्द्रप्राणगिे बुधे ॥ १६॥ 

16. Moon-Mercury-Gift of Chamar and Chhatra by the king, acquisition of a kingdom, even mindedness in people. 

शिागग्नरिपुजा पीडा तर्र्षागग्नाः कु सक्षिोगिा । पुरदाितर्योगि चन्द्रप्राणगिे र्ध्जे ॥ १७॥ 

17, Moon-Ketu-Danger from weapons, fire, the enemy and poison, stomach troubles, separation from wife and children. 

पुरतमरकलराब्दप्ततर्देशाच्च धनागमाः । सुखसम्पथत्तिथवि चन्द्रप्राणगिे भृगौ ॥ १८॥ 

18. Moon-Venus-Acquisition of friends and wife (marriage), gain of wealth from foreign lands, all kinds of enjoyments. 

क्रू ििा कोपर्ृणद्धि प्राणहातनमवनोव्यथ 

देशत्यागो महाभीतििन्द्रप्राणगिे िर्ौ ॥ १९॥ 

19. Moon-Sun-Brutality, increase in anger, fear of death, agony, going away from the homeland, dangers. 

Sookshma Dasha of Mars 

कलहो रिपुथभबवन्धाः िक्तष्टपत्ताद्वदिोगभीाः । 

तनजसूक्ष्मदशामध्ये कु ज प्राणगिे फलम् ॥ २०॥ 

20. Mars-Mars- Quarrels with the enemy, imprisonment, bilious and blood pollution troubles. 

तर्च्युिाः सुिदािैि बन्धूपद्रर्पीष्टडिाः । 

प्राणत्यागो तर्र्षेणैर् भौमप्राणगिेऽप्यहौ ॥ २१॥ 

21. Mars-Rahu- Separation from wife and children, distress as a result of oppression by kinsmen, fear of death, poison. 

देर्ाचवनपिाः स्र्/ईमान्मिानुष्ठानित्पिाः । 

पुरपौरसुखार्ाब्दप्तभौमप्राणगिे गुिौ ॥ २२॥ 

22. Mars-Jupiter--Devotion towards deities, gain of wealth, competence in mantra rituals. 

अगग्नबाधा भर्ेन्मृत्युिथवनाशाः पदच्युतिाः । 

बन्धुथभबन्धुिार्ाब्दप्तभौमप्राणगिे शनौ ॥ २३॥ 

23. Mars-Saturn-Danger from fire, death, loss of wealth, loss of position but good relations with kinsmen. 

द्वदव्याम्बिसमुत्पथत्तद्वदवव्याभिणभूष्टर्षिाः । 

द्वदव्याङ्गनायााः सम्प्राब्दप्तभौमप्राणगिे बुधे ॥ २४॥ 

24. Mars-Mercury- Gains of splendid garments, ornaments, marriage. 

पिनोत्पातिपीडा च नेरक्षोभो महद्भयम् । 

भुजङ्गाद् द्रव्यहातनि भौमप्राणगिे र्ध्जे ॥ २५॥ 

25. Mars-Ketu--Fear of falling down from a high place, eye troubles, danger from snakes, and loss of reputation. 

धनधान्याद्वदसम्पथत्तलोकपूजा सुखागमा । 

नानाभोगैभवर्ेद्भोगी भौमप्राणगिे भृगौ ॥ २६॥ 

26. Mars-Venus- Gain of wealth, reverence amongst people (popularity), enjoyment of many kinds of luxuries. 

ज्विोन्मादाः क्षयोऽथवस्य िाजतर्स्नेहसम्भर्ाः । दीघविोगी दरिद्राः स्याद्भौमप्राणगिे िर्ौ ॥ २७॥ 

27. Mars-Sun-Fevers, lunacy, loss of wealth, wrath of the king, poverty. 

भोजनाद्वदसुखप्राब्दप्तर्विाभिणजं सुखम् । शीिोष्णव्याथधपीडा च भौमप्राणगिे तर्धौ ॥ २८॥ 

28. Mars-Moon-Comforts of good food and garments, distress from heat and cold. - 

Sookshma Dasha of Rahu 

अन्नाशने तर्िक्ति तर्र्षभीतिस्तथैर् च । साहसाद्धननाशि िाहौ प्राणगिे भर्ेि् ॥ २९॥ 

29. Rahu-Rahu-- Loss of taste in eating, danger from poison, loss of wealth through rashness. 

अङ्गसौख्यं तर्तनभीतिर्ाहनादेि सङ्गिा । नीश्रचाः कलहसम्प्राप्ती िाहोाः प्राणगिे गुिौ ॥ ३०॥ 

30. Rahu-Jupiter - Physical well-being, fearlessness, gain of conveyance and quarrels with menials. 

गृहदाहाः शिीिे रुङ् नीचैिपहृि धनम् । िथा बन्धनसम्प्राप्ती िाहोाः प्राणगिे शनौ ॥ ३१॥ 

31. Rahu-Saturn-Danger from fire, diseases, loss of wealth through menials, imprisonment. 

गुरूपदेशतर्भर्ो गुरुसत्कािर्द्धवनम् । गुणर्ाञ्छीलर्ांिाष्टप िाहोाः प्राणगिे बुधे ॥ ३२॥ 

32. Rahu-Mercury- Devotion towards the preceptor and increase of wealth through his beneficence, good qualities and well cultured. 

िीपुराद्वदतर्िोधि गृहागन्नष्क्रमणादष्टप । साहसात्कायहातनि िाहोाः प्राणगिे र्ध्जे ॥ ३३॥ 

33. Rahu-Ketu- Antagonism with wife and children, going away from home, loss of wealth through rashness. 

छरर्ाहनसम्पथत्ताः सर्ाथवफलसञ्चयाः । 

सशर्ाचवनगृहािम्भो िाहोाः प्राणगिे भृगौ ॥ ३४॥ 

34. Rahu-Venus-Acquisition of Chhatra, Chamar, conveyances etc., success in all ventures, worship of Lord Shiva, construction of a house. 

अशाद्वदिोगभीतिि िाज्योपद्रर्सम्भर्ाः । 

चिुष्पादाद्वदहातनि िाहोाः प्राणगिे िर्ौ ॥ ३५॥ 

35. Rahu-Sun-Affliction with piles, wrath of the King, loss of cattle. 

सौमनस्यं च सद्बणद्धाः ु सत्कािो गुरुदशवनम् । 

पापाद्भीतिमवनाःसौख्यं िाहोाः प्राणगिे तर्धौ ॥ ३६॥ 

36. Rahu-Moon-Development of mental powers and intelligence, popularity, visits of preceptors (elders), danger of committing sins. 

चाण्डालागग्नर्शाद्भीतिाः स्वपदच्युतििापदाः । 

मसलनाः श्वाद्वदर्ृथत्ति िाहोाः प्राणगिे कु जे ॥ ३७॥ 

37. Rahu-Mars-Dangers from menials and fire, loss of position, disaster, filthiness and meanness. 

Sookshma Dasha of Jupiter 

हर्षागमो धनाथधक्यमगग्नहोरं सशर्ाचवनम् । 

र्ाहनं छरसंयुक्तं तनज प्राणगिे गुिौ ॥ ३८॥ 

38. Jupiter-Jupiter-Happiness, increase in wealth, performance of Havana, worship of Lord Shiva, acquisition of Chhatra and conveyances. 

व्रिहातनतर्वर्षादि तर्देशे धननाशनम् । 

तर्िोधो बन्धुर्गैि गुिोाः प्राणगिे शनौ ॥ ३९॥ 

39. Jupiter-Saturn-Failure in fasting, unhappiness, going away to foreign lands, loss of wealth, antagonism with kinsmen. 

तर्द्याबुणद्धतर्र्ृणद्धि लोके पूजा धनागमाः । 

िीपुराद्वदसुखप्राब्दप्तगुविोाः प्राणगिे बुधे ॥ ४०॥ 

40, Jupiter-Mercury-Progress in education, increase in intelligence, happiness to wife and children, popularity, gain of wealth. 

ज्ञानं तर्भर्पाण्डण्डत्यं शािज्ञानं सशर्ाचवनम् । 

अगग्नहोरं गुिोभवगक्तगुविोाः प्राणगिे र्ध्जे ॥ ४१॥ 

41. Jupiter Ketu--Opulence and glory, learnedness, gain of knowledge of Shastras, worship of Lord Shiva, performance of Havana, devotion towards preceptor. 

िोगान्मुगक्ताः सुखं भोगो धनधान्यसमागमाः । पुरदािाद्वदजं सौख्यं गुिोाः प्राणगिे भृगौ ॥ ४२॥ 

42. Jupiter-Venus-Freedom from diseases, enjoyments, increase in wealth, happiness from wife and children. 

र्ािष्टपत्तप्रकोपं च श्लेष्मोद्रेकं िु दारुणम् । िसव्याथधकृ िं शूलं गुिोाः प्राणगिे िर्ौ ॥ ४३॥ 

43. Jupiter-Sun-Disorder of wind, bile and phlegm, pains due to disorders of juices in the body. 

छरचामिसंयुक्तं र्ैभर्ं पुरसम्पदाः । नेरकु सक्षगिा पीडा गुिोाः प्राणगिे तर्धौ ॥ ४४॥ 

44. Jupiter-Moon-Acquisition of Chhatra with royal symbol, opulence and glory, increase in children, eye and stomach trouble. 

िीजनाच्च तर्र्षोत्पथत्तबवन्धनं चातितनग्रहाः । देशाििगमो भ्रान्तिगुविोाः प्राणगिे कु जे ॥ ४५॥ 

45. Jupiter-Mars-Danger of administration of poison by wife, imprisonment, foreign journeys, confusion of mind. 

व्याथधथभाः परिभूिाः स्याच्चौिैिपहृिं धनम् । सपवर्ृसिकभीतिि गुिोाः प्राणगिेऽप्यहौ ॥ ४६॥ 

46. Jupiter-Rahu- Distress from diseases, troubles from, thieves, danger from snakes, scorpions etc. 

Sookshma Dasha of Saturn 

ज्विेण ज्वसलिा कान्तिाः कु ष्ठिोगोदिाद्वदरुक् । जलागग्नकृ िमृत्युाः स्यागन्नजप्राणगिे शनौ ॥ ४७॥ 

47. Saturn-Saturn-Loss of lustre due to fevers, Leprosy, stomach trouble, danger of death from fire. 

धनं धान्यं च माङ्गल्यं व्यर्हािाथभपूजनम् । देर्ब्राह्मणभगक्ति शनेाः प्राणगिे बुधे ॥ ४८॥ 

48. Saturn-Mercury - Gain of wealth and grains, profits in business, reverence, devotion towards deities and Brahmins. 

मृत्युर्ेदनदाःखंु च भूिोपद्रर्सम्भर्ाः । पिदािाथभभूित्वं शनेाः प्राणगिे र्ध्जे ॥ ४९॥ 

49. Saturn-Ketu - Death like distress, creation of turbulence by evil spirits, insult from a woman other than wife. 

पुराथवतर्भर्ैाः सौख्यं सक्षतिपालाद्वदिाः सुखम् । अगग्नहोरं तर्र्ाहि शनेाः प्राणगिे भृगौ ॥ ५०॥ 

50. Saturn-Venus-Enjoyments through wealth, son and beneficence of the king, performance of Havana, marriage etc. 

असक्षपीडा सशिोव्याथधाः सपवशरुभयं भर्ेि् । अथवहातनमवहाक्लेशाः शनेाः प्राणगिे िर्ौ ॥ ५१॥ 

51. Saturn-Sun-Troubles in the eyes and forehead, danger from snakes and enemies, loss of wealth, distress. 

आिोग्यं पुरलाभि शान्तिपौष्टष्टकर्धवनम् । देर्ब्राह्मणभगक्ति शनेाः प्राणगिे तर्धौ ॥ ५२॥ 

52. Saturn-Moon-Sound health, birth of a son, relief, thriving strength, devotion towards deities and Brahmins. 

गुल्मिोगाः शरुभीतिमृवगया प्राननाशनम् । सपागग्नतर्र्षिो भीतिाः शनेाः प्राणगिे कु जे ॥ ५३॥ 

53. Saturn-Mars-Affliction with Gulma disease, danger from enemy, danger of death during hunting, danger from snakes, fire and poison. 

देशत्यागो नृपाद्भीतिमोहनं तर्र्षभक्षणम् । र्ािष्टपत्तकृ िा पीडा शनेाः प्राणगिेऽप्यहौ ॥ ५४॥ 

54. Saturn-Rahu-Going away from homeland, danger from the king, bewitchment, taking of poison, troubles from wind and bile. 

सेनापत्यं भूतमलाभाः सङ्गमाः स्वजनैाः सह । गौिर्ं नृपसम्मानं शनेाः प्राणगिे गुिौ ॥ ५५॥ 

55. Saturn-Jupiter-Attainment of the position of a Commander in the army, gain of land, association with ascetics, reverence from the king. 

Sookshma Dasha of Mercury आिोग्यं सुखसम्पथत्तधवमवकमाद्वदसाधनम् । 

# समत्वं सर्वभुिेर्षु तनजप्राणगिे बुधे ॥ ५६॥

56. Mercury-Mercury-Increase in enjoyments, wealth and religious mindedness, even mindedness in all living beings. 

र्तििस्कििो भीतिाः पिमाथधतर्वर्षोद्भर्ाः । 

देहािकिणं दाःखं ु बुधप्राणगिे र्ध्जे ॥ ५७॥ 

57. Mercury-Ketu- Danger from thieves, fire and poison, death like suffering. 

प्रभुत्वं धनसम्पथत्ताः कीतिवधवमवाः सशर्ाचवनम् । 

पुरदािाद्वदकं सौख्यं बुधप्राणगिे भृगौ ॥ ५८॥ 

58. Mercury-Venus- Supremacy over others, increase in wealth, reputation and religious mindedness, devotion to Lord Shiva, happiness from son. 

अिदाहो ज्विोन्मादौ बान्धर्ानां िति ण्डियााः । 

प्राप्यिे स्तीयसम्पथत्तबुवधप्राणगिे िर्ौ ॥ ५९॥ 

59. Mercury-Sun - Agony, fevers, lunacy, affectionate relations with wife and kinsmen, receipt of stolen property. 

िीलाभिाथवसम्पथत्ताः कन्यालाभो धनागमाः । 

लभिे सर्विाः सौख्यं बुधप्राणगिे तर्धौ ॥ ६०॥ 

60. Mercury-Moon-Happiness from wife, birth of a daughter, gain of wealth, and enjoyments all round. 

पतििाः कु सक्षिोगी च दिनेराद्वदजा व्यथा । 

अशांसस प्राणसन्देहो बुधप्राणगिे कु जे ॥ ६१॥ 

61. Mercury-Mars-Tendency to indulge in nefarious activities, pain in eyes, teeth and stomach, piles, danger from death. 

र्िाभिणसम्पथत्ततर्वयोगो तर्प्रर्ैरििा । 

सगन्नपािोद्भर्ं दखं ु बुधप्राणगिेऽप्यहौ ॥ ६२॥ 

62. Mercury-Rahu - Gain of clothes, ornaments and wealth, separation from own people, antagonism with Brahmins delirium. 

गुरुत्वं धनसम्पथत्ततर्वद्या सद्गणसङ् ग्रहाः ु । 

व्यर्सायेन सिाभो बुधप्राणगिे गुिौ ॥ ६३॥ 

63. Mercury-Jupiter-Sublimity, progress in education, increase in wealth and good qualities, profits in business. 

# चौयेण तनधनप्राब्दप्ततर्वधनत्वं दरिद्रिा । याचकत्वं तर्शेर्षेण बुधप्राणगिे शनौ ॥ ६४॥

64. Mercury-Saturn - Danger of death from thieves, poverty, beggary. Sookshma Dasha of Ketu 

अश्वपािेन घािि शरुिाः कलहागमाः । तनतर्वचािर्धोत्पथत्ततनवजप्राणगिे र्ध्जे ॥ ६५॥ 

65. Ketu-Ketu - Danger of fall from a conveyance, quarrels with the enemy, committing a murder inadvertently. 

क्षेरलाभो र्ैरिनाशो हयलाभो मनाःसुखम् । पशुक्षेरधनाब्दप्ति के िोाः प्राणगिे भृगौ ॥ ६६॥ 

66. Ketu -Venus-Gain of land and conveyance, happiness, destruction of enemy, increase in cattle wealth. 

स्तेयागग्नरिपुभीतिि धनहातनमवनोव्यथा । प्राणािकिणं कष्टं के िोाः प्राणगिे िर्ौ ॥ ६७॥ 

67. Ketu-Sun-Danger from fire and enemy, loss of wealth, mental agony, death like suffering; 

देर्द्वद्वजगुिोाः पूजा दीघवयारा धनं सुखम् । कणे र्ा लोचने िोगाः के िोाः प्राणगिे तर्धौ ॥ ६८॥ 

68. Ketu-Moon-Devotion towards deities and Brahmins, journeys to distant places, gain of wealth and happiness, eye and ear troubles. 

ष्टपत्तिोगो नसार्ृणद्धतर्वभ्रमाः सगन्नपािजाः । स्वबन्धुजनतर्द्वेर्षाः के िोाः प्राणगिे कु जे ॥ ६९॥ 

69. Ketu-Mars- Bilious troubles, enlargement of veins, delirium, antagonism with kinsmen. 

तर्िोधाः िीसुिाद्यैि गृहागन्नष्क्रमणं भर्ेि् । स्वसाहसात्कायवहातनाः के िोाः प्राणगिेऽप्यहौ ॥ ७०॥ 

70. Ketu-Rahu-Antagonism with son and wife, going away from home, loss in ventures due to rashness. 

स/िव्रणैमवहािोगो हृत्पीडाद्वदसमुद्भर्ाः । सुिदाितर्योगि के िोाः प्राणगिे गुिौ ॥ ७१॥ 

71. Ketu-Jupiter-Injuries from weapons, wounds, heart disease, separation from wife and children. 

मतितर्भ्रमिीक्ष्णत्वं क्रू िकमवितिाः सदा । व्यर्सनाद्बन्धनं दाःखंु के िोाः प्राणगिे शनौ ॥ ७२॥ 

72. Ketu-Saturn-Confusion of mind, tendencies towards nefarious deeds, imprisonment on account of addictions (in drugs -etc.), distress. 

कु सुमं शयनं भूर्षा लेपनं भोजनाद्वदकम् । सौख्यं सर्ाङ्गभोग्यं च के िोाः प्राणगिे बुधे ॥ ७३॥ 

73. Ketu-Mercury- Enjoyments of bed, perfumery, ornaments and sandal, good food and availability of all kinds of comforts. 

Sookshma Dasha of Venus 

ज्ञानमीश्विभगक्ति सिोर्षि धनागमाः । पुरपौरसमृणद्धि तनजप्राणगिे भृगौ ॥ ७४॥ 

74. Venus-Venus - Learning, devotion to deities, satisfaction, gain of wealth, increase in the number of children. 

लोकप्रकाशकीतिवि सुिसौख्यतर्र्सजविाः । उष्णाद्वदिोगजं दखंु शुक्रप्राणगिे िर्ौ ॥ ७५॥ 

75. Venus-Sun - Good reputation in public, loss of happiness in respect of children, heat troubles. 

देर्ाचवने कमवितिमवन्त्रिोर्षणित्पिाः । धनसौभाग्यसम्पथत्ताः शुक्रप्राणगिे तर्धौ ॥ ७६॥ 

76. Venus-Moon - Devotion towards deities, competence, relief from mantras, increase in wealth and fortune. 

ज्विो मसूरिकास्फोटकण्डूश्रचष्टपटकाद्वदकााः । देर्ब्राह्मणपूजा च शुक्रप्राणगिे कु जे ॥ ७७॥ 

77. Venus-Mars - Fevers, wounds, ringworms, itches, devotion towards deities and Brahmins. 

तनत्यं शरुकृ िा पीडा नेरकु सक्षरुजादयाः । तर्िोधाः सुहृदां पीडा शुक्रप्राणगिेऽप्यहौ ॥ ७८॥ 

78. Venus-Rahu - Distress from enemy, eye and stomach troubles, antagonism with friends. 

आयुिािोग्यमैश्वयं पुरिीधनर्ैभर्म् । छरर्ाहनसम्प्राब्दप्ताः शुक्रप्राणगिे गुिौ ॥ ७९॥ 

79. Venus- Jupiter - Good longevity, sound health, happiness from wealth, wife and children, acquisition of Chhatra and conveyances. 

िाजोपद्रर्जा भीतिाः सुखहातनमवहारुजाः । नीचैाः सह तर्र्ादि भृगोाः प्राणगिे शनौ ॥ ८०॥ 

80. Venus-Saturn - Danger from the king, loss of happiness, critical disease, controversy with menials. 

सिोर्षो िाजसम्मानं नानाद्वदग्भूतमसम्पदाः । तनत्यमुत्साहष्ट्द्धाः स्याच्छु क्रप्राणगिे बुधे ॥ ८१॥ 

81. Venus-Mercury- Satisfaction, reverence from the Icing, gains of land and wealth from many directions, increase in enthusiasm. 

जीतर्िात्मयशोहातनधवनधान्यपरिक्षयाः । त्यागभोगधनातन स्युाः शुक्रप्राणगिे र्ध्जे ॥ ८२॥ 

82. Venus-Ketu - Loss of life, wealth, and reputation, only some money is left for charities and sustenance. 

एर्मृक्षदशानां द्वह साििागां मया द्वद्वज । फलातन कथथिान्यर संक्षेपादेर् िेऽग्रिाः ॥ ८३॥ 

83. The revered Sage Parāśara said-O Brahmin! Here I have described to you the effects of Nakshatra (Vimshottari) Dasha etc. The good or adverse predictions should be made after assessing judiciously the auspiciousness and inauspiciousness of all the five, namely Dasha, Antardasa, Pratyantar Dasha, Sookshma Dasha and Prana Dasha. 

# अथ कालचक्रान्तदिशाफलाध्यायः ॥६४॥

# Chapter 64. Effects of Antardasa in the Kalachakra Dasha

जगष्टध्यढथाय प्रोक्थातन पुिा यातन पुिारिणा । 

थातन चक्रािधवशाफलातन कठयाम्यहम् ॥ १॥ 

1. The Sage Said-Now I am going to describe to you the effects of Antardasa in the Kalachakra Dasha as related by Lord Shiva to the Goddess Parvati. 

Example of the method of calculating the Antardasa in the Kalachakra Dasha (Please see Savya Chakra in Chapter 46). 

<table><tr><td colspan="11">Table showing Dasha years in Aries Amsa</td></tr><tr><td>Rash i</td><td>ARS</td><td>TRS</td><td>GM N</td><td>CR</td><td>LE O</td><td>VR G</td><td>LBR</td><td>SC P</td><td>SA G</td><td></td></tr><tr><td>Lord</td><td>MR S</td><td>VE N</td><td>MCY N</td><td>M N</td><td>SN</td><td>MC Y</td><td>VE N</td><td>MR</td><td>JUP</td><td>Aries Amsa</td></tr><tr><td>Year s</td><td>7</td><td>16</td><td>9</td><td>21</td><td>5</td><td>9</td><td>16</td><td>17</td><td>10</td><td>Total 100</td></tr></table>

ARS-Aries, TRS-Taurus. GMN-Gemini, CR-Cancer, LEO-Leo, VRG-Virgo, LBR-Libra, SCP-Scorpio, SAG-Sagittarius, CAP-Capricorn, AQS-Aquarius, PSC-Pisces, MRS-Mars, VEN-Venus, MCY-Mercury, MN-Moon, SN-Sun, JUP-Jupiter, SAT Saturn, RH-Rahu, KT-Ketu. 

Multiply the Dasha years of Aries in Aries Amsa, namely 7 by 7 the years of Aries and divide the product by 100 (the total years of Aries Amsa). This will give us 0/5/26/24 (0 years, 5 months, 26 days and 24 Ghatikas) as the Antardasa of Aries or Mars in the Dasha of Aries. 

Multiply Dasha years of Aries 7 by 16 the Dasha years of Taurus, the product will be 112. Divide this figure by 100. We will get 1 year, 1 month, 13 days and 12 Ghatikas as the Antardasa of Taurus or Venus in the Dasha of Aries. The Antardasa of all the Rāśhis in all the Dasha of the other Rāśhis should be calculated in the same manner. However, we give below this information in the following tables for ready reference by the readers.

Notes: The above tables show the Antardasa of the Rāśhis in the Savya chakra. In the same manner, the Antardasa in be worked out for the Apsavya chakra. It is not possible to give those tables here for lack of space. 


# Effect of Antardasa

मेर्षांशे स्वाििे भौमे ज्विि व्रणसम्भर्ाः । 

बुधशुक्रे न्दजीर्ेर्षु ु सुखं शरुभयं िर्ौ ॥ २॥ 

2. Dasha or Aries Amsa-There will be wounds and fever in the Antardasa of Mars (that is Aries or Scorpio) in the Dasha of Aries Amsa. In the same Dasha and Antardasa of the Rāśhis owned by Mercury, Venus, Moon and Jupiter all kinds of happiness will be enjoyed. Danger from enemy will be experience in the Antardasa of the Sun. 

र्ृर्षांशे स्वाििे सौिे कलहो िोगसम्भर्ाः । 

तर्द्यालाभस्तनौ सौख्यं गुिौ िर गिे फलम् ॥ ३॥ 

देशत्यागो मृतिर्ाष्टप शिघािो ज्विोऽथर्ा । 

र्ृर्षभस्वांशके तर्प्र कु जे िर गिे फलम् ॥ ४॥ 

र्िाभिणलाभि िीसुयोगो महि् सुखम् । 

शुक्रे न्दसुिचन्द्रेर्षु ु र्ृर्षभस्वांशके फलम् ॥ ५॥ 

3-5. Dasha or Taurus Amsa-Effects like quarrels, diseases will be experienced in Antardasa of Saturn (that is Capricorn or Aquarius). There will be gains of education and physical felicity in the Antardasa of Jupiter (Sagittarius or Pisces), going away from home, death or distress from fevers in the Antardasa of Mars (Aries and Scorpio) and gains of garments, happy association with women in the Antardasa of the rāśhis owned by Venus and Mercury. Danger from the king and violent animals may be expected in the Antardasa of rashi (Leo) owned by the Sun. 

नृपाद् भयं ष्टपिृमृतिाः स्वर्दाद्यैभवयं िर्ौ । 

तमथुने स्वांशके शुक्रे धनर्िसमागमाः ॥ ६॥ 

ष्टपिृमािृमृिेभीतिज्वविि व्रणसम्भर्ाः । 

दिदेशप्रयाणं ू च तमथुने स्वांशके कु जे ॥ ७॥ 

बुणद्धतर्द्यातर्र्ृणद्धि महातर्भर्सम्भर्ाः । 

लोके मानि प्रीतिि तमथेने स्वांशके गुिौ ॥ ८॥ 

तर्देशगमनं व्याथधमविणं धननाशनम् । 

बन्धुनाशोऽथर्ा तर्प्र तमथुने स्वांशके शनौ ॥ ९॥ 

तर्द्यार्िाद्वदलाभि दािपुराद्वदजं सुखम् । 

सर्वर मानमाप्नोति तमथुने स्वांशके बुधे ॥ १०॥ 

6-10. Dasha of Gemini Amsa-The effects in the Antardasa of the rāśhis concerned will be as follows-

Venus (Taurus or Libra)-Gain of wealth and garments. Mars (Aries and Scorpio)-Death of parents, danger, fever, wounds and travels to distant places. 

Jupiter (Sagittarius or Pisces)-Increase in intelligence, success in education, opulence and glory, popularity and affection towards others. 

Saturn (Capricorn or Aquarius)-Foreign journeys, diseases, fear of death, loss of wealth and kinsmen. 

Mercury (Gemini or Virgo)-Success in education, gains of garments etc., happiness from the wife and children and reverence from all quarters. 

ककव स्वांशगिे चन्द्रे पुरदािसुखं महि् । 

ऐश्वयं लभिे लोके मानं प्रीतिं िथैर् च ॥ ११॥ 

शरुभ्यि पशुभ्यि भयं िाजकु लाि् िथा । 

आथधव्याथधभयं चैर् कके स्वांशगिे िर्ौ ॥ १२॥ 

पुरदािसुहृत्सौख्यं धनर्ृणद्धस्तथैर् च । 

लोके मानं यशिैर् ककांशे बुधशुक्रयोाः ॥ १३॥ 

तर्र्षशिमृिेभीतिं ज्वििोगाद्वदसम्भर्ाम् । 

पीडां चैर् समाप्नोति कके स्वांशगिे कु जे ॥ १४॥ 

तर्भर्स्यातिलाभि शिीिेऽष्टप सुखं िथा । 

नृपाि् सम्मानलाभि कके स्वांशगिे गुिौ ॥ १५॥ 

र्ादव्याथधभयं घोिं सपवर्ृसिकिो भयम् । 

नानाकष्टमर्ाप्नोति कके स्वांशगिे शनौ ॥ १६॥ 

11-16. Dasha of Cancer Amsa - The effects in the various Antardasa of the rāśhis concerned will be as follows-

Moon (Cancer) - Happiness from wife and children, gain of wealth and reverence from the public (popularity). 

Sun (Leo) - Danger from enemies, animals and the royal family, mental agony and fear of diseases. 

Mercury (Gemini or Virgo) and Venus (Taurus and Libra)-Happiness from wife, children and friends, increase in wealth, popularity and name and fame. 

Mars (Aries or Scorpio)-Danger from poison, weapons and diseases like fever. 

Jupiter (Sagittarius or Pisces)-Gains of wealth, physical felicity, honours from the king. 

Saturn (Capricorn or Aquarius) - Rheumatism, danger from snakes, scorpions and distress of all kinds. 

सस ंहांशे स्वांशगे भौमे मुखिोगभयं द्वदशेि् । 

ष्टपत्तज्विकृ िां र्ाधां शिक्षिमथाष्टप र्ा ॥ १७॥ 

धनर्िाद्वदलाभि िीपुराद्वदसुखं िथा । 

बुधभागवर्योतर्वप्र ससंहांशे स्वाििियोाः ॥ १८॥ 

उच्चाि् पिनभीतिि स्वल्पद्रव्यसमागमाः । 

तर्देशगमनं चैर् ससंहे स्वािगविे तर्धौ ॥ १९॥ 

भयं शरुजनेभ्यि ज्विाद्वदव्याणद्धसम्भर्ाः । 

ज्ञानहातनमृविेभीतिाः ससंहे स्वािगविे िर्ौ ॥ २०॥ 

धनधान्याद्वदलाभं च प्रसादं द्वद्वजभूपयोाः । 

तर्द्यार्ृणद्धमर्ाप्नोति ससंहे स्वािगविे गुिौ ॥ २१॥ 

17-21. Dasha or Leo Amsa--The effects in the various Antardasa of rāśhis concerned will be as follows-- 

Mars (Aries and Scorpio) --Diseases of the mouth, bilious fever and danger from weapon. 

Mercury, (Gemini or Virgo), Venus (Taurus and Libra) Gain of clothes, happiness from wife and children. 

Moon (Cancer)-Danger from fall from some height, meagre gains of wealth, foreign journeys. 

Sun (Leo) - Danger from enemies, fevers, loss of wisdom, fear of death. 

Jupiter (Sagittarius or Pisces)-Gains of wealth and grains, beneficence of the king and Brahmins, progress in education. 

Notes: The effects which are being described here are of the Antardasa of the rāśhis concerned. Their lords have been mentioned because they (rāśhis) yield effects according to the characteristics of their lords. For example, when we describe effects of the Antardasa of Jupiter; it means that the effects are of the Antardasa, of rāśhis owned by Jupiter, namely Sagittarius and Pisces. This clarification has been given so that there mal' be no confusion in the mind of the readers. 

द्रयाणं च ज्विं चैर् क्षुद्भर्ं र्ैक्लर्ं िथा ॥ २२॥ 

नृपप्रसादमैश्वयं सुहृद्बन्धुसमागमम् । 

तर्द्यार्ृणद्धमर्ाप्नोति कन्यायां स्वांशके गुिौ ॥ २३॥ 

ष्टपत्तज्विभर्ा पीडा तर्देशे गमनं िथा । 

शिघािोऽगग्नभीतिि कन्यायां स्वाििे कु जे ॥ २४॥ 

भृत्यपुराथवलाभि नानासुखसमागमाः । 

बन्धुभागवर्चन्द्रेर्षु कन्यास्वांशगिेर्षु च ॥ २५॥ 

प्रयाणं िोगभीतिि कलहो बन्धुथभाः सह । 

शिघािभयं चैर् कन्यांशे स्वांशगे िर्ौ ॥ २६॥ 

22-26. Dasha or Virgo Amsa-The effects in the various Antardasa of the rāśhis concerned will be as follows-

Saturn (Capricorn or Aquarius) - Many kinds of troubles, travels to distant places, fevers, distress from hunger. 

Jupiter (Sagittarius or Pisces)-Gains of wealth through the beneficence of the king, arrival of friends and kinsmen and success in education. 

Mars (Aries or Scorpio)-Bilious fever, travels to distant places, danger from fire and weapons. 

Mercury (Gemini or Virgo), Venus (Taurus and Libra) and Moon (Cancer)- Gains of wealth through sons and employees, many enjoyments. 

Sun (Leo)-Travel to distant lands, danger from diseases, quarrels with kinsmen, danger of assaults by weapons. 

िुले स्वािगविे शुक्रे सद्बणद्धि ु सुखोदयाः । 

िीपुरधननर्िाद्वदलाभो भर्ति तनसििाः ॥ २७॥ 

ष्टपिृकष्टं सुहृद्वैिं सशिोिोगो ज्विोदयाः । 

तर्र्षशिागग्नभीतिि िुले स्वािगविे कु जे ॥ २८॥ 

द्रव्यित्नाद्वदलाभि धमवकायं नृपादयाः । 

सर्वर सुखसम्प्राब्दप्तस्तुले स्वांशगिे गुिौ ॥ २९॥ 

प्रयाणं च महाव्याथधाः क्षेरदेाः क्षतििेर् च । 

शरुर्ाधा च कायेर्षु िुले स्वांशगिे शनौ ॥ ३०॥ 

पुरजन्म धनप्राब्दप्ताः िीसुखं च मनाःष्टप्रयम् । 

भाग्योदयि तर्ज्नेयस्तुले स्वािगविे बुधे ॥ ३१॥ 

27-31. Dasha of Libra Amsa-The effects in the various Antardasa of the rāśhis concerned will be as follows-

Venus (Taurus and Libra)-Wisdom, comforts, happiness from wife, children, wealth, garments etc. 

Mars (Aries or Scorpio)-Distress to father, enmity with friends, danger from disease of forehead, fevers, poison, weapons etc. 

Jupiter (Sagittarius or Pisces)-Gain of wealth, acquisition of a kingdom, performance of religious rites, honours from the king and happiness all round. 

Saturn (Capricorn or Aquarius)-Travels to distant places, critical diseases, loss in agricultural sphere, danger from enemies. 

Mercury (Gemini or Virgo)-Birth of a son, gain of wealth, happiness from wife, joy, dawn of fortune. 

शशाङ्कबुधशुक्रे र्षु र्ृसिके स्वांशगेर्षु च । 

नानाधान्यधनप्राब्दप्तव्याथधतर्नाशो महि् सुखम् ॥ ३२॥ 

शरुक्षोभभयं व्याथधमथवनाशं ष्टपिुभवयम् । 

श्वापदाद् भयमाप्नोति र्ृसिके स्वांशगे िर्ौ ॥ ३३॥ 

32-33. Dasha of Scorpio Amsa-The following effects will be experienced in the Antardasa of the rāśhis concerned-

Moon (Cancer); Mercury (Gemini or Virgo), Venus (Taurus or Libra)-Gain of wealth and grains in different ways, freedom from diseases, enjoyments of many kinds. 

Sun (Leo)-Danger from enemies, loss of wealth, distress to father, danger from wild and violent animals. 

Mars (Aries or Scorpio)-Troubles from wind and bile, wounds, danger from fire and weapon. 

Jupiter (Sagittarius or Pisces)-Gains of wealth, grains and gems, devotion towards deities and Brahmins, beneficence of the king. 

Saturn (Capricorn or Aquarius)-Loss of wealth, separation from kinsmen, mental anxiety, danger from enemies, diseases. 

र्ािष्टपत्तभयं चैर् मसूिीव्रणमाद्वदशेि् । 

अगग्नशिाद्वदभीतिि र्ृसिके स्वांशगे कु जे ॥ ३४॥ 

धनं धान्यञ्च ित्नं च देर्ब्राह्मणपूजनम् । 

िाजप्रसादमाप्नोति र्ृसिके स्वांशगे गुिौ ॥ ३५॥ 

धनबन्धुतर्नाशि जायिे मानसी व्यथा । 

शरुर्ाधा महाव्याथधर्ृवसिके स्वांशगे शनौ ॥ ३६॥ 

अतिदाहं ज्विं छद्वदव मुखिोगं तर्शेर्षिाः । 

नानाक्लेशमर्ाप्नोति चापांशे स्वांशगे कु जे ॥ ३७॥ 

श्रियं तर्द्यां च सौभाग्यं शरुनाशं नृपाि् सुखम् । 

भागवर्ेन्दचन्द्राणां ु चापे स्वस्वांशके द्वदशेि् ॥ ३८॥ 

भायातर्त्ततर्नाशं च कलहं च नृपाद् भयम् । 

दियारा ू मर्ाप्नोति चापांशे स्वांशगे िर्ौ ॥ ३९॥ 

दानधमविपोलाभं िाजपूजनमाप्नुयाि् । 

भायातर्भर्लाभं च चापे स्वांशगिे गुिौ ॥ ४०॥ 

34-40. Dasha of Sagittarius Amsa-The following effects will be derived in the various Antardasa or the rāśhis owned by-

Mars (Aries or Scorpio}-Heart burn, fevers, cold, disease of the mouth, many kinds of troubles. 

Venus (Taurus or Libra), Mercury (Gemini or Virgo), Moon (Cancer)-increase in wealth and property and fortune, progress in education, destruction of enemies, happiness from the king. 

Sun (Leo)-Loss of wife and wealth, quarrels, danger from the king, travels to distant lands. 

Jupiter (Sagittarius or Pisces) --Charity, self-mortifications, honours from the king, increase in religious mindedness, happiness from wife, gain of wealth. 

द्वद्वजदेर्नृपोद्भिं ू कोपं बन्धुतर्नाशनम् । 

देशत्यागमर्ाप्नोति मकिस्वांशगे शनौ ॥ ४१॥ 

देर्ाचवनं िपोध्यानं सम्मानं भूपिेाः कु ले । 

भागवर्ज्ञेन्दजीर्ानां ु मृगांशेऽिदवशाफलम् ॥ ४२॥ 

सशिोिोगं ज्विं चैर् किपादक्षिं द्वदशेि् । 

िक्तष्टपत्तातिसािांि मृगस्वांशगिे कु जे ॥ ४३॥ 

तर्नाशं ष्टपिृबन्धूनां ज्वििोगाद्वदकं द्वदशेि् । 

नृपशरुभयं चैर् मृगांशस्वांशगे शनौ ॥ ४४॥ 

41-44. Dasha of Capricorn Amsa-The following effects will be experienced in the various Antardasa of the rāśhis owned by-

Saturn (Capricorn or Aquarius)-Wrath of Brahmins, deities and the king, loss of kinsmen, abandonment of the homeland. 

Venus (Taurus or Libra), Mercury (Gemini or Virgo), Moon (Cancer), Jupiter (Sagittarius or Pisces)-Devotion towards deities, self-mortification, honours from government. 

Mars (Aries or Scorpio)-Disease of the forehead, assaults on hands and feet, danger from dysentery, blood pollution and bilious troubles. 

Saturn (Capricorn or Aquarius) - Loss of father and kinsmen, fevers, danger from the king and the enemies. 

नानातर्द्याथवलाभि पुरिीतमरजं सुखम् । 

शिीिािोग्यमैश्वयं कु म्भे स्वांशगिे भृगौ ॥ ४५॥ 

ज्विागग्नचोिजा पीडा शरुणां च महद् भयम् । 

मनोव्यथामर्ाप्नोति घटांशस्वाििे कु जे ॥ ४६॥ नैरुज्यं च सुखं चैर् सम्मानं भूपिेाः द्वद्वजाि् । मनाःप्रसादमाप्नोति कु म्भांशस्वांशगे गुिौ ॥ ४७॥ धािुरयप्रकोपं च कलहं देशतर्भ्रमम् । क्षयव्याथधमर्ाप्नोति कु म्भांशस्वांशगे शनौ ॥ ४८॥ पुरतमरधनिीणां लाभं चैर् मनाःष्टप्रयम् । सौभाग्यर्ृणद्धमाप्नोति कु म्भांशस्वांशगे बुधे ॥ ४९॥ 

45-49. Dasha of Aquarius Amsa-The following effects will be experienced in the Antardasa of the rāśhis owned by-

Venus (Taurus or Libra)-Many kinds of educational attainments, gains of property, happiness from wife and children, sound health and increase in wealth. 

Mars (Aries or Scorpio)-Fevers, danger from fire and enemies, distress from enemies and mental agony. 

Saturn (Capricorn or Aquarius)-Danger of troubles from wind, bile and phlegm, quarrels, foreign journey, danger of suffering from tuberculosis. 

Jupiter (Sagittarius or Pisces) - Freedom from ill health, happiness honours from the king and joy. 

Mercury (Gemini or Virgo)-Happiness from wife, children and Wealth, joy, increase in good fortune. 

तर्द्यार्ृणद्धमर्ाप्नोति िीसुखं व्याथधनाशनम् । सुहृत्सङ्गं मनाःप्रीतिं मीनांशस्वांशगे तर्धौ ॥ ५०॥ बन्धुथभाः कलहं चैर् चौिभीतिं मनोव्यथाम् । िानभ्रंशमर्ाप्नोति मीनांशस्वांशगे िर्ौ ॥ ५१॥ िणे तर्जयमाप्नोति पशुभूतमसुिागमम् । धनर्ृणद्धि मीनांशे स्वांशयोबुवधशुक्रयोाः ॥ ५२॥ ष्टपत्तिोगं तर्र्ादञ्च स्वजनैिष्टप मानर्ाः । शरुणां भयमाप्नोति मीनांशस्वांशगे कु जे ॥ ५३॥ धनर्िकलराणां लाभो भूपसमादिाः । प्रतिष्ठा बहुधा लोके मीनांशस्वांशगे गुिौ ॥ ५४॥ धननाशो मनस्तापो र्ेश्यादीनां च सङ्गमाि् । देशत्यागो भर्ेद्वाष्टप मीनांशस्वांशगे शनौ ॥ ५५॥ 

50-55. Dasha or Pisces Amsa-The following will be the effects in the various Antardasa of the rāśhis owned by-

Moon (Cancer)-Increase in wisdom and educational attainments, happiness from wife, freedom from disease, association with friends, joy and happiness. 

Sun (Leo)-Quarrels with kinsmen, danger from thieves, mental agony, loss of position. 

Mercury (Virgo or Gemini) and Venus (Taurus or Libra) Victory in war, birth of a son, gains of land and cattle, increase in wealth. 

Mars (Aries or Scorpio) --Bilious troubles, dissension with members of the family, danger from enemies. 

Jupiter (Sagittarius or Pisces) - Gain of wealth and grains, happiness from wife, honours from the king, name and fame. 

Saturn (Capricorn or Aquarius)-Loss of wealth, mental agony, abandonment of the home land on account of association with prostitutes. 

एर्ं प्राज्ञैि तर्ज्ञेयं कालचक्रदशाफलम् । अिदवशाफलं चैर् र्ामक्षेऽप्येर्मेर् च ॥ ५६॥ इदं फलं मया प्रोक्तं धमाऽधमवकृ िं पुिा । ित्सर्ं पाणणथभतनवत्यं प्राप्यिे नाऽर संशयाः ॥ ५७॥ सुहृदोऽिदवशा भव्या पापस्याष्टप द्वद्वजोत्तम । शुभस्याष्टप रिपोिैर्मशुभा च प्रकीतिविा ॥ ५८॥ 

56-58. The Sage said to Maitreya- O Brahmin! The effects of Antardasa in the Kalachakra Dasha which have been described above are based on Savya chakra. The effects of Antardasa in the Dasha of rāśhis in Apsavya chakra have to be assessed after taking into account the benefice and malefic natures of the lords of the rāśhis. People have to enjoy the good or suffer the bad results according to their good or bad actions in the previous births. Everybody suffers or enjoys accordingly. The peculiarity in this respect is that inauspicious results have been ascribed to malefic. But if during the Antardasa if the planet concerned be a friend of the lord of the Dasha, the results of the Antardasa will be favourable. If the planet concerned be a benefice but an enemy of the lord of the Dasha, his Antardasa effects will not prove favourable. This is how the Antardasa effects have to be analysed and conclusion arrived at. 

# अथ कालचक्रनिांशदशाफलाध्यायः ॥६५॥

# Chapter 65. Effects of Dasha of Rashi in Aries Amsa

मेर्षे थु िक्थजा पीदा व्र्र्षभे ढान्यर्ध्यढवनम् । 

तमठु ने ज्ञानष्टव्र्ध्यढि कके ढनपथथभवर्ेथ् ॥ १॥ 

ससंहभे शथ्रुबाढा स्याथ् कन्यायां चथ्रीजनाथ् सुखम् । 

थुलभे िाजमष्टन्द्रथ्रथ्वं ष्टव्र्िके म्र्थ्युथो भयम् ॥ २॥ 

अठव लाभो भर्ेच्चापे मेर्षस्य नर्भागके । 

फलमेर्ं तर्जानीयं धशाकाले ण्डर्ध्जोथ्थम ॥ ३॥ 

1-3. The following will be the effects in the Dasha of Rashi in Aries Amsa-Aries-Distress from diseases caused by blood pollution. 

Taurus-Increase in grain production. 

Gemini-Dawn of knowledge (ज्ञानोदय) 

Cancer-Increase in wealth. 

Leo-Danger from enemies. 

Virgo-Happiness from wife. 

Libra-Ministership. 

Scorpio-Danger of death. 

Sagittarius-Gains of wealth. 

मकिे पापकमाणण कु म्भे र्ाणणज्यथो ढनम् । 

मीने सर्ाठव ससष्टध्यढि ष्टव्र्िके र्तिथो भयम् ॥ ४॥ 

थुलभे िाजपूजा च कन्यायां शथ्रुथो भयम् । 

कके पथ्नीजने कष्णिं ससंहभे नेथ्रपीदनम् ॥ ५॥ 

तमठु ने तर्र्षथो भीथथव्र्र्षवस्य नर्मांशके । 

4-5½: The following will be the effects in the Dasha of rāśhis in the Taurus Amsa-

Capricorn-Tendency to indulge in sinful action 

Aquarius-Profits in business. 

Pisces-Success in all ventures. 

Scorpio-Danger from fire 

Libra-Honours from the king 

Virgo- Danger from enemies 

Cancer-Distress to wife. 

Leo-Eye troubles. 

Gemini-Danger from poison. 

व्र्र्षभे ढनलाभाः चठान्मेर्षे थु ज्विसंभर्ाः ॥ ६॥ 

मीने च माथुलप्रीथथाः कु म्भे शथ्रुप्रर्ढवनम् । 

मकिे चोिथो भीथथिापे तर्ध्यातर्र्ढवनम् ॥ ७॥ 

मेर्षे थु शचथ्रसंघाथो व्र्र्षे थु कलहो भर्ेथ् । 

तमठु ने सुखमाप्नोथथ तमठु नांशे फलं स्तथ्वधम् ॥ ८॥ 

6-8: The following will be the effects in the Dasha of rāśhis in Gemini Amsa-Taurus-Gains of wealth 

Aries- Fever. 

Pisces - Affectionate relations with maternal uncle. 

Aquarius - Increase in enemies. 

Capricorn - Danger from thieves. 

Sagittarius - Progress in education 

Aries - Assaults from enemies. 

Taurus - Quarrels 

Gemini - Happiness. 

ककव िे सुखमाप्नोथथ ससंहे भूपालथो भयम् । 

कन्यायां बन्द्रढु थाः सौख्यं थुलभे कीथथवमाप्नुयाथ् ॥ ९॥ 

ष्टव्र्िके च ष्टपथुाः कष्णिं चापे ज्ञानढनागमाः । 

मकिे थ्वयशो लोके कु म्भे र्ाणणज्यथाः क्षथथाः ॥ १०॥ 

मीने सुखमाप्नोथथ ककांशे फलमीध्यर्शम् । 

9-10½: The following effects will be experienced in the Dasha of rāśhis in Cancer Amsa-

Cancer-Enjoyments. 

Leo - Danger from the king. 

Virgo-Happiness from kinsmen.

Scorpio-Distress from father.

ष्टव्र्िके कलहाः पीदा थुलभे सुखसम्पधाः ॥ ११॥ 

कन्यायां ढनढान्यातन कके पशुगणाध् भयम् । 

ससंहे सुखं च धुाःखं च तमठु ने शथ्रुर्ढवनम् ॥ १२॥ 

व्र्र्षे च सुखसम्पष्टथ्थाः मेर्षे कष्णिमर्ाप्नुयाथ् । 

मीने थु धीघवयाथ्रा स्याथ् ससंहांशे फलमीध्यर्शम् ॥ १३॥ 

11-13. The following will be the effects in the Dasha, of rāśhis in Leo Amsa-Scorpio-Quarrels, distress. 

Libra - Gain of wealth, happiness. 

Virgo-Increase in wealth and grains. 

Cancer-Danger from animals. 

Leo - Both happiness and sorrows. 

Gemini - Increase in enemies. 

Taurus - Gain of property, happiness. 

Aries - Distress. 

Pisces - Long journey. 

कु म्भभे ढनलाभाः स्यान्मकिेऽष्टप ढनागमाः । 

चापे भ्राथ्र्जनाथ् सौख्यं मेर्षे माथ्र्सुखं र्धेथ् ॥ १४॥ 

व्र्र्षभे पुथ्रसौख्यं च तमठु ने शथ्रुथो भयम् । 

कके धािजनैाः प्रीथथाः ससंहे व्याष्टढतर्र्ढवनम् ॥ १५॥ 

कन्यायां च सुथोथ्पष्टथ्थाः कन्यांशे फलमीध्यर्शम् । 

14-15½: The following will be the effects in the Dasha, of rāśhis in Virgo Amsa-Aquarius-Gain of wealth.

थुलभे ढनसम्पष्टथ्थव्र्श्वश्रचके भ्राथ्र्थाः सुखम् ॥ १६॥ 

ष्टपथ्र्र्गवसुखं चापे माथ्र्कष्णिं म्र्गे र्धेथ् । 

कु म्भे र्ाणणज्यथो लाभं मीने च सुखसम्पधम् ॥ १७॥ 

ष्टव्र्िके च चथ्रीयााः पीदा थुले च जलथो भयम् । 

# कन्यायां सुखसम्पष्टथ्थिुलांशे फलमीध्यर्शम् ॥ १८॥

मेर्षे थु िक्थजा पीदा मीने च सुखमाथधशेथ् । 

कु म्भे र्ाणणज्यथो लाभो मकिे च ढनसक्षथाः ॥ २०॥ 

चापे च सुखसम्पष्टथ्थव्र्श्वश्रचकांशे फलं स्तथ्वधम् ।

मेर्षे च ढनलाभाः स्याथ् व्र्र्षे भूतमतर्र्ध्यढवनम् ॥ २१॥

मीनभे धीघवयाथ्रा स्याथ् कु म्भे ढनतर्र्ढवनम् । 

मकिे सर्वससष्टध्यढाः स्याच्चापे ज्ञानतर्र्ढवनम् ॥ २७॥

तमठु ने सुखसम्पष्टथ्थाः कु म्भांशे फलमीध्यर्शम् ॥ २८॥

थथाः शुभमर्ाप्नोथथ थध्यधशायां न संशयाः ॥ ३२॥ 

32. There is no doubt that observance of remedial measures in the form of prescribed religious rites destroy the evil effects of the inauspicious Dasha and yield happiness. 

Dictionary of Astrology 

-J. N. Bhasin 

A unique and bold attempt, first of its kind, to compile an exhaustive Astrological Dictionary. 

You will be proud of owning such a useful book. Always a Guide and Companion in your pursuits of the unknown future. 

# अठाष्तकिगाढ्यायः ॥ ६६॥

# Chapter 66. Ashtaka Varga

भगर्न् भर्थाऽख्याथं ग्रहभार्ाथधजं फलम् । 

बहुनाष्टम्र्र्षर्याणामाचायाणां च सम्मथम् ॥ १॥ 

संकिाथ् थथ्फलानां च ग्रहाणां गथथसङ्किाथ् । 

इथ्ठमेर्ेथथ नो सर्े ज्ञाथ्वा र्क्थुमलं निााः ॥ २॥ 

कलौ पापिथानां च मन्धा बुष्टध्यढयुवथो न्द्रर्णाम् । 

अथोऽल्पबुष्टध्यढगम्यं यथ् शाचथ्रमेथध् र्धस्य मे ॥ ३॥ 

थथ्थथ्कालग्रहष्टचठथ्या मानर्ानां परिस्फु िम् । 

सुखधुाःखपरिज्ञानमायुर्षो तनणवयं थठा ॥ ४॥ 

1-4. Maitreya said-O Venerable Sage! You have described many kinds of effects relating to the planets and Bhavas houses) after incorporating the views of many sages and Acharya (learneds) but it is not possible to say with certainty if particular effect is quite correct after considering the contradictions in the effects by the movements of the various planets. As because of sinful deeds committed by people in Kaliyuga, their minds have become blunt, be kind enough to describe a method which would enable even the shallow minded persons to ascertain their happiness and sorrows and determine their longevity on the basis of the positions of the planets in transit. 

साढु प्त्ऱर्ष्णिं थ्वया ब्रह्मन् कठयातम थर्ाग्रथाः । 

लोके याथ्रापरिज्ञानमायुर्षो तनणवयं थठा ॥ ५॥ 

संकिस्यातर्िोढञ्च शाचथ्रस्याष्टप प्रयोजनम् । 

जनानामुपकािाठं सार्ढानमनााः श्त्र्णु ॥ ६॥ 

5-6: The sage replied-O Brahmin! You have put a very intelligent question. I will now describe the Shastra for the benefit of all-the Shastra in which there will be no contradictions in judging the effects of happiness and sorrows and for determination of the longevity. You now listen to me carefully: 

लग्नाथधव्ययपयविं भार्ा संज्ञानुरूपथाः । 

फलधााः शुभसंध्यर्ष्णिा युक्था र्ा शोभना मथााः ॥ ७॥ 

थे थूच्चाथधभगैाः खेिैनव चािारिभनीचगैाः । 

पापैध्यर्र्ष्वियुथा भार्ााः कल्याणेथिधायकााः ॥ ८॥ 

R:enRReRp: एर्ं समान्यथाः प्रोक्थं होिाशाचथ्रज्ञसूरिथभाः ॥ ९॥ मयैयथ् सकलं प्रोक्थं पूर्ाचायानुर्थथवना । आयुि लोकयाथ्रां च शाचथ्रस्यास्यथे प्रयोजनम् ॥ १०॥ तनिेथुं थन्न सक्नोथथ र्ससष्टो र्ा ब्त्र्हस्पथथाः । ष्टकं पुनमवनुजािथ्र तर्शेर्षाथ्थु कलौ युगे ॥ ११॥ 

7-11. If the twelve houses including the Ascendant are occupied by or aspected by benefice planets, they yield auspicious results according to their characteristics but this happens where the planets concerned are in their sign of exaltation, own sign or posited in a benefice house. There will be no good effects if such planets are in depression or posited in an inauspicious house. Similarly, the houses associated with or aspected by malefic in depression or posited in malefic houses, yield adverse results according to their characteristics. If such planets be in their signs of exaltation, the effects will not be adverse. This is how the general effects have been described by the Daivajnas. I have only repeated those effects. The main purposes of this Shastra (astrology) are to determine the longevity and joys and sorrows of the people but because the movements of the planets are so subtle, even sages like Vashista and Brihaspati have not been able to be quite definite in this respect. Then how can a common man, particularly in Kaliyuga a can do so. 

लग्नाथधव्ययपयविं भार्ा संज्ञानुरूपथाः । फलधााः शुभसंध्यर्ष्णिा युक्था र्ा शोभना मथााः ॥ ७॥ थे थूच्चाथधभगैाः खेिैनव चािारिभनीचगैाः । पापैध्यर्र्ष्वियुथा भार्ााः कल्याणेथिधायकााः ॥ ८॥ एर्ं समान्यथाः प्रोक्थं होिाशाचथ्रज्ञसूरिथभाः ॥ ९॥ मयैयथ् सकलं प्रोक्थं पूर्ाचायानुर्थथवना । आयुि लोकयाथ्रां च शाचथ्रस्यास्यथे प्रयोजनम् ॥ १०॥ तनिेथुं थन्न सक्नोथथ र्ससष्टो र्ा ब्त्र्हस्पथथाः । ष्टकं पुनमवनुजािथ्र तर्शेर्षाथ्थु कलौ युगे ॥ ११॥ 

12. There are two divisions or parts of the Jyotish Shastra (Science of Astrology), namely, general and particular. I have already dealt with the general part. I now come to the other part which deals with this subject in particular. 

यठा लग्नाच्च चन्ध्राच्च ग्रहाणां भार्जं फलम् । थठाऽन्येभ्योऽष्टप खेिेभ्यो तर्श्रचन्थ्यं धैर्तर्र्ध्िैाः ॥ १३॥ 

अथो िव्याथधखेिानां सलग्नानां प्त्ऱर्ठक् प्त्ऱर्ठक् । अष्णिानां सर्वभार्ोथ्ठं यठोक्थमशुभं शुभम् ॥ १४॥ ज्ञाथ्वाऽधौ किणं चठानं तबन्धुिेखोपलसक्षथम् । क्रमाधष्णिकर्गवस्य र्ाच्यं स्पष्णिफलं यठा ॥ १५॥ 

13-15: As the effects of the twelve houses are judged from the Ascendant and the Moon, effects of the twelve houses and the various planets are judged in the same manner. Therefore, the inauspicious places (houses) named as Karana (करण) from the seven planets beginning from the Sun and the Ascendant (total 8) should be marked by dots (bindus) and auspicious places named as Sthan (िान) by small vertical lines (rekhas) and on the basis of their assessment should the judgment of the horoscope and predictions he made. 

Notes: The above arrangement is known as Ashtakaa Varga. The meaning of Ashtaka-Varga is literally the group of 8 things. In other words, it is the combination of the good and bad positions of a planet with reference to the 7 planets and the Ascendant (8 things). So, it is the combination of the benefice and malefic marks (rekhas and bindus) in a planet's chart with reference to the position of the 8 planets (here Ascendant is to be treated as a planet). 

Ashtaka Varga of the Sun 

थथुस्वायुष्टचथ्ररिष्फे र्षु पञ्च कामे सुखेऽणवर्ााः । अिौ भाग्ये थ्रयाः पुथ्रे र्षि् किौ खे भर्े च भूाः ॥ १६॥ 

16. Five planets in 1st, 2nd, 8th, 3rd and the 12th houses from the Sun are Karana-Prada (dot significator). Similarly, 4 planets in the, 7th and 4th; three planets the 6th and 9th; six planets in the 5th; 2 planets in the 10th and one (planet in the 11th) are dot significator. 

लग्नेन्धुजीर्शुक्रज्ञािनौ स्वे मिणेऽष्टप च । ितर्भौमाष्टकव चन्ध्राया व्यये ज्ञेन्धुससथायकााः ॥ १७॥ सुखे होिेन्धुशुक्राि ढमेऽकाष्टकव कु जा अिौ । होिाज्ञायेन्धर्ाः कामे भर्े धैथ्येन्ध्रपूसजथाः ॥ १८॥ सहजेऽकाष्टकव शुक्रायवभौमााः खे गुरुभागवर्ौ । सुथेऽकाकीन्धुलग्नािशुक्रााः स्युाः किणं िर्ेाः ॥ १९॥ 

17-19. Thus the Ascendant, Moon, Jupiter, Venus and Mercury five planets) in the 1st, 2nd and 8th from the Sun; the Sun, Mars, Saturn, Moon and Jupiter (5 planets) in the 12th: Mercury, Moon, Venus, Jupiter (4 planets) in the 4th; the Ascendant, Moon, Venus (3) in the 9th; the Sun, Saturn and Mars (3) in the 6th; Lagna, Mercury, Jupiter, Moon (4) in the 7th; Venus (1) in the 11th the Sun, Saturn, Venus, 

Jupiter, Mars ( 5) in the 3rd; Jupiter, Venus (2) in the 10th; the Sun, Saturn. Moon, Ascendant Mars and Venus (6) in the 5th are Karana-Prada or dot indicators. 

Notes: To identify the auspicious and in auspicious houses in the Ashtaka-Varga, a chart should be prepared with 14 horizontal lines and ten vertical lines. The form of the chart so prepared will consist of 117 apartments (कोष्ठक). In this chart in the first line (horizontally) incorporate the names of the seven planets and the Ascendant. In the first column (vertically) write the numbers of all the 12 houses. After this mark dots under the planet and against the Karana-Prada houses. By doing so the Karan-Prada houses of all the 8 planets including the Ascendant will become known clearly and whenever the Ashtaka Varga planet will pass in transit the dot marked houses, he will yield unfavourable results. In his transit to other houses he would give favourable effects. The following table shows the dots in the Ashtaka Varga of the Sun. 

Chart Showing Dots in the Sun's Ashtaka Varga

It will be seen that there are dots in the 3rd, 5th, 6th and 12th houses from the Sun. Therefore, those four houses are inauspicious, that is, unfavourable results will be derived whenever the natal Sun transits those four houses from him. The transit results to, other houses, namely 1, 2, 4, 7, 8, 9, 10 and 11 will not be unfavourable. Similarly, the results of transit of the Sun in 3, 5, 6, 12 from Mars and Saturn and in 1, 2, 4, 5, 7, 8, 9, 12 from the Moon will be unfavourable. Similar assessment bas to be made in case of dots under other planets in the above chart. Transit of the Sun to other places without dots will not produce unfavourable effects. 

Ashtaka Varga or the Moon 

भाग्यस्वयोि र्षद् र्ेश्मष्टम्र्थहोिासु पञ्च च । 

मानधुसिक्ययोिेकाः सुथे र्ेधा अरिष्टचथ्रयोाः ॥ २०॥ 

थ्रयो व्ययेष्णिार्ाये च शून्यं शीथकिस्य थु । 

होिाकािाष्टकव भ्र्गर्ोङ्गज्ञाके न्ध्वाकव भागवर्ााः ॥ २१॥ 

जीर्ोकाकीन्धुलग्नािा होिेन्धुगुरुभास्किााः । 

ससथज्ञायााः कु जथनुमन्धािे ससथशीथगू ॥ २२॥ 

20-22. In the Moon's Ashtaka Varga, 6 planets in the 9th and the 2nd: 5 planets in the 4th, 8th and the 1st: one planet in the 10th and the 3rd: 4 planets in the 5th: 3 planets in the 6th and the 7th and 11th: eight (7 planets and Ascendant) in the 12th are Karan-Prada (dot significator). Thus, the Ascendant, the Sun, Mars, Saturn and Venus, these five in the 1st: The Ascendant, Mercury, the Sun, the Moon, Saturn and Venus, these 6 in the 2nd: Jupiter in the 3rd: The Sun, Saturn, the Moon, the Ascendant and Mars, these five in the 4th; the Ascendant, the Moon, Jupiter and the Sun, these 4 in the 5th: Venus. Mercury and Jupiter, these 3 in the 6th: Mars, the Ascendant and Saturn, these 3 in the 7th: Mars, the Ascendant, Saturn. Venus and the Moon, these five in the 8th: The Ascendant, the Sun, Mars, Saturn, Mercury and Jupiter, these 6 in the 9th: Saturn only in the 10th: none in the 11th: all the eight in the 12th from their own places are Karan-Prada (dot significator). These planets in the other houses are Rekhaprada (line significator). 

Chart showing dots in the Moon's Ashtaka Varga

Notes: The above chart indicates that in the birth chart when the Moon transits to the 1st, the 2nd, the 4th, the 5th, the 9th and the 12th from the natal Sun, the effects produced will be unfavourable. The results will not be unfavourable by the Moon's transit to other houses from the Sun. The results will be unfavourable when the Moon 

transits 1, 2, 4, 5, 7, 8, 9 and 12 from the Ascendant. For the remaining houses (3, 6, 10, 11), the transit results will be favourable. 

Ashtaka Varga of Mars 

होिाकािाष्टकव तर्ज्जीर्ााः शतनाः खं सकलााः क्रमाथ् । व्ययर्ेश्मसुथचथ्रीर्षु र्षद् सप्त्ऱथ ढनढमवयोाः ॥ २३॥ होिाम्र्थ्युर्ोाः शिा र्ेधा तर्क्रमे खे थ्रयाः क्षथे । र्ध्ौ भर्े शून्यमेर्ं स्याथ् किणं भूतमजस्य थु ॥ २४ कु जस्याके न्धुतर्ज्जीर्ससथ लग्नशनी च थु । ससथािगुरुमन्धााः स्युढवमोक्थेर्षु कु जं तर्ना ॥ २५॥ चन्ध्रािगुरुशुक्राष्टकव लग्नातन कु जभास्किी । ज्ञेन्ध्वकव ससथलग्नाया एर्षु शुक्रं तर्ना थथाः ॥ २६॥ तर्ना शतनं सप्त्ऱथ ढमे ससथेन्धुज्ञा तर्यथ्थथाः । अकाष्टकव ज्ञेन्धुलग्नािााः किणं प्रोच्यथे क्रमाथ् ॥ २७ 

23-27. In the Ashtaka Varga of Mars 6 planets in the 12th, the 4th, the 5th and the 7th: 7 planets in the 2nd and the 9th: 5 planets in the 1st and the 8th: 4 planets in the 3rd: 3 planets in the 10th and 2 planets in the 6th are Karana-Prada (dot significator). In the 11th no planet is Karana-Prada. In other words, all the planets in the 11th from their own places are Rekhaprada (line significator). Thus the Sun, the Moon, Mercury, Jupiter and Venus, these five in the 1st: the Ascendant, the Sun, the Moon, the Mercury, Jupiter and Saturn, these 7 in the 2nd: Venus, Mars, Jupiter and Saturn, these 4 in the 3rd: the Sun, the Moon, Mercury, Jupiter, Venus and the Ascendant, these 6 in the 4th: the Moon, Mars, Jupiter, Venus, and the Ascendant, these 5 in the 5th: Mars and Saturn, these 2 in the 6th: Mercury, the Moon, the Sun, Venus, Jupiter and the Ascendant, these 6 in the 7th: Mercury the Moon, the Sun, the Ascendant and Jupiter, these five in the 8th: the Sun, the Moon, Mars, Mercury, Jupiter, Venus and the Ascendant, these 7 in the 9th: Venus, the Moon and Mercury, these 3 in the 10th: none in the 11th: the Sun, Saturn, Mercury, the Moon, the Ascendant and Mars, these 6 in the 12th, from their own places are Karana-Prada (dot significator)

Notes: The Chart indicates that inauspicious effects will be derived whenever Mars transits the 1st, 2nd, 4th, 5th, 7th, 8th, 9th and 12th houses from the natal Sun. The results of transits in other houses namely the 3rd, 6th, 10th and 11th will be favourable. 

# Ashtaka Varga or Mercury

थनुस्वग्र्हकमारिढमेष्वगग्नम्र्गौ किौ । 

भ्राथ्र्ि्रियो िसा लाभे शून्यं पुथ्रे व्यये शिााः ॥ २८॥ 

बुढास्यके न्धुगुिर्ो गुरुसूयवबुढााः क्रमाथ् । 

लग्नाकािाष्टकव चन्ध्राया ज्ञाकाया द्वह बुढस्य थु ॥ २९॥ 

जीर्ािेन्ध्वाष्टकव लग्नातन शुक्रमन्नढिासुथााः । 

ज्ञेन्धुलग्नाकव शुक्राया ज्ञाकौ जीर्ेन्धुलग्नकााः ॥ ३०॥ 

अकायवशुक्राः शून्यं च होिेन्ध्वािाष्टकव भागवर्ााः । 

28-30½: In the Ashtaka Varga of Mercury 3 planets in the 1st, the 2nd, the 4th, the 10th, the 6th and the 9th: 2 planets in the 8th: 6 planets in the 3rd and the 7th: none in the 11th: 5 planets in the 5th and the 12th are Karana-Prada (dot significator). Thus the Sun, the Moon and Jupiter, these 3 in the 1st: Jupiter, the Sun and Mercury, these 3 in the 2nd: the Ascendant, the Sun, Mars, Saturn, the Moon and Jupiter, these 6 in the 3rd: Mercury, the Sun and Jupiter, these 3 in the 4th: Jupiter, Mars, the Moon, Saturn and the Ascendant, these 5 in the 5th: Venus, Saturn and Mars, these 3 in the 6th: Mercury, the Moon, the Ascendant, the Sun, Venus and Jupiter, these 6 in the 7th: Mercury and the Sun, these 2 in the 8th: Jupiter, the Moon and the Ascendant, these 3 in the 9th: the Sun, Jupiter and Venus, these 3 in the 10th: none in the 11th: the Ascendant, the Moon, Mars, Saturn and Venus these 5 in the 12th from their own places are Karana-Prada (dot significator).

Notes: This chart indicates that the houses with dots are inauspicious and the others are auspicious. 

Ashtaka Varga of Jupiter 

रूपं ढनाययोाः खे र्ध्ौ व्यये सप्त्ऱथ क्षथेऽणवर्ााः ॥ ३१॥ 

ष्टम्र्थतर्क्रमयो पञ्च गुिोाः शेर्षेर्षु र्खन्हयाः । 

लग्ने शुक्रे न्धुमन्धााः स्वे आये मन्धि तर्क्रमे ॥ ३२॥ 

लग्नािेन्धुज्ञभ्र्गर्ाः सुथेकायवकु जा ग्र्हे । 

शुक्रमन्धेन्धर्ो ध्यूने बुढशुक्रशनैििााः ॥ ३३॥ 

जीर्ािाके न्धर्ाः शथ्रौ सर्े मन्धं तर्ना व्यये । 

कमवणीन्धुशनी ढमे मन्धािगुिर्ो म्र्गौ ॥ ३४॥ 

लग्नाष्टकव ससथचन्ध्रज्ञााः किणं च गुिोरिधम् । 

31-34½: In the Ashtaka-Varga of Jupiter one planet in the 2nd and the 11th, 2 planets in the 10th, 7 planets in the 12th, 4 planets in the 6th, 5 planets in the 8th and the 3rd, 3 planets in the remaining houses (1st, 4th, 5th, 7th, 9th) are Karana-Prada (dot significator). Thus Venus, the Moon and Saturn, these 3 in the 1st: Saturn in the 2nd and 11th: the Ascendant, Mars, the Moon, Mercury and Venus, these 5 in the 3rd: the Sun, Jupiter and Mars, these 3 in the 5th Venus, Saturn and the Moon, these 3 in 4th: Mercury, Venus and Saturn, these 3 in the 7th: Jupiter, Mars, the Sun and the Moon, these 4 in the 6th: all except Saturn, these 7 in the 12th: the Moon and Saturn, these 2 in the 10th: Saturn, Mars and Jupiter, these 3 in the 9th: the Ascendant, Saturn, Venus, the Moon and Mercury, these five in the 8th, from their own places are Karana-Prada (dot significator).

Ashtaka Varga of Venus 

<table><tr><td>सुधागुविक्योर्वेयँ अनुस्थल्तागर्षेयँ जिकुँ Ⅱ 3511</td></tr><tr><td>अकली सिंधागारी दये शूडँमे मिंधाशँ 5611 खँ बोँ Ⅰ</td></tr><tr><td>लप्र सरेयसकार्वेयँ विकुँ जिकुँ Ⅱ 3611</td></tr><tr><td>अकलो किसिकार्वेयँ विकुँसकार्वेयँ विकुँ Ⅰ</td></tr><tr><td>सुधागुविक्योर्वेयँ सूडँमे मिंधाशँ 5611 Ⅱ 3611</td></tr><tr><td>सुधागुविक्योर्वेयँ विकुँसकार्वेयँ विकुँ Ⅰ</td></tr><tr><td>सुधागुविक्योर्वेयँ विकुँसकार्वेयँ विकुँ Ⅱ 3611</td></tr><tr><td>सुधागुविक्योर्वेयँ विकुँसकार्वेयँ विकुँ Ⅰ</td></tr><tr><td>सुधागुविक्योर्वेयँ विकुँसकार्वेयँ विज् चये Ⅱ 3611</td></tr><tr><td>सुधागुविक्योर्वेयँ विकुँसकार्वेयँ विज् Ⅰ</td></tr><tr><td>सुधागुविक्योर्वेयँ विकुँसकार्वेयँ विज् Ⅱ</td></tr><tr><td>सुधागुविक्योर्वेयँ विकुँसकार्वेयँ विज् Ⅲ</td></tr></table>

35-38. In the Ashtaka Varga of Venus, 2 planets in the 5th, the 8th and the 3rd, 5 planets in the 1st, the 2nd, the 12th, the 10th, 8 planets in the 7th, 6 planets in the 6th, one in the 9th, 3 in the 4th, none in the 11th are Karana-Prada. Thus the sun, Mars, Mercury, Jupiter and Saturn, these 5 in the 1st and the 2nd: all the 8 planets (including the Ascendant) in the 7th: Jupiter and the Sun. these 2 in the 3rd: The Sun and Mars, these 2 in the 5th: the Sun in the 2nd: the Sun, Mercury and Jupiter, these 3 in the 4th Mars and Mercury, these 2 in the 8th: Venus, the Sun, the Moon, Saturn, the Ascendant and Jupiter, these 6 in the 6th: none in the 11th: the Ascendant, Saturn, Mercury, Venus and Jupiter, these 5 in the 12th: the Ascendant, Mars, Mercury, the Moon, the Sun, these 5 in the 10th, from their own places are Karana-Prada (Bindu or dot Significator). 

Chart showing dots in the Ashtaka Varga of Venus
