By performing these remedial measures, he will not -only beget a son, the lineage of family will also be prolonged. 

Yogas for lack of male Issue as result of the curse of the brother in the previous birth 

अथो योगान् प्रर्क्ष्यातम भ्रािृशापसमुद्भर्ान् । यज्ज्ञात्वाऽपत्यिक्षाथं यत्नं कु याद् तर्चक्षणाः ॥ ५१॥ भ्रािृिानाथधपे पुरे कु जिाहुसमन्तििे । पुरलग्नेश्विौ िन्ध्रे भ्रािृशापाि् सुिक्षयाः ॥ ५२॥ लग्ने सुिे कु जे मन्दे भ्रािृपे भाग्यिासशगे । कािके नाशभार्िे भ्रािृशापाि् सुिक्षयाः ॥ ५३॥ भ्रािृिाने गुरुनीचे मन्दाः पञ्चमगिे यद्वद । नाशिाने िु चन्द्रािौ भ्रािृशापाि् सुिक्षयाः ॥ ५४॥ िनुिानाथधपे रिष्फे भौमाः पञ्चमगो यद्वद । िन्ध्रे सपापपुरेशे भ्रािृशापाि् सुिक्षयाः ॥ ५५॥ पापमध्यगिे लग्ने पापमध्ये सुिेऽष्टप च । लग्नेशपुरपौ दाःिौ ु भ्रािृशापाि् सुिक्षयाः ॥ ५६॥ 

कमेशे भ्रािृभार्िे पापयुक्ते िथा शुभे । 

पुरगे कु जसंयुक्ते भ्रािृशापाि् सुिक्षयाः ॥ ५७॥ 

पुरिाने बुधक्षेरे शतमिाहुसमन्तििे । 

रिष्फे तर्दािौ तर्ज्ञेयो भ्रािृशापाि् सुिक्षयाः ॥ ५८॥ 

लग्नेशे भ्रािृभार्िे भ्रािृिानाथधपे सुिे । 

लग्नभ्रािृसुिे पापे भ्रािृशापाि् सुिक्षयाः ॥ ५९॥ 

भ्रारीशे मृत्युभार्िे पुरिे कािके िथा । 

िाहुमन्देयुिे दृष्टे भ्रािृशापाि् सुिक्षयाः ॥ ६०॥ 

नाशिानाथधपे पुरे भ्रािृनाथेन संयुिे । 

िन्ध्रे आिाष्टकव संयुक्ते भ्रािृशापाि् सुिक्षयाः ॥ ६१॥ 

51-61: A person will be without a male issue as result or the curse of the brother, if at birth-

(1) The lord of the 3rd with Rahu and Mars is in the 5th and the lords of the Ascendant and the 5th are in the 8th. 

(2) The Ascendant and the 5th are occupied by Mars and. Saturn respectively, the lord of the 3rd is in the 9th, and Mars the significator for brothers is in the 8th, 

(3) Jupiter in his sign of debilitation is in the 3rd, Saturn is in the 5th and the Moon and Mars are in the 8th. 

(4) The lord of the Ascendant is in the 12th, Mars is in the 5th and the lord of the 5th associated with a malefic is in the 8th, 

(5) The Ascendant and the 5th house are hemmed in between malefic and the lord of the Ascendant and the 5th are in the 6th, the 8th or the 12th, 

(6) The 3rd is occupied by the lord of the 10th along with a malefic and a benefice is with Mars in the 5th, 

(7) The 5th house in a sign of Mercury is occupied by Saturn and Rahu and Mercury and Mars are in the 12th, 

(8) The 3rd is occupied by the lord of the Ascendant, the lord of the 3rd occupies the 5th and the Ascendant, the 3rd and the 5th houses are with malefic, 

(9) The lord of the 3rd is in the 8th, and Jupiter is associated with Saturn in the 5th, and 

(10) The lord of the 8th is in the 5th along with the lord of the 3rd and Mars and Saturn are in the 8th. 

Remedial measures for getting deliverance from the brother's curse 

भ्रािृशापतर्मोक्षाथं र्ंशस्य िर्णं हिेाः । 

चान्द्राय्सं चिेि् पिाि् कार्ेय्या तर्ष्णुसगन्नधौ ॥ ६२॥ 

अश्वत्थिापनं कु याद् दशधेनूि दापयेि् । 

पत्नीहस्तेन पुरेच्छु भूवतमं दद्याि् फलान्तििाम् ॥ ६३॥ 

एर्ं याः कु रुिे भक्त्या धमवपत्न्ा समन्तििाः । 

ध्रुर्ं िस्य भर्ेि् पुराः कु लर्ृणद्धि जायिे ॥ ६४॥ 

62-64: The person concerned will, without doubt, get release from the curse, will be blessed with a son and the prolongation of his family lineage will be ensured if the following remedial measures are adopted-

(1) He should observe the Chandra Yana fast after listening to Haribansa Purana, 

(2) He should plant a sapling of pipal in front of Saligram (शालीराम) on the banks of the Caveri River or on the Ganges or Mahanadi and offer prayers to it, 

(3) He should give 10 cows in charity through his wife, 

(4) He should give in charity land with mango trees planted on it. 

Yoga for lack of male Issue as a result of the curse of maternal uncle in the previous birth 

पुरिाने बुधे जीर्े कु जिाहुसमन्तििे । 

लग्ने मन्दे सुिभार्ो ज्ञेयो मािुलशापिाः ॥ ६५॥ 

लग्नेपुरेश्विौ पुरे बुधभौमाष्टकव संयुिौ । 

ज्ञेयं मािुलशापत्वाज्जनस्य सितिक्षयाः ॥ ६६॥ 

लुप्ते पुराथधपे लग्ने सप्तमे भानुनन्दने । 

लग्नेशे बुधसंयुक्ते िस्याष्टप सितिक्षयाः ॥ ६७॥ 

ज्ञातििानाथधपे लग्ने व्ययेशेन समन्तििे । 

शसशसौम्यकु जे पुरे तर्ज्ञेयाः सितिक्षयाः ॥ ६८॥ 

65-68: A person will be without a male issue as a result of the curse of the maternal uncle, if at birth-

(1) The 5th house is occupied by Mercury, Jupiter, Mars and Rahu and Saturn is in the Ascendant, 

(2) The 5th is occupied by the lords of the Ascendant and the 5th along with Saturn, Mars and Mercury, 

(3) The Ascendant is occupied by a combust lord of the 6th (perhaps the Sun will also be there), Saturn is in the 7th, and the lord of the Ascendant is associated with Mercury, and 

(4) Lords of the Ascendant and the 4th are in the Ascendant and the Moon, Mercury and Mars are in the 5th. 

िद्दोर्षपरिहािाथं तर्ष्णुिापिमाचिेि् । 

र्ापीकू पिडागाद्वदखननं सुिबन्धुनम् ॥ ६९॥ 

पुरर्ृणद्धभवर्ेत्तस्य संपद्वणद्धाः ृ प्रजायिे । 

इति योगर्शादेर्ं शान्तिं कु याद् तर्चक्षणाः ॥ ७०॥ 

69-70: To get release from the curse and for being blessed with a son and for ensuring the prolongation of the lineage of the family, the following remedial measures are to' be adopted-

(1) Installation of an idol of lord Vishnu 

(2) Construction of a deep or ordinary well, dam or reservoir or all of them. 

Yogas for lack of male Issue as a result of curse of Brahmins in the previous birth 

बलगर्व्व यो मत्यो ब्राह्मणानर्मन्यिे । 

िद्दोर्षाद् ब्रह्मशापाच्च िस्य स्याि् सितिक्षयाः ॥ ७१॥ 

गुरुक्षेरे यदा िाहुाः पुरे जीर्ािभानुजााः । 

धमविानाथधपे नाशे ब्रह्मशापाि् सुिक्षयाः ॥ ७२॥ 

धमेशे पुरभार्िे पुरेशे नाशिासशगे । 

जीर्ाििाहुथभयुवक्ते ब्रह्मशापाि् सुिक्षयाः ॥ ७३॥ 

धमवभार्ाथधपे नीचे व्ययेशे पुरभार्गे । 

िाहुयुिेसक्षिे र्ाष्टप ब्रह्मशापाि् सुिक्षयाः ॥ ७४॥ 

जीर्े नीचगिे िाहौ लग्ने र्ा पुरिासशगे । 

पुरिानाथधपे दाःिे ु ब्रह्मशापाि् सुिक्षयाः ॥ ७५॥ 

पुरभार्ाथधपे जीर्े िन्ध्रे पापसमन्तििे । 

पुरेशे साकव चन्द्रे र्ा ब्रह्मशापाि् सुिक्षयाः ॥ ७६॥ 

मन्दांशे मन्दसंयुक्ते जीर्े भौमसमन्तििे । 

पुरेशे व्ययिासशिे ब्रह्मशापाि् सुिक्षयाः ॥ ७७॥ 

लग्ने गुरुयुिे मन्दे भाग्ये िाहुसमन्तििे । 

व्यय र्ा गुरुसंयुक्ते ब्रह्मशापाि् सुिक्षयाः ॥ ७८॥ 

71-78: If a person mad with power and wealth, insults a Brahmin, be remains without a male issue in the next birth. A person will be without male issue as a result of the curse of a Brahmin, if at birth-- 

(1) Rahu is in the sign of Jupiter and Jupiter is in the 5th, 

(2) The lord of the 9th is in the 5th and the lord of the 5th is in the 8th along with Jupiter, Mars and Rahu, 

(3) The lord of the 9th is in his sign of debilitation and the lord of the 12th associated with Rahu is in the 5th. 

(4) Jupiter is in his sign of debilitation, Rahu is in the Ascendant or the 5th and the lord of the 5th is in the 6th, the 8th or the 12th, 

(5) The lord of the 5th and Jupiter associated with malefic are in the 8th or the lord of the 5th associated with the Sun and the Moon is in the 8th, 

(6) Jupiter being in Navamsha of Saturn is associated with Saturn and Mars and the lord of the 5th is in the 12th, and 

(7) Jupiter is associated with Saturn in the Ascendant and I Rahu is in the 9th or Rahu with Jupiter is in the 12th, 

These are yogas which reveal the curse of Brahmin in the previous birth. 

Remedial measures 

िस्य दोर्षस्य शान्त्यथं कु याच्चान्द्रायणं निाः । 

ब्रह्मकृ च्छर त्र्यं कृ त्वा धनुं दद्याि् सदसक्षणाम् ॥ ७९॥ 

पञ्चित्नातन देयातन सुर्णवसद्वहिातन च । 

ब्राह्मणान् भोजयेि् पिाद्यथाशगक्त द्वद्वजोत्तम ॥ ८०॥ 

एर्ं कृ िे िु सत्पुरं लभिे नाऽर संशयाः । 

मुक्तशापो तर्शुद्धात्मा स निाः सुखमेधिे ॥ ८१॥ 

79-81: To obtain relief from the evil effects of the above yogas the remedial measures are-

(1) To observe Chandra Yana fast and to do penance three times and 

(2) To give in charity a cow and five gems with gold after feeding Brahmins according to one's means and giving them presents in cash (दशक्षणा). 

Then the person will be released from the curse and will be endowed with happiness after performing the above remedial measures. 

Yogas for lack of male issue as a result of the curse or the wife in the previous birth 

दािेशे पुरभार्िे दािेशस्यांशपे शनौ । 

पुरेशे नाशिासशिे पत्नीशापाि् सुिक्षयाः ॥ ८२॥ 

नाशसंिे कलरेशे पुरेशे नाशिासशगे । 

कािके पापसंयुक्ते पत्नीशापाि् सुिक्षयाः ॥ ८३॥ 

पुरिानगिे शुक्रे कामपे िन्ध्रमाश्रििे । 

कािके पापसंयुक्ते पत्नीशापाि् सुिक्षयाः ॥ ८४॥ 

कु टुम्बे पापसंयुक्ते कामपे नाशिासशगे । 

पुरे पापग्रहैयुवक्ते पत्नीशापाि् सुिक्षयाः ॥ ८५॥ 

भाग्यिानगिे शुक्रे दािेशे नाशिासशगे । 

लग्ने सुिे च पापढ्ये पत्नीशापाि् सुिक्षयाः ॥ ८६॥ 

भाग्यिानाथधपे शुक्रे पुरेशे शरुिासशगे । 

गुरुलग्नेशदािेशा दाःु िािेि् सितिक्षयाः ॥ ८७॥ 

पुरिाने भृगुक्षेरे िाहुचन्द्रसमन्तििे । 

व्यये लग्ने धने पापे पत्नीशापाि् सुिक्षयाः ॥ ८८॥ 

सप्तमे मन्दशुक्रौ च िन्ध्रेशे पुरभे िर्ौ । लग्ने िाहुसमायुक्ते पत्नीशापाि् सुिक्षयाः ॥ ८९॥ धने कु जे व्यये जीर्े पुरिे भृगुनन्दने । शतनिाहुयुिे दृष्टे पत्नीशापाि् सुिक्षयाः ॥ ९०॥ नाशिौ तर्त्तदािेशौ पुरे लग्ने कु जे शनौ । कािके पापसंयुक्ते पत्नीशापाि् सुिक्षयाः ॥ ९१॥ लग्नपञ्चमभाग्यिा िाहुमन्दकु जााः क्रमाि् । िन्ध्रिौ पुरदािेशौ पत्नीशापाि् सुिक्षयाः ॥ ९२॥ 

82-92: A person does not beget a male issue, as a result of the curse of the wife, if at birth - 

(1) The lord of the Ascendant is in the 5th, Saturn is in the Navamsha of the lord of the 7th and the lord of the 5th is in the 8th, 

(2) The lord of the 7th is in the 8th, the lord of the 12th is in the 5th and Jupiter is associated with a malefic, 

(3) Venus is in the 5th, the lord of the 7th is in, he 8th and the 5th is occupied by a malefic, 

(4) The 2nd and the 5th are occupied by a malefic and the lord of the 7th is in the 8th, 

(5) Venus is in the 9th, the lord of the 7th is in the 8th and the Ascendant and the 5th are occupied by malefics, 

(6) Venus is lord of the 9th, lord of the 5th is an inimical sign and the lord of the Ascendant and 7th and Jupiter are in the 6th, the 8th or the 12th, 

(7) The 5th is Taurus or Libra occupied by the Sun and the Moon and the 12th; the Ascendant and the 2nd are occupied by malefic, 

(8) Saturn and Venus are in the 7th, the lord of the 8th is in the 5th and the Ascendant is occupied by the Sun and Rahu, 

(9) Mars occupies the 2nd, Jupiter is in the 12th and the Venus and Rahu are in the 5th, 

(10) The lords of the 2nd and the 7th are in the 8th, Mars and Saturn occupy the 5th and the Ascendant respectively and Jupiter is associated with a malefic, and 

(11) Rahu is in the Ascendant, Saturn is in the 5th, Mara is in the 9th and the lords of the 5th and the 7th are in the 8th. 

Remedial measures 

शापमुक्त्यै च कन्यायां सत्यां िद्दानमाचिेि् । कन्याभार्े च िीतर्ष्णोमूवतिव लक्ष्मीसमन्तििाम् ॥ ९३॥ दद्याि् स्वणवमयीं तर्प्र दशदेनुसमन्तििाम् । शय्यां च भूर्षणं र्िं दम्पतिभ्यां द्वद्वजन्मनाम् ॥ ९४॥ 

93—94: The person concerned gets release from the curse and is blessed with a son if he performs the marriage of an unmarried girl (Kanyadana), or if such a girl is not available a gold idol of the Lakshminara Yana fertile cow, a bed, ornaments and garments to a Brahmin couple. 

Notes: According to our view 'Kanyadana' does not mean giving a girl in charity but helping in the performance of the marriage of an unmarried girl not his own daughter. 

Yogas for lack of male issue as a result of the curse or a departed soul 

ध्रुर्ं िस्य भर्ेि् पुरो भाग्यर्ृणद्धि जायिे । 

कमवलोपे ष्टपिृणां च प्रेित्वं िस्य जायिे ॥ ९५॥ 

िस्य प्रेिस्य शापाच्च पुराभार्ाः प्रजायिे । 

अिोऽर िादृशान् योगाि् जन्मलग्नाि् प्रर्च्च्म्यहम् ॥ ९६॥ 

पुरिानौ मन्दसूयौ क्षीणचन्द्रि सप्तमे । 

लग्ने व्यये िाहुजीर्ौ प्रेिशापाि् सुिक्षयाः ॥ ९७॥ 

पुरिानाथधपे मन्दे नाशिे लग्नगे कु जे । 

कािके नाशभार्े च प्रेिशापाि् सुिक्षयाः ॥ ९८॥ 

लग्ने पापे व्यये भानौ सुिे चािाष्टकव सोमजााः । 

पुरेशे िन्ध्रभार्िे प्रेिशापाि् सुिक्षयाः ॥ ९९॥ 

लग्ने स्वभानुना युक्ते पुरिे भानुनन्दने । 

गुिौ च नाशिासशिे प्रेिशापाि् सुिक्षयाः ॥ १००॥ 

लग्ने िाहौ सशुक्रे ज्ये चन्द्रे मन्दयुिे िथा । 

लग्नेशे मृत्युिासशिे प्रेिशापाि् सुिक्षयाः ॥ १०१॥ 

पुरिानाथधपे नीचे कािके नीचिासशगे । 

नीचिग्रहदृष्टे च प्रेिशापाि् सुिक्षयाः ॥ १०२॥ 

लग्ने मन्दे सुिे िाहौ िन्ध्रे भानुसमन्तििे । 

व्यये भौमेन संयुक्ते प्रेिशापाि् सुिक्षयाः ॥ १०३॥ 

कामिानाथधपे दाःिे ु पुरे चन्द्रसमन्तििे । 

मन्दमाब्दन्दयुिे लग्ने प्रेिशापाि् सुिक्षयाः ॥ १०४॥ 

र्धिानाथधपे पुरे शतनशुक्रसमन्तििे । 

कािके नाशिासशिे प्रेिशापाि् सुिक्षयाः ॥ १०५॥ 

95-105. If the person whose duty is to do so does not perform Shraddha of his father or mother in his previous birth, departed soul is formed into an evil spirit and he is deprived of a male issue in the next birth. This is revealed by the following yogas at birth-

(1) Saturn and the Sun in the 5th, the waning Moon in the 7th and Rahu and Jupiter in the 12th, 

(2) Saturn as lord of the 5th in the 8th, Mars in the Ascendant and Jupiter in the 8th, 

(3) Malefic are in the Ascendant, the Sun is in the 12th, Mars, Saturn and Mercury are in the 5th and the lord of the 5th is in the 8th, 

(4) Rahu is in the Ascendant, Saturn is in the 5th and Jupiter is in the 8th, 

(5) Venus, Jupiter and Rahu are in the Ascendant associated with the Moon and Saturn and the lord of the Ascendant are in the 8th, 

(6) The lord of the 5th and Jupiter are in their signs of debilitation aspected by debilitated planets, 

(7) Saturn is in the Ascendant, Rahu is in the 5th, the Sun is in the 8th and Mars is in the 12th, 

(8) The lord of the 7th is- in the 6th, the 8th, or the 12th, the Moon is in the 5th, Saturn and Gulika are in the Ascendant. 

(9) The lord of the 8th along with Saturn and Venus is in the 5th and Jupiter is in his sign of debilitation. 

अस्य दोर्षस्य शान्त्यथं गयािाद्धं समाचिेि् । 

कु यांद्रद्राथभर्षेकञ्च ु ब्रह्ममूतिव प्रदापयेि् ॥ १०६॥ 

धेनुं िजिपारं च िथा नीलमणणं द्वद्वज । 

ब्राह्मणान् भोजयेि् पिाि् िेभ्यि दसक्षणां द्वदशेि् ॥ १०७॥ 

एर्ं कृ िे मनुष्यस्य शापमोक्षा प्रजायिे । 

पुरोत्पथत्तभवर्ेत्तस्य कु लर्ृणद्धि जायिे ॥ १०८॥ 

106-108: The person concerned gets release from the curse and is blessed with a son if he undertakes the following remedial measures-

(I) Performance of a Pinda Dana (व्पण्ड दान) 

(2) Rudra Abhishek (रुद्र अभभषेक) 

(3) Giving in charity a gold idol of Brahma, a cow, a vessel made of silver and a neelamani (नीलमणी) 

(4) Feeding Brahmins and giving them presents in cash (दशक्षणा). 

Remedial measures for male issue as a result of malevolence of planets at birth 

िथा ज्ञशुक्रजे दोर्षे पुराब्दप्ताः शम्भुपूजनाि् । 

जीर्चन्द्रकृ िे तर्प्र मन्त्रयन्त्रौर्षधाद्वदिाः ॥ १०९॥ 

िाहुजे कन्यकादानाि् सूयवजे हरिकीिवनाि् । 

गोदानाि् के िुजे दोर्षे रुद्रजापाि् कु जाऽष्टकव जे ॥ ११०॥ 

सर्वदोर्षतर्नाशाय शुभसिानलब्धये । 

# हरिर्ंशकथा भक्त्या िोिव्या तर्थधना द्वद्वज ॥ १११॥

109- 111. If a person is deprived of a male issue as a result of malevolence of planets at birth, he will be blessed with a son if he undertakes the following remedial measures-

(1) Worshipping lord Shiva if the harm is as a result of the malevolence of Mercury and Venus, 

(2) Reciting of Santan Gopal mantra, wearing and worshipping appropriate yantra and taking suitable medicines, if the childlessness is a result of the malevolence of Jupiter and the Moon, 

(3) Kanyadana if the childlessness is due to malevolence of Rahu, 

(4) Worshipping of lord Vishnu if it is due to malevolence of the Sun, 

(5) Rudriya Japa if it is due to the malevolence of Mars and Saturn, 

Listening with devotion to Haribansh Purana removes all kinds of blemishes $( \overrightarrow { \sf G I O } )$ and blesses the person concerned with a son. 

# अथः ग्रहशान्त्यध्यायः ॥८४॥

# Chapter 84. Remedial Measures to Obtain Relief from the Malevolence of the Planets

ग्रहाणां दोर्षशान्त्यथं िेर्षां पूजातर्थधं र्द । 

मानर्ानां द्वहिाथाय संक्षेपाि् कृ पया मुने ॥ १॥ 

1. Maitreya said-O venerable Sage please describe for the good of the mankind the remedial measures for appeasement of the malevolent planets. 

ग्रहा सूयादयाः पूर्ं मया प्रोक्ता द्वद्वजोत्तम । 

जगत्यां सर्वजिूनां िदधीनं सुखाऽसुखम् ॥ २॥ 

2. The Sage replied-I have already described the names and characteristic features and qualities of the planets. Joys and sorrows of all the creatures in the world are dependent on these planets. Therefore, persons desirous o, peace, wealth and prosperity, rainfall, good health and longevity, should worship the planets (by prayers, recitation of mantras, charity etc.). 

िस्माि् सुशान्तिकामो र्ा िीकामो र्ा सुचेिसा । 

र्ृष्टायायुाः पुष्टष्टकामो र्ा िेर्षां यज्ञं समाचिेि् ॥ ३॥ 

िाभ्राच्च स्फष्टटकाद्रक्तचन्दनाि् स्वणवकादभौ ु । 

िजिादयसाः सीसाि् कांस्याि् कायााः क्रामद् ग्रहााः ॥ ४॥ 

पूर्ोक्तै ाः स्वस्वर्णैर्ा पटे लेख्या द्वद्वजोत्तमैाः । 

स्वस्वोक्तद्वदन्तग्वभागेर्षु गन्द्रद्याद्यैमवण्डनेर्षु र्ा ॥ ५॥ 

3-5. For the purpose of worshipping them, the idols of the Sun, the Moon, Mars, Mercury. Jupiter, Venus, Saturn, Rahu and Ketu should be made of copper, sphatika (rock crystal), red sandal, wood, gold (of both Mercury and Jupiter), Silver, iron, glass and bell metal respectively). Alternatively, the sketches of all the above planets should be drawn in the colours belonging to them on a piece of cloth by sandal etc., and they should be placed in their own directions. 

Forms of the planets for worship and contemplation 

पद्मासनाः पद्महस्ताः पद्मपरसमद्युतिाः । 

सप्ताश्विथसंिि द्वद्वभुजि द्वदर्ाकिाः ॥ ६॥ 

6. Contemplate of the Sun well adorned with two arm seated on a lotus, with a lotus flower in one hand, red coloured like lotus, and aboard a chariot of seven horses. 

श्वेिाः श्वेिाम्बिो देर्ो दशाश्वाः श्वेिभूर्षणाः । गदाहस्तो द्वद्वबाहुि तर्धािव्यो तर्धुद्वद्ववज ॥ ७॥ 

7. Contemplate of the Moon as white coloured, dressed in white robes, with two arms carrying a mace in one hand and a vara (वर) in the other, adorned with white coloured ornaments and aboard a chariot of ten horses. 

िक्तमाल्याम्बिधिो शगक्तशूलगदाधिाः । र्िदस्तु चिुबाहुमवङ्गलो मेर्षर्ाहनाः ॥ ८॥ 

8. Contemplate of Mars with a red necklace, dressed in red coloured robes, with four arms, carrying Shakti (शगक्त) Shoola (शूल), gada (mace) and vara (वर) and mounted on a lamb. 

पीिमाल्याम्बिधिाः कणणवकािसमद्युतिाः । खड् गचमवगदापाणणाः ससंहिो र्िदो बुधाः ॥ ९॥ 

9. Contemplate of Mercury with a yellow coloured garland, dressed in yellow robes, with four arms carrying a sword, a shield, a mace and vara $( { \overline { { \mathsf { q } } } } { \overline { { \mathsf { e } } } } )$ , mo1nted on a lion. 

गुरुशुक्रौ क्रमाि् पीिश्वेिर्णौ चिुभुवजौ । दण्डण्डनौ र्िदौ कायौ साक्षसूरकमण्डलू ॥ १०॥ 

10. Contemplate of Jupiter as yellow complexion, and of Venus of fair complexion, both with four arms carrying a danda (दण्ड), akshasutra (अक्ष सूि), kamandal (कमण्डल) and vara (वर). 

इन्द्रनीलद्युतिाः शूली र्िदो गृध्रर्ाहनाः । र्ाणर्ाणासनधिो तर्ज्ञेयोऽकव सुिो द्वद्वज ॥ ११॥ 

11. O Maitreya! Contemplate of Saturn with the lustre like that of Indraneela (इन्द्रनील), with four arms carrying shoola (शूल), bow, arrow and vara $( { \overline { { \mathsf { q } } } } { \overline { { \mathsf { e } } } } )$ , mounted on a donkey. 

किालर्दनाः खड् गचमवशूली र्िप्रदाः । ससंहिो नीलर्णवि िाहुिेर्ं प्रकल्प्प्यिे ॥ १२॥ 

12. Contemplate of Rahu with a hideous face, with four arms carrying a sword, a shield, a shoola (शूल) and a vara (वर), blue coloured and mounted on a lion. 

धूम्रा द्वद्वबाहर्ाः सर्े गद्वदनो तर्कृ िाननााः । 

गृध्रासना तनत्यं के िर्ाः स्युर्विप्रदा ॥ १३॥ 

13. There are many ketus. All of them are of smoky colour, with two arms carrying a mace and a vara (वर), with a hideous face and mounted on a donkey. 

सर्े ष्टकिीष्टटनाः काया ग्रहा लोकद्वहिप्रदााः । 

स्वांगुलेनोच्छच्छर िा तर्ज्ञैाः शिमष्टोत्तिं सदा ॥ १४॥ 

14. All the idols should be so made that they are 108 fingers tall by one's own fingers (अंगुल). 

Notes: Such a measurement is taken from the middle finger. Procedure for worshipping the planets 

यथार्णं प्रदेयातन सुदष्पाणण ् र्सनातन च । 

गन्धो दीपो बसलिैर् धूपो देयि गुग्गुलुाः ॥ १५॥ 

यस्य ग्रहस्य यदद्रव्यमन्नं ् यस्य च यि् ष्टप्रयम् । 

िच्च िस्यै प्रदािव्यं भगक्तयुक्ते न चेिसा ॥ १६॥ 

15-16. Dedicate with devotion to the planet concerned the flowers and garments of the colour belonging to him, sandal, deep (दीप), guggul etc. (गुग्गुलाद्वद), his metal and the grains dear to him and distribute all these things to Brahmins to appease the planet. 

Mantras of planets 

आकृ ष्णेन इमं देर्ा अगग्नमूवधा द्वदर्ाः ककु ि् । 

उद्बध्यस्वेति ु मन्त्रांि जपेदथ बृहस्पिे ॥ १७॥ 

अन्नाि् परििुििेति शन्नो देर्ीिभीष्टये । 

कया नसिर इत्येर्ं के िु कृ ण्वगन्नमांस्तथा ॥ १८॥ 

सप्त रुद्रा द्वदशो नन्दा नर्चन्द्रा नृपास्तथा । 

ष्टरपक्षा अष्टचन्द्राि सप्तचन्द्रास्तथैर् च ॥ १९॥ 

इमााः संख्यााः सहस्रघ्ना जपसंख्यााः प्रकीतिविााः । 

क्रमादकाद्वदखेटानां प्रीत्यथं द्वद्वजपुङ्गर् ॥ २०॥ 

17-20: The mantras of all the planets and the prescribed number of their recitation are given below. The recitation of mantras should be done after worshipping the planets as indicated in verses 15-16- 

<table><tr><td>Planet</td><td>Mantra</td><td>Prescribed number</td></tr><tr><td>Sun</td><td>अपकुप्वान रजाता etc.</td><td>7000</td></tr><tr><td>Moon</td><td>डमे देश्ता असपाले etc.</td><td>11000</td></tr><tr><td>Mars</td><td>अपिकमूधादिके etc.</td><td>11000</td></tr><tr><td>Mercury</td><td>अनुधान्यर्षा etc.</td><td>9000</td></tr><tr><td>Jupiter</td><td>धुहरस्यों अतिलिवया etc.</td><td>19000</td></tr><tr><td>Venus</td><td>अनुतार्ति परिकुलो करसे etc.</td><td>16000</td></tr><tr><td>Saturn</td><td>अनुतों देश्तीर्षान्यों त्रय etc.</td><td>23000</td></tr><tr><td>Rahu</td><td>कर्वा ितिमिता अपमुलो etc.</td><td>18000</td></tr><tr><td>Ketu</td><td>केलुँ कृपुलाना करतारे etc.</td><td>17000</td></tr></table>

Procedure for Havana (हवन) 

अकव ाः पलाशाः खद्वदिस्त्वपामागवस्तु ष्टपप्पलाः । 

उदम्बिाः ु शमी दर्ा ु कु शाि सतमधाः क्रमाि् ॥ २१॥ 

होिव्या मधुसष्टपवभ्यां दध्ना क्षीिेण र्ा युिााः । 

एकै कस्य त्वष्ट शिमष्टातर्ंशतििेर् र्ा ॥ २२॥ 

21-22. Havana should be performed with Aak (आक), Palash (पलाश), Khair $( \frac { \partial } { \partial \alpha } )$ , Chirchiri $( \sqrt { 9 - 1 7 } \sqrt { 9 - 1 } )$ , Pipal (पीपल), Goolar (गूलर), Shami (शमी), Wood pieces, Doob $( \overline { { \mathfrak { g } \mathfrak { d } } } )$ and Kush (कु श), for the Sun, the Moon, Mars, Mercury, Jupiter, Venus, Saturn, Rahu and Ketu respectively, mixed with honey, ghee, curd or milk. The number of offerings to the sacred fire is 108 or 28. 

गुडैदनं पायसं च हतर्ष्यं क्षीिर्षाष्टष्टकम् । 

दध्योदनं हतर्िणं ू मांसं श्रचरान्नमेर् च ॥ २३॥ 

दद्याद् ग्रहक्रमादेर्ं तर्प्रेभ्यो भोजनं द्वद्वज । 

शगक्तिो र्ा यथालाभं देयं सत्कािपूर्वकम् ॥ २४॥ 

23-24: To appease the Sun and other eight planets, Brahmins, should be fed with (I) of rice cooked with jiggery, (2) rice cooked in milk, (3) havishya (हतवष्य), (4) paddy cooked in milk, (5) curd and rice, (6) rice with ghee. (7) Rice cooked with powder of sesame seeds (ततल), (8) rice cooked with meat, (9) rice cooked with cereals (खखचडी), respectively. 

धेनुाः शङ् खस्तथाऽनड् र्ान् हेम र्ासो हयाः क्रमाि् । 

कृ ष्णा गौिायसं छाग एिा िव्याद्वददसक्षणााः ॥ २५॥ 

25. To appease the Sun and other planets the things to be given in charity are (1) cow with calf, (2) conch, (3) bullock (4) gold, (5) robes, (6) horse, (7) black cow, (8) weapons made of iron and (9) goat, respectively. 

यस्य यि यदा दाःिाः ु स िं यत्नेन पूजयेि् । 

एर्षां धारा र्िो दत्ताः पूसजिााः पूजगयष्यथ ॥ २६॥ 

मानर्ानां ग्रहाधीना उञ्छर ायााः पिनातन च । 

भार्ाऽभार्ौ च जगिां िस्माि् पूज्यिमा ग्रहााः ॥ २७॥ 

26-27: The planet who is the cause of adverse effects to a person at any time should be worshipped and appeased because Brahma has blessed the planets with the boon "Do good to the persons who worship you." And the development and, progress and downfall of the people and the creation and destruction of the universe are all under the administration and authority of the planets. Therefore, they are most venerable. 

# अथऽशुभजन्मकथनाध्यायः॥८५॥

# Chapter 85. Inauspicious Births

अथाऽन्यि् संप्रर्क्ष्यातम सुलग्ने सुग्रहेष्वष्टप । 

यदन्यकािणेनाष्टप भर्ेज्जन्माऽशुभप्रदम् ॥ १॥ 

दशे कृ ष्णाचिुदवश्यां तर्ष्ट्यां सोदिभे िथा । 

ष्टपिृभे सूयवसंक्रािौ पािेऽके न्दग्रु हे िथा ॥ २॥ 

व्यिीपािाद्वददयोगे ु गण्डािे ष्टरतर्धेऽष्टप र्ा । 

यमघण्टेऽर्भे दग्धयोगे रीििजन्म च ॥ ३॥ 

प्रसर्स्य ष्टरकािेऽष्टप ज्ञेयं जन्माऽशुभप्रदम् । 

शान्त्या भर्ति कल्याणं िदपायं ु च र्च्च्म्यहम् ॥ ४॥ 

1-4. The Venerable sage said-O Maitreya! Now I will, describe to you the circumstances in which the births are inauspicious in spite of the Ascendant and the planets being well disposed, Although the Ascendant may be well disposed births will be inauspicious if they take place on Amavasya (the last day of the dark half of the month), on Chaturdasi (14th tithi) Krishna Paksha (dark half of the month, in Bhadra Karana, in the Nakshatra of the brother, in the Nakshatras of father and mother, at the time of entry of the Sun in a sign (संिान्तन्त), the time of Pata (पात), at the time of solar and lunar eclipses, at the time of Vyati pata (व्यतीपात), in gandantas of all the three kinds, in yamaghant(यमघट), Tithikshaya (ततथक्षय), in Dagdba yoga etc. The birth of a son after three daughters and birth of a daughter after three sons and the birth of a freak are inauspicious. But there are remedial measures for obtaining relief from the evil effects of such births which are being described in the foregoing chapters. 

# दशिजन्मशान्त्यध्यायः ॥८६॥

# Chapter 86. Remedial Measures for Birth on Amavasya

मैरेय दशवजािानां मािाष्टपरोदवरिद्रिा । 

िद्दोर्षपरिहािाय शान्तिं कु याद् तर्चक्षणाः ॥ १॥ 

कलशिापनं कृ त्वा प्रथमं तर्थधपूर्वकम् । 

उदम्बिटाश्वत्थचूिानां ु पिर्ांस्तथा ॥ २॥ 

सतनम्बानां च मूलतन त्वचस्तर तर्तनसक्षपेि् । 

पंचित्नातन तनसक्षप्य र्ियुग्मेन चेष्टयेि् ॥ ३॥ 

सर्े समुद्र इति चाऽपोद्वहष्ठाद्वदत्र्यृचेन च । 

आमन्त्र्य कलशे िच्च िापयेद् र्तिकोणके ॥ ४॥ 

दशवस्य देर्योिाऽथ चन्द्रभास्कियोाः क्रमाि् । 

प्रतिमां स्वणवजां तनत्यं िाजिीं िाम्रजां िथा ॥ ५॥ 

आप्यायस्वेति मन्त्रेनऽ सतर्िा पिात्तमेर् च । 

उपचािैाः समािाध्य ििो होमं समाचिेि् ॥ ६॥ 

सतमधि चरुं तर्द्वान् क्रमेण जुहुयाि् व्रिी । 

भक्त्या सतर्िृमन्त्रेण सोमो धेनुि मन्त्रिाः ॥ ७॥ 

अष्टोत्तिशिं र्ाष्टप अष्टतर्ंशतििेर् र्ा । 

अथभर्षेकं िथा कु याि् दम्पत्योि सुपुरयोाः ॥ ८॥ 

द्वहिण्यं िजिं चैर् कृ ष्णधेनुि दसक्षणा । 

ब्राह्मणान् भोजयेि् शक्त्या ििाः क्षेममर्ाप्नुयाि् ॥ ९॥ 

1-9. The Sage Parāśara said-O Maitreya! The person born on Amavasya is always poverty stricken. It is therefore essential to adopt remedial measures to obtain relief from the evil effects of such births, which are as follows - 

Take a Kalash (कलश water vessel) and then put in it fresh leaves of Goolar (a wild fig) Vata (banyan), pipal, mango and neema (Margo) trees and cover it with two pieces of cloth. 

Then install the Kalash in the South West direction after reciting (सवे समुद्रा), etc., and (आपो द्वहष्ठा), etc., mantras. Then worship the idols of the Sun and the Moon 

ruling deities of Amavasya made of gold and silver mixed with copper respectively by recitation of (आप्यायस्व), mantras etc., for the Sun and (सतवता) etc., mantras etc., for the Moon 16 or 5 times. Thereafter perform Havana with 108 or 28 oblations of the mixture of prescribed fuels(सतमर्ा)and cooked food $( \overline { { \mathbf { \overline { { q } } \mathbf { \otimes } } } } )$ with recitation of mantras of the Sun and the Moo Later sprinkle the water on child born and his parents and offer in charity gold, silver and a black cow together with feeding the Brahmins according to one's means. By performing these remedial rites, the child born gains freedom and protection from the evil effects of the birth on Amavasya. 

# अथः कृ ष्णचतुदिशीजन्म शान्त्यध्यायः ॥८७॥

# Chapter 87. Remedies from the Evil Effects of birth on Krishna Chaturdashi

कृ ष्णपक्षचिुदवश्यााः र्षड् भागेर्षु फलं क्रमाि् । जन्म चेि् प्रथमे भागे िदा ज्ञेयं शुभं द्वद्वज ॥ १॥ द्वद्विीये ष्टपििं हन्ति माििं च िृिीयके । चिुथे मािुलं चैर् पञ्चमे र्ंशनाशनम् ॥ २॥ र्षष्ठे िु धननाशाः स्यादात्मनो नाश एर् र्ा । िद्दोर्षपरिहािाथं शान्तिं कु याद् प्रयत्निाः ॥ ३॥ 

1-3. The Sage Said-Divide the span of Chaturdashi in 6 parts. The birth in the first part is auspicious. The birth in the second part causes destruction or death of father. The birth in the third part results in death of the mother. The birth in the fourth part take away the maternal uncle. The birth in the fifth part, destroys the entire family (कु ल generation). The birth in the sixth part causes loss of wealth or destruction (death) of the native. 

Therefore, it is essential to take immediate remedial measures to escape these evil effects. 

सशर्स्य प्रतिमां कु याि् सौर्णीं कर्षवसन्तम्मिाम् । िदधाधवतमिां र्ाऽष्टप यथातर्त्तं मनोहिाम् ॥ ४॥ बालचन्द्रष्टकिीटाञ्च श्वेिमाल्याम्बिान्तििाम् । ष्टरनेरां च र्ृर्षासीनां र्िाभयकिामथ ॥ ५॥ 

4-5. Have an idol of Lord Shiva made of one karsha (equal in weight to the former silver rupee) of gold or of weight one can afford. The idol should-

(1) Have a New Moon on the forehead, 

(2) have a white garland round the neck, 

(3) have three eyes (one being on, he forehead), 

(4) be dressed in white robes, 

(5) be seated on a bull, and 

(6) be two armed, and 

(7) carry Vara $( { \overline { { \mathsf { q } } } } { \overline { { \mathsf { e } } } } )$ and Abhaya (अभय). 

रयम्बकं चेति मन्त्रेण पूजां कु यादिब्दन्द्रिाः । आर्ाह्य र्ारुणैमवन्त्रैिाचायो मन्त्रित्त्वतर्ि् ॥ ६॥ इमं मे र्रुणे त्येर्ं ित्त्वा यामी त्यृचा पुनाः । त्त्वन्न अग्ने इत्यनया सत्वं नो इत्यृचाष्टप च ॥ ७॥ आग्नेयं कु म्भमािभ्य पूजयेद् भगक्तिाः क्रमाि् । आ नोभद्रेति सूक्तं च भद्रा अग्नेि सूक्तकम् ॥ ८॥ जप्त्ऱत्वा पुरुर्षसूक्तं च कन्द्रद्रेतिु िथा जपेि् । शङ्किस्याऽथभर्षेकं च ग्रहपूजां च काियेि् ॥ ९॥ सतमदाज्यचरूं िैर् तिलमार्षांि सपवपान् । अश्विल्पक्षपालासखाद्वदिााः सतमधाः शुभााः ॥ १०॥ अष्टोत्तिशिं र्िौ जुहुयाद् तर्थधपूर्वकम् । अष्टतर्ंशतिसंख्या र्ा होमं कु याि् पृथक् पृथक् ॥ ११॥ मन्त्रेण त्र्यम्बके नाथ तिलान् व्याहृतिथभस्तथा । ग्रहहोमं च तर्थधर्ि् कु याद् क्षेमं ििो भर्ेि् ॥ १२॥ अथभर्षेकं च जािस्य िब्दत्परोिाष्टप मन्त्रतर्ि् । कु याि् ििो यथाशगक्त ब्राह्मणान् भोजयेि् सुधीाः ॥ १३॥ 

6-13: Then after invocation with Varun (वरुण) mantra, worship should be performed by chanting ‘ियम्बक’ etc., mantras. Thereafter a kalash (कलश) should be placed in the North-East direction with chanting of 'इमं मे वरुण', 'तत्वायातम', 'त्वन्नोअग्ने' mantras followed by Japa of, 'आ नोभद्रा' etc., and 'भद्राअग्नेश् ्च' suktas and the chanting of 'कु द्रदेत्याद्वद ु ' mantra- Then after sprinkling water over the idol of Lord Shiva (अभभषेक), the nine planets should be worshipped. This should be followed by Havana by using ghee, powder of sesame seeds (ततल), urda (माष), sarson (सरसो) and wood pieces of Pipal, Pakar, Palas and Khadir trees. 108 or 28 oblations should be mad separately for the nine planets. Thereafter along with chanting of 'व्ियम्बकं ' etc. mantras, Havana should be performed with sesame seeds (ततल) for the nine planets. Lastly the water of the Kalash should be sprinkled on the native and his parents, and the Brahmins should be fed according to means. 

# अथःभदािमदयोगशान्त्यध्यायः॥ ु  ८८॥

# Chapter 88. Remedies from evil Effects of birth in Bhadra and Inauspicious Yogas

अथाऽहं संप्रर्क्ष्यातम भद्रायामर्मे िथा । 

व्यािूपािाद्वददयोगे ु यमघण्टाद्वदके च यि् ॥ १॥ 

जन्माशुभफलं प्रोक्तं िस्य शान्तितर्थधं द्वद्वज । 

प्राप्ते प्रसूतिदयोगे ु शान्तिं कु याद् तर्चक्षणाः ॥ २॥ 

1 2. The Sage said-O Brahmin! Now I am going to describe the remedial measures for relief from the evil effects of birth in Bhadra, Tithi Kshaya (ततभथ क्षय) Vyatipata, Paridba, Vajra etc., inauspicious Yogas and Yamagbants etc. The remedial rites should be performed on the day when the same inauspicious Yoga operates again. 

दैर्ज्ञैदवसशविे र्ाऽष्टप सुलग्ने सुद्वदने गृही । 

पूजनं देर्िानां च ग्रहाणां यजनं िथा ॥ ३॥ 

शङ्किस्याऽथभर्षेकं च घृिदीपं सशर्ालये । 

आयुर्ृवणद्धकिं कु यादश्वत्थस्य प्रदसक्षणम् ॥ ४॥ 

हर्नं तर्ष्णुमन्त्रेण स/िमष्टोत्तिं सुधीाः । 

ब्राह्मणान् भोजयेि् शक्त्या ििाः कल्याणमाप्नुयाि् ॥ ५॥ 

3-5: The remedial rites are to be performed in the following order by the parents of the child in the above inauspicious Yogas-

(1) puja (worship) of Lord Vishnu and other deities on &n auspicious day and auspicious Lagna on the advice of a proficient astrologer, 

(2) burning of deep (दीप) with ghee in a Shiva temple, 

(3) Abhishek (अभभषेक) of Lord Shiva, 

(4) going around (प्रदशक्षणा) a pipal tree 108 times prolongs longevity, and 

(5) perform Havana with 108 oblations along with the recitation of "तवष्णो रराटमसीत्याद्वद'' mantra of Lord Vishnu and 

(6) feeding Brahmins to the best of one's means. 

The observance of these remedial measures will give deliverance to the native from all the evil effects of his inauspicious birth and he will enjoy happiness. 

# अथैक नक्षत्र जातशान्त्यध्यायः ॥८९॥

# Chapter 89. Remedies from

# Nakshatra Birth

अथ यद्येकनक्षरे भ्रारोर्ा ष्टपिृपुरयोाः । 

प्रसूतिि ियोमृविुिथैर्कस्य तनियाः ॥ १॥ 

िर शान्तिं प्रर्क्ष्यातम गगाद्वदमुतनभाष्टर्षिम् । 

सुद्वदने शुभनक्षरे चन्द्रिािाबलान्तििे ॥ २॥ 

रिक्तार्तर्ष्टष्टतर्र्ज्ये च समय शान्तिमाचिेि् । 

शनेिीशानद्वदग्भागे नक्षरप्रतिमां शुभाम् ॥ ३॥ 

िन्नक्षरोक्तमन्त्रेण पूजयेि् कलशोपरि । 

िक्तर्िेण संछाद्य र्ियुग्मेन र्ेष्टयेि् ॥ ४॥ 

स्वस्वशाखोक्तमागेण कु यादगग्नमुखं िथा । 

पुनस्तेनैर् मन्त्रेण हुनदष्टोत्तिं शिम् ॥ ५॥ 

प्रत्येकं सतमदन्नाज्यैाः प्रायसित्तािमेर् द्वह । 

अथभर्षेकं ििाः कु यादाचायवि द्वयोिष्टप ॥ ६॥ 

ऋन्तत्वग्भ्यो दसक्षणां दद्यादाचायाय तर्शेर्षिाः । 

ब्राह्मणान् भोजयेद् भक्त्या तर्त्तशाठ्यतर्र्सजविाः ॥ ७॥ 

1-7. The Sage Parāśara said-O Maitreya! If the birth takes place in the Nakshatras of the brother and the parents, death takes place, without doubt of the brother and father or mother or they have to undergo death like suffering. Therefore, I am going to describe the remedial measures to be adopted to escape from these evil effects. The remedial rites should be performed in a Muhurta (मुहूतध) when the Moon and stars are favourable and on a day on which there is no Rikta-Bhadra dosha (दोष). The remedial rites should be performed in the following order-

(1) Install an idol of the Janma Nakshatra on a Kalasha (कलश) in the northeast direction from the fire. Cover it with a red piece of cloth and then warp two pieces of cloth round it. 

(2) Worship the idol by chanting the mantras of the Janma Nakshatra. 

(3) According to one's gotra (गोि) perform Havana 108 times with the recitation of the same mantra, facing the fire, with ghee and other Havana material (described in earlier chapters). 

(4) Then the priest performing the puja should sprinkle water on the parents and brother (whoever is concerned). 

(5) Give presents in cash (दशक्षणा) to the priest and his colleagues associated with the ceremony, to the best of one's means, and 

(6) Then feed the Brahmin, to the best of one's means. 

For Details please consult 

REMEDIAL MEASURES IN ASTROLOGY-By G.S. Kapoor 

# अथ सिंक्रान्तन्तजन्मशान्त्यध्यायः ॥९०॥

# Chapter 90. Remedies from Sankranti Birth

घोिार्ध्ांक्षीमहोदयो मन्दा मन्दाष्टकनी िथा । 

तमिा च िाक्षसी सूयवसंक्रान्तिाः सूयवर्ासिाि् ॥ १॥ 

संक्रािौ च निो जािो भर्ेद् दारिद्र्य दाःखभाक् ु । 

शान्त्या सुखमर्ाप्नोति ििाः शान्तितर्थध ब्रुर्े ॥ २॥ 

1-2: The sage said-O Brahmin! the names of the Sankranti on the seven days of the week beginning from Sunday are Ghorā (घोरा), Dhhvankshi (ध्वांक्षी), Mahodari (महोदरी), Manda (मन्दा), Mandakini (मन्दाव्कनी), Mishra (तमश्रा), and Rakshasi (राक्षसी), in that order, the person born at the Sankranti (entry of the Sun in a new sign) is poor and unhappy but he becomes well to do and happy if remedial measures are undertaken. I am now going to describe the remedial measures to nullify these evil effects. 

नर्ग्रहमखं कु याि् िस्य दोर्षोपशािये । 

गृहस्य पूर्वद्वदग्भागे गोमयेनोपसलप्य च ॥ ३॥ 

स्वलंकृ िप्रदेशे िु ब्रीद्वहिासशं प्रकल्पयेि् । 

पञ्चद्रोणतमिं धान्यैस्तदधं िण्डुलैस्तथा ॥ ४॥ 

िदधं च तिलैाः कु याद्रासशं च द्वद्वजसत्तम । 

पृथक् ष्टरियिाशौ िु सलखेदष्टदलं बुधैाः ॥ ५॥ 

पुण्याहं र्ाचगयत्वा िु आचायं र्ृणुयाि् पुिा । 

धमवज्ञं मन्त्रित्त्वज्ञं शान्तिकमवणण कोतर्दम् ॥ ६॥ 

3-6: The yajna of the nine planets should be performed to obtain relief from the evil effects of the birth at Sankranti. A clean spot in the eastern part of the house should be purified by besmearing with cow dung. Then prepare three separate heaps of the following-

(1) 5 dronas (80 seers) of paddy (साठी) 

(2) 2½ dronas (40 seers) of rice. 

(3) 1¼ dronas (20 seers) of sesame seeds (ततल). 

On these heaps of grains make a figure of lotus with eight leaves (अष्टदल पदम् ्् ), and then decorate them with flowers. 

After doing this, select arid invite a priest who is well versed in. the performance of religious rites and recitation of mantras. 

िासशर्षु िापयेि् कु म्भानव्रणान् सुमनोहिान् । 

िीथोदके न सम्पूयव समृदौर्षधपिर्म् ॥ ७॥ 

पंचगव्यं सक्षपेत्तर र्ियुग्मेन र्ेष्टयेि् । 

कु म्भोपरि न्यसेि् पारं सूक्ष्मर्िेण र्ेष्टष्टिम् ॥ ८॥ 

प्रतिमां िापयेि् िर साथधप्रत्यथधदैर्िाम् । 

अथधदैर्ं भर्ेि् सूयविन्द्राः प्रत्यथधदैर्िम् ॥ ९॥ 

चन्द्राद्वदत्याकृ िी पाश्वे मध्ये संक्रान्तिमचवयेि् । 

प्रतिमां पूजने पूर्ं र्ियुग्मं तनर्ेदयेि् ॥ १०॥ 

ििो व्याहृतिपूि्वर्ेण ित्तन्मन्त्रेण पूजयेि् । 

रैयम्बके ण मन्त्रेण प्रधानप्रतिभां पूजयेि् ॥ ११॥ 

उत्सूयव इति मन्त्रेण सूयवपूजां समाचिेि् । 

आप्यायस्वेति मन्त्रेण चन्द्रपूजां समाचिेि् ॥ १२॥ 

उपचािैाः र्षोडशथभयवद्वा पञ्चोपचािकै ाः । 

मृत्युंजयन मन्त्रेण प्रधानप्रतिमां स्पृशन् ॥ १३॥ 

अष्टोत्तिसहस्रं चाऽप्यष्टोत्तिशिं जपेि् । 

अथाऽष्टातर्ंशतिं र्ाष्टप जपेन्मन्त्रं स्वशगक्तिाः ॥ १४॥ 

कु म्भेभ्याः पसिमे देशे िण्डण्डलेऽगग्नं प्रकल्पयेि् । 

स्वगृह्योक्ततर्धानेन काियेि् संस्कृ िानलम् ॥ १५॥ 

रयम्बके न मन्त्रेण सतमदाज्यचरून् हुनेि् । 

अष्टोत्तिसहस्रं र्ा अष्टोत्तिशिं यथा ॥ १६॥ 

अष्टतर्ंशतिमेर्ाष्टप कु याद् होमं स्वशगक्तिाः । 

मृत्युंजयेन मन्त्रेण तिलहोमि काियेि् ॥ १७॥ 

ििाः स्तस्वष्टकृ िं हुत्वाअथभर्षेकं च काियेि् । 

ब्रह्मणान् भोजयेि् पिादेर्ं शान्तिमर्ाप्नुयाि् ॥ १८॥ 

7-18: The religious rites are then to lie performed in the following order-

(1) Install Kalashas without any holes on all the three heaps and put in each of them water from holy places, Sapta mrattika (सप्तमृततका), Shataushadhi (शतौषभर्); Panchapallava (पंचपल्लव) and Panchagavya (पंचगव्य). Then wrap the Kalashas with pieces of cloth. 

(2) Place small earthen pots wrapped with thin cloth on the Kalashas. 

(3) Then install the idol of Sankranti along with the idol or symbols of Adhideva (अभर्देव) and Pratyadhideva (प्रत्याभर्देव). (Here the Sun is Adhideva and the Moon is Pratyadhideva). Their idols should be placed on either side of the main idols of Sankranti. 

(4) Two robes may be given as offering to each of the idols. 

(5) Perform worship of all the three idols according to prescribed procedure. The main idol should be worshipped with the chanting of 'ियम्बकं यजामहे' etc., the idol of the San with mantra, उत्सुयध and the idol of the Moon with the mantra 'आप्यायश् ्व' etc. The worship should be performed with Shod shopchar (शोडषोपचार) or Panchopchar (पंचोपचार) as may be possible. 

(6) After touching the main idol, Mrityunjaya Japa should be recited. 1008 (अष्टोतर सहस्त्र), 108 (अष्टोतर शत), or 28 times as may be possible. 

(7) Make a small platform in the wet of the installed kalashas, kindle fire on it and perform the prescribed rites. Then perform Havana 1008, 108, or 28 times with Samidha (सतमर्ा), ghrit (ghee) and charu (powder of sesame seeds (ततल) within one's means, along with chanting of 'ियम्बकं यजामहे' etc., mantra. 

(8) Again, perform Havana, first with the fuel of sesame seeds along with recitation of Mrityunjaya mantra. 

(9) After performing another svistkrita (श्मस्वष्तकृ त) Havana, sprinkle the holy water on the child born and his parents (अभभषेक). 

(10) Lastly feed as many Brahmins as one can afford. 

By performing the remedial rites described above, the evil effects are nullified and the native and his parents enjoy happiness. 

# Chapter 91. Remedies from Birth in Eclipses

सूयेन्दग्रहणे ु काले येर्षां जन्म भर्ेद् द्वद्वज । 

व्याथधाः कष्टं च दारिद्र्यं िेर्षां मृत्युभयं भर्ेि् ॥ १॥ 

अिाः शान्तिं प्रर्क्ष्यातम जनानां द्वहिकाङ् क्षया । 

सूयवस्येन्दोि ग्रहेणं यस्तस्मनृक्षे प्रजायिे ॥ २॥ 

िन्नक्षरपिे रूपं सुर्णेन प्रकल्पयेि् । 

सूयवग्रहे सूयवरूपं सुर्णेन स्वशगक्तिाः ॥ ३॥ 

चन्द्रग्रहे चन्द्ररूपं िजिेन िथैर् च । 

िाहुरूपं प्रकु र्ीि सीसके न तर्चक्षणाः ॥ ४॥ 

शुचौ देशे समं िानं गोमयेन प्रलेपयेि् । 

िर च िापयेद् र्िं नूिनं सुमनोहिम् ॥ ५॥ 

रयाणामेर् रूपाणां िापनं िर काियेि् । 

सूयवग्रहे प्रदािव्यं सूयवप्रीतिकिं च यि् ॥ ६॥ 

िक्ताक्षिं िक्तगन्धं िक्तमाल्याम्बिाद्वदकम् । 

चन्द्रग्रहे प्रदािव्यं चन्द्रप्रीतिकिं च यि् ॥ ७॥ 

श्वेिगन्धं श्वेिपुष्पं श्वेिमाल्याम्बिाद्वदकम् । 

िाहर्े च प्रदािव्यं कृ ष्णपुष्पाम्बिाद्वदकम् ॥ ८॥ 

दद्यान्नक्षरनाथाय श्वेिगन्धाद्वदकं िथा । 

सूयं सम्पूजयेद्धीमानाकृ ष्णेति च मन्त्रिाः ॥ ९॥ 

अथा चन्द्रं इमे देर्ा इति मन्त्रेण भगक्तिाः । 

दर्ाथभ ू पूजयेद्राहुं कया न इति मन्त्रिाः ॥ १०॥ 

सूयेन्द्वोिकव पालाशतमखद्भजुवहुयाि् क्रमाि् । 

िथा च िाहोाः प्रीत्यथं दर्ाथभद्वद्ववजसत्तम ू ॥ ११॥ 

ब्रह्मर्ृक्षसतमखद्भि भेशाय जुहुयाि् पुनाः । 

अथभर्षेकं ििाः कु याि् जािस्य कलहोदकै ाः ॥ १२॥ 

आचायं पूजयेद्भक्त्या सुशािो तर्सजिेब्दन्द्रयाः । 

# ब्राह्मणान् भोजयेत्वा िु यथाशगक्त तर्सजवयेि् ॥ १३॥

# एर्ं ग्रहणजािस्य शान्तिं कृ त्वा तर्धानिाः ।

# सर्वतर्घ्नं तर्तनसजवत्वा सौभाग्यं लभिे निाः ॥ १४॥

1-14. The Sage said-O Brahmin! A person whose birth takes place at the time of solar or lunar eclipse, suffers from ailments, distress and poverty and faces danger of death. Therefore, I am going to describe for the benefit of the mankind the remedial measures required to be undertaken to nullify the above evil effects. 

The remedial rites are to be performed in the following order-

(1) The following idols should be got prepared according to one's means-

(a) in gold of the deity of the Nakshatra in which the eclipse takes place (for details regarding deities of Nakshatras see 'notes' on verse 18 of Chapter 3 Vol. I), 

(b) in gold of the Sun if the birth takes place during solar eclipse, and 

(c) in silver of the Moon if the birth takes place during lunar eclipse. 

(d) in lead of Rahu. 

(2) Besmear a clean spot on the ground (in the house) with cow dung, cover it with a new (unused) beautiful piece of cloth and install the three idols on it. 

(3) Make offerings of the following to the idols-

(a) in case of birth during solar eclipse, all things dear to the Sun, and red coloured akshat (अक्षत-rice), red sandal, garland of red coloured flowers, red clothes etc., 

(b) in case of birth during lunar eclipse, all things dear to the Moon, and white sandal, white flowers, white clothes etc. 

(c) for Rahu, blackish clothes, blackish flowers etc. 

(d) white flowers for the deity of the Nakshatra in which the eclipse takes place. 

(4) The worship should be performed as follows-

(a) of the Sun with the chanting of 'आकृ ष्णेन' etc., mantra, 

(b) of the Moon with the chanting of 'इमं देवा' etc., mantra, and 

(c) of Rahu with doorva (दवा ू -a kind of grass) and with the chanting of 'कयानश् ्चि ' etc., mantra. 

(5) Thereafter Havana should be performed as follows 

(a) with the fuel (सतमर्ा) of Aaak wood pieces for the Sun, 

(b) with the fuel (सतमर्ा) of Palas tree wood pieces for the Moon. 

(c) with doorva (दवा ू ) (or Rahu. 

(d) with Pipal tree wood pieces for the deity of the Shastra. 

(6) Sprinkle the holy water of the Kalasha on the child born (and his parents), 

(7) Offer worshipful regards to the priest performing the remedial rites, and 

(8) Lastly feed as many Brahmins as possible within one's means. 

By performance of the remedial rites in the manner described above, evil effects of the inauspicious birth are wiped off and the native enjoys happiness and is blessed with good fortune. 

# अथ गण्डान्तजातशान्त्यध्यायः ॥९२॥

# Chapter 92. Remedies from Birth in Gandanta

तिथथनक्षरलग्नानां गण्डािं ष्टरतर्धं स्मृिम् । 

जन्मयारातर्र्ाहादौ भर्ेत्तगन्नधनप्रदम् ॥ १॥ 

1: The Sage said-O Brahmin! Gandanta is of the three ands, namely of Tithi, Nakshatra and Lagna. Birth, travelling etc. performance of auspicious functions like marriage etc., luring Gandanta are likely to cause death of the person concerned. 

पूणानन्दाख्ययोस्तस्तथ्योाः सन्धौ नाडीचिुष्टयम् । 

अध ऊर्ध्ं च मैरेय तिथथगण्डािमुच्यिे ॥ २॥ 

2. O Maitreya! The--last 2 Ghatikas of Poorna tithi (5th, 10th, 15th) and the first 2 Ghatikas of Nanda tithi 1st, 6th, 11th) (total 4 Ghatikas) are known as Tithi Gandanta (ततभथ गण्डान्त) Nakshatra Gandanta. 

िेर्िीदास्रयोाः साप्रमघयोाः शाक्रमूलयोाः । 

सन्धौ नक्षरगण्डािमेर्ं नाडीचिुष्टयम् ॥ ३॥ 

3. Similarly the last two Ghatikas of Revti and first two Ghatikas of Ashwini, the last two Ghatikas of Ashlesha and first two Ghatikas of Makha and the last two Ghatikas of Jyeshtha and first two Ghatikas of Moola (total 4 Ghatikas) are own as Nakshatra Gandanta. 

मीनाजयोाः कष्टकव हयोलवग्नयोिसलचापयोाः । 

सन्धौ च लग्नगण्डािमधऊर्ध्व घटीतमिम् ॥ ४॥ 

4. The last half Ghatika of Pisces and first half Ghatika of Aries, the last half Ghatika of Cancer and first half Ghatika of Leo, the last half Ghatika of Scorpio and first half Ghatika of Sagittarius, are known as Lagna Gandanta. 

एर्षु चाभुक्तमूलाख्यं महातर्घ्नपदं स्मृिम् । 

इन्द्रिाक्षसयोाः सन्धौ पञ्चाष्टघष्टटकााः क्रमाि् ॥ ५॥ 

5. Amongst these Gandantas the last 6 Ghatikas of Jyeshtha and first 8 Ghatikas of Moola are known as Abhukta Moola (अभुक्त मूल). This period is considered extremely inauspicious. 

अथ गण्डािजािस्य सशशोाः शान्तितर्थधं ब्रुर्े । 

गण्डािकालजािस्य सूिकान्त्यद्वदने ष्टपिा ॥ ६॥ 

शान्तिंशुभेऽति र्ा कु याि् पश्येि् िार्न्न िं सशशुम् । 

र्ृर्षभं तिथथगण्डािे नक्षरे धनुमेर् च ॥ ७॥ 

काञ्चनं लग्नगण्डािे दद्यात्तद्दोर्षप्रशािये । 

आद्यभागे प्रजािस्य ष्टपिुिाप्यथभर्षेचनम् ॥ ८॥ 

6-8: Now I will tell you the remedial measures to be adopted to release the child born during gandanta from its evil effects. The father should see the child born only on the morning next to the end of the days of Sutaka (सूतक) or on any auspicious day after the performance of the remedial measures. The remedial measures are-

(1) Giving a bullock in charity, in the case of Tithi Gandanta. 

(2) Giving a cow with calf in charity in the case of Nakshatra gandanta. 

(3) Giving gold in charity in the case of Lagna Gandanta. 

(4) Performing Abhiseka (अभभषेक) of the child along with father if the birth is in the first part of gandanta and along with mother if the birth is in the second part of gandanta. 

द्वद्विीये िु सशशोमािुिथभर्षेकं च काियेि् । 

सुर्णेन िदधेण यथातर्त्तं द्वद्वजोत्तम । 

तिथथभेर्षाद्वदरूपं च कृ त्वा र्िसमन्तििम् ॥ ९॥ 

उपचािैयवथाशगक्त कलहोपरि पूजयेि् । 

पूजािे सतमदन्नज्यैहोम। 

कु याद्यथातर्थध ॥ १०॥ 

ब्राह्मणान् भोजयेि् पिादेर्ं दोर्षात्प्रमुच्यिे । 

आयुिािोग्यमैश्वयं सम्प्राप्नोति द्वदने द्वदने ॥ ११॥ 

9-11. Performance of Puja on the holy Kalasha of the idol of the deities of tithi (in case of tithi gandanta), Nakshatra in case of Nakshatra Gandanta) and Lagna (in case of Lagna Gandanta) made of 16 masas, 8 masas or 4 masas of gold as nay be possible followed by Havana and abhisheka according to procedure already described earlier. At the end as many Brahmins as may be possible within one's means should be fed. 

These remedial measures will ensure long life, good health and prosperity for the child. 

Notes: Unless one is himself fully conversant - with performance of religious rites, the remedies recommended' in his chapter, earlier and later chapters should be got performed by and under the directions of a learned priest because the full effects 

will be derived if the rites are performed correctly and according to procedure prescribed in the religious scriptures on his subject. 

# अथ अभुक्तमूलशान्त्यध्यायः ॥९३॥

# Chapter 93. Remedies from Birth in Abhukta Moola

ज्येष्ठामूलमयोयवस्मादथधपातर्न्द्रिाक्षसौ । 

महार्ैिाि् ियोाः सन्तन्धमवहादोर्षप्रदाः स्मृिाः ॥ १॥ 

अभुक्तमूलजं पुरं पुरीं र्ाऽष्टप परित्यजेि् । 

अथर्ाऽब्दाष्टकं िािस्तन्मुखं न तर्लोकयेि् ॥ २॥ 

1-2. The Sage Parāśara said-the ruling deity of Jyeshtha is Indra and the ruling deity of Moola is Rakshasa (राक्षस). As both the deities are inimical to each other, this gandanta is considered as the most evil. A boy or girl born during the period of Abhukta Moola should either be abandoned or the father should not see the face of the child for 8 years. Now I shall describe the remedial measures to obtain deliverance from the evil effects of birth during this extremely inauspicious period. 

िद्दोर्षपरिहािाथवमथ शान्तितर्थधं ब्रुर्े । 

िराऽदौ दोर्षबहुल्यान् मूलशान्तितनवगद्यिे ॥ ३॥ 

जन्मिो द्वादशाहे र्ा िदृक्षे र्ा शुभे द्वदने । 

जािस्य र्ाऽष्टमे र्र्षे शान्तिं कु याद् तर्धानिाः ॥ ४॥ 

3-4. In view of the extremely inauspicious effects of birth during Abhukta, I shall first describe the remedial measures to obtain relief from Moola (मूल शान्ती). The religious remedial rites should be performed after the 12th day after the birth, the next Janma Nakshatra day or on an auspicious day when the Moon and the stars are favourable. 

सुसमे च शुभे िाने गोमयेनोपलेष्टपिे । 

मण्डपं स्वगृहाि् प्राच्यामुदीच्यां र्ा प्रकल्पयेि् ॥ ५॥ 

चिुद्वािसमायुक्तं िोिणाद्यैिलङ्कृ िम् । 

कु ण्डं ग्रहाद्वदयज्ञाथं िद्बद्वहि प्रकल्पयेि् ॥ ६॥ 

सुर्णेन िदधेन िदधाधेन र्ा पुनाः । 

नक्षरदेर्िारूपं कु याद् तर्त्तानुसाििाः ॥ ७॥ 

श्यामर्णं महोग्रं च द्वद्वसशिस्कं र्ृकाननम् । 

# खड् गचमवधिं िद्वद् ध्येयं कु णपर्ाहनम् ॥ ८॥

5-8. Erect a canopy (मण्डप) with four arched gateways embellished with festoons (तोरणाद्वद से सुशोभभत) on a sacred spot besmeared with cow dung paste to the east or the north of house. Prepare there a pit $( \overrightarrow { \mathfrak { P } ^ { \mathfrak { V } } } )$ or (place there a square vessel of clay or metal) for performing Havana. Then according to one's means prepare or get prepared an idol of Rakshasa (the deity of the Nakshatra) of 16, 8 or 4 masas of gold as may be possible within one's means. 

The idol should be with a horrible looking face, black in colour, with two heads, two arms carrying a sword and a shield and seated on a dead body. 

सुर्णवस्य च मूल्यं र्ा िापगयत्वा प्रपूजयेि् । 

सुर्णं सर्वदैर्त्यं यिाः शािेर्षु तनसििम् ॥ ९॥ 

9: In the absence of an idol a piece of gold of the weight mentioned above should be used for worship, as gold is dear to all the deities. 

आचायं र्ियेि् पिाि् स्वस्तस्तर्ाचनुपूर्वकम् । 

कलशिापनं कु याि् स्वगृह्योक्ततर्धानिाः ॥ १०॥ 

पञ्चगव्याद्वदकं क्षेप्यं कलशे िीथवर्ारि च । 

शिौर्षध्याद्वदकं िर शिच्छच्छद्रघटे सक्षपेि् ॥ ११॥ 

र्ंशपारं च संिाप्य िर र्ै पसिमामुखम् । 

अचेयेगन्नऋव तिं देर्ं शुक्लर्िाक्षिाद्वदथभाः ॥ १२॥ 

इन्द्रं िदथधदेर्ं च जलं प्रत्यथधदैर्िम् । 

स्वस्वशाखोक्तमन्त्रेण प्रधानादीन्प्रपूजयेि् ॥ १३॥ 

देर्ाथधदेर्प्रीत्यथं होमं कु याद्यथातर्थध । 

अष्टोत्तिं सहस्रं र्ा शिं र्ा तनयिेब्दन्द्रयाः ॥ १४॥ 

मृत्युप्रशमनाथं च मन्त्रं रयम्बकं जपेि् । 

प्राथवयेच्च ििो देर्मथभर्षेकाथवमादिाि् ॥ १५॥ 

भद्रासनोपतर्ष्टस्य सिीपुरस्य मन्त्रतर्ि् । 

आचायो यजमानस्य कु याि् प्रीत्याथभर्षेचनम् ॥ १६॥ 

र्िािरििकु म्भाभ्यां स्नापयेत्तदनििम् । 

शुक्लाम्बिधिस्तद्वि् श्वेिगन्धानुलेपनाः ॥ १७॥ 

धेनुं पयस्तस्वनीं दद्यादाचायाय च शगक्तिाः । 

ऋन्तत्वग्भ्यो दसक्षणां दद्याद् ब्राह्मणांिाष्टप भोजयेि् ॥ १८॥ 

यत्पापं यच्च मे दौाःस्थ्यं सर्वगारेष्वर्स्थििम् । 

ित्सर्ं भक्षयाज्य त्वं लक्ष्मीं पुष्टष्टं च र्धवय ॥ १९॥ 

अनेनैर् िु मन्त्रेण सम्यगाज्यं तर्लोकयेि् । 

मूलगण्डोद्भर्स्तैर्ं सपवपापं प्रणश्यति ॥ २०॥ 

10-20: Thereafter the remedial rites should be performed in the following order-

(1) Select a learned priest to perform the religious rites according to prescribed procedure. 

(2) Install a kalasha and put in it Panchagavya (five articles yielded by a cow, namely, milk; curd, ghee, dung and urine) Shataushadhi (शतौषभर्) and water of the holy river (Ganges etc.). 

(3) Then install the idol of the Rakshasa of facing west on an earthen pot (घट) with one hundred tiny holes. After placing bamboo leaves on it, perform the worship of the idol by offering it white flowers, sandal and clothes etc. 

(4) Also, perform worship of its Adhideva Indra and Pratyadhideva Jala (जल - water). 

(5) Theo perform Havana to appease the deities. According to one's means 1008 or 108 oblations should be offered in the Havana. 

(6) After this to obtain deliverance from death, Mrityunjaya mantra (िंयम्बकं ) etc., should be recited and prayers offered' to all the deities for the purpose of Abhisheka. 

(7) The father, mother and the child should thereafter take bath from the water of the two kalashas. Then the parents dressed in white clothes and with white sandal paste besmeared on their foreheads, should give a cow with calf as a present (दशक्षणा) to the chief priest and feed the other priests and Brahmins according to one's means. 

(8) Lastly after reciting the (यत्पापं) etc., (see verse 19) mantra, the father, mother and the child should see the reflection of their faces in the ghee (melted ghee). 

By the performance of the remedial rites in the manner described, all evil effects of the birth during Abhukta Moola are completely wiped out. 

# अथ ज्येष्ठादद गण्डशान्त्यध्यायः ॥९४॥

# Chapter 94. Remedies from Effects of Birth in Jyeshtha Gandanta

ज्येष्ठागण्डािजािस्तु ष्टपिुाः स्वस्य च नाशकाः । 

िस्य शान्तितर्थधं र्क्ष्ये सर्वतर्घ्नोपशािये ॥ १॥ 

मूलशान्तिसमं सर्वमाराष्टप मण्डपाद्वदकम् । 

इन्द्रोऽर देर्िा िद्वदथधदेर्ोऽनलस्तथा ॥ २॥ 

तर्ज्ञेयं च िथा तर्प्र िक्षाः प्रत्यथधदैर्िम् । 

यथाशगक्त सुर्णेन कु याद्वदन्द्रस्वरूपकम् ॥ ३॥ 

र्ज्राङ्कशधिं द्वदव्यं गजिाजोपरिस्थििम् । 

शासलिण्डुलसंयुक्तकु म्भस्योपरि पूजयेि् ॥ ४॥ 

स्वस्वगृह्योक्तमन्त्रेण गन्धपुष्पाक्षिाद्वदथभाः । 

अथभर्षेकं च होमं च कु याद् ब्राह्मणभोजनम् ॥ ५॥ 

1-5. The Sage said-O Maitreya! Now I will describe to you the remedial measures to be adopted to ensure relief from the evil effects of Jyeshtha Gandanta. The erection of a canopy (मण्डप), installation of Kalasha, selection of a priest etc., will be done in the same manner as has been recommended for the Ahhukta Moola in the previous chapter. In this ceremony, Indra will be the Deity-in-chief, Adhideva will be Agni (Fire) and the Pratyadhideva will be Rakshasa. 

इन्द्रसूक्तं जपेद् भक्त्या मन्त्रं मृत्युञ्जयं िथा । 

प्राथवयेद्वदन्द्रदेर्ं च ििाः शान्तिमर्ाप्नुयाि् ॥ ६॥ 

6. Then the remedial sites should be performed in the following order-

(1) Install on a Kalasha full of paddy rice an idol of gold (according to ones means) with Indra seated on Airavat (एरावत) with Vajra Ankusha in his hands. 

(2) Perform worship of the chief deity Indra along with that of the Adhideva and the Pratyadhideva, with the recitation of their appropriate Mantras. 

(3) Perform Havana, Abhisheka and then feed the Brahmins in accordance with one’s means. 

In addition to the above, after doing Indrasukta and Mrityunjaya Japas, prayers may be offered to Indra. These measures will wipe out the evil effects of the Gandanta. 

# अथ र्ा शक्त्यभार्े िु कु याद् गोदानमेर् द्वह । यिाः समस्तभूदानाद् गोदानमतिरिच्यिे ॥ ७॥

7. In case the performance of remedial sites described above is beyond the means of any person, he should give a cow in charily. This will also appease the deities and promote relief from the evil effect, of the Gandanta. Because the giving a cow in charity has been considered superior remedial measure than giving in charity all the lands belonging to a person. 

मूलेन्द्राद्वहमघागण्डजािे दद्याद् गर्ां रयम् । गोयुग्मं पौष्णदास्रोत्थे गण्डािे च द्वद्वजन्मने ॥ ८॥ अन्यगण्डे च दयोगे ु गामेकां द्वह प्रदापयेि् । गोिभार्े च तर्प्राय दद्याि् िन्मूल्यमेर् द्वह ॥ ९॥ 

8-9. According to prescribed remedial measures, 3 cows, are to be given in charity in the case of Jyeshtha Moola and Ashlesha, Makha gandantas, 2 cows in Relief Ashwini gandantas and 1 cow in other gandantas or in any inauspicious Yoga. If cow or cows are not available, their actual value should be given in cash to a Brahmin. 

ज्येष्ठनक्षरजा कन्या तर्तनहन्ति धर्ाग्रजम् । तर्शाखान्त्यपदोत्पन्ना कन्या देर्िघातिनी ॥ १०॥ 

10. A girl born in Jyeshtha Nakshatra destroys (is the cause of death of) the elder brother of her husband and a girl born in fourth quarter of Visakha Nakshatra destroys (is the cause or death of) her husband's younger brother. Therefore, a cow should be given in charity at the time of the marriage of such girls to wipe out the aforesaid evil effects. 

िस्यााः प्रदानकालेऽिो गोदानमष्टप काियेि् । आश्लेर्षान्त्यष्टरपादोत्थौ मूलाद्यष्टरपदोद्भर्ौ ॥ ११॥ कन्यासुिौ हिाः श्विूं श्वशुिञ्च यथाक्रमम् । ियोतर्वर्ाहकालेऽिाः शान्तिं कु याद् तर्चक्षणाः ॥ १२॥ ित्तदोर्षतर्नाशाय यथातर्त्तानुसाििाः । धर्ाग्रजद्यभार्े िु न दोर्षाय प्रजायिे ॥ १३॥ 

11-13. A boy or girl born in the 2nd, 3rd or 4th quarter of Ashlesha Nakshatra destroys his/her mother-in-law and a boy or a girl born in 1st, 2nd or 3rd quarter of Moola Nakshatra becomes the destroyer (cause of death) of his/her father-in-law. 

Therefore, suitable measures, as may be possible within one's means, should be taken at the time of the marriage of such boys and girls. There will be no evil effect if the husband has no elder brothers (अरज). 

# अथ त्रीतरजन्मशान्त्यध्यायः ॥९५॥

# Chapter 95. Remedies from Effects of Birth of a Daughter after 3 sons

अथाऽन्यि् संप्रर्क्ष्यातम जन्मदोर्षप्रदं द्वद्वज । 

सुित्र्ये सुिाजन्म िररये सुिजन्म चेि् ॥ १॥ 

िदाऽरिष्टभयं ज्ञेयं ष्टपिृमािृकु लद्वये । 

िर शान्तितर्थधं कु याद् तर्त्तशाठ्यतर्र्सजविाः ॥ २॥ 

1-2. The Sage said-O Brahmin! I will now tell you about other kinds of inauspicious births. The birth of a daughter after the birth of three sons or the birth of a son after the birth of three daughters is ominous for both the maternal and paternal families of such children. Therefore, remedial measures described below may be taken to get deliverance from these evil effects. 

सूिकािेऽथ र्ा शुद्धे समये च शुभे द्वदने । 

आचायवमृन्तत्वजो र्ृत्वा ग्रहयज्ञपुिस्सिम् ॥ ३॥ 

ब्रह्मतर्ष्णु महेशेन्द्रप्रतिमााः स्वणवजााः शुभााः । 

पूजयेद् धान्यिासशिकलशोपरि भगक्तिाः ॥ ४॥ 

चत्वारि रुद्रसूक्तातन शान्तिसूक्तातन सर्वशाः । 

तर्प्र एको जपेद् होमकाले च सुश्रचसंयिाः ॥ ५॥ 

आचायो जुहुयात्तर सतमदाज्यतिलांिरुम् । 

अष्टोत्तिं सहस्रं र्ा शिं र्ाऽष्टौ च तर्ंशतिम् ॥ ६॥ 

ब्रह्माद्वदसर्वदेर्ेभ्याः स्वस्वगृह्योक्तमन्त्रिाः । 

ििाः स्तस्वष्टकृ िं हुत्वा बसलं पूणाहुतिं पुनाः ॥ ७॥ 

अथभर्षेकं च जािस्य सकु टुम्बस्य काियेि् । 

ऋन्तत्वग्भ्यो दसक्षणां दद्याद् ब्राह्मणांिाष्टप भोजयेि् ॥ ८॥ 

कांस्याज्यर्ीक्षणं कृ त्वा दीनानाथांि िपवयेि् । 

एर्ं शान्त्या च मैरेय सर्ारिष्टं तर्लीयिे ॥ ९॥ 

3-9: The rites should be performed on the morning next to the last day of Sutak (सूतक), or on any other auspicious day in the following order-

(1) After selecting a priest and some Brahmins to perform the remedial religious rites, the priest after paying obeisance to the nine planets should install four Kaiashas on a beep of paddy, place the idols of Brahma, Vishnu, Mahesha and Indra made of gold on them and perform their worship in the prescribed manner., 

(2) A Brahmin (an assistant of the priest) after taking bath etc. should recite four Rudra Suktas and the whole of Shanti Sukta. 

(3) The priest should perform Havana with samidha (सतमघा), ghee and seaman seeds (ततल) 1008, 108 or 28 times (as may be possible within one's means) with the recitation of the, prescribed mantras of Brahma, Vishnu, Mahesha and Indra. 

(4) Svistkrata and Poornahuti (श्मस्वष्टकृ त और पूणध आहुतत) and Abhishek of the child with his family should be done and presents in cash should be given to the priest and his assistants according to one's means, 

(5) The Brahmins should be fed-this also be done according to one's mean. 

(6) The father and mother of the child should see their reflections in the ghee kept in a bronze vessel. 

(7) Lastly grains and clothes should be distributed to the poor and the needy. 

By the performance of the above remedial rites, the evil effects are wiped out and the child and his parents etc. enjoy happiness. 

# अथ प्रसितिकारशान्त्यध्यायः ॥९६॥

# Chapter 96. Remedies from Evil Effects of Unusual Delivery

अथाऽहं सम्प्रर्क्ष्यातम तर्कािं प्रसर्ोद्भर्म् । 

येनाऽरिष्टं समस्तस्य ग्रामस्य च कु लस्य च ॥ १॥ 

अत्यल्पे र्ाऽथधके काले प्रसर्ो यद्वद जायिे । 

हीनाङ्गोर्ाऽथधकाङ्गो र्ा तर्सशिा द्वद्वसशिास्तथा ॥ २॥ 

नाया पश्वाकृ तिर्ाष्टप पशुष्वष्टप निाकृ तिाः । 

प्रसर्स्य तर्कािोऽयं तर्नाशायोपजायिे ॥ ३॥ 

1-3. The Sage said-O Brahmin! I will now tell you about suspicious and unusual deliveries by women which are ominous for the village, town and the country. These may be of the following kinds-

(1) Delivery of a child 2, 3 or 4 months earlier or later from the approximate due date. 

(2) Delivery of a child without hands, feet or any other limba, without head or with two heads. 

(3) Delivery of an animal shaped being by a woman or a human shaped being by an animal. 

यस्य ण्डियााः पशुनां र्ा तर्कािााः प्रसर्ोद्भर्ाः । 

अतनष्टं भर्ने िस्य कु लेऽष्टप च महद् भर्ेि् ॥ ४॥ 

िद्दोर्षपरिहािाथं शान्तिाः काया प्रयत्निाः । 

िी र्ा गौर्ंडर्ा र्ाष्टप परित्याज्या द्वहिाथथवना ॥ ५॥ 

4-5. Deliveries of these kinds by women or cows in a house are ominous for all the member of the family living there. Therefore, remedial measures are essential for obtaining relief from their e evil effects. The best remedial measure will to abandon (or turn out from the house) such women and animal, (cows, mare etc.). 

नायााः पञ्चदशे र्र्षे जन्मिाः र्षोडशोऽष्टप र्ा । 

गभो र्ा प्रसर्ो र्ाऽष्टप न शुभाय प्रजायिे ॥ ६॥ 

ससंहिासशस्थििेऽकव गौनक्रिे मद्वहर्षी िथा । 

प्रसूिा स्वातमनं हन्ति स्वयं चाष्टप तर्नश्यति ॥ ७॥ 

ब्राह्मणाय प्रदद्याि् िां शान्तिं र्ाष्टप समाचिेि् । ब्रह्मतर्ष्णुमहेशानां ग्रहाणां चैर् पूजनम् ॥ ८॥ सर्ं होमाद्वदकं कमव कु याि् ष्टरििशान्तिर्ि् । ििो गृहो सुखी भूत्वा सर्वपापैाः प्रमुच्यिे ॥ ९॥ 

6-9: It is considered inauspicious for a girl to become pregnant or to deliver a child in her 15th or 16th year of birth. If a cow delivers when the Sun is in Leo, or a female buffalo delivers when the Sun is in Capricorn, they are disastrous to their owner and the person who looks after them. Therefore, either such cow or buffalo should be given away to a Brahmin or suitable remedial measures should be taken to escape from the e foresaid evil effects. The remedial measures to be adopted are the same as given in verses 3.9 in chapter 95(previous chapter) 

एर्ं त्वरिष्टे सम्प्राप्ते निाः शान्तिं किोति याः । सर्ान् कामानर्ाप्नोति श्रचिजीर्ी सुखी च साः ॥ १०॥ 

10. Thus whenever there is any kind of Arishta (अररष्ट), adoption of appropriate remedial measures will ensure long life, happiness and prosperity for the person concerned. 

# अथोपसिंहाराध्यायः ॥९७॥

# Chapter 97. Conclusion

यच्छािं ब्रह्मणा प्रोक्तं नािदाय महात्मने । 

िदेर् शौनकाद्वदभ्यो नािदाः प्राह सादिम् ॥ १॥ 

ििो मया यथा ज्ञािं िुभ्यमुक्तं िथा द्वद्वज । 

नासूयकाय दािव्यं पितनन्दाििाय र्ा ॥ २॥ 

जडाय दतर्वनीिाय ु नाज्ञािाय कदाचन । 

देयमेित्सुरिलाय भक्ताय सत्यर्ाद्वदने ॥ ३॥ 

मेधातर्ने तर्नीिाय सम्यग् ज्ञािकु लाय च । 

पुण्यदं ज्यौतिर्षं शािमग्र्यं र्ेदाङ्गमुत्तमम् ॥ ४॥ 

1-4. Maharishi Parāśara said-O Brahmin! I have described to you the Jyotisha Shastra as narrated by Lord Brahma to the Sage Narada and by Narada to Shaunaka and other Sages from whom I received the knowledge of this Shastra. I have narrated the same Jyotisha Shastra which I learnt from them. Do not impart the knowledge of this Shastra to one who is insignificative, slanders or calumniates others, is not intelligent, is wicked and unknown to you. Teach this supreme Vedanga. Jyotisha Shastra (Science of Astrology) only to one who is gentle and amiable, devoted, truthful, brilliant and welt known to you. 

जानाति कालमानं यो ग्रहक्षाणां च संस्थितिम् । 

होिाशाितमदं सम्यक् स तर्जानाति नाऽपिाः ॥ ५॥ 

होिाशािाथवित्त्वज्ञाः सत्यर्ाग् तर्सजिेब्दन्द्रयाः । 

शुभाऽशुभं फलं र्गक्त सत्यं िद्वचनं भर्ेि् ॥ ६॥ 

5-6: Only that person who possesses adequate knowledge of time and the positions of planets and constellation (oak Shastras) can understand this Horā Shastra. Only that person who has complete knowledge of the Horā Shastra and who is truthful can make correct favourable or unfavourable predictions. 

ये सुशािं पठिीदं ये र्ा शृण्वन्ति भगक्तिाः । 

िेर्षांमायुबवलं तर्त्तं र्ृणद्धमेति यशाः सदा ॥ ७॥ 

7. One who leads or listens with attention and devotion to this most excellent Horā Shastra, becomes long-lived and is blessed with increase in his strength, wealth and good reputation 

इत्थं पिाशिेणोक्तं होिाशािं चमत्कृ िम् । नर्ं नर्जनप्रीत्यै तर्तर्धाध्यायसंयुिम् ॥ ८॥ िेष्ठं जगणद्धिायेदं मैरेयाय द्वद्वजन्मने । ििाः प्रचरििं पृथ्व्यामादृिं सादिं जनैाः ॥ ९॥ 

8-9. Thus, was narrated by Maharishi Parāśara to Maitreya, this novel Horā Shastra containing invaluable and uncommon material from (many) ancient scriptures on Astrology, for the benefit of the world at large. Afterwards it came into usage on the earth and received reverence from all. 

ग्रिेऽस्तस्मन् पृथगध्यायैतर्वर्षया तर्तनर्ेसशिााः । सृष्टष्टक्रमोऽर्िािाि गुणााः खेटस्य भस्य च ॥ १०॥ तर्शेर्षलग्नं र्गाि िद्वद्वर्ेकि िासशदृक् । अरिष्टं िद्वद्वभङ्गि तर्र्ेको भार्जस्तथा ॥ ११॥ भार्ानां च फलाध्यायो भार्ेशोत्थफलं िथा । अप्रकाशफलं स्पष्टखेटदृष्टष्टप्रसाधनम् ॥ १२॥ ििाः स्पष्टबलाध्यायाः इष्टकष्टप्रसाधनम् । पदं चोपपदं िद्वदगवला त्वथ कािकााः ॥ १३॥ कािकांशफलं योगकािकाध्याय एर् च । नाभसा तर्तर्धा योगािन्द्रयोगोऽकव योगकाः ॥ १४॥ िाजयोगस्तिाः प्रोक्तो िाजसम्बन्धयोगकाः । तर्शेर्षधनयोगाि योगा दारिद्र्यकािकााः ॥ १५॥ नानातर्धदशाध्यायास्तत्फलाध्यायाः संयुिााः ॥ १६॥ अिाःप्रत्यििप्राणसूक्ष्मसंज्ञाि िखद्भदााः । सूयाद्यष्टकर्गवि ष्टरकोणपरिशोधनम् ॥ १७॥ एकाथधपत्यसंशुणद्धस्तिाः ष्टपण्डप्रसाधनम् । िििाऽष्टकर्गाणां प्रस्फु टातन फलातन च ॥ १८॥ ििोऽप्यष्टकर्गायुाःसाधनं च ििाः पिम् । समुदायाष्टर्गोत्थफलाध्यायाः परिस्फु टाः ॥ १९॥ ग्रहिस्तश्मफलाध्यायाः सुदशवनफलं िथा । महापुरुर्षश्रचिातन महाभूिफलातन च ॥ २०॥ गुणरयफलाध्यायस्तिोऽप्यज्ञािजन्मनाम् । 

जन्मलग्नाद्वदतर्ज्ञानं प्रव्रज्यालक्षणातन च ॥ २१॥ 

िीणां च फलर्ैष्ट्यमङ्गलक्ष्मफलातन च । 

पूर्वपापोत्थशापोत्थयोगा र्ैपुत्र्यकािकााः ॥ २२॥ 

सत्पुरप्राप्त्युपायाि सहैर् प्रतिपाद्वदिााः । 

जन्मन्यतनष्टलग्नक्षवतिथ्याद्वदप्रतिपादनम् ॥ २३॥ 

ित्तच्छान्तितर्थधिैर् संक्षेपेण प्रदसशविाः । 

प्रसर्स्य तर्कािाि कथथिााः शान्तिसंयुिााः ॥ २४॥ 

एर्ं जािकर्येऽर तनतर्ष्टा तर्र्षयााः शिम् । 

तर्ज्ञाय तर्बुधास्त्वेिान् प्राप्नुर्िु यशाः श्रियम् ॥ २५॥ 

10-25: In these verses, have been described the subject matters of all the chapters contained in this book and their importance. This information has been given in detail in the Table of contents in Vol I and II of this book.
